
 
	Śrīpūjyapādācāryaviracitā Sarvārthasiddhiḥ
	 
	  Prathamo ’dhyāyaḥ

	   
 mokṣamārgasya netāraṃ bhetāraṃ karmabhūbhṛtām | 
 jñātāraṃ viśvatattvānāṃ vande tadguṇalabdhaye ||1|| 
 
 §§ 1–250 
 § 1. kaścid bhavyaḥ pratyāsannaniṣṭhaḥ prajñāvān svahitam upalipsur vivivkte paramaramye bhavyasattvaviśrāmāspade kvacid āśramapade munipariṣan madye saṃniṣaṇṇaṃ mūrttam iva mokṣamārgam avāgvisargaṃ vapuṣā nirūpayantaṃ yuktyāgamakuśalaṃ parahitapratipādanaikakāryam āryaniṣevyaṃ nirgranthācāryavaryam upasadya savinayaṃ paripṛcchati sma. bhagavan, kiṃ nu khalu ātmane hitaṃ syād iti ? sa āha mokṣa iti. sa eva punaḥ pratyāha — kiṃ svarūpo ’sau mokṣaḥ kaścāsya prāptyupāya iti? ācārya āha — niravaśeṣanirākṛtakarmamalakalaṃkasyāśarīrasyātmano ’cintyasvābhāvikajñānādiguṇam avyābādhasukham ātyantikam avasthāntaraṃ mokṣa iti. 
 § 2. tasyātyantaparokṣatvāc chadmasthāḥ pravādinas tīrthakaraṃ manyās tasya svarūpam aspṛśantībhir vāgbhir yuktyābhāsanibandhanābhir anyathaiva parikalpayanti  caitanyaṃ puruṣasya svarūpam, tacca jñeyākāraparicchedaparāṅmukham  iti. tat sad apy asad eva nirākāratvād iti.  buddhyādivaiśeṣikaguṇocchedaḥ puruṣasya mokṣaḥ  iti. tad api parikalpanam asad eva, viśeṣalakṣaṇaśūnyasyāvastutvāt.  pradīpanirvāṇakalpam ātmanirvāṇam  iti ca. tasya kharaviṣāṇakalpanā tair evāhatya nirūpitā. ity evam ādi. tasya svarūpam anavadyam uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ. 
 § 3. tatprāptyupāyaṃ praty api te visaṃvadante —  jñānād eva cāritranirapekṣāt tatprāptiḥ, śraddhānamātrād eva vā, jñānanirapekṣāc cāritramātrād eva  iti ca. vyādhyabhibhūtasya tadvinivṛttyupāyabhūtabheṣajaviṣayavyastajñānādisādhanatvābhāvavad vyastaṃ jñānādir mokṣaprātyupāyo na bhavati. * 
 § 4. kiṃ tarhi? tat tritayaṃ samuditam ity āha — 
 samyagdarśanajñānacāritrāṇi mokṣamārgaḥ || 
 § 5. samyag ity avyutpannaḥ śabdo vyutpanno vā. añcateḥ kvau samañcatīti samyag iti. asyārthaḥ praśaṃsā. sa pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate. samyagdarśanaṃ samyagjñānaṃ samyakcāritram iti. eteṣāṃ svarūpaṃ lakṣaṇato vidhānataś ca purastād vistareṇa nirdekṣyāmaḥ. uddeśamātraṃ tv idam ucyate — padārthānāṃ yāthātmyapratipattiviṣayaśraddhānasaṃgrahārthaṃ darśanasya samyagviśeṣaṇam. yena yena prakāreṇa jīvādayaḥ padarthā vyavasthitās tena tenāvagamaḥ samyagjñānam. vimohasaṃśayaviparyayanivṛttyarthaṃ samyagviśeṣaṇam. saṃsārakāraṇanivṛttiṃ pratyāgūrṇasya jñānavataḥ karmādānanimittakriyoparamaḥ samyakcāritram. ajñānapūrvakācaraṇanivṛttyarthaṃ samyagviśeṣaṇam. 
 § 6. paśyati dṛśyate ’nena dṛṣṭimātraṃ vā darśanam. jānāti jñāyate ’nena jñaptimātraṃ vā jñānam. carati caryate ’nena caraṇamātram vā cāritram. nanv evaṃ sa eva kartā sa eva karaṇam ity āyātam. tac ca viruddham. satyaṃ, svapariṇāmapariṇāminor bhedavivakṣāyāṃ tathābhidhānāt. yathāgnir dahatīndhanaṃ dāhapariṇāmena. uktaḥ kartrādisādhanabhāvaḥ paryāyaparyāyiṇor ekatvānekatvaṃ pratyanekāntopapattau svātantryapāratantryavivakṣopapatter ekasminn apy arthe na virudhyate. agnau dahanādikriyāyāḥ kartrādisādhanabhāvavat. 
 § 7. jñānagrahaṇam ādau nyāyyaṃ, darśanasya tatpūrvakatvāt alpāctaratvāc ca. naitad yuktaṃ, yugapad utpatteḥ. yadāsya darśanamohasyopaśamāt kṣayāt kṣayopaśamād vā ātmā samyagdarśanaparyāyeṇāvirbhavati tadaiva tasya matyajñānaśrutājnānanivṛttipūrvakaṃ matijñānaṃ śrutajñānaṃ cāvirbhavati ghanapaṭalavigame savituḥ pratāpaprakāśābhivyaktivat. alpāctarād abhyarhitaṃ pūrvaṃ nipatati. katham abhyarhitatvam? jñānasya samyagvyapadeśahetutvāt. cāritrāt pūrvaṃ jñānaṃ prayuktaṃ, tatpūrvakatvāc cāritrasya. 
 § 8. sarvakarmavipramokṣo mokṣaḥ. tatprāptyupāyo mārgaḥ. mārga iti caikavacananirdeśaḥ samas tasya mārgabhāvajñāpanārthaḥ. tena vyastasya mārgatvanivṛttiḥ kṛtā bhavati. ataḥ samyagdarśanaṃ samyagjñānaṃ samyakcāritram ity etat tritayaṃ samuditaṃ mokṣasya sākṣān mārgo veditavyaḥ. 
 § 9. tatrādāv uddiṣṭasya samyagdarśanasya lakṣaṇanirdeśārtham idam ucyate — 
 tattvārthaśraddhānaṃ samyagdarśanam || 
 § 10. tattvaśabdo bhāvasāmānyavācī. katham? tad iti sarvanāmapadam. sarvanāma ca sāmānye vartate. tasya bhāvas tattvam. tasya kasya? yo ’rtho yathāvasthitas tathā tasya bhavanam ity arthaḥ. aryata ity artho niścīyata iti yāvat. tattvenārthas tattvārthaḥ. athavā bhāvena bhāvavato ’bhidhānam, tadavyatirekāt. tattvam evārthas tattvārthaḥ. tattvārthasya śraddhānaṃ tattvārthaśraddhānaṃ samyagdarśanaṃ pratyetavyam. tattvārthaś ca vakṣamāṇo jīvādiḥ. 
 § 11. dṛśer ālokārthatvāt śraddhānārthagatir nopapadyate? dhātunām anekārthatatvād adoṣaḥ. prasiddhārthatyāgaḥ kuta iti cet? mokṣamārgaprakaraṇāt. tattvārthaśraddhānaṃ hy ātmapariṇāmo mokṣasādhanaṃ yujyate, bhavyajīvaviṣayatvāt. ālokakas tu cakṣurādinimittaḥ sarvasaṃsārijīvasādhāraṇatvān na mokṣamārgo yuktaḥ. 
 § 12. arthaśraddhānām iti cet? sarvārthaprasaṃgaḥ. tattvaśraddhānam iti cet? bhāvamātraprasaṃgaḥ. ‘sattādravyatvaguṇatvakarmatvādi tattvam’ iti kaiścit kalpyata iti. tattvam ekatvam iti vā sarvaikyagrahaṇaprasaṃgaḥ. ‘puruṣa evedaṃ sarvam’ ity ādi kaiścit kalpyata iti. evaṃ sati dṛṣṭeṣṭavirodhaḥ. tasmād avyabhicārārtham ubhayor upādānam. tad dvividhaṃ, sarāgavītarāgaviṣayabhedāt praśamasaṃvegānukampāstikyādyabhivyaktilakṣaṇaṃ prathamam. ātmaviśuddhimātram itarat. 
 § 13. athaitat samyagdarśanaṃ jīvādipadārthaviṣayaṃ katham utpadyata ity ata āha — 
 tannisargād adhigamād vā || 
 § 14. nisargaḥ svabhāva ity arthaḥ. adhigamo ’rthāvabodhaḥ. tayor hetutvena nirdeśaḥ. kasyāḥ? kriyāyāḥ. kā ca kriyā? utpadyata ity adhyāhriyate, sopaskāratvāt sūtrāṇām. tad etat samyagdarśanaṃ nisargād adhigamād votpadyata iti. 
 § 15. atrāha — nisargaje samyagdarśane ’rthādhigamaḥ syād vā na vā. yady asti, tad api adhigamajam eva nārthāntaram. atha nāsti, katham anavabuddhatattvasyārthaśraddhānām iti? naiṣa doṣaḥ, ubhayatra samyagdarśane antaraṅgo hetus tulyo darśanamohasyopaśamaḥ kṣayaḥ kṣayopaśamo vā. tasmin sati yad bāhyopadeśāvṛte prādur bhavati tan naisargikam. yat paropadeśapūrvakaṃ jīvādy adhigamanimittaṃ tad uttaram. ity anayor ayaṃ bhedaḥ. 
 § 16. tadgrahaṇaṃ kim artham? anantaranirdeśārtham. anantaraṃ samyagdarśanaṃ tadity anena nirdiśyate. itarathā mokṣamārgo ’pi prakṛtas tasyābhisaṃbandhaḥ syāt. nanu ca ‘anantarasya vidhir vā bhavati pratiṣedho vā’ ity anantarasya samyagdarśanasya grahaṇaṃ siddham iti cet? na, ‘pratyāsatteḥ pradhānaṃ balīyaḥ’ iti mokṣamārga eva saṃbadyeta. tasmāt tadvacanaṃ kriyate. 
 § 17. tattvārthaśraddhānaṃ samyagdarśanam ity uktam. atha kiṃ tattvam ity ata idam āha — 
 jīvājīvāsravabandhasaṃvaranirjarāmokṣās tattvam || 
 § 18. tatra cetanālakṣaṇo jīvaḥ. sā ca jñānādibhedād anekadhā bhidyate. tadviparyayalakṣaṇo ’jīvaḥ. śubhāśubhakarmāgamadvārarūpaṃ āsravaḥ. ātmakarmaṇor anyo ‘nyapradeśānupraveśātmako bandhaḥ. āsravanirodhalakṣaṇaḥ saṃvaraḥ. ekadeśakarmasaṃkṣayalakṣaṇā nirjarā. kṛtsnakarmaviyogalakṣaṇo mokṣaḥ. eṣāṃ prapañca uttaratra vakṣyate. sarvasya phalasyātmādhīnatvād ādau jīvagrahaṇam. tadupakārāthatvāt tadanantaram ajīvābhidhānam. tadubhayaviṣayatvāt tadanantaram āsravagrahaṇam. tatpūrvakatvāt tadanantaraṃ bandhābhidhānam. saṃvṛtasya bandhābhāvāt tatpratyanīkapratipattyarthaṃ tadanantaraṃ saṃvaravacanam. saṃvare sati nirjaropapattes tadantike nirjarāvacanam. ante prāpyatvān mokṣasyānte vacanam. 
 § 19. iha puṇyapāpagrahaṇaṃ kartavyam. ‘nava padārthāḥ’ iti anyair apy uktatvāt. na kartavyam āsrave bandhe cāntarbhāvāt. yady evam āsravādigrahaṇam anarthakam, jīvājīvayor antarbhāvāt. nānarthakam. iha mokṣaḥ prakṛtaḥ. so ’vaśyaṃ nirdeṣṭavyaḥ. sa ca saṃsārapūrvakaḥ. saṃsārasya pradhānahetur āsravo bandhaś ca. mokṣasya pradhānahetuḥ saṃvaro nirjarā ca. ataḥ pradhānahetuhetumatphalanidarśanārthatvāt pṛthagupadeśaḥ kṛtaḥ. dṛśyate hi sāmānye ’ntarbhūtasyāpi viśeṣasya pṛthagupādānaṃ prayojanārtham. ‘kṣatriyā āyātāḥ sūravarmā ’pi’ iti. 
 § 20. tattvaśabdo bhāvavācīty uktaḥ. sa kathaṃ jīvādibhir dravyavacanaiḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ pratipadyate? avyatirekāt tadbhāvādhyāropāc ca sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ bhavati. yathā ‘upayoga evātmā’ iti. yady evaṃ tattalliṅgasaṃkhyānuvṛttiḥ prāpnoti? ‘viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyasaṃbande saty api śabdaśaktivyapekṣayā upāttaliṅgasaṃkhyāvyatikramo na bhavati.’ ayaṃ krama ādisūtre ’pi yojyaḥ. 
 § 21. evam eṣām uddiṣṭāṇāṃ samyagdarśanādīnām jīvādīnāṃ ca saṃvyavahāraviśeṣavyabhicāranivṛtttyartham āha — 
 nāmasthāpanādravyabhāvatas tannyāsaḥ || 
 § 22. atadguṇe vastuni saṃvyavahārārthaṃ puruṣakārān niyujyamānaṃ saṃjñākarma nāma. kāṣṭhapustacitrakarmākṣanikṣepādiṣu so ’yam iti sthāpyamānā sthāpanā. guṇair guṇān vā drutaṃ gataṃ guṇair droṣyate guṇān droṣyatīti vā dravyam. vartamānatatparyāyopalakṣitaṃ dravyaṃ bhāvaḥ. tad yathā, nāmajīvaḥ sthāpanājīvo dravyajīvo bhāvajīva iti caturdhā jīvaśabdārtho nyasyate. jīvanaguṇam anapekṣya yasya kasyacin nāma kriyamāṇaṃ nāma jīvaḥ. akṣanikṣepādiṣu jīva iti vā manuṣyajīva iti va vyavasthāpyamānaḥ sthāpanājīvaḥ. dravyajīvo dvividhaḥ āgamadravyajīvo noāgamadravyajīvaś ceti. tatra jīvaprābhṛtajñāyī manuṣyajīvaprābhṛtajñāyī vā anupayukta ātmā āgamadravyajīvaḥ. noāgamadravyajīvas tredhā vyavatiṣṭhate jñāyakaśarīrabhāvitadvyatiriktabhedāt. tatra jñātur yac charīraṃ trikālagocaraṃ taj jñāyakaśarīraṃ. sāmānyāpekṣayā noāgamabhāvijīvo nāsti, jīvanasāmānyasya sadāpi vidyamānatvāt. viśeṣāpekṣayā tv asti. gatyantare jīvo vyavasthito manuṣyabhavaprāptiṃ pratyabhimukho manuṣyabhāvijīvaḥ. tadvyatiriktaḥ karmanokarmavikalpaḥ. bhāvajīvo dvividhaḥ āgamabhāvajīvo noāgamabhāvajīvaś ceti. tatra jīvaprābhṛtaviṣayopayogāviṣṭo manuṣyajīvaprābhṛtaviṣayopayogayukto vā ātmā āgamabhāvajīvaḥ. jīvanaparyāyeṇa manuṣyajīvatvaparyāyeṇa vā samāviṣṭa ātmā noāgamabhāvajīvaḥ. evam itareṣām api padārthānāṃ nāmādinikṣepavidhir niyojyaḥ. sa kim arthaḥ? aprakṛtanirākaraṇāya prakṛtanirūpaṇāya ca. nikṣepavidhinā śabdārthaḥ prastīryate. tac chabdagrahaṇaṃ kim artham? sarvasaṃgrahārtham. asati hi tacchabde samyagdarśanādīnāṃ pradhānānām eva nyāsenābhisaṃbandhaḥ syāt, tadviṣayabhāvenopagṛhītānāṃ jīvādīnāṃ apradhānānāṃ na syāt. tacchabdagrahaṇe punaḥ kriyamāṇe sati sāmarthyāt pradhānānām apradhānānāṃ ca grahaṇaṃ siddhaṃ bhavati. 
 § 23. evaṃ nāmādibhiḥ prastīrṇānām adhikṛtānāṃ tattvādhigamaḥ kutaḥ ity ata idam ucyate — 
 pramāṇanayair adhigamaḥ || 
 § 24. nāmādinikṣepavidhinopakṣiptānāṃ jīvādīnāṃ tattvaṃ pramāṇābhyāṃ nayaīś cādhigamyate. pramāṇanayā vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇavikalpāḥ. tatra pramāṇaṃ dvividhaṃ svārthaṃ parārthaṃ ca. tatra svārthaṃ pramāṇaṃ śrutavarjjam. śrutaṃ punaḥ svārthaṃ bhavati parārthaṃ ca. jñānātmakaṃ svārthaṃ vacanātmakaṃ parārtham. tadvikalpā nayāḥ. atrāha — nayaśabdasya alpāctaratvāt pūrvanipātaḥ prāpnoti. naiṣa doṣaḥ. abhyarhitatvāt pramāṇasya pūrvanipātaḥ. abhyarhitatvaṃ ca sarvato balīyaḥ. kuto ’bhyarhitatvam? nayaprarūpaṇaprabhavayonitvāt. evaṃ hy uktaṃ  pragṛhya pramāṇataḥ pariṇativiśeṣād arthāvadhāraṇaṃ nayaḥ  iti. sakalaviṣayatvāc ca pramāṇasya. tathā coktaṃ  sakalādeśaḥ pramānādhīno vikalādeśo nayādhīnaḥ  iti. nayo dvividhaḥ dravyārthikaḥ paryāyārthikaś ca. paryāyārthikanayena bhāvatattvam adhigantavyam. itareṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ dravyārthikanayena, sāmānyātmakatvāt. dravyam arthaḥ prayojanam asyety asau dravyārthikaḥ. paryāyo ’rthaḥ prayojanam asyety asau paryāyārthikaḥ. tatsarvaṃ samuditaṃ pramāṇenādhigantavyam. 
 § 25. evaṃ pramāṇanayair adhigatānāṃ jīvādīnāṃ punar apy adhigamopāyāntarapradarśanārtham āha — 
 nirdeśasvāmitvasādhanādhikaraṇasthitividhānataḥ || 
 § 26. nirdeśaḥ svarūpābhidhānam. svāmitvam ādhipatyam. sādhanam utpattinimittam. adhikaraṇam adhiṣṭhānam. stithiḥ kālaparicchedaḥ. vidhānaṃ prakāraḥ. tatra samyagdarśanaṃ kim iti praśne tattvārthaśraddhānām iti nirdeśo nāmādir vā. kasyety ukte sāmānyena jīvasya. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau sarvāsu pṛthivīṣu nārakāṇām paryāptakānām aupaśamikaṃ kṣāyopaśamikaṃ cāsti. prathamāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ paryāptāparyāptakānāṃ kṣāyikaṃ kṣāyopaśamikaṃ cāsti. tiryaggatau tiraścāṃ paryāptakānām aupaśamikam asti. kṣāyikaṃ kṣāyopaśamikaṃ ca paryāptāparyāptakānām asti. tiraścīnāṃ kṣāyikaṃ nāsti. aupaśamikaṃ kṣāyopaśamikaṃ ca paryāptikānām eva nāparyāptikānām. manuṣyagatau manuṣyāṇāṃ paryāptāparyāptakānāṃ kṣāyikaṃ kṣāyopaśamikaṃ cāsti. aupaśamikaṃ paryāptakānām eva nāparyāptakānām. mānuṣīṇāṃ tritayam apy asti paryāptikānām eva nāparyāptikānām. devagatau devānāṃ paryāptāparyāptakānāṃ tritayam apy asti. aupaśamikam aparyāptakānāṃ katham iti cec cāritramohopaśamena saha mṛtān prati. bhavanavāsivyantarajyotiṣkāṇāṃ devānāṃ devīnāṃ ca saudharmaiśānakalpavāsinīnāṃ ca kṣāyikaṃ nāsti. teṣāṃ paryāptakānām aupaśamikaṃ kṣāyopaśamikaṃ cāsti. 
 § 27. indriyānuvādena pañcendriyāṇāṃ saṃjñināṃ tritayam apy asti netareṣām. kāyānuvādena trasakāyikānāṃ tritayam apy asti netareṣām. yogānuvādena trayāṇāṃ yogānāṃ tritayam apy asti. ayogināṃ kṣāyikam eva. vedānuvādena trivedānāṃ tritayam apy asti. apagatavedānām aupaṣamikaṃ kṣāyikaṃ cāsti. kaṣāyānuvādena catuṣkaṣāyāṇāṃ tritayam apy asti. akaṣāyāṇām aupaṣamikaṃ kṣāyikaṃ cāsti. jñānānuvādena ābhinibodhikaśrutāvadhikamanaḥparyayajñānināṃ tritayam apy asti. kevalajñānināṃ kṣāyikam eva. saṃyamānuvādena sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanāsaṃyatānāṃ tritayam apy asti. parihāraviśuddhisaṃyatānām aupaśamikaṃ nāsti, itarad dvitayam apy asti, sūkṣmasāṃparāyayathākhyātasaṃyatānām aupaśamikaṃ kṣāyikaṃ cāsti, saṃyatāsaṃyatānām asaṃyatānām ca tritayam apy asti. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśanācakṣurdarśanāvadhidarśanināṃ tritayam apy asti, kevaladarśanināṃ kṣāyikam eva. leśyānuvādena ṣaḍleśyānāṃ tritayam apy asti, aleśyānāṃ kṣāyikam eva. bhavyānuvādena bhavyānāṃ tritayam apy asti, nābhavyānām. samyaktvānuvādena yatra yat samyagdarśanaṃ tatra tad eva jñeyam. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñināṃ tritayam apy asti, nāsaṃjñinām, tadubhayavyapadeśarahitānāṃ kṣāyikam eva. āhārānuvādena āhārakāṇāṃ tritayam apy asti, anāhārakāṇāṃ chadmasthānāṃ tritayam apy asti, kevalināṃ samudghātagatānāṃ kṣāyikam eva. 
 § 28. sādhanaṃ dvividham abhyantaraṃ bāhyaṃ ca. abhyantaraṃ darśanamohasyopaśamaḥ kṣayaḥ kṣayopaśamo vā. bāhyaṃ nārakāṇāṃ prakcaturthyāḥ samyagdarśanasya sādhanaṃ keṣāṃcij jātismaraṇaṃ keṣāṃcid dharmaśravaṇaṃ keṣāṃcid vedanābhibhavaḥ. caturthīm ārabhya ā saptamyā nārakāṇām jātismaraṇaṃ vedanābhibhavaś ca. tiraścāṃ keṣāṃcij jātismaraṇaṃ keṣāṃcid dharmaśravaṇaṃ keṣāṃcij jinabimbadarśanam. manuṣyāṇām api tathaiva. devānāṃ keṣaṃcij jātismaraṇaṃ keṣāṃcid dharmaśravaṇaṃ keṣāṃcij jinamahimadarśanaṃ keṣāṃcid devardhidarśanam. evaṃ prāgānatāt. ānataprāṇatāraṇācyutadevānāṃ devardhidarśanaṃ muktvānyat tritayam apy asti. navagraiveyakavāsināṃ keṣāṃcij jātismaraṇaṃ keṣaṃcid dharmaśravaṇam. anudiśānuttaravimānavāsinām iyaṃ kalpanā na saṃbhavati; prāgeva gṛhītasamyaktvānāṃ tatrotpatteḥ. 
 § 29. adhikaraṇaṃ dvividham — abhyantaraṃ bāhyaṃ ca. abhyantaraṃ svasvāmisaṃbandhārha eva ātmā, vivakṣātaḥ kārakapravṛtteh. bāhyaṃ lokanāḍī. sā kiyatī? ekarajjuviṣkambhā caturdaśarajjvāyāmā. 
 § 30. sthitir aupaśamikasya jaghanyotkṛṣṭā cāntarmauhūrtikī. kṣāyikasya saṃsāriṇo jaghanyāntamauhūrtikī. utkṛṣṭā trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi sāntarmuhūrtāṣṭavarṣahīnapūrvakoṭidvayādhikāni. muktasya sādir aparyavasānā. kṣāyopaśamikasya jaghanyāntarmauhūrttikī utkṛṣṭāṣaṭṣaṣṭisāgaropamāṇi. 
 § 31. vidhānaṃ sāmānyād ekaṃ samyagdarśanam. dvitayaṃ nisargajādhigamajabhedāt. tritayaṃ aupaśamikakṣāyikakṣāyopaśamikabhedāt. evaṃ saṃkhyeyā vikalpāḥ śabdataḥ. asaṃkhyeyā anantāś ca bhavanti śraddhātṛśraddhātavyabhedāt. evam ayaṃ nirdeśādividdhir jñānacāritrayor jīvājīvādiṣu cāgamānusāreṇa yojayitavyaḥ. 
 § 32. kim etair eva jīvādīnām adhigamo bhavati uta anyo ’py adhigamopāyo ’stīti paridṛṣṭo ’stīty āha — 
 satsaṃkhyākṣetrasparśanakālāntarabhāvālpabahutvaiś ca || 
 §§ 33–162 
 § 33. sad ity astitvanirdeśaḥ. sa praśaṃsādiṣu vartamāno neha gṛhyate. saṃkhyā bhedagaṇanā. kṣetraṃ nivāso vartamānakālaviṣayaḥ. tad eva sparśanaṃ trikālagocaram. kālo dvividhaḥ — mukhyo vyāvahārikaś ca. tayor uttaratra nirṇayo vakṣhyate. antaraṃ virahakālaḥ. bhāvaḥ aupaśamikādilakṣaṇaḥ. alpabahutvam anyo ’nyāpekṣayā viśeṣapratipattiḥ. etaiś ca samyagdarśanādīnāṃ jīvādīnāṃ cādhigamo veditavyaḥ. nanu ca nirdeśād eva sadgrahaṇaṃ siddham. vidhānagrahaṇāt saṃkhyāgatiḥ. adhikaraṇagrahaṇāt kṣetrasparśanāvabodhaḥ. sthitigrahaṇāt kālasaṃgrahaḥ. bhāvo nāmādiṣu saṃgṛhīta eva. punar eṣāṃ kim arthaṃ grahaṇam iti. satyasiddham. vineyāśayavaśāt tattvadeśanādikalpaḥ. kecit saṃkṣeparucayaḥ kecit vistararucayaḥ. apare nātisaṃkṣepeṇa nātivistareṇa pratipādyāḥ. sarvasattvānugrahārtho hi satāṃ prayāsa iti adhigamābhyupāyabhedoddeśah kṛtaḥ. itarathā hi  pramāṇanayair adhigamaḥ  ity anenaiva siddhatvād itareṣāṃ grahaṇam anarthakaṃ syāt. 
 § 34. tatra jīvadravyam adhikṛtya sadādyanuyogadvāranirūpaṇaṃ kriyate. jīvāś caturdaśasu guṇasthāneṣu vyavasthitāḥ. mithyādṛṣṭiḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭiḥ samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭiḥ asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭiḥ saṃyatāsamyataḥ pramattasaṃyataḥ apramattasaṃyattaḥ apūrvakaraṇasthāne upaśamakaḥ kṣapakaḥ anivṛttibādarasāṃparāyasthāne upaśamakaḥ kṣapakaḥ sūkṣmasāmparāyasthāne upaśamakaḥ kṣapakaḥ upaśāntakaṣāyavītarāgachadmasthaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyavītarāgachadmasthaḥ sayogakevalī ayogakevalī ceti. eteṣām eva jīvasamāsānāṃ nirūpaṇārthaṃ caturdaśa mārgaṇāsthānāni jñeyāni. gatīndriyakāyayogavedakaṣāyajñānasaṃyamadarśanaleśyābhavyasamyaktvasaṃjñāhārakā iti. 
 § 35. tatra satprarūpaṇā dvividhā sāmānyena viśeṣeṇa ca. sāmānyena asti mithyādṛṣṭiḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭir ity evam ādi. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau sarvāsu pṛthivīṣu ādyāni catvāri guṇasthānāni santi. tiyaggatau tāny eva saṃyatāsaṃyatasthānādhikāni santi. manuṣyagatau caturdaśāpi santi. devagatau nārakavat. indriyānuvādena ekendriyādiṣu caturindriyaparyanteṣu ekam eva mithyādṛṣṭisthānam. pañcendriyeṣu caturdaśāpi santi. kāyānuvādena pṛthivīkāyādivanaspatikāyānteṣu ekam eva mithyādṛṣṭisthānam. trasakāyeṣu caturdaśāpi santi. yogānuvādena triṣu yogeṣu trayodaśa guṇasthānāni bhavanti. tataḥ paraṃ ayogakevalī. vedānuvādena triṣu vedeṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādyanivṛttibādarāntāni santi. apagatavedesu anivṛttibādarādyayogakevalyantāni. 
 § 36. kaṣāyānuvādena krodhamānamāyāsu mithyādṛṣṭyādīni anivṛttibādarasthānāntāni santi. lobhakaṣāye tāny eva sūkṣmasāṃparāyasthānādhikāni. akaṣāyaḥ upaśāntakaṣāyaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyaḥ sayogakevalī ayogakevalī ceti. 
 § 37. jñānānuvādena matyājñānaśrutājñānavibhaṅgajñāneṣu mithyādṛṣṭiḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭiś cāsti. ābhinibodhikaśrutāvadhijñāneṣu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādīni kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāni santi. manaḥparyayajñāne pramattasaṃyatādayaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāḥ santi. kevalajñāne sayogo ’yogaś ca. 
 § 38. saṃyamānuvādena saṃyatāḥ pramattādayo ’yogakevalyantāḥ. sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanāśuddhisaṃyatāḥ pramattādayo ’nivṛttisthānāntāḥ. parihāraviśuddhisaṃyatāḥ pramattāś ca pramattāś ca. *  sūkṣmasāṃparāyaśuddhisaṃyatā ekasminn eva sūkṣmasāṃparāyasthāne. yathākhyātavihāraśuddhisaṃyatā upaśāntakaṣāyādayo ’yogakevalyāntāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatā ekasminn eva saṃyatāsaṃyatasthāne. asaṃyatā ādy eṣu caturṣu guṇasthāneṣu. 
 § 39. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśanācakṣurdarśanayor mithyādṛṣṭyādīni kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāni santi. avadhidarśane asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādīni kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāni santi. kevaladarśane sayogakevalī ayogakevalī ca. 
 § 40. leśyānuvādena kṛṣṇanīlakapotaleśyāsu mithyādṛṣṭyādīni asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyantāni santi. tejaḥpadmaleśyayor mithyādṛṣṭyādīni apramattasthānāntāni. śuklaleśyāyāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādīni sayogakevalyantāni. aleśyā ayogakevalinaḥ. 
 § 41. bhavyānuvādena bhavyeṣu caturdaśāpi santi. abhavyā ādya eva sthāne. 
 § 42. samyaktvānuvādena kṣāyikasamyaktve asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādīni ayogakevalyantāni santi. kṣāyopaśamikasamyaktve asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādīni apramattāntāni. aupaśamikasamyaktve asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādīni upaśāntakaṣāyāntāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭiḥ samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭir mithyādṛṣṭiś ca sve sve sthāne. 
 § 43. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñiṣu dvādaśa guṇasthānāni kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāni. asaṃjñiṣu ekam eva mithyādṛṣṭisthānam. tadubhayavyapadeśarahitaḥ sayogakevalī ayogakevalī ca. 
 § 44. āhārānuvādena āhārakeṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādīni kevalyantāni. anāhārakeṣu vigrahagatyāpanneṣu trīṇi guṇasthānāni mithyādṛṣṭiḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭir asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭiś ca. samudghātagataḥ sayogakevalī ayogakevalī ca. siddhāḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ atītaguṇasthānāḥ. uktā satprarūpaṇā. 
 § 45. saṃkhyāprarūpaṇocyate. sā dvividhā sāmānyena viśeṣeṇa ca. sāmānyena tāvad jīvā mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantānantāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāś ca palyopmāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. pramattasaṃyatāḥ koṭīpṛthaktvasaṃkhyāḥ. pṛthaktvam ity āgamasaṃjñā tisṝṇāṃ koṭīnāmam upari navānām adhaḥ. *  apramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. catvāra upaśamakāḥ praveśena eko vā dvau vā trayo vā. utkarṣeṇa catuḥpañcāśat. svakālena samuditāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. catvāraḥ kṣapakā ayogakevalinaś ca praveśena eko vā dvau vā trayo vā. utkarṣeṇāṣṭottaraśatasaṃkhyāḥ. svakālena samuditāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. sayogakevalinaḥ praveśena eko vā dvau vā trayo vā. utkarṣeṇāṣṭottaraśatasaṃkhyāḥ. svakālena samuditāḥ śatasahasrapṛthaktvasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 46. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau prathamāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ nārakā mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ śreṇayaḥ pratarāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. dvitīyādiṣv ā saptamyā mithyādṛṣṭayaḥ śreṇyasaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. sa cāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ asaṃkhyeyā yojanakoṭīkoṭyaḥ. sarvāsu pṛthivīṣu sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭayo ’samyatasamyagdṛṣṭayaś ca palyopmāsaṃkyeyabhḡapramitāḥ. tiryaggatau tiraścāṃ madhye mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantānantāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādayaḥ saṃyatāsamyatāntāḥ palyopamāsaṃkyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. manuṣyagatau manuṣyā mithyādṛṣṭayaḥ śreṇyasaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. sa cāsamkhyeyabhāgaḥ asaṃkhyeyā yojanakoṭīkoṭyaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādayaḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāntāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. pramattādīnāṃ sāmānyoktā saṃkhyā. devagatau devā mithyādṛṣṭayo ’samkhyeyāḥ śreņayaḥ pratarāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. 
 § 47. indriyānuvādena ekendriyā mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantānantāḥ. dvīndriyās trīndriyāś caturindriyā asaṃkhyeyāḥ śreṇayaḥ pratarāsaṃkhyeyabhāgamitāḥ. *  pañcendriyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ śreṇayaḥ pratarāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādayo ’yogakevalyantāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 48. kāyānuvādena pṛthivīkāyikā apkāyikās tejaḥkāyikā vāyukāyikā asaṃkhyeyā lokāḥ. vanaspatikāyikāḥ anantānantāḥ. trasakāyikasaṃkhyā pañcendriyavat. 
 § 49. yogānuvādena manoyogino vāgyoginaś ca mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ śreṇayaḥ pratarāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. kāyayogino mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantānantāḥ. trayānām api yogināṃ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādayaḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāntāḥ palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. pramattasaṃyatādayaḥ sayogakevalyantāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. ayogakevalinaḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 50. vedānuvādena strīvedāḥ puṃvedāś ca mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ śreṇayaḥ pratarāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. napuṃsakevedā mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantānantāḥ. strīvedā napuṃsakavedāś ca sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādayaḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāntāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. pramattasaṃyatādayo ’nivṛttibādarāntāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. puṃvedāḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādayo nivṛttibādarāntāḥ sāmanyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. apagatavedā anivṛttibādarādayo ’yogakevalyantāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 51. kaṣāyānuvādena krodhamānamāyāsu mithyādṛṣṭyādyaḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāntāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. pramattasaṃyatādayo ’nivṛttibādarāntāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. lobhakaṣāyāṇāṃ ukta eva kramaḥ. ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ sūkṣmasāṃparāyasaṃyatāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. akaṣāyā upaśāntakaṣāyādayo ’yogakevalyantāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 52. jñānānuvādena matyajñāninaḥ śrutājñāninaś ca mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. vibhaṅgajñānino mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkyeyāḥ śreṇayaḥ pratarāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgapramitāḥ. matiśrutajñānino ’saṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādayaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. avadhijñānino ’saṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭisaṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. pramattasaṃyatādayaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. manaḥparyayajñāninaḥ pramattasaṃyatādayaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. kevalajñāninaḥ sayogā ayogāś ca sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 53. saṃyamānuvādena sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanaśuddhisaṃyatāḥ pramattādayo ’nivṛttibādarāntāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. parihāraviśuddhisaṃyatāḥ pramattāś cāpramattāś ca saṃkhyeyāḥ. sūkṣmasāṃparāyaśuddhisaṃyatā yathākhyātavihāraśuddhisaṃyatāḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatā asaṃyatāś ca sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 54. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśanino mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkheyāḥ śreṇayaḥ pratarāsaṃkheyabhāgapramitāḥ. acakṣurdarśanino mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantānantāḥ. ubhaye ca sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādayaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. avadhidarśanino ’vadhijñānivat kevaladarśaninaḥ kevalajñānivat. 
 § 55. leśyānuvādena kṛṣṇalīlakāpotaleśyā mithyādṛṣṭyādayo ’saṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyantāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. tejaḥpadmaleśyā mithyādṛṣṭyādayaḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāntāḥ strīvedavat. pramattāpramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. śuklaleśyā mithyādṛṣṭyādayaḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāntāḥ palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāḥ. pramattāpramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkyeyāḥ. apūrvakaraṇādayaḥ sayogakevalyantā aleśyāś ca sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 56. bhavyānuvādena bhavyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādayo ’yogakevalyantāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. abhavyā anantāḥ. 
 § 57. samyaktvānuvādena kṣāyikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ palyopa–māsaṃkheyabhāgapramitāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatādaya upaśāntakaṣāyāntāḥ saṃkheyāḥ. catvāraḥ kṣapakāḥ sayogakevalino ’yogakevalinaś ca sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. kṣāyopaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣụ asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādayo ’pramattāntāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. aupaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭisaṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ palyopmāsaṃkheyabhāgapramitāḥ. pramattāpramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkheyāḥ. catvāra aupaśamikāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭayo mithyādṛṣṭayaś ca sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 58. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñiṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādayaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntāś cakṣurdarśanivat. asaṃjñino mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantānantāḥ. tadubhayavyapadeśarahitāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. 
 § 59. āhārānuvādena āhārakeṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādayaḥ sayogakevalyantāḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. anāhārakeṣu mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. sayogakevalinaḥ saṃkhyeyāḥ. ayogakevalinaḥ sāmānyoktasaṃkhyāḥ. saṃkhyā nirṇītā. 
 § 60. kṣetram ucyate. tad dvividhaṃ sāmānyena viśeṣeṇa ca. sāmānyena tāvad — mithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ sarvalokaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādīnām ayogakevalyantānāṃ lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. sayogakevalināṃ lokasyāsaṃkyeyabhāgo ’saṃkyeyā bhāgāḥ sarvaloko vā. 
 § 61. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau sarvāsu pṛthivīṣu nārakāṇāṃ caturṣu guṇasthāneṣu lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. tiryaggatau tiraścāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādisaṃyatāsamyatāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. manuṣyagatau manuṣyāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. sayogakevalināṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram devagatau devānāṃ sarveṣāṃ caturṣu guṇasthāneṣu lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. 
 § 62. indriyānuvādena ekendriyāṇāṃ kṣetraṃ sarvalokaḥ. vikalendriyāṇāṃ lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. pañcendriyāṇāṃ manuṣyavat. 
 § 63. kāyānuvādena pṛthivīkāyādivanaspatikāyāntānāṃ sarvalokaḥ. trasakāyikānāṃ pañcendriyavat. 
 § 64. yogānuvādena vāṅmanasayogināṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādisayogakevalyantānāṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. kāyayoginām mithyādṛṣṭyādisayogakevalyantānām ayogakevalināṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. 
 § 65. vedānuvādena strīpuṃvedānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyanivṛttibādarāntānāṃ lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. napuṃsakavedānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyanivṛttibādarāntānām apagatavedānāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. 
 § 66. kaṣāyānuvādena krodhamānamāyākaṣāyāṇāṃ lobhakaṣāyāṇāṃ ca mithyādṛṣṭyādyanivṛttibādarāntānāṃ sūkṣmasāṃparāyāṇām akaṣāyāṇāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. 
 § 67. jñānānuvādena matyajñāniśrutājñānināṃ mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. vibhaṅgajñānināṃ mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. ābhinibodhikaśrutāvadhijñāninām asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādīnāṃ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ manaḥparyayajñānināṃ ca pramattādīnāṃ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ kevalajñānināṃ sayogānām ayogānāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. 
 § 68. saṃyamānuvādena sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanāśuddhisaṃyatānāṃ caturṇāṃ parihāraviśuddhisaṃyatānāṃ pramattāpramattānāṃ sụkṣmasāṃparāyaśuddhisaṃyatānāṃ yathākhyātavihāraśuddhisaṃyatānāṃ caturṇāṃ saṃyatāsaṃyatānām asaṃyatānāṃ ca caturṇāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. 
 § 69. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśanināṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. acakṣurdarśanināṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. avadhidarśaninām avadhijñānivat. kevaladarśanināṃ kevalajñānivat. 
 § 70. leśyānuvādena kṛṣṇanīlakāpotaleśyānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyantānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. tejaḥpadmaleśyānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānāṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. śuklaleśyānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. sayogakevalinām aleśyānāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. 
 § 71. bhavyānuvādena bhavyānāṃ caturdaśānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. abhavyānāṃ sarvalokaḥ. 
 § 72. samyaktvānuvādena kṣāyikasamyagdṛṣṭīnām asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ kṣāyopaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭīnām asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānām aupaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭīnām asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyupaśāntakaṣāyāntānāṃ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ mithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. 
 § 73. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñināṃ caksurdarśanivat. asaṃjñināṃ sarvalokaḥ. tadubhayavyapadeśarahitānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. 
 § 74. āhārānuvādena āhārakāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetram. sayogakevalināṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. anāhārakāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyayogakevalināṃ sāmānyoktaṃ kṣetraṃ. sayogakevalināṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyā bhāgāḥ sarvaloko vā. kṣetranirṇayaḥ kṛtaḥ. 
 § 75. sparśanam ucyate. tad dvividhaṃ sāmānyena viśeṣeṇa ca. sāmānyena tāvan mithyādṛṣṭibhiḥ sarvalokaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau dvādaśa caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatair lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ ṣaṭ caturdaśabhāgā vā desonāḥ. pramattasaṃyatādīnām ayogakevalyantānāṃ kṣetravatsparśanam. 
 § 76. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau prathamāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ nārakaiś caturguṇasthānair lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ. dvitīyādiṣu prāksaptamyā mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣtibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgāḥ eko dvau trayaḥ catvāraḥ pañca caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. saptamyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ mithyādṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkyeyabhāgaḥ ṣaṭ caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. śeṣais tribhir lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. tiryaggatau tiraścāṃ mithyādṛṣṭibhiḥ sarvalokaḥ spṛṣtaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ sapta caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭisaṃyatāsaṃyatair lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ ṣaṭ caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. manuṣyagatau manuṣyair mithyādṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ sarvaloko vā spṛṣṭaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣtibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ sapta caturdaśabhāgā vā desonāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyādīnām ayogakevalyantānāṃ kṣetravatsparśanam. devagatau devair mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣtibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau nava caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. 
 § 77. indriyānuvādena ekendriyaiḥ sarvalokaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ. vikalendriyair lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ sarvaloko vā. pañcendriyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ sarvaloko vā. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. 
 § 78. kāyānuvādena sthāvarakāyikaiḥ sarvalokaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ. trasakāyināṃ pañcendriyavat sparśanam. 
 § 79. yogānuvādena vāṅmanasayogināṃ mithyādṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ sarvaloko vā. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādīnāṃ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. sayogakevalināṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. kāyayogināṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādīnāṃ sayogakevalyantānām ayogakevalināṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. 
 § 80. vedānuvādena strīpuṃvedair mithyādṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ aṣṭau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ sarvaloko vā. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭibhiḥ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau nava caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyādyanivṛttibādarāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. napuṃsakavedeṣu mithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭisamyatāsaṃyatair lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ ṣaṭ caturdaśabhāgā vā deṡonāḥ. pramattādyanivṛttibādarāntānām apagatavedānāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. 
 § 81. kaṣāyānuvādena catuṣkaṣāyāṇām akaṣāyāṇāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. 
 § 82. jñānānuvādena matyajñāniśrutājñāninaṃ mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. vibhaṅgajñānināṃ mithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ sarvaloko vā. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. ābhinibodhikaśrutāvadhimanaḥparyayakevalajñānināṃ sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. 
 § 83. saṃyamānuvādena saṃyatānāṃ sarveṣāṃ saṃyatāsaṃyatānām asaṃyatānāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. 
 § 84. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśanināṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ pañcendriyavat. acakṣurdarśanināṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānām adhikevaladarśanināṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. * 
 § 85. leśyānuvādena kṛṣṇanīlakāpotaleśyair mithyādṛṣṭibhiḥ sarvalokaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ pañca catvāro dvau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. tejoleśyair mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau nava caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasaṃyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatair lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ adhyardha caturdaśa bhāgā vā deśonāḥ. pramattāpramattair lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. padmaleśyair mithyādṛṣṭyādyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyantair lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ aṣṭau caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatair lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ pañca caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. pramattāpramattair lokasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. śuklaleśyair mithyādṛṣṭyādisaṃyatāsamyatāntair lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ ṣaṭ caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. pramattādisayogakevalyantānām aleśyānāṃ ca sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. 
 § 86. bhavyānuvādena bhavyānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ sāmānyoktaṃ sparśanam. abhavyaiḥ sarvalokaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ. 
 § 87. samyaktvānuvādena kṣāyikasamyagdṛṣṭīnām asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ sāmānyoktam. kiṃtu saṃyatāsaṃyatānāṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. kṣāyopaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ sāmānyoktam. aupaśamikasamyaktvānām asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ sāmānyoktam. śeṣāṇāṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭimithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ sāmānyoktam. 
 § 88. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñināṃ caksurdarśanivat. asaṃjñibhiḥ sarvalokaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ. tadubhayavyapadeśarahitānāṃ sāmānyoktam. 
 § 89. āhārānuvādena āhārakāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ sāmānyoktam. sayogakevalināṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. anāhārakeṣu mithyādṛṣṭibhiḥ sarvalokaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭibhir lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ ekādaśa caturdaśabhāgā vā deśonāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭibhiḥ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ ṣaṭ caturdaśa bhāgā vā deśonāḥ. sayogakevalināṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgāḥ sarvaloko vā. ayogakevalināṃ lokasyāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. sparśanaṃ vyākhyātam. 
 § 90. kālaḥ prastūyate. sa dvividhaḥ — sāmānyena viśeṣeṇa ca. sāmānyena tāvad mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvāpekṣayā trayo bhaṅgāḥ. anādir aparyavasānaḥ anādiḥ saparyavasānaḥ sādiḥ saparyavasānaś ceti. tatra sādiḥ saparyavasāno jaghanyenāntarmuhūrttaḥ. utkarṣeṇārdhapudgalaparivartto deśonaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ṣaḍāvalikāḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenāntarmuhūrttaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyaḥ utkṛṣṭaś cāntarmuhūrttaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdrṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrttaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. saṃyatāsaṃyatasya nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrttaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭī deśonā. pramattāpramattayor nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāntarmuhūrttaḥ. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpeksayā ca jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāntarmuhūrttaḥ. caturṇāṃ kṣapakāṇām ayogakevalināṃ ca nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca jaghanyaś cotkṛṣṭaś cāntarmuhūrttaḥ. sayogakevalināṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭī deśonā. 
 § 91. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau nārakeṣu saptasu pṛthivīṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa yathāsaṃkhyaṃ eka-tri-sapta-daśa-saptadaśa-dvāviṃśati-trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭeḥ samyagmithyādṛṣṭeś ca sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ukta evotkṛṣṭo deśonaḥ. 
 § 92. tiryaggatau tiraścāṃ mithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇānantaḥ kālo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ pudgalaparivartāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭisaṃyatāsaṃyatānāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trīṇi palyopamāni. 
 § 93. manuṣyagatau manuṣyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarseṇa trīṇi palyopamāni pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhikāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāntarmuhūrtaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ṣaḍāvalikāḥ. samyagmithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca jaghanyaś cotkṛṣṭaś cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trīṇi palyopamāni sātirekāṇi. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. 
 § 94. devagatau deveṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarseṇaikatriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭeḥ samyagmithyādṛṣṭeś ca sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarseṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāni. 
 § 95. indriyānuvādena ekendriyāṇāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena kṣudrabhavagrahaṇaṃ. utkarṣeṇānantaḥ kālo ’saṃkheyāḥ pudgalaparivartāḥ. vikalendriyāṇāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena kṣudrabhavagrahaṇam. utkarṣeṇa saṃkheyāni varṣasahasrāṇi. pañcendriyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamasahasraṃ pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhikam. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. 
 § 96. kāyānuvādena pṛthivyaptejovāyukāyikānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena kṣudrabhavagrahaṇam. utkarṣeṇāsaṃkhyeyā lokāḥ. vanaspatikāyikānām ekendriyavat. trasakāyikeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa dve sagaropamasahasre pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhike. śeṣānāṃ pañcendriyavat. 
 § 97. yogānuvādena vāṅmanasayogiṣu mithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭisaṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattasayogakevalināṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāntarmuhūrtaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭeḥ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikasamayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāntarmuhūrtaḥ. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ kṣapakāṇāṃ ca nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca jaghanyenaikasamayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāntarmuhūrtaḥ. kāyayogiṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikasamayaḥ. utkarṣeṇānantaḥ kālo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ pudgalaparivartāḥ. śeṣaṇāṃ manoyogivat. ayogānāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 98. vedānuvādena strīvedeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamaśatapṛthaktvam. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādyanivṛttibādarāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. kintu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvakālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pañcapañcāśatpalyopamāni deśonāni. puṃvedeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamaśatapṛthaktvam. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭādyanivṛttibādarāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. napuṃsakavedeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇānantaḥ kālo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ pudgalaparivarttāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭādyanivṛttibādarāntānāṃ sāmānyavat. kiṃtv asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. apagatavedānāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 99. kaṣāyānuvādena catuṣkaṣāyāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānāṃ manoyogivat. dvayor upaśamakayor dvayoḥ kṣapakayoḥ kevalalobhasya ca akaṣāyāṇāṃ ca sāmānyotaḥ kālaḥ. 
 § 100. jñānānuvādena matyajñāniśrutājñāniṣu mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyoḥ sāmānyavat. vibhaṅgajñāniṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭeḥ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. ābhinibodhikaśrutāvadhimanaḥparyayakevalajñānināṃ ca sāmānyoktaḥ. 
 § 101. saṃyamānuvādena sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanaparihāraviśuddhisūkṣmasāṃparāyayathākhyātaśuddhisaṃyatānāṃ saṃyatāsaṃyatānām asaṃyatānāṃ ca caturṇāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. 
 § 102. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśaniṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropamasahasre. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādīnāṃ kṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. acakṣurdarśaniṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. avadhikevaladarśaninor avadhikevalajñānivat. 
 § 103. leśyānuvādena kṛṣṇanīlakāpotaleśyāsu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsaptadaśasaptasāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyoḥ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsaptadaśasaptasāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. tejaḥpadmaleśyayor mithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropame aṣṭādaśa ca sāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyoḥ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarśeṇāntarmuhūrtaḥ. śuklaleśyānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇaikatriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādisayogakevalyantānām aleśyānāṃ ca sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. kiṃ tu saṃyatāsaṃyatasya nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāntarmuhūrtaḥ. 
 § 104. bhavyānuvādena bhavyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvāpekṣayā dvau bhaṅgau anādiḥ saparyavasānaḥ sādiḥ saparyavasānaś ca. tatra sādiḥ saparyavasāno jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇārddhapudgalaparivarto deśonaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. abhavyānām anādir aparyavasānaḥ. 
 § 105. samyaktvānuvādena kṣāyikasamyagdṛṣṭīnām asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭādyayogakevalyantānāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. kṣāyopaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ caturṇāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. aupaśamikasamyaktveṣu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭisaṃyatāsaṃyator nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyaś cotkṛṣṭaś cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. pramatāpramattayoś caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ ca nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāntarmuhūrtaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭimithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. 
 § 106. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñiṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādyanivṛttibādarāntānāṃ puṃvedavat. śeṣāṇām sāmānyoktaḥ. asaṃjñināṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena kṣudrabhavagrahaṇam. utkarṣenānantaḥ kalo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ pudgalaparivartāḥ. tadubhayavyapadeśarahitānāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ. 
 § 107. āhārānuvādena āhārakeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghayenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇāṃgulāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ asaṃkheyāsaṃkheyā utsarpiṇyavasarpiṇyaḥ. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyoktaḥ kālaḥ. anāhārakeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sarvaḥ kālaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ utkarṣeṇa trayaḥ samayāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayāḥ jaghanenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇāvalikāyā asaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenaikaḥ samayāḥ. utkarṣeṇa dvau samayau. sayogakevalino nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyena trayaḥ samayāḥ. utkarṣeṇa saṃkheyāḥ samayāḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyaś cotkṛṣṭaś ca trayaḥ samayāḥ. ayogakevalināṃ sāmānyokataḥ kālaḥ. kālo varṇitaḥ. 
 § 108. antaraṃ nirūpyate. vivakṣitasya guṇasya guṇāntarasaṃkrame sati punastatprāpteḥ prāṅmadhyam antaram. tad dvividhaṃ sāmānyena viśeṣaṇa ca. sāmānyena tāvad mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenārmuhūrtaḥ. *  utkarṣeṇa dve ṣaṭṣaṣtī deśone sāgaropamāṇām. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭer antaraṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. utkarṣeṇārddhapudgalaparivarto deśonaḥ. samyagmithyādṛṣṭer antaraṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāsādanavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇārddhapudgalaparivarto deśonaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭādyapramattāntānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇārddhapudgalaparivarto deśonaḥ. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa varṣapṛthaktvam. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇārddhapudgalaparivarto deśonāḥ. caturṇāṃ kṣapakāṇām ayogakevalināṃ ca nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ṣaṇmāsāḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. sayogakevalināṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. 
 § 109. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau nārakāṇāṃ saptasu pṛthivīṣu mithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaraṃ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa eka-tri-sapta-daśa-saptadaśa-dvāviṃśati-trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇa eka-tri-sapta-daśa-saptadaśa-dvāviṃśati-trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. 
 § 110. tiryaggatau tiraścāṃ mithyādrster nānājīvāpekeṣayā nasty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trīṇi palyopamāni deśonāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādīnāṃ caturṇāṃ sāmānyoktam antaram. 
 § 111. manuṣyagatau manuṣyāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭes tiryagvat. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇa trīṇi palyopamāni pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhikāni. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trīṇi palyopamāni pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadikāni. saṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nasty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvāni. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvāni. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 112. devagatau devānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyor nānājīāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ekatriṃśatsāgaropmāṇi deśonāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇaikatriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. 
 § 113. indriyānuvādena ekendriyāṇāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvāpekṣayā jaghanyena kṣudrabhavagrahaṇam. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropamasahasre pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhike. vikalendriyāṇāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena kṣudrabhavagrahaṇam. utkarṣeṇānantaḥ kālo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ pudgalaparivartāḥ. evam indriyaṃ praty antaram uktam. guṇaṃ praty ubhayato ’pi nāsty antaram. pañcendriyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭeḥ sāmānyavat. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarseṇa sāgaropmasahasraṃ pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhikam. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamasahasraṃ pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhikam. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamasahasraṃ pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhikam. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyoktam. 
 § 114. kāyānuvādena pṛthivyaptejovāyukāyikānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena kṣudrabhavagrahaṇam. utkarṣeṇānantaḥ kālo ’saṃkhyeyāḥ pudgalaparivartāḥ. vanaspatikāyikānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvāpekṣayā jaghanyena kṣudrabhavagrahaṇam. utkarṣeṇāsaṃkhyeyā lokāḥ. evaṃ kāyaṃ praty antaram uktam. guṇaṃ praty ubhayato ’pi nāsty antaram. trasakāyikeṣu mithyādṛṣṭeh sāmānyavat. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. urkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropamasahasre pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhike. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropamasahasre pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhike. caturṇāṃ upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropamasahasre pūrvakoṭīpṛthaktvair abhyadhike. śeṣāṇāṃ pañcendriyavat. 
 § 115. yogānuvādena kāyavāṅmanasayogināṃ mithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭisaṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattasayogakevalināṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. caturṇām kṣapakāṇām ayogakevalināṃ ca sāmānyavat. 
 § 116. vedānuvādena strīvedeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pañcapañcāśatpalyopamāni deśonāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣaya sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇa palyopamaśatapṛthaktvam. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamaśatapṛthaktvam. dvayor upaśamakayor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamaśatapṛthaktvam. dvayoḥ kṣapakayor nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa varṣapṛthaktvam. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. 
 § 117. puṃvedeṣu mithyādṛṣṭeḥ sāmānyavat. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopmāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamaśatapṛthaktvam. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamaśatapṛthaktvam. dvayor upaśamakayor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamaśatapṛthaktvam. dvayoḥ kṣapakayor nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa saṃvatsaraḥ sātirekaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. 
 § 118. napuṃsakavedeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādyanivṛttyupaśamakāntānāṃ sāmānyoktam. dvayoḥ kṣapakayoḥ strīvedavat. apagatavedeṣu anivṛttibādaropaśamakasūkṣmasāṃparāyopaśamakayor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyoktam. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyam utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. upaśāntakaṣāyasya nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 119. kaṣāyānuvādena krodhamānamāyālobhakaṣāyāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭādyanivṛttyupaśamakāntānāṃ manoyogivat. dvayoḥ kṣapakayor nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa saṃvatsaraḥ sātirekaḥ. kevalalobhasya sūkṣmasāṃparāyopaśamakasya nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. kṣapakasya tasya sāmānyavat. akaṣāyeṣu upaśāntakaṣāyasya nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. śeṣāṇāṃ trayāṇāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 120. jñānānuvādena matyajñānaśrutājñānavibhaṅgajñāniṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. ābhinibodhikaśrutāvadhijñāniṣu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭī deśonā. saṃyatāsaṃyatasya nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ṣaṭṣaṣṭisāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. pramattāpramattayor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarsena trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ṣaṭṣaṣṭisāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. caturṇāṃ kṣapakāṇāṃ sāmānyavat. kiṃ tu avadhijñāniṣu nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa varṣapṛthaktvam. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. manaḥparyayajñāniṣu pramattāpramattasaṃyatayor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyam utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. caturṇāṃ upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭī deśonā. caturṇāṃ kṣapakāṇām avadhijñānivat. dvayoḥ kevalajñāninoḥ sāmānyavat. 
 § 121. saṃyamānuvādena sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanaśuddhisaṃyateṣu pramattāpramattayor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyam utkṛṣṭam cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. dvayor upaśamakayor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭī deśonā. dvayoḥ kṣapakayoḥ sāmānyavat. parihāraśuddhisaṃyateṣu pramattāpramattayor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyam utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. sūkṣmasāmparāyaśuddhisaṃyateṣūpaśamakasya nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. tasyaiva kṣapakasya sāmānyavat. yathākhyāte akaṣāyavat. saṃyatāsaṃyatasya nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. asaṃyateṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsy antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. śeṣāṇāṃ trayāṇām sāmānyavat. 
 § 122. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśaniṣu mithyādṛṣṭeḥ sāmānyavat. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropamasahasre deśone. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ utakrṣeṇa dve sāgaropamasahasre deśone. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyoktam. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropamasahasre deśone. caturṇāṃ kṣapakāṇāṃ sāmānyoktam. acakṣurdarśaniṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādikṣīṇakaṣāyāntānāṃ sāmānyoktam antaram. avadhidarśanino ’vadhijñānivat. kevaladarśaninaḥ kevalajñānivat. 
 § 123. leśyānuvādena kṛṣṇalīlakāpotaleśyāsu mithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsaptadaśasaptasāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsaptadaśasaptasāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. 
 § 124. tejạhpadmaleśyayor mithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropame aṣṭādaśa ca sāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyagmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇa dve sāgaropame aṣṭādaśa ca sāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. saṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattasaṃyatānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. 
 § 125. śuklaleśyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇaikatriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deṣonāni. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇaikatriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. saṃyatāsaṃyatapramattasaṃyatos tejoleśyāvat. apramattasaṃyatsya nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyam utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. trayāṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyam utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. upaśāntakaṣāyasya nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. caturṇāṃ kṣapakāṇāṃ sayogakevalinām aleśyānāṃ ca sāmānyavat. 
 § 126. bhavyānuvādena bhavyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ sāmānyavat. abhavyānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. 
 § 127. samyaktvānuvādena kṣāyikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣv asamyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭī deśonā. saṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattasaṃyatānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 128. kṣāyopaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣv asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa pūrvakoṭī deśonā. saṃyatāsaṃyatasya nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ṣaṭṣaṣṭisāgaropamāṇi deśonāni. pramattāpramattasaṃyatayor nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi sātirekāṇi. 
 § 129. aupaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣv asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sapta rātriṃdināni. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyaṃ utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatasya nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa caturdaśa rārtriṃdināni. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyam utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. pramattāpramattasaṃyatayor nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa paṃcadaśa rātriṃdināni. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyaṃ utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. trayāṇam upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa varṣapṛthaktvam. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyam utkṛṣṭaṃ cāntarmuhūrtaḥ. upaśāntakaṣāyasya nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamāsaṃkheyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. 
 § 130. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñiṣu mithyādṛṣṭeḥ sāmānyavat. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamaśatapṛthaktvam. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādyapramattāntānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamaśatapṛthaktvam. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇa sāgaropamaśatapṛthaktvam. caturṇāṃ kṣapakāṇāṃ sāmānyavat. asaṃjñināṃ nānājīvāpekṣayaikajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. tadubhayavyapadeśarahitānāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 131. āhārānuvādena āhārakeṣu mithyādṛṣṭeḥ sāmānyavat. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣtisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyor nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyena palyopmāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’ntarmuhūrtaś ca. utkarśeṇāṅgulāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’saṃkhyeyāsaṃkhyeyā utsarpiṇyavasarpiṇyaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyapramattāntānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā nāsty antaram. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarśeṇāṅgulāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’saṃkhyeyā utsarpiṇyavasarpiṇyaḥ. caturṇām upaśamakānāṃ nānājīvāpekṣayā sāmānyavat. ekajīvaṃ prati jaghanyenāntarmuhūrtaḥ. utkarṣeṇāṅgulāsaṃkhyeyabhāgo ’saṃkhyeyāsaṃkhyeyā utsarpiṇyavsarpiṇyaḥ. caturṇāṃ kṣapakāṇāṃ sayogakevalināṃ ca sāmānyavat. 
 § 132. anāhārakeṣu mithyādṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā ekajīvāpekṣayā ca nāsty antaram. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣena māsapṛthaktvam. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. sayogakevalinaḥ nānājīvāpekṣayā jaganyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa varṣapṛthaktvam. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. ayogakevalinaḥ nānājīvāpekṣayā jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ. utkarṣeṇa ṣaṇmāsāḥ. ekajīvaṃ prati nāsty antaram. antaram avagatam. 
 § 133. bhāvo vibhāvyate. sa dvividhaḥ sāmānyena viśeṣeṇa ca. sāmānyena tavat mithyādṛṣṭir ity audayiko bhāvaḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭir iti pāriṇāmiko bhāvaḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭir iti kṣāyopaśamiko bhāvaḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭir iti aupaśamiko vā kṣāyiko vā kṣāyopaśamiko vā bhāvaḥ. asaṃyataḥ punar audayikena bhāvena. saṃyatāsaṃyataḥ pramattasaṃyato ’pramattasaṃyata iti kṣāyopaśamiko bhāvaḥ. caturṇām upaśamakānām aupaśamiko bhāvaḥ. caturṣu kṣapakeṣu sayogāyogakevalinoś ca kṣāyiko bhāvaḥ. 
 § 134. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau prathamāyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ nārakāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyantānāṃ sāmānyavat. dvitīyādiṣv ā saptamyā mithyādṛṣṭisāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭīnāṃ sāmānyavat. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer aupaśamiko vā kṣāyopaśamiko vā bhāvaḥ. asaṃyataḥ punar audayikena bhāvena. tiryaggatau tiraścāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādisaṃyatāsaṃyatāntānāṃ sāmānyavat. manuṣyagatau manuṣyāṇāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ sāmānyavat. devagatau devānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyantānāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 135. indriyānuvādena ekendriyavikalendriyāṇām audayiko bhāvaḥ. pañcendriyeṣu mithyādṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 136. kāyānuvādena sthāvarakāyikānām audayiko bhāvaḥ. trasakāyikānāṃ sāmānyam eva. 
 § 137. yogānuvādena kāyavāṅmanasayogināṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādisayogakevalyantānāṃ ca sāmānyam eva. 
 § 138. vedānuvādena strīpunnapuṃsakavedānāṃ avedānāṃ ca sāmānyavat. 
 § 139. kaṣāyānuvādena krodhamānamāyālobhakaṣāyāṇām akaṣāyāṇāṃ ca sāmānyavat. 
 § 140. jñānānuvādena matyajñāniśrutājñānivibhaṅgajñānināṃ matiśrutāvadhimanaḥparyayakevalajñānināṃ ca sāmānyavat. 
 § 141 saṃyamānuvādena sarveṣāṃ saṃyatānāṃ saṃyatāsaṃyatānāṃ ca sāmānyavat. 
 § 142. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśanācakṣurdarśanāvadhidarśanakevaladarśanināṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 143. leśyānuvādena ṣaḍleśyāleśyānāṃ ca sāmanyavat. 
 § 144. bhavyānuvādena bhavyānāṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādyayogakevalyantānāṃ sāmānyavat. abhavyānāṃ pāriṇāmiko bhāvaḥ. 
 § 145. samyaktvānuvādena kṣāyikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭeḥ kṣāyiko bhāvaḥ. kṣāyikaṃ samyaktvam. asaṃyatatvam audayikena bhāvena. saṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattasaṃyatānāṃ kṣāyopaśamiko bhāvaḥ. kṣāyikaṃ samyaktvam. caturṇām upaśamakānām aupaśamiko bhāvaḥ. kṣāyikaṃ samyaktvam. śeṣāṇāṃ sāmānyavat. kṣāyopaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭeḥ kṣāyopaśamiko bhāvaḥ. kṣāyopaśamikaṃ samyaktvam. asaṃyataḥ punar audayikena bhāvena. saṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattasaṃyatānāṃ kṣāyopaśamiko bhāvaḥ. kṣāyopaśamikaṃ samyaktvam. aupaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣu asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭer aupaśamiko bhāvaḥ. aupaśamikaṃ samyaktvam. asaṃyataḥ punar audayikena bhāvena. saṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattasaṃyatānāṃ kṣāyopaśamiko bhāvaḥ. aupaśamikaṃ samyaktvam. caturṇāṃ upaśamakānām aupaśamiko bhāvaḥ. aupaśamikaṃ samyaktvam. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭeḥ pāriṇāmiko bhāvaḥ. samyaṅmithyādṛṣṭeḥ kṣāyopaśmiko bhāvaḥ. mithyādṛṣṭer audayiko bhāvaḥ. 
 § 146. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñināṃ sāmānyavat. asaṃjñinām audayiko bhāvaḥ. tadubhayavyapadeśarahitānāṃ sāmānyavat. 
 § 147. āhārānuvādena āhārakāṇām anāhārakāṇāṃ ca sāmānyavat. bhāvaḥ parisamāptaḥ. 
 § 148. alpabahutvam upavarṇyate. tad dvividhaṃ sāmānyena viśeṣeṇa ca. sāmānyena tāvat sarvataḥ stokāḥ traya upaśamakāḥ svaguṇasthānakāleṣu praveśena tulyasaṃkhyāḥ. upaśāntakaṣāyās tāvanta eva. trayaḥ kṣapakāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. kṣīṇakaṣāyavītarāgacchadmasthās tāvanta eva. sayogakevalino ’yogakevalinaś ca praveśena tulyasaṃkhyāḥ. sayogakevalinaḥ svakālena samuditāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. apramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. pramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatā asaṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. samyagmithyādṛṣṭayaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantaguṇāḥ. 
 § 149. viśeṣeṇa gatyanuvādena narakagatau sarvāsu pṛthivīṣu nārakeṣu sarvataḥ stokāḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ. samyagmithyādṛṣṭayaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. tiryaggatau tiraścāṃ sarvataḥ stokāḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ. itareṣāṃ sāmānyavat. manuṣyagatau manuṣyāṇām upaśamakādipramattasaṃyatāntānāṃ sāmānyavat. tataḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. samyagmithyādṛṣṭayaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. devagatau devānāṃ nārakavat. 
 § 150. indriyānuvādena ekendriyavikalendriyeṣu guṇasthānabhedo nāstīty alpabahutvābhāvaḥ. pañcendriyāṇāṃ sāmānyavat. ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. 
 § 151. kāyānuvādena sthāvarakāyeṣu guṇasthānabhedābhāvād alpabhahutvābhāvaḥ. traskāyikānāṃ pañcendriyavat. 
 § 152. yogānuvādena vāṅmanasayogināṃ pañcendriyavat. kāyayogināṃ sāmānyavat. vedānuvādena strīpuṃvedānāṃ pañcendriyavat. napuṃsakavedānāṃ avedānāṃ ca sāmānyavat. 
 § 153. kaṣāyānuvādena krodhamānamāyākaṣāyāṇāṃ puṃvedavat. ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantaguṇāḥ. lobhakaṣāyāṇāṃ dvayor upaśamakayos tulyā saṃkhyā. kṣapakāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. sūkṣmasāṃparāyaśuddhyupaśamakasaṃyatā viśeṣādhikāḥ. sūkṣmasāṃparāyakṣapakāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. śeṣāṇām sāmānyavat. 
 § 154. jñānānuvādena matyajñāniśrutājñāniṣu sarvataḥ stokāḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ. mithyādṛṣṭayo ’nantaguṇāḥ. vibhaṅgajñāniṣu sarvataḥ stokāḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ. mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. matiśrutāvadhijñāniṣu sarvataḥ stokāś catvāra upaśamakāś catvāraḥ kṣapakāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. apramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. pramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ asaṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ asaṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. manaḥparyayajñāniṣu sarvataḥ stokāś catvāra upaśamakāḥ. catvāraḥ kṣapakāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. apramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. pramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. kevalajñāniṣu ayogakevalibhyaḥ sayogakevalinaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. 
 § 155. saṃyamānuvādena sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanāśuddhisaṃyateṣu dvayor upaśamakayos tulyā saṃkhyā. tataḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇau kṣapakau. apramattāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. pramattāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. parihāraśuddhisaṃyateṣu apramattebhyaḥ pramattāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. sūkṣmasaṃparāyaśuddhisaṃyateṣu upaśamakebhyaḥ kṣapakāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. yathākhyātavihāraśuddhisaṃyateṣu upaśāntakaṣāyebhyaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. ayogakevalinas tāvanta eva. sayogakevalinaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatānāṃ nāsty alpabahutvam. asaṃyateṣu sarvataḥ stokāḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ. samyaṅmityādṛṣṭayaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. mityādṛṣṭayo ’nantaguṇāḥ. 
 § 156. darśanānuvādena cakṣurdarśanināṃ manoyogivat. acakṣurdarśanināṃ kāyayogivat. avadhidarśaninām avadhijñānivat. kevaladarśanināṃ kevalajñānivat. 
 § 157. leśyānuvādena kṛṣṇalīlakāpotaleśyānāṃ asaṃyatavat. tejaḥpadmaleśyānāṃ sarvataḥ stokā apramattāḥ. pramattāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. evam itareṣāṃ pañcendriyavat. śuklaleśyānāṃ sarvaḥ stokā upaśamakāḥ. kṣapakāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. sayogakevalinaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. apramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. pramattasaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatā asaṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. samyagmithyādṛṣṭayaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. mithyādṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. 
 § 158. bhavyānuvādena bhavyānāṃ sāmānyavat. abhavyānāṃ nāsty alpabahutvam. 
 § 159. samyaktvānuvādena kṣhāyikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣu sarvataḥ stokāś catvāra upaśamakāḥ. itareṣāṃ pramattāntānāṃ sāmānyavat. tataḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. kṣāyopaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭiṣu sarvataḥ stokā apramattā. pramattāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ asaṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. aupaśamikasamyagdṛṣṭīnāṃ sarvataḥ stokāś catvāra upaśamakāḥ. apramattāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. pramattāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ asaṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. śeṣāṇāṃ nāsty alpabahutvam. 
 § 160. saṃjñānuvādena saṃjñināṃ cakurdarśanivat. asaṃjñināṃ nāsty apabahutvam. tadubhayavyapadeśarahitānāṃ kevalajñānivat. 
 § 161. āhārānuvādena āhārakāṇāṃ kāyayogivat. anāhārakāṇāṃ sarvataḥ stokāḥ sayogakevalinaḥ. ayogakevalinaḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭayo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. mithyādṛṣṭyo ’nantaguṇāḥ. 
 § 162. evaṃ mithyādṛṣṭyādīnāṃ gatyādiṣu mārgaṇā kṛtā sāmānyena. tatra sūkṣmabheda āgamāvirodhenānusartavyaḥ. 
 TAS 1.8 commentary §§ 33–162 
 § 163. evaṃ samyagdarśanasyādāv uddiṣṭasya lakṣaṇotpattisvāmiviṣayanyāsādhigamopāyā nirdiṣṭāḥ. tatsaṃbandhena ca jīvādīnāṃ saṃjñāparimāṇādi nirdiṣṭam. tadantaraṃ samyagjñānaṃ vicārārham ity āha — 
 matiśrutāvadhimanaḥparyayakevalāni jñānam || 
 § 164. jñānaśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate. matijñānaṃ śrutajñānaṃ avadhijñānaṃ manaḥparyayajñānaṃ kevalajñānam iti. indriyair manasā ca yathā svam artho manyate anayā manute mananamātraṃ vā matiḥ. tadāvaraṇakarmakṣayopaśame sati nirūpyamāṇaṃ śrūyate anena tat śṛṇoti śravaṇamātraṃ vā śrutam. anayoḥ pratyāsannanirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvāt. tathā ca vakṣyate  śrutaṃ matipūrvam  iti. avāgdhānād avacchinnaviṣayād vā avadhiḥ. parakīyamanogato ’rtho mana ity ucyate. sāhacaryāt tasya paryayaṇaṃ parigamanaṃ manaḥparyayaḥ. matijñānaprasaṅga iti cet; na; apekṣāmātratvāt. kṣayopaśamaśaktimātravijṛmbhitaṃ hi tatkevalaṃ svaparamanobhir vyapadiśyate. yathā abhre candramasaṃ paśyeti. bāhyenābhyantareṇa ca tapasā yadartham arthino mārgaṃ kevante sevante tatkevalam. asahāyam iti vā. tadante prāpyate iti ante kriyate. tasya pratyāsannatvāt tatsamīpe manaḥparyayagrahaṇam. kutaḥ pratyāsattiḥ. saṃyamaikādhikaraṇatvāt. tasya avadhir viprakṛṣṭaḥ. kutaḥ viprakṛṣṭāntaratvāt. pratyakṣāt parokṣaṃ pūrvam uktaṃ sugamatvāt. śrutaparicitānubhūtā hi matiśrutapaddhatiḥ sarveṇa prānigaṇena prāyaḥ prāpyate yataḥ. evam etat pañcavidhaṃ jñānam. tadbhedādayaś ca purastād vakṣyante. 
 § 165.  pramāṇanayair adhigamaḥ  ity uktam. pramāṇaṃ ca keṣāṃcit jñānam abhimatam. keṣaṃcit saṃnikarṣaḥ keṣāṃcid indriyam iti. ato ’dhikṛtānāṃ eva matyādīnāṃ pramāṇatvakhyāpanārtham āha — 
 tatpramāṇe || 
 § 166. tadvacanaṃ kim artham. pramāṇāntaraparikalpanānivṛttyartham. saṃnikarṣaḥ pramāṇam indriyaṃ pramāṇam iti kecit kalpayanti tannivṛttyarthaṃ tadity ucyate. tadeva matyādi pramāṇaṃ nānyad iti. 
 § 167. atha saṃnikarṣe pramāṇe sati indriye vā ko doṣaḥ? yadi saṃnikarṣaḥ pramāṇaṃ, sūkṣmavyavahitaviprakṛṣṭānām arthānām agrahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ. na hi te indriyaiḥ saṃnikṛṣyante. ataḥ sarvajñatvābhāvaḥ syāt. indriyam api yadi pramāṇaṃ sa eva doṣaḥ; alpaviṣayatvāt cakṣurādīnāṃ jñeyasya cāparimāṇatvāt. 
 § 168. sarvendriyasaṃnikarṣābhāvaś ca; cakṣurmanasoḥ prāpyakāritvābhāvāt. aprāpyakāritvaṃ ca uttaratra vakṣyate. 
 § 169. yadi jñānaṃ pramāṇaṃ phalābhāvaḥ. adhigamo hi phalam iṣṭaṃ na bhāvāntaram. sa cet pramāṇaṃ, na tasyānyat phalaṃ bhavitum arhati. phalavatā ca pramāṇena bhavitavyam. saṃnikarṣe indriye vā pramāṇe sati adhigamaḥ phalam arthāntarabhūtaṃ yujyate iti. tad ayuktam. yadi saṃnikarṣaḥ pramāṇam arthādhigamaḥ phalaṃ, tasya dviṣṭhatvāt tatphalenādhigamenāpi dviṣṭhena bhavitavyam iti arthādīnām apy adhigamaḥ prāpnoti. ātmanaś cetanatvāt tatraiva samavāya iti cet. na; jñasvabhāvābhāve sarveṣām acetanatvāt. jñasvabhāvābhyupagame vā ātmanaḥ svamatavirodhaḥ syāt. 
 § 170. nanu coktaṃ jñāne pramāṇe sati phalābhāva iti. naiṣaḥ doṣaḥ; arthādhigame prītidarśanāt. jñasvabhāvasyātmanaḥ karmamalīmasasya karaṇālambanād arthaniścaye prītir ūpajāyate. sā phalam ity ucyate. upekṣā ajñānanāśo vā phalam. rāgadveṣayor apraṇidhānam upekṣā. andhakārakalpājñānanāśo vā phalam ity ucyate. 
 § 171. pramiṇoti pramīyate ’nena pramitimātraṃ vā pramāṇam. kim anena pramīyate. jīvādir arthaḥ. yadi jīvāder adhigame pramāṇaṃ pramāṇādhigame ca anyat pramāṇaṃ parikalpayItavyam. tathā saty anavasthā. nānavasthā pradīpavat. yathā ghaṭādīnāṃ prakāśane pradīpo hetuḥ svasvarūpaprakāśane ’pi sa eva, na prakāśāntaraṃ mṛgyaṃ tathā pramāṇam apīti avaśyaṃ caitad abhyupagantavyam. prameyavat pramāṇasya pramāṇāntaraparikalpanāyāṃ svādhigamābhāvāt smṛtyabhāvaḥ. tadabhāvād vyavahāralopaḥ syāt. 
 § 172. vakṣyamānabhedāpekṣayā dvivacananirdeśaḥ. vakṣyate hi  ādye parokṣam, pratyakṣam anyad  iti sa ca dvivacananirdeśaḥ pramāṇāntarasaṃkhyānivṛttyarthaḥ. 
 § 173. uktasya pañcavidhasya jñānasya pramāṇadvayāntaḥpātitve pratipādite pratyakṣānumānādipramāṇadvayakalpanānivṛttyartham āha — 
 ādye parokṣam || 
 § 174. ādiśabdaḥ prāthamyavacana. ādau bhavam ādyam. kathaṃ dvayoḥ prathamatvam? mukhyopacārakalpanayā. matijñānaṃ tāvan mukhyakalpanayā prathamam. śrutam api tasya pratyāsattyā prathamam ity upacaryate. dvivacananirdeśasāmarthyād gauṇasyāpi grahaṇam. ādyaṃ ca ādyaṃ ca ādye matiśrute ity arthaḥ. tadubhayam api parokṣaṃ pramāṇam ity abhisaṃbadhyate. kuto ’sya parokṣatvam. parāyattatatvāt  matijñānaṃ indriyānindriyanimittam  iti vakṣyate  śrutam anindriyasya  iti ca. ataḥ parāṇīndriyāṇi manaś ca prakāśopadeśādi ca bāhyanimittaṃ pratītya tadāvaraṇakarmakṣayopaśamāpekṣasyātmano matiśrutam utpadyamānaṃ parokṣam ity ākhyāyate. ata upamānāgamādīnām atraivāntarbhāvaḥ. 
 § 175. abhihitalakṣaṇāt parokṣād itarasya sarvasya pratyakṣatvapratipādanārtham āha — 
 pratyakṣam anyat || 
 § 176. akṣṇoti vyāpnoti jānātīty akṣa ātmā. tam eva prāptakṣayopaśamaṃ prakṣīṇāvaraṇaṃ vā pratiniyataṃ pratyakṣam. avadhidarśanaṃ kevaladarśanam api akṣam eva pratiniyatam atas tasyāpi grahaṇaṃ prāpnoti. naiṣa doṣaḥ; jñānam ity anuvartate, tena darśanasya vyudāsah. evam api vibhaṅgajñānam akṣam eva pratiniyatam ato ’syāpi grahaṇaṃ prāpnoti. samyagity adhikārāt tannivṛttiḥ. samyagity anuvartate tena jñānaṃ viśiṣyate tato vibhaṅgajñānasya nivṛttiḥ kṛtā. tad dhi mithyādarśanodayād viparītārthaviṣayam iti na samyak. 
 § 177. syān matam indriyavyāpārajanitaṃ jñānaṃ pratyakṣaṃ vyatītendriyaviṣayavyāpāraṃ parokṣam ity etad avisaṃvādi lakṣaṇam abhyupagantavyam iti. tad ayuktam, āptasya pratyakṣajñānābhāvaprasaṅgāt yadi indriyanimittam eva jñānaṃ pratyakṣam iṣyate evaṃ sati āptasya pratyakṣajñānaṃ na syāt. na hi tasyendriyapūrvo ’rthādhigamaḥ. atha tasyāpi karaṇapūrvakam eva jñānaṃ kalpyate, tasyāsarvajñatvaṃ syāt. tasya mānasaṃ pratyakṣam iti cet; manaḥpraṇidhānapūrvakatvāt jñānasya sarvajñatvābhāva eva. āgamatas tatsiddhir iti cet. na; tasya pratyakṣajñānapūrvakatvāt. 
 § 178. yogipratyakṣam anyaj jñānaṃ divyam apy astīti cet. na tasya pratyakṣatvaṃ; indriyanimittatvābhāvāt; akṣam akṣaṃ prati yad vartate tat pratyakṣam ity abhyupagamāt. 
 § 179. kiṃ ca sarvajñatvābhāvaḥ pratijñāhānir vā. asya yogino yaj jñānaṃ tat pratyarthavaśavarti vā syād anekārthagrāhi vā. yadi pratyarthavaśavarti, sarvajñatvam asya nāsti yoginaḥ, jñeyasyānantyāt. athānekārthagrāhi, yā pratijñā —
	   vijānāti na vijñānam ekam arthadvayaṃ yathā | 
 ekam arthaṃ vijānāti na vijñānadvayam tathā | 
	  sā hīyate. 
 § 180. athavā  kṣaṇikāḥ sarvasaṃskārāḥ  iti pratijñā hīyate; anekakṣaṇa vṛttyekavijñānābhyupagamāt. anekārthagrahaṇaṃ hi krameṇeti. yugapad eveti cet. yo ’sya janmakṣaṇaḥ sa ātmalābhārtha eva. labhdātmalābhaṃ hi kiṃcit svakāryaṃ prati vyāpriyate. pradīpavad iti cet. tasyāpy anekakṣaṇaviṣayatāyāṃ satyām eva prakāśyaprakāśanābhyupagamāt. vikalpātītatvāt tasya śūnyatāprasaṅgaś ca. 
 § 181. abhihitobhayaprakārasya pramāṇasya ādiprakāraviśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 matiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃjñā cintābhinibodha ity anarthāntaram || 
 § 182. ādau uddiṣṭaṃ yaj jñānaṃ tasya paryāyaśabdā ete veditavyāḥ; matijñānāvaraṇakṣayopaśamāntaraṃganimittajanitopayogaviṣayatvād eteṣām śrutādiṣv apravṛtteś ca. mananaṃ matiḥ, smaraṇaṃ smṛtiḥ, saṃjñānaṃ saṃjñā, cintanaṃ cintā, abhinibodhanam abhinibodha iti. yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vigrahāntaraṃ vijñayam. 
 § 183. saty api prakṛtibhede rūḍhibalalābhāt paryāyaśabdatvam. yathā indraḥ śakraḥ purandara iti indanādikriyāhede ’pi śacīpater ekasyaiva saṃjñā. samabhirūḍhanayāpekṣayā teṣām arthāntarakalpanāyāṃ matyādiṣv api sa kramo vidyata eva. kiṃ tu matijñānāvaraṇakṣayopaśamanimittopayogaṃ nātivartanta iti ayam atrārtho vivakṣitaḥ. ‘iti’ śabdaḥ prakārāthaḥ evaṃ prakārā asya paryāyaśabdā iti. abhidheyārtho vā. matiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃjñā cintā abhinibodha ity etair yo ‘rtho ’bhidhīyate sa eka eva iti. 
 § 184. athāsyātmalābhe kiṃ nimittam ity ata āha — 
 tadindriyānindriyamittam || 
 § 185. indatīti indra ātmā. tasya jñasvabhāvasya tadāvaraṇakṣayopaśame sati svayam arthān grahītum asamarthasya yad arthopalabdhiliṃgaṃ tad indrasya liṃgam indriyam ity ucyate. athavā līnam arthaṃ gamayatīti liṃgam. ātmanaḥ sūkṣmasyāstitvādhigame liṃgam indriyam. yathā iha dhūmo ’gneḥ. evam idaṃ sparśanādi karaṇaṃ nāsati kartary ātmani bhavitum arhatīti jñātur astitvaṃ gamyate. athavā indra iti nāmakarmocyate. tena sṛṣtam indriyam iti. tatsparśanādi uttaratra vakṣyate. 
 § 186. anindriyaṃ manaḥ antaḥkaraṇam ity anarthāntaram. kathaṃ punar indriyapratiṣedhena indraliṃge eva manasi anindriyaśabdasya vṛtti. īṣadarthasya nañaḥ prayogāt. īṣadindriyam anindriyam iti. yathā anudarā kanyā iti. katham īṣadarthaḥ. imānīndriyāṇi pratiniyatadeśaviṣayāṇi kālāntarāvasthāyīni ca. na tathā manaḥ indrasya liṃgam api satpratiniyatadeśaviṣayaṃ kālāntarāvasthāyi ca. 
 § 187. tadantaḥkaraṇam iti cocyate. guṇadoṣavicārasmaraṇādivyāpare indriyānapekṣatvāc cakṣurādivad bahiranupabdheś ca antargataṃ karaṇam antaḥakaraṇam ity ucyate. * 
 § 188. tad iti kim artham. matijñānanirdeśārtham. nanu ca tadanantaraṃ ‘anantarasya vidhir vā bhavati pratiṣedho vā’ iti tasyaiva grahaṇaṃ bhavati. ihārtham uttarārthaṃ ca tad ity ucyate. yanmatyādiparyāyaśabdavācyaṃ jñānaṃ tadindriyānindriyanimittaṃ tadevāvagrahehāvāyadhāraṇā iti. itarathā hi prathamaṃ matyādiśabdavācyaṃ jñānam ity uktvā indriyānindriyanimittaṃ śrutam. tadevāvagrahehāvāyadhāraṇā ity aniṣṭam abhisaṃbadhyeta. 
 § 189. evaṃ nirjñātotpattinimittam anirṇītabhedam iti tadbhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 avagrahehāvāyadhāraṇā || 
 § 190. viṣayaviṣayisaṃnipātasamanantaram ādyaṃ grahaṇam avagrahaḥ. viṣayaviṣayisaṃnipāte sati darśanaṃ bhavati. tadanantaram arthagrahaṇam avagrahaḥ. yathā — cakṣuṣā śuklaṃ rūpam iti grahaṇam avagrahaḥ. avagrahagṛhīte ’rthe tadviśeṣākāṅkṣaṇam īhā. yathā śuklaṃ rūpaṃ kiṃ valākā patākā veti. viśeṣanirjñānād yāthātmyāvagamanam avāyaḥ. utpatananipatanapakṣavikṣepādibhir valākaiveyaṃ na patāketi. avetasya kālāntare ’vismaraṇakāraṇaṃ dhāraṇā. yathā saiveyaṃ balākā pūrvāhṇe yām aham adrākṣam iti. eṣām avagrahādīnām upanyāsakrama utpattikramakṛtaḥ. 
 § 191. uktānām avagrahādīnāṃ prabhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 bahubahuvidhakṣiprāniḥsṛtānuktadhruvāṇāṃ setarāṇām || 
 § 192. avagrahādayaḥ kriyāviśeṣāḥ prakṛtāḥ. tadapekṣo ’yaṃ karmanirdeśaḥ. bahvādīnāṃ setarāṇām iti. bahuśabdasya saṃkhyāvaipulyavācino grahaṇam aviśeṣāt. saṃkhyāvācī yathā, eko dvau bahava iti. vaipulyavācī yathā, bahur odano bahuḥ sūpa iti. vidhaśabdaḥ prakāravācī. kṣipragrahaṇam acirapratipattyartham. aniḥsṛtagrahaṇam asakalapudgalodgamārtham. anuktam abhiprāyeṇa grahaṇam. dhruvaṃ nirantaraṃ yathārthagrahaṇam. setaragrahaṇaṃ pratipakṣasaṃgrahārtham. 
 § 193. bahūnām avagrahaḥ alpasyāvagrahaḥ bahuvidhasyāvagrahaḥ ekavidhasyāvagraḥ kṣipram avagrahaḥ cireṇāvagrahaḥ aniḥsṛtasyāvagrahaḥ niḥsṛtasyāvagrahaḥ anuktasyāvagrahaḥ uktasyāvagrahaḥ dhruvasyāvagrahaḥ adhruvasyāvagrahaś ceti avagraho dvādaśavikalpaḥ. evam īhādayo ’pi. ta ete pañcabhir indriyadvārair manasā ca pratyekaṃ pradurbhāvyante. tatra bahvavagrhādayaḥ matijñānāvaraṇakṣayopaśamaprakarṣāt prabhavanti netare iti. teṣām abhyarhitatvād ādau grahaṇaṃ kriyate. 
 § 194. bahubahuvidhayoḥ kaḥ prativiśeṣaḥ; yāvatā bahuṣv api bahutvam asti bahuvidheṣv api bahutvam asti? ekaprakāranānāprakārakṛto viśeṣaḥ. uktaniḥsṛtayoḥ kaḥ prativiśeṣaḥ; yāvatā sakalaniḥsaraṇān niḥsṛtam. uktam apy evaṃ vidham eva? ayam asti viśeṣaḥ; anyopadeśapūrvakaṃ grahaṇam uktam. svata eva grahaṇaṃ niḥsṛtam. 
 § 195. apareṣāṃ kṣipraniḥsṛta iti pāṭhaḥ. ta evaṃ varṇayanti śrotrendriyeṇa śabdam avagṛhyamāṇaṃ mayūrasya vā kurarasya veti kaścit pratipadyate. aparaḥ svarūpam evāsṛitya iti. 
 § 196. dhruvāvagrahasya dhāraṇāyāś ca kaḥ prativiśeṣaḥ? ucyate, kṣayopaśamaprāptikāle viśuddhapariṇāmasaṃtatyā prāptāt kṣayopaśamāt prathamasamaye yathāvagrahas tathaiva dvitīyādiṣv api samayeṣu nono nābhyadhika iti dhruvāvagraha ity ucyate. yadā punarviśuddhapariṇāmasya saṃkleśapariṇāmasya ca miśraṇāt kṣayopaśamo bhavati tata utpadyamāno ’vagrahaḥ kadācit bahūnāṃ kadācid alpasya kadācid bahuvidhasya kadācid ekavidhasya veti nyūnādhikabhāvād adhruvāvagraha ity ucyate. dharaṇā punargṛhītārthāvismaraṇakāraṇam iti mahad anayor antaram. 
 § 197. yady avagrahādayo bahvādīnāṃ karmaṇām ākṣeptāraḥ, bahvādīni punarviśeṣaṇāni kasyety ata āha — 
 arthasya || 
 § 198. cakṣurādiviṣayo ’rthaḥ. tasya bahvādiviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭasya avagrahādayo bhavantīty abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate. kim artham idam ucyate yāvatā bahvādir artha eva? satyam evam, kintu pravādiparikalpanānivṛttyarthaṃ ‘arthasya’ ity ucyate. kecit pravādino manyante rūpādayo guṇā eva indriyaiḥ saṃnikṛṣyante tenaiteṣām eva grahaṇam iti. tad ayuktam; na hi te rūpādayo guṇā amūrtā indriyasaṃnikarṣam āpadyante. na tarhi idānīm idaṃ bhavati ‘rūpaṃ mayā dṛṣṭaṃ, gandho vā ghrāta’ iti. bhavati ca. katham? iyarti paryāyāṃs tair vā ’ryata ity artho dravyaṃ, tasminn indriyaiḥ saṃnikṛṣṇyamāṇe tadavyatirekād rūpādiṣv api saṃvyavahāro yujyate. 
 § 199 kim ime avagrahādayaḥ sarvasyendriyānindriyasya bhavanti uta kaścid viṣayaviśeṣo ’stīty ata āha —
