 vyañjanasyāvagrahaḥ || 
 § 200. vyañjanam avyaktaṃ śabdādijātaṃ tasyāvagraho bhavati nehādayaḥ. kim artham idam? niyamārtham, avagraha eva nehādaya iti. sa tarhi evakāraḥ kartavyaḥ? na kartavyaḥ, ‘siddhe vidhir ārabhyamāno niyamārtha’ iti antareṇaivakāraṃ niyamārtho bhaviṣyati. nanu avagrahagrahaṇam ubhayatra tulyam tatra kiṃ kṛto ’yaṃ viśeṣaḥ? arthāvagrahavyañjanāvagrahayor vyaktāvyaktakṛto viśeṣaḥ. katham? abhinavaśarāvādrīkaraṇavat. *  yathā jalakaṇadvitrāsiktaḥ sarāvo ’bhinavo nādrībhavati, *  sa eva punaḥ punaḥ sicyamānaḥ śanais timyati, evaṃ śrotrādiṣv indriyeṣu śabdādipariṇatāḥ pudgalā dvitrādiṣu samayeṣu gṛhyamānā na vyaktībhavanti, punaḥ punar avagrahe sati vyaktībhavanti. ato vyaktagrahaṇāt prāgvyañjanāvagrahaḥ vyaktagrahaṇam arthāvagrahaḥ. tato ’vyaktāvagrahaṇād īhādayo na bhavanti. 
 § 201. sarvendriyāṇām aviśeṣeṇa vyañjanāvagrahaprasaṅge yatrāsaṃbhavas tadarthapratiṣedam āha — 
 na cakṣuranindriyābhyām || 
 § 202. cakṣuṣā anindriyena ca vyañjanāvagraho na bhavati. kutaḥ? aprāpyakāritvāt. yato ’prāptam artham avidikkaṃ yuktaṃ saṃnikarṣaviṣaye ’vasthitaṃ bāhyaprakāśābhivyaktam upalabhate cakṣuḥ manaś cāprāptam ity anayor vyañjanāvagraho nāsti. 
 § 203. cakṣuṣo ’prāpyakāritvaṃ katham adhyavasīyate? āgamato yuktitaś ca. āgamatas tāvat 
 puṭṭhaṃ suṇodi saddaṃ apuṭṭhaṃ ceva passade rūaṃ |
	  gaṃdhaṃ rasaṃ ca phāsaṃ baddhaṃ puṭṭhaṃ viyāṇādi ||  
 § 204. yuktitaś ca — aprāpyakāri cakṣuḥ, spṛṣṭānavagrahāt. yadi prāpyakāri syāt tvagindriyavat spṛṣṭam añjanaṃ gṛhṇīyāt, na tu gṛhṇāty ato manovadaprāpyakārīty avaseyam. tataś cakṣurmanasī varjayitvā śeṣāṇām indriyāṇāṃ vyañjanāvagrahaḥ. sarveṣām indriyānindriyāṇām arthāvagraha iti siddham. 
 § 205. āha nirdiṣṭaṃ matijñānaṃ lakṣaṇato vikalpataś ca; tadanantaram uddhiṣṭaṃ yat śrutaṃ tasyedānīṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vikalpaś ca vaktavya ity ata āha — 
 śrutaṃ matipūrvaṃ dvyanekadvādaśabhedam || 
 § 206. śrutaśabdo ’yaṃ śravaṇam upādāya vyutpādito ’pi rūḍhivaśāt kasmiṃś cij jñānaviśeṣe vartate. yathā kuśalavanakarma pratītya vyutpādito ’pi kuśalaśabdo rūḍhivaśāt paryavadāte vartate. kaḥ punar asau jñānaviśeṣa iti? ata āha ‘śrutaṃ matipūrvam’ iti. śrutasya pramāṇatvaṃ pūrayatīti pūrvaṃ nimittaṃ kāraṇam ity anarthāntaram. matir nirdiṣṭā. matiḥ pūrvam asya matipūrvaṃ matikāraṇam ity arthaḥ. yadi matipūrvaṃ śrutaṃ tadapi matyātmakaṃ prāpnoti ‘kāraṇasadṛśaṃ hi loke kāryaṃ dṛṣṭam’ iti. naitad aikāntikam. daṇḍādikāraṇo ’yaṃ ghaṭo na daṇḍādyātmakaḥ. api ca sati tasmiṃs tadabhāvāt. saty api matijñāne bāhyaśrutajñānanimittasaṃnidhāne ’pi prabalaśrutāvaraṇodayasya śrutābhāvaḥ. śrutāvaraṇakṣayopaśamaprakarṣe tu sati śrutjañānam utpadyata iti matijñānaṃ nimttamātraṃ jñeyam. 
 § 207. āha, śrutam anādinidhanam iṣyate. tasya matipūrvakatve tadabhavāḥ; ādimato ’ntavattvāt. tataś ca puruṣakṛtitvād aprāmāṇyam iti? naiṣa doṣaḥ; dravyādisāmānyārpaṇāt śrutam anādinidhanam iṣyate. na hi kenacit puruṣeṇa kvacit kadācit kathaṃcid utprekṣitam iti. teṣām eva viśeṣāpekṣayā ādir antaś ca saṃbhavatīti ‘matipūrvam’ ity ucyate. yathāṅkuro bījapūrvakaḥ sa ca saṃtānāpekṣayā anādinidhana iti. na cāpauruṣeyatvaṃ prāmāṇyakāraṇam; caurādyupadeśasyāsmaryamāṇakartṛkasya prāmāṇyaprasaṅgāt. anityasya ca pratyakṣādeḥ prāmāṇye ko virodhaḥ. 
 § 208. āha, prathamasamyaktvotpattau yugapaj jñānapariṇāmān matipūrvakatvaṃ śrutasya nopapadyata iti? tad ayuktam; samyaktvasya tadapekṣatvāt. ātmalābhas tu kramavān iti matipūrvakatvavyāghātābhāvaḥ. 
 § 209. āha, matipūrvaṃ śrutam ity etal lakṣaṇam avyāpi śrutapūrvam api śrutam iṣyate. tadyathā — śabdapariṇatapudgalaskandhād āhitavarṇapadavākyādibhāvāc cakṣurādiviṣayāc ca ādyaśrutaviṣayabhāvam āpannād avyabhicāriṇaḥ kṛtasaṃgītir jano ghaṭāj jaladhāraṇādi kāryaṃ saṃbandhyantaraṃ pratipadyate, dhūmāder vāgnyādidravyaṃ, tadā śrutāt śrutapratipattir iti? naiṣa doṣaḥ; tasyāpi matipūrvakatvam upacārataḥ. śrutam api kvacin matir ity upacaryate, matipūrvakatvād iti. 
 § 210. bhedaśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate — dvibhedam anekabhedaṃ dvādaśabhedam iti. dvi bhedaṃ tāvat — aṅgabāhyam aṅgapraviṣṭam iti. aṅgabāhyam anekavidhaṃ daśavaikālikottarādhyayanādi. aṅgapraviṣṭaṃ dvādaśavidham. tadyathā, ācāraḥ sūtrakṛtaṃ sthānaṃ samavāyaḥ vyākhyāprajñaptiḥ jñātṛdharmakathā upāsakādhyayanaṃ antakṛddaśaṃ anuttaraupapādikadaśaṃ praśnavyākaraṇaṃ vipākasūtraṃ dṛṣṭivāda iti. dṛṣṭivādaḥ pañcavidhaḥ — parikarma sūtraṃ prathamānuyogaḥ pūrvagataṃ cūlikā ceti. tatra pūrvagataṃ caturdaśavidham — utpādapūrvam agrāyaṇīyaṃ vīryānupravādam astināstipravādaṃ jñānapravādaṃ satyapravādam ātmapravādaṃ karmapravādaṃ pratyākhyānanāmadheyaṃ vidyānupravādaṃ kalyāṇanāmadheyaṃ prāṇāvāyaṃ kriyāviśālaṃ lokabindusāram iti. tadetat śrutaṃ dvibhedam anekabhedaṃ dvādaśabhedam iti. 
 § 211. kiṃ kṛto ’yaṃ viśeṣaḥ? vaktṛviśeṣakṛtaḥ. trayo vaktāraḥ — sarvajñas tīrthakara itaro vā śrutakevalī ārātīyaś ceti. tatra sarvajñena paramarṣiṇā paramācintyakevalajñānavibhūtiviśeṣeṇa arthata āgama uddiṣṭaḥ. tasya pratyakṣadarśitvāt prakṣīṇadoṣatvāc ca prāmāṇyam. tasya sākṣāc chiṣyair buddhyatiśayarddhiyuktair gaṇadharaiḥ śrutakevalibhir anusmṛtagrantharacanam aṅgapūrvalakṣaṇam. tatpramāṇam; tatprāmāṇyāt. ārātīyair punar ācāryaiḥ kāladoṣāt saṃkṣiptāyurmatibalaśiṣyānugrahārthaṃ daśavaikālikādyupanibaddham. tatpramāṇam arthatas tadevedam iti kṣīrārṇavajalaṃ ghaṭagṛhītam iva. 
 § 212. vyākhyātaṃ parokṣam. pratyakṣam idānīṃ vaktavyam. tad dvedhā — deśapratyakṣaṃ sarvapratyakṣaṃ ca. deśapratyakṣam avadhimanaḥparyayajñāne. sarvapratyakṣaṃ kevalam. yady evam idam eva tāvad avidhijñānaṃ triḥprakārasya pratyakṣasyādyaṃ vyākriyatām ity atrocyate — dvividho ’vadhir bhavapratyayaḥ kṣayopaśamanimittaś ceti. tatra bhavapratyaya ucyate — 
 bhavapratyayo ’vadhir devanārakāṇām || 
 § 213. bhava ity ucyate. ko bhavaḥ? āyurnāmakarmodayanimitta ātmanaḥ paryāyo bhavaḥ. pratyayaḥ kāraṇaṃ nimittam ity anarthāntaram. bhavaḥ pratyayo ’sya bhavapratyayo ’vadhir devanārakāṇāṃ veditavyaḥ. yady evaṃ tatra kṣayopaśamanimittatvaṃ na prāpnoti? naiṣa dośaḥ; tadāśrayāt tatsiddheh. bhavaṃ pratītya kṣayopaśamaḥ saṃjāyata iti kṛtvā bhavaḥ pradhānakāraṇam ity upadiśyate. yathā patatriṇo gamanam ākāśe bhavanimittam, na śikṣāguṇaviśeṣaḥ tathā devanārakāṇāṃ vrataniyamādyabhāve ’pi jāyata ‘iti bhavapratyayaḥ’ ity ucyate. itarathā hi bhavaḥ sādhāraṇa iti kṛtvā sarveṣām aviśeṣaḥ syāt. iṣyate ca tatrāvadheḥ prakarṣāprakarṣavṛttiḥ. ‘devanārakāṇām’ ity aviśeṣābhidhāne ’pi samyagdṛṣṭīnām eva grahaṇam. kutaḥ? avadhigrahaṇāt. mityādṛṣṭīnāṃ ca vibhaṅga ity ucyate. prakarṣāprakarṣavṛttiś ca āgamato vijñeyā. 
 § 214. yadi bhavapratyayo ’vadhir devanārakāṇām, atha kṣayopaśamahetukaḥ keṣām ity āha — 
 kṣayopaśamanimittaḥ ṣaḍvikalpaḥ śeṣāṇām || 
 § 215. avadhijñānāvaraṇasya deśaghātisparddhakānām udaye sati sarvaghātisparddhakānām udayābhāvaḥ kṣayaḥ teṣām evānudayaprāptānāṃ sadavasthā upaśamaḥ. tau nimittam asyeti kṣayopaśamanimittaḥ. sa śeṣāṇām veditavyaḥ. ke punaḥ śeṣāḥ. manuṣyās tiryañcaś ca. teṣv api yatra sāmarthyam asti tatraiva veditavyaḥ. na hy asaṃjñinām aparyāptakānāṃ ca tatsāmarthyam asti. saṃjñināṃ paryāptakānāṃ ca na sarveṣām. keṣāṃ tarhi? yathoktasamyagdarśanādinimttasaṃnidhāne sati śāntakṣīṇakarmaṇāṃ tasyopalabdhir bhavati. sarvasya kṣayopaśamanimittatve kṣayopaśam agrahaṇaṃ niyamārthaṃ kṣayopaśama eva nimittaṃ na bhava iti. sa eṣo ’vadhiḥ ṣaḍvikalpaḥ. kutaḥ? anugāmyananugāmivardhamānahīyamānāvasthitānavasthitabhedāt. kaścid avadhir bhāskaraprakāśavad gacchantam anugacchati. kaścin nānugacchati tatraivātipatati unmukhapraśnādeśipuruṣavacanavat. aparo ’vadhiḥ araṇinirmathanotpannaśuṣkaparṇopacīyamānendhananicayasamiddhapāvakavatsamyagdarśanādiguṇaviśuddhipariṇāmasaṃnidhānād yat -parimāṇa utpannas tato varddhate ā asaṃkhyeyalokebhyaḥ. aparo ’vadhiḥ paricchinnopādānasaṃtatyagniśikhāvatsamyagdarśanādiguṇahānisaṃkleśapariṇāmavṛddhiyogād yat- parimānā utpannas tato hīyate ā aṅgulasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgāt. itaro ’vadhiḥ samyagdarśanādiguṇāvasthānād yat parimāṇa utpannas tat primāṇā evāvasthiṣṭhate; na hīyate nāpi vardhate liṅgavat ā bhavakṣayād ā kevalajñānotpatter vā. anyo ’vadhiḥ samyagdarśanādiguṇavṛddhihāniyogād yatparimāṇa utpannas tato vardhate yāvad anena vardhitavyaṃ hīyate ca yāvad anena hātavyaṃ vāyuvegapreritajalormivat. evaṃ ṣaḍvikalpo ’vadhir bhavati. 
 § 216. evaṃ vyākhyātam avadhijñānaṃ, tadantaram idānīṃ manaḥparyayajñānaṃ vaktavyam. tasya bhedaḥ puraḥsaraṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vyācikhyāsur idam āha — 
 ṛjuvipulamatī manaḥparyayaḥ || 
 § 217. ṛjvī nirvartitā praguṇā ca. kasmān nirvartitā? vākkāyamanaḥkṛtārthasya paramanogatasya vijñānāt. ṛjvī matir yasya so ’yaṃ ṛjumatiḥ. anirvartitā kuṭilā ca vipulā. kasmād anirvartitā? vākkāyamanaḥkṛtārthasya parakīyamanogatasya vijñānāt. vipulā matir yasya so ’yaṃ vipulamatiḥ. ṛjumatiś ca vipulamatiś ca ṛjuvipulamatī. ekasya matiśabdasya gatārthatvād aprayogaḥ. athavā ṛjuś ca vipulā ca ṛjuvipule. ṛjuvipule matī yayos tau ṛjuvipulamatī iti. sa eṣa manaḥparyayo dvividhaḥ ṛjumatir vipulamatir iti. 
 § 218. āha, ukto bhedaḥ, lakṣaṇam idānīṃ vaktavyam ity atrocyate — vīryāntarāyamanaḥparyayajñānāvaraṇakṣayopaśamāṅgopāṅganāmalābhāvaṣṭambhād ātmanaḥ parakīyamanaḥsaṃbandena labdhavṛttir upayogo manaḥparyayaḥ. matijñānaprasaṅga iti cet? uktottaraṃ purastāt. apekṣākāraṇaṃ mana iti. parakīyamanasi vyavasthito ’rthaḥ anena jñāyate ity etāvad atrāpekṣyate. tatra ṛjumatir manaḥparyayaḥ kālato jaghanyena jīvānām ātmanaś ca dvitrāṇi bhavagrahaṇāni, utkarṣeṇa saptāṣṭau gatyāgatyādibhiḥ prarūpayati. kṣetrato jaghanyena gavyūtipṛthaktvaṃ, utkarṣeṇa yojanapṛthaktvasyābhyantaraṃ, na bahiḥ. dvitīyaḥ kālato jaghanyena saptāṣṭau bhavagrahaṇāni, utkarṣeṇāsaṃkhyeyāni gatyāgatyādibhiḥ prarūpayati. kṣetrato jaghanyena yojanapṛthaktvaṃ, utkarṣeṇa mānuṣottaraśailasyābhyantaraṃ, na bahiḥ. 
 § 219. uktayor anayoḥ punar api viśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 viśuddhyapratipātābhyāṃ tadviśeṣaḥ || 
 § 220. tadāvaraṇakṣayopaśame sati ātmanaḥ prasādo viśuddhiḥ. pratipatanaṃ pratipātaḥ. na pratipātaḥ apratipātaḥ. upaśāntakaṣāyasya cāritramohodrekāt pracyutasaṃyamaśikharasya pratipāto bhavati. kṣīṇakaṣāyasya pratipātakāraṇābhāvād apratipātaḥ. viśuddhiś ca apratipātaś ca viśuddhyapratipātau. tābhyāṃ viśuddhyapratipātābhyām. tayor viśeṣas tadviśeṣaḥ. tatra viśuddhyā tāvat — ṛjumater vipulamatir dravyakṣetrakālabhāvair viśuddhataraḥ. katham? iha yaḥ kārmaṇadravyānantabhāgo ’ntyaḥ sarvāvadhinā jñātas tasya punar anantabhāgīkṛtasyāntyo bhāga ṛjumater viṣayaḥ. tasya ṛjumativiṣayasyānantabhāgīkṛtasyāntyo bhāgo vipulamater viṣayaḥ. anantasyānantabhedatvāt. dravyakṣetrakālato viśuddhir uktā. bhāvato viśuddhiḥ sūkṣmataradravyaviṣayatvād eva veditavyā, prakṛṣṭakṣayopaśamaviśuddhiyogāt. apratipātenāpi vipulamatir viśiṣṭaḥ; svāmināṃ pravardhamānacāritrodayatvāt. ṛjumatiḥ punaḥ pratipātī; svāmināṃ kaṣāyodrekād dhīyamānacāritrodayatvāt. 
 § 221. yady asya manaḥparyayasya pratyātmamayaṃ viśeṣaḥ, athānayor avadhimanaḥparyayayoḥ kuto viśeṣaḥ ity ata āha — 
 viśuddhikṣetrasvāmiviṣayebhyo ’vadhimanaḥparyayayoḥ || 
 § 222. viśuddhiḥ prasādaḥ. kṣetraṃ yatrasthān bhāvān pratipadyate. svāmī prayoktā. viṣayo jñeyaḥ. tatrāvadher manaḥparyayo viśuddhataraḥ. kutaḥ? sūkṣmaviṣayatvāt. kṣetram uktam. viṣayo vakṣyate. svāmitvaṃ pratyutyate. prakṛṣṭacāritraguṇopeteṣu vartate pramattādiṣu kṣīṇakaṣayānteṣu. tatra cotpadyamānaḥ pravarddhamānacāritreṣu na hīyamānacāritreṣu. pravarddhamānacāritreṣu cotpadyamānaḥ saptavidhānyatamarddhiprāpteṣūpajāyate netareṣu. ṛddhiprāpteṣu keṣucin na sarveṣu. ity asyāyaṃ svāmiviśeṣo viśiṣṭasaṃyamagrahaṇaṃ vā vākye prakṛtam. avadhiḥ punaś cāturgatikeṣv iti svāmibhedād apy anayor viśeṣaḥ. 
 § 223. idānīṃ kevalajñānalakṣaṇābhidhānaṃ prāptakālam. tadullaṅghya jñānāṃ viṣayanibandhaḥ parīkṣyate. kutaḥ? tasya ‘mohakṣayāj jñānadarśanāvaraṇāntarāyakṣayāc ca kevalam’ ity atra vakṣyamānatvāt. yady evam ādyayor eva tāvan matiśrutayor viṣayanibandha ucyatām ity ata āha — 
 matiśrutayor nibandho dravyesv asarvaparyāyeṣu || 
 § 224. nibandhanaṃ nibandhaḥ. kasya? viṣayasya. tadviṣayagrahaṇaṃ kartavyam? na kartavyam. prakṛtaṃ viṣayagrahaṇam. kva prakṛtam? ‘viśuddhikṣetrasvāmiviṣayebhyaḥ’ ity atra. atas tasyārthavaśād vibhaktipariṇāmo bhavatīti ‘viṣayasya’ ity abhisaṃbadhyate. ‘dravyeṣu’ iti bahuvacananirdeśaḥ sarveṣāṃ jīvadharmādharmakālākāśapudgalānāṃ saṃgrahārthaḥ. tadviśeṣaṇārthaṃ ‘asarvaparyāya’ grahaṇam. tāni dravyāṇi matiśrutayor viṣayabhāvam āpadyamānāni katipayair eva paryāyair viṣayabhāvam āskandanti na sarvaparyāyair anantair apīti. atrāha — dharmāstikāyādīny atīndriyaṇi teṣu matijñānaṃ na pravartate. ataḥ sarvadravyeṣu matijñānaṃ vartata ity ayuktam? naiṣa doṣaḥ; anindriyākhyaṃ karaṇam asti tadālambano noindriyāvaraṇakṣayopaśamalabdhipūrvaka upayogo ’vagrahādirūpaḥ pragevopajāyate. tatas tatpūrvaṃ śrutajñānaṃ tadviṣayeṣu svayogyeṣu vyāpriyate. 
 § 225. atha matiśrutayor anantaranirdeśārhasyāvadheḥ ko viṣayanibandha ity ata āha — 
 rūpiṣv avadeḥ || 
 § 226. ‘viṣayanibandhaḥ’ ity anuvartate. ‘rūpiṣu’ ity anena pudgalāḥ pudgaladravyasaṃbandhāś ca jīvāḥ parigṛhyante. rūpiṣv evāvadher viṣayanibandho nārūpiṣv iti niyamaḥ kriyate. rūpiṣv api bhavan na sarvaparyāyeṣu, svayogyeṣv evety avadhāraṇārtham asarvaparyāyeṣv ity abhisaṃbadhyate. 
 § 227. atha tadanantaranirdeśabhājo manaḥparyayasya ko viṣayanibandha ity ata āha — 
 tadanantabhāge manaḥparyayasya || 
 § 228. yad etad rūpi dravyaṃ sarvāvadhijñānaviṣayatvena samarthitaṃ tasyānantabhāgīkṛtasyaikasmin bhāge manaḥparyayaḥ pravartate. 
 § 229. athānte yan nirdiṣṭaṃ kevalajñānaṃ tasya ko viṣayanibandha ity ata āha — 
 sarvadravyaparyāyeṣu kevalasya || 
 § 230. dravyāṇi ca paryāyāś ca dravyaparyāyā iti itaretarayogalakṣaṇo dvandvaḥ. tadviśeṣaṇaṃ ‘sarva’ grahaṇaṃ pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate, sarveṣu dravyeṣu sarveṣu paryāyeṣv iti. jīvadravyāṇi tāvad anantānantāni tato ’py anantānantāni pudgaladravyāṇi ca aṇuskandhabhedabhinnāni, dharmādharmākāśāni trīṇi, kālaś cāsaṃkhyeyas teṣāṃ paryāyāś ca trikālabhuvaḥ pratyekam anantānantās teṣu. dravyaṃ paryāyajātaṃ vā na kiṃcit kevalajñānasya viṣayabhāvam atikrāntam asti. aparimitamāhātmyaṃ hi tad iti jñāpanārthaṃ ‘sarvadravyaparyāyeṣu’ ity ucyate. 
 § 231. āha viṣayanibandho ’vadhṛto matyādīnām. idaṃ tu na nirjñātam ekasminn ātmani svanimittasaṃnidhānopajanitavṛttīni jñānāni yaugapadyena kati bhavantīty ucyate —  
 ekādīni bhājyāni yugapad ekasminn ā caturbhyaḥ || 
 § 232. ekaśabdaḥ saṃkhyāvacī, ādiśabdo ’vayavavacanaḥ. eka ādir yeṣāṃ tāni imāny ekādīni. bhājyāni vibhaktavyāni. yaugapadyenaikasminn ātmani. ā kutaḥ? ā caturbhyaḥ. tadyathā ekaṃ tāvat kevalajñānaṃ, na tena sahānyāni kṣāyopaśamikāni yugapadavatiṣṭhante. dve matiśrute. trīṇi matiśrutāvadhijñānāni, matiśrutamanaḥparyayajñānāni vā. catvāri matiśrutāvadhimanaḥparyayajñānāni. na pañca santi, kevalasyāsahāyatvāt. 
 § 233. atha yathoktāni matyādīni jñānavyapadeśam eva labhante utānyathāpīty ata āha — 
 matiśrutāvadhayo viparyayaś ca || 
 § 234. viparyayo mithyety arthaḥ. kutaḥ? samyagadhikārāt. ‘ca’ śabdah samuccayārthaḥ. viparyayaś ca samyak ceti. kutaḥ punar eṣāṃ viparyayaḥ? mithyādarśanena sahaikārthasamavāyāt sarajaskakaṭukālābugatadugdhavat. nanu ca tatrādhāradoṣād dugdasya rasaviparyayo bhavati. na ca tathā matyajñānādīnāṃ viṣayagrahaṇe viparyayaḥ. tathā hi, samyagdṛṣṭir yathā cakṣurādibhī rūpādīn upalabhate tathā mityādṛṣṭir api matyajñānena. yathā ca samyagdṛṣṭiḥ śrutena rūpādin jānāti nirūpayati ca tathā mithyādṛṣṭir api śrutājñānena. yathā cāvadhijñānena samyagdṛṣṭiḥ rūpiṇo ’rthānavagacchati tathā mithyādṛṣṭir vibhaṅgajñāneneti. 
 § 235. atrocyate — 
 sadasator aviśeṣād yadṛcchopalabdher unmattavat || 
 § 236. sad vidyamānam asad avidyamānam ity arthaḥ. tayor aviśeṣeṇa yadṛchhayā upalabder viparyayo bhavati. kadācid rūpādi sad apy asad iti pratipadyate, asad api sad iti, kadācit sat sad eva, asad apy asad eveti mithyādarśanodayād adhyavasyati. yathā pittodayākulitabuddhir mātaraṃ bhāryeti, bhāryām api māteti manyate. yadṛcchayā yadāpi mātaraṃ mātaiveti bhāryam api bhāryeveti ca tadāpi na tatsamyagjñānam. *  evaṃ matyādīnām api rūpādiṣu viparyayo veditavyaḥ. tathā hi, kaścin mityādarśanapariṇāma ātmany avasthito rūpādyupalabdhau satyām api kāraṇaviparyāsaṃ bhedābhedaviparyāsaṃ svarūpaviparyāsaṃ ca janayati. 
 § 237. kāraṇaviparyāsas tāvad — rūpādīnām ekaṃ kāraṇam amūrtaṃ nityam iti kecit kalpayanti. apare pṛthivyādijātibhinnāḥ paramāṇavaś catustridvyeka guṇās tulyajātīyānāṃ kāryāṇām ārambhakā iti. anye varṇayanti — pṛthivyādīni catvāri bhūtāni, bhautikadharmā varṇagandharasasparśāḥ, eteṣāṃ samudāyo rūpaparamāṇur aṣṭaka ity ādi. itare varṇayanti — pṛthivyaptejovāyavaḥ kāṭhinyādidravatvādyuṣṇatvādīraṇatvādiguṇā jātibhinnāḥ paramāṇavaḥ kāryasyārambhakāḥ. 
 § 238. bhedābhedaviparyāsaḥ kāraṇāt kāryam arthāntarabhūtam eveti anarthāntarabhūtam eveti ca parikalpanā. 
 § 239. svarūpaviparyāso rūpādiyo nirvikalpāḥ santi na santy eva vā. tadākārapariṇataṃ vijñānam eva. na ca tadālambanaṃ vastu bāhyam iti. evam anyān api parikalpanābhedān dṛṣṭeṣṭaviruddhān mithyādarśanodayāt kalpayanti tatra ca śraddhānam utpādayanti. tatas tanmatyajñānaṃ śrutājñānam vibhaṅgajñānaṃ ca bhavati. samyagdarśanaṃ punas tatvārthādhigame śraddhānam utpādayati. tatas tanmatijñānaṃ śrutajñām avadhijñānānaṃ ca bhavati. 
 § 240. āha pramāṇaṃ dvi prakāraṃ varṇitam. pramāṇaikadeśāś ca nayās tadanantaroddeśabhājo nirdeṣṭavyā ity ata āha — 
 naigamasaṃgrahavyavahārarjusūtraśabdasamabhirūḍhaivaṃbhūtā nayāḥ || 
 § 241. eteṣāṃ sāmānyaviśeṣalakṣaṇaṃ vaktavyam. sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tāvad vastuny anekāntātmany avirodhena hetvarpaṇāt sādhyaviśeṣasya yathātmyaprāpaṇapravaṇaḥ prayogo nayaḥ. sa dvedhā dravyārthikaḥ paryāyārthikaś ceti. dravyaṃ sāmānyam utsargaḥ anuvṛttir ity arthaḥ. tadviṣayo dravyārthikaḥ. paryāyo viśeṣo ’pavādo vyāvṛttir ity arthaḥ. tadviṣayaḥ paryāyārthikaḥ. tayor bhedā naigamādayaḥ. 
 § 242. teṣāṃ viśeṣalakṣaṇam ucyate — anabhinirvṛttārthasaṃkalpamātragrāhī naigamaḥ. kaṃcit puruṣaṃ parigṛhītaparaśuṃ gacchantam avalokya kaścit pṛcchati kim arthaṃ bhavān gacchatīti. sa āha prastham ānetum iti. nāsau tadā prasthaparyāyaḥ saṃnihitaḥ. tadabhinirvṛttaye saṃkalpamātre prasthavyavhāraḥ. tathā edhodakādyāharaṇe vyāpriyamāṇaṃ kaścit pṛcchati kiṃ karoti bhavān iti. sa āha odanaṃ pacāmīti. na tadaudanaparyāyaḥ, saṃnihitaḥ, tadarthe vyāpāre sa prayujyate. evaṃ prakāro lokasaṃvyavahāraḥ anabhinirvṛttārthasaṃkalpamātraviṣayo naigamasya gocaraḥ. 
 § 243. svajātyavirodhenaikadhyam upānīya paryāyān ākrāntabhedān aviśeṣeṇa samastagrahaṇāt saṃgrahaḥ. sat, dravyaṃ, ghaṭa ity ādi. sad ity ukte sad iti vāgvijñanānupravṛttiliṅgānumitasattādhārabhūtānām aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣāṃ saṃgrahaḥ. dravyam ity ukte ’pi dravati gacchati tāṃs tān paryāyān ity upalakṣitānāṃ jīvājīvatadbhedaprabhedānāṃ saṃgrahaḥ. tathā ghaṭa ity ukte ’pi ghaṭabuddhyabhidhānānugamaliṅgānumitasakalārthasaṃgrahaḥ. evam prakāro ’nyo ’pi saṃgrahanayasya viṣayaḥ. 
 § 244. saṃgrahanayākṣiptānām arthānāṃ vidhipūrvakam avaharaṇaṃ vyavahāraḥ. ko vidhiḥ? yaḥ saṃgrahagṛhīto ’rthas tadānupūrveṇaiva vyavahāraḥ pravartata ity ayaṃ vidhiḥ. tad yathā — sarvasaṃgraheṇa yat sattvaṃ gṛhītaṃ tac cānapekṣitaviśeṣaṃ nālaṃ saṃvyavahārāyeti vyavahāranaya āśrīyate. yat sat tad dravyaṃ guṇo veti. dravyeṇāpi saṃgrahākṣiptena jīvājīvaviśeṣānapekṣeṇa na śakyaḥ saṃvyavahāra iti jīvadravyam ajīvadravyam iti vā vyavahāra āśrīyate. jīvājīvāv api ca saṃgrahākṣiptau nālaṃ saṃvyavahārāyeti pratyekaṃ devanārakādir ghaṭādiś ca vyavahāreṇāśrīyate. evam ayaṃ nayas tāvad vartate yāvat punar nāsti vibhāgaḥ. 
 § 245. ṛjuṃ praguṇaṃ sūtrayati tan trayatīti ṛjusūtraḥ. pūrvāparāṃs trikālaviṣayān atiśayya vartamānakālaviṣayān ādatte atītānāgatayor vinaṣṭānutpannatvena vyavahārābhāvāt. tac ca vartamānaṃ samayamātram. tadviṣayaparyāyamātragrāhyam ṛjusūtraḥ. nanu saṃvyavahāralopaprasaṅga iti ced? na; asya nayasya viṣayamātrapradarśanaṃ kriyate. sarvanayasamūhasādhyo hi lokasaṃvyavahāraḥ. 
 § 246. liṅgasaṃkhyāsādhanādivyabhicāranivṛttiparaḥ śabdanayaḥ. tatra liṅgavyabhicāraḥ — puṣyas tārakā nakṣatram iti. saṃkhyāvyabhicṝaḥ — jalam āpaḥ, varṣā ṛtuḥ, āmrā vanam, varaṇā nagaram iti. sādhanavyabhicāraḥ — senā parvatam adhivasati. puruṣavyabhicāraḥ — ehi manye rathena yāsyasi, na hi yāsyasi, yātas te piteti. kālavyabhicāraḥ — viśvadṛśvā ’sya putro janitā. bhāvi kṛtyam āsīd iti. upagrahavyabhicāraḥ — saṃtiṣṭhate pratiṣṭhate viramaty uparamatīti. evaṃ prakāraṃ vyavahāramanyāyyaṃ manyate; anyārthasyānyārthena saṃbandhābhāvāt. lokasamayavirodha iti cet? virudhyatām. tattvam iha mīmāṃsyate, na bhaiṣajyam āturecchānuvarti. 
 § 247. nānārthaśamabhirohaṇāt samabhirūḍhaḥ. yato nānārthān samatīty aikam artham ābhimukhyena rūḍhaḥ samabhirūḍhaḥ. gaur ity ayaṃ śabdo vāgādiṣv artheṣu vartamānaḥ paśāv abhirūḍhaḥ. athavā arthagatyarthaḥ śabdaprayogaḥ. tatraikasyārthasyaikena gatārthatvāt paryāyaśabdaprayogo ’narthakaḥ. śabdabhedāś ced asti arthabhedenāpy avaśyaṃ bhavitavyam iti. nānārthasamabhirohaṇāt samabhirūḍhaḥ. indanād indraḥ śakanāc chakraḥ pūrdāranāt puradara *  ity evaṃ sarvatra. athavā yo yatrābhirūḍhaḥ sa tatra sametyābhimukhenārohaṇāt samabhirūḍhaḥ. yathā kva bhavān āste? ātmanīti. kutaḥ? vastv antare vṛttyabhāvāt. yady anyasyānyatra vṛttiḥ syāt, jñānādīnāṃ rūpādīnāṃ cākaśe vṛttiḥ syāt. 
 § 248. yenātmanā bhūtas tenaivādhyavasāyayatīti evaṃbhūtaḥ. svābhipretakriyāpariṇatikṣaṇe eva sa śabdo yukto nānyadeti. yadaivendati tadaivendro nābhiṣecako na pūjaka iti. yadaiva gacchati tadaiva gaur na sthito na śayita iti. athavā yenātmanā yena jñānena bhūtaḥ pariṇatas tenaivādhyavasāyayati. yathendrāgnijñānapariṇata ātmaivendro ’gniś ceti. 
 § 249. uktā naigamādayo nayāḥ. uttarottarasūkṣmaviṣayatvād eṣāṃ kramaḥ pūrvapūrvahetukatvāc ca. evam ete nayāḥ pūrvapūrvaviruddhamahāviṣayā uttarottarānukūlālpaviṣayā dravyasyānantaśakteḥ pratiśakti vibhidyamānā bahuvikalpā jāyante. ta ete guṇapradhānatayā parasparatantrāḥ samyagdarśanahetavaḥ puruṣārthakriyāsādhanasāmarthyāt tantvādaya iva yathopāyaṃ viniveśyamānāḥ paṭādisaṃjñāḥ svatantrāś cāsamarthāḥ. 
 § 250. tantvādaya iveti viṣama upanyāsaḥ. tantvādayo nirapekṣā api kāṃcid arthamātrāṃ janayanti. bhavati hi kaścit pratyekaṃ tantus tvaktrāṇe samarthaḥ. ekaś ca balvajo bandhane samarthaḥ. ime punar nayā nirapekṣāḥ santo na kāṃcid api samyagdarśanamātrāṃ prādur bhāvayantīti? naiṣa doṣaḥ; abhihitānavabodhāt. abhihitam artham anavabudhya pareṇedam upālabhyate. etad uktaṃ, nirapekṣeṣu tantvādiṣu paṭādikāryaṃ nāstīti. yat tu tenopadarśitaṃ na tat paṭādikāryam. kiṃ tarhi? kevalaṃ tantvādikāryam. tantvādikaryam api tantvādyavayaveṣu nirapekṣeṣu nāsty eva ity asmatpakṣasiddhir eva. atha tantvādiṣu paṭādikāryaṃ śaktyapekṣayā astīty ucyate. nayeṣv api nirapekṣeṣu buddhyabhidhānarūpeṣu kāraṇavaśāt samyagdarśanahetutvavipariṇatisadbhāvāt. śaktyātmanāstitvam iti sāmyam evopanyāsasya. 
 iti tattvārthavṛttau sarvārthasiddhisaṃjñāyāṃ prathamo ’dhyāyaḥ 
 
 
	  atha dvitīyo ’dhyāyaḥ
	   §§ 251–365 
 § 251. āha, samyagdarśanasya viṣayabhāvenopadiṣṭeṣu jīvādiṣv ādāv upanyas tasya jīvasya kiṃ svatattvam ity ucyate — 
 aupaśamikakṣāyikau bhāvau miśraś ca jīvasya svatattvam audayikapāriṇāmikau ca || 
 § 252. ātmani karmaṇaḥ svaśakteḥ kāraṇavaśād anudbhūtir upaśamaḥ. yathā katakādidravyasaṃbandhād ambhasi paṃkasya upaśamaḥ. kṣaya ātyantikī nivṛttiḥ. yathā tasminn evāmbhasi śucibhājanāntarasaṃkrānte paṃkasyātyantābhāvaḥ. ubhayātmako miśraḥ. yathā tasminn evāmbhasi katakādidravyasaṃbandhāt paṃkasya kṣīṇākṣīṇavṛttiḥ. dravyādinimittavaśāt karmaṇāṃ phalaprāptir udayaḥ. dravyātmalābhamātrahetukaḥ pariṇāmaḥ. upaśamaḥ prayojanam asyety aupaśamikaḥ. evaṃ kṣāyikaḥ kṣāyopaśamikaḥ audayikaḥ pariṇāmikaś ca. ta ete pañca bhāvā asādharaṇā jīvasya svatattvam ity ucyante. 
 § 253. samyagdarśanasya prakṛtatvāt tasya triṣu vikalpeṣu aupaśamikam ādau labhyata iti tasyādau grahaṇaṃ kriyate. tadanantaraṃ kṣāyikagrahaṇam; tasya pratiyogitvāt saṃsāry apekṣayā dravyatas tato ’saṃkyeyaguṇatvāc ca. tata uttaraṃ miśragrahaṇam; tadubhayātmakatvāt tato ’saṃkyeyaguṇatvāc ca. teṣāṃ sarveṣām anantaguṇatvād audayikapāriṇāmikagrahaṇam ante kriyate. atra dvandanirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ — aupaśamikakṣāyikamiśraudayikapāriṇāmikā iti. tathā sati dviḥ ‘ca’ śabdo na kartavyo bhavati. naiva śaṅkyam; anyaguṇāpekṣayā iti pratīyate. vākye punaḥ sati ‘ca’ sabdena prakṛtobhayānukarṣaḥ kṛto bhavati. tarhi kṣāyopaśamikagrahaṇam eva kartavyam iti cet. na; gauravāt. miśragrahaṇaṃ madhye kriyate ubhayāpekṣārtham. bhavyasya aupaśamikakṣāyikau bhāvau. miśraḥ punar abhavyasyāpi bhavati, audayikapāriṇāmikābhyāṃ saha bhavyasyāpīti. bhāvāpekṣayā talliṅgasaṃkhyāprasaṅgaḥ svatattvasyeti cet? na; upāttaliṃgasaṃkhyatvāt. tadbhāvas tattvam. svaṃ tattvaṃ svatattvam iti. 
 § 254. atrāha tasyaikasyātmano ye bhāvā aupaśamkādayas te kiṃ bhedavanta utābhedā iti. attrocyate, bhedavantaḥ. yady evaṃ, bhedā ucyantām ity ata āha — 
 dvinavāṣṭādaśaikaviṃśatitribhedā yathākramam || 
 § 255. dvyādīnāṃ saṃkhyāśabdānāṃ kṛtadvandvānāṃ bhedaśabdena saha svapadārthe ’nyapadārthe vā vṛttir veditavyā. dvau ca nava ca aṣṭādaśa ca ekaviṃśatiś ca trayaś ca dvinavāṣṭādaśaikaviṃśatitrayaḥ. te ca te bhedās ca, ta eva bhedā yeṣām iti vā vṛttir dvinavāṣṭādaśaikaviṃśatitribhedā ity. yadā svapadārthe vṛttis tadā aupaśamikādīnā bhāvānāṃ dvinavāṣṭādaśaikaviṃśatitrrayo bhedā ity abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate; arthavaśād vibhaktipariṇāma iti. yadānyapadārthe vṛttis tadā nirdiṣṭavibhaktyantā evābhisaṃbadhyante, aupaśamikādayo bhāvā dvinavāṣṭādaśaikaviṃśatitribhedā iti. ‘yathākrama’ vacanam yathāsaṃkhyapratipattyārtham. aupaśamiko dvibhedaḥ. kṣāyiko navabhedaḥ. miśro ’ṣṭādaśabhedaḥ. audayika ekaviṃśatibhedaḥ. pāriṇāmikas tribhedaḥ iti. 
 § 256. yady evam aupaśamikasya kau dvau bhedāv ity ata āha — 
 samyaktvacāritre || 
 § 257. vyākhyātalakṣaṇe samyaktvacāritre. aupaśamikatvaṃ katham iti cet? ucyate — cāritramoho dvividaḥ kaṣāyavedanīyo nokaṣāyavedanīyaś ceti. tatra kaṣāyavedanīyasya bhedā anantānubandhinaḥ krodhamānamāyālobhāś catvāraḥ. darśanamohasya trayo bhedāḥ samyaktvaṃ mithyātvaṃ samyagmithyātvam iti. āsāṃ saptānāṃ pakṛtīnāmupaśamād aupaśamikaṃ samyaktvam. 
 § 258. anādimithyādṛṣṭer bhavyasya karmodayāpāditakāluṣye sati kutas tadupaśamaḥ? kālalabdhyādinimittatvāt. tatra kālalabdhis tāvat — karmāviṣṭa ātmā bhavyaḥ kāle ’rddhapudgalaparivarttanākhye ’vaśiṣṭe prathamasamyaktvagrahaṇasya yogyo bhavati nādhike iti. iyam ekā kālalabdhiḥ. aparā karmasthitikā kālalabdhiḥ. utkṛṣṭasthitikeṣu karmasu jaghanyasthitikeṣu ca prathamasamyaktvalābho na bhavati. kva tarhi bhavati? antaḥkoṭīkoṭīsāgaropamasthitikeṣu karmasu bandham āpadhyamāneṣu viśuddhapariṇāmavaśāt satkarmasu ca tataḥ saṃkheyasāgaropamasahasronāyām antaḥkoṭīkoṭīsāgaropamasthitau sthāpiteṣu prathamasamyaktvayogyo bhavati. aparā kālalabdhir bhavāpekṣayā. bhavyaḥ pañcendriyaḥ saṃjñī paryāptikaḥ sarvaviśuddhaḥ prathamasamyaktvam utpādayati. ‘ādi’ śabdena jātismaraṇādiḥ parigṛhyate. 
 § 259. kṛtsnasya mohanīyasyopaśamād aupaśamikaṃ cāritram. tatra samyaktvasyādau vacanaṃ; tatpūrvakatvāc cāritrasya. 
 § 260. yaḥ kṣāyiko bhāvo navavidha uddiṣṭas tasya bhedasvarūpapratipādanārtham āha — 
 jñānadarśanadānalābhabhogopabhogavīryāṇi ca || 
 § 261. ‘ca’ śabdaḥ samyaktvacāritrānukarṣaṇārthaḥ. jñānāvaraṇasyātyantakṣāyāt kevalajñānaṃ kṣāyikaṃ tathā kevaladarśanam. dānāntarāyasyātyantakṣayād anantaprāṇigaṇānugrahakaraṃ kṣāyikam abhayadānam. lābhāntarāyasyāśeṣasya nirāsāt parityaktakavalāhārakriyāṇāṃ kevalināṃ yataḥ śarīrabalādhānahetavo ’nyam anujāsādhāraṇāḥ paramaśubhāḥ sukṣmāḥ anantāḥ pratisamayaṃ pudgalāḥ saṃbandham upayānti sa kṣāyiko lābhaḥ. kṛtsnasya bhogāntarāyasya tirobhāvād āvirbhūto ’tiśayavān ananto bhogaḥ kṣāyikaḥ. yataḥ kusumavṛṣṭyādayo viśeṣāḥ prādurbhavanti. niravaśeṣasyopabhogāntarāyasya pralayāt prādurbhūto ’nanta upabhogaḥ kṣāyikaḥ. yataḥ siṃhāsanacāmaracchatrayādayo vibhūtayaḥ. vīryāntarāyasya karmaṇo ’tyantakṣayād āvirbhūtam anantavīryaṃ kṣāyikam. pūrvoktānāṃ saptānāṃ prakṛtīnām atyantakṣayāt kṣāyikaṃ samyaktvam. cāritram api tathā. yadi kṣāyikadānādibhāvakṛtam abhayadānādi, siddheṣv api tatprasaṅgaḥ? naiṣa doṣaḥ; śarīranāmatīrthakaranāmakarmodayādyapekṣatvāt. teṣāṃ tadabhāve tadaprasaṃgaḥ. kathaṃ tarhi teṣāṃ siddheṣu vṛttiḥ? paramānandāvyābādharūpeṇaiva teṣāṃ tatra vṛttiḥ. kevalajñānarūpeṇānantavīryavṛttivat. 
 § 262. ya uktaḥ kṣāyopaśamiko bhāvo ’ṣṭādaśavikalpas tadbhedanirūpaṇārtham āha — 
 jñānājñānadarśanalabdhayaś catustritripañcabhedāḥ samyaktvacāritrasaṃyamāsaṃyamāś ca || 
 § 263. catvāraś ca trayaś ca trayaś ca pañca ca catustritripañca. te bhedāḥ yāsāṃ tāścatustritripañcabhedāḥ. yathākramam ity anuvartate. tenābhisaṃbandhāc caturādibhir jñānādīny abhisaṃbadhyante. catvāri jñānāni, trīṇy ajñānāni, trīṇi darśanāni, pañca labdhaya iti. sarvaghātisparddhakānām udayakṣayāt teṣām eva sadupaśamād deśaghātisparddhakānām udaye kṣāyopaśamiko bhāvo bhavati. tatra jñānādīnāṃ vṛttiḥ svāvaraṇāntarāyakṣayopaśamād vyākhyātavyā. ‘samyaktva’ grahaṇena vedakasamyaktvaṃ gṛhyate. anantānubandhikaṣāyacatuṣtayasya mithyātvasamyaṅmithyātvayoś codayakṣayāt sadupaśamāc ca samyaktvasya deśaghātisparddhakasyodaye tattvārthaśraddhānaṃ kṣayopaśamikaṃ samyaktvam. anantānubandhyapratyākhyānapratyākhyānadvādaśakaṣāyodayakṣayāt sadupaśamāc ca saṃjvalanakaṣāyacatuṣṭayānyatamadeśaghātisparddhakodaye nokaṣāyanavakasya yathāsaṃbhavodaye ca nivṛttipariṇāma ātmanaḥ kṣāyopaśamikaṃ cāritram. anantānubandhyapratyākhyānakaṣāyāṣṭakodakṣayāt *  sadupaśamāc ca pratyākhyānakaṣāyodaye saṃjvalanakaṣāyasya deśaghātisparddhakodaye nokaṣāyanavakasya yathāsaṃbhavodaye ca viratāviratapariṇāmaḥ kṣāyopaśamikaḥ saṃyamāsaṃyama ity ākhyāyate. 
 § 264. ya ekaviṃśativikalpa audayiko bhāva uddiṣṭas tasya bhedasaṃjñāsaṃkīrtanārtham idam ucyate — 
 gatikaṣāyaliṅgamithyādarśanājñānāsaṃyatāsiddhaleśyāś catuścatustryekaikaikaikaṣaḍbhedāḥ || 
 § 265. yathākramam ity anuvartate, tenābhisaṃbandhād gatiś caturbhedā, narakagatis tiryagatir manuṣyagtir devagatir iti. tatra narakagatināmakarmodayān nārako bhāvo bhavatīti narakagatir audayikī. evam itaratrāpi. kaṣāyaś caturbhedaḥ, krodho māno māyā lobha iti. tatra krodhanirvartanasya karmaṇa udayāt krodhaḥ audayikaḥ. evam itaratrāpi. liṅgaṃ tribhedaṃ, srtīvedaḥ puṃvedo napuṃsakaveda iti. strīvedakarmaṇa udayāt strīveda audayikaḥ. evam itaratrāpi. mithyādarśanam ekabhedam. mityādarśanakarmaṇa udayāt tattvārthāśraddhānapariṇāmo mithyādarśanam audayikam. jñānāvaraṇakarmaṇa udayāt padārthānavabodho bhavati tadajñānam audayikam. cāritramohasya sarvaghātisparddhakasyodayād asaṃyata audayikaḥ. karmodayasāmānyāpekṣo ’siddha audayikaḥ. leśyā dvividhā, dravyaleśyā bhāvaleśyā ceti. jīvabhāvādhikārād dravyaleśyā nādhikṛtā. bhāvaleśyā kaṣāyodayarañjitā yogapravṛttir iti kṛtvā audayikīty ucyate. sā ṣaḍvidhā — kṛṣṇaleśyā nīlaleśyā kāpotaleśyā tejoleśyā padmaleśyā śuklaleśyā ceti. 
 § 266. nanu ca upaśāntkaṣāye kṣīṇakaṣāye sayogakevalini ca śuklaleśyā ’stīty āgamaḥ. tatra kaṣāyānurañjanābhāvād audayikatvaṃ nopapadyate. naiṣa doṣaḥ; pūrvabhāvaprajñāpananayāpekṣayā yāsau yogapravṛttiḥ kaṣāyānurañjitā saivety upacārād audayikīty ucyate. tadabhāvād ayogakevalyaleśya iti niścīyate. 
 § 267. yaḥ pāriṇāmiko bhāvas tribheda uktas tadbhedasvarūpapratipādanārtham āha — 
 jīvabhavyābhavyatvāni ca || 
 § 268. jīvatvaṃ bhavyatvam abhavyatvam iti trayo bhāvāḥ pāriṇāmikā anyadravyāsādhāraṇā ātmano veditavyāḥ. kutaḥ punar eṣāṃ pāriṇāmikatvam. karmodayopaśamakṣayakṣayopaśamānapekṣitvāt. jīvatvaṃ caitanyam ity arthaḥ. samyagdarśanādibhāvena bhaviṣyatīti bhavyaḥ. tadviparīto ’bhavyaḥ. ta ete trayo bhāvā jīvasya pāriṇāmikā. 
 § 269. nanu cāstitvanityatvapradeśavattvādayo ’pi bhāvāḥ pāriṇāmikāḥ santi, teṣām iha grahaṇaṃ kartavyam. na kartavyam; kṛtam eva. katham? ‘ca’ śabdena samuccitatvāt. yady evaṃ traya iti saṃkhyā virudhyate. na virudhyate, asādharaṇā jīvasya bhāvāḥ pāriṇāmikās traya eva. astitvādayaḥ punar jīvājīvaviṣayatvāt sādhāraṇā iti ‘ca’ śabdena pṛthaggṛhyante. āha, aupaśmikādibhāvānupapattir amūrtatvād ātmanaḥ karmabandhāpekṣā hi te bhāvāḥ. na cāmūrteḥ karmaṇāṃ bandho yujyata iti. tan na; anekāntāt. nāyam ekāntaḥ amūrtir evātmeti. karmabandhaparyāyāpekṣayā tadāveśāt syān mūrtaḥ. śuddhasvarūpāpekṣayā syād amūrtaḥ. yady evaṃ karmabandhāveśād asyaikatve saty avivekaḥ prāpnoti. naiṣa doṣaḥ; bandhaṃ pratyekatve saty api lakṣaṇabhedād asya nānātvam avasīyate. uktaṃ ca —
	   baṃdhaṃ paḍi eyattaṃ lakkhaṇado havai tassa ṇāṇattaṃ | 
 tamhā amuttibhāvo ṇeyaṃto hoi jīvassa ||  iti | 
 § 270.yady evaṃ tadeva lakṣaṇam ucyatāṃ yena nānātvam avasīyate ity ata āha — 
 upayogo lakṣaṇam || 
 § 271. ubhayanimittavaśād utpadyamānaś caitanyānuvidhāyī pariṇāma upayogaḥ. tena bandhaṃ pratyekatve saty apy ātmā lakṣyate suvarṇarajatayor bandhaṃ pratyekatve saty api varṇādibhedavat. 
 § 272. tadbhedapradarśanārtham āha — 
 sa dvividho ’ṣṭacaturbhedaḥ || 
 § 273. sa upayogo dvividhaḥ — jñānopayogo darśanopayogaś ceti. jñānopayogo ’ṣṭabhedaḥ — matijñānaṃ śrutajñānaṃ avadhijñānaṃ manaḥparyayajñānaṃ kevalajñānaṃ matyajñānaṃ śrutājñānaṃ vibhaṅgajñānaṃ ceti. darśanopayogaś caturvidhaḥ — cakṣurdarśanam acakṣurdarśanam avadhidarśanaṃ kevaldarśanaṃ ceti. tayo kathaṃ bhedaḥ? sākārānakārabhedāt. sākāraṃ jñānam anākāraṃ darśanam iti. tacchadmastheṣu krameṇa vartate. nirāvaraṇeṣu yugapat pūrvakālabhāvino ’pi darśanāj jñānasya prāgupanyāsaḥ; abhyarhitatvāt. samyagjñānaprakaraṇāt pūrvaṃ pañcavidho jñānopayogo vyākhyātaḥ. iha punar upayogagrahaṇād viparyayo ’pi gṛhyate ity aṣṭavidha iti ucyate. 
 § 274. yathoktenānenābhihitapariṇāmena sarvātmasādhāraneṇopayogena ye upalakṣitā upayoginas te dvividhāḥ — 
 saṃsāriṇo muktāś ca || 
 § 275. saṃsaraṇaṃ saṃsāraḥ parivartaṇam ity arthaḥ. sa eṣām asti te saṃsāriṇaḥ. tatparivartanaṃ pañcavidham — dravyaparivartanaṃ kṣetraparivartanaṃ kālaparivartanaṃ bhavaparivartanaṃ bhāvaparivartanaṃ ceti. tatra dravyaparivartanaṃ dvividham — nokarmadravyaparivartanaṃ karmadravyaparivartanaṃ ceti. tatra nokarmadravyaparivartanaṃ nāma trayāṇāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ paryāptīnāṃ ca yogyā ye pudgalā ekena jīvena ekasmin samaye gṛhītāḥ snigdharūkṣavarṇagandhādibhis tīvramandamadhyamabhāvena ca yathāvasthitā dvitīyādiṣu samayeṣu nirjīrṇā agṛhītān anantavārān atītya miśrakāṃś cānantavārān atītya madhye gṛhītāṃś cānantavārān atītya ta eva tenaiva prakāṛeṇa tasyaiva jīvasya norkarmabhāvam āpadyante yāvat tāvat samuditaṃ nokarmadravyaparivartanam. karmadravyaparivartanaṃ ucyate — ekasmin samaye ekena jīvenāṣṭavidhakarmabhāvena ye gṛhītāḥ pudgalāḥ samayādhikām āvalikām atītya dvitīyādiṣu samayeṣu nirjīrṇāḥ, pūrvoktenaiva krameṇa ta eva tenaiva prakāreṇa tasya jīvasya karmabhāvam āpadyante yāvat tāvat karmadravyaparivartanam. uktaṃ ca — 
 savve vi puggalā khalu kamaso bhuttujjhiyā ya jīveṇa |
	  asaiṃ aṇaṃtakhutto puggalapariyaṭṭasaṃsāre ||
	   § 276. kṣetraparivartanam ucyate — sūkṣmanigodajīvo ’paryāptikaḥ sarvajaghanyapradeśaśarīro lokasyāṣṭamadhyapradeśān svaśarīramadhye kṛtvotpannaḥ kṣudrabhavagrahaṇaṃ jīvitvā mṛtaḥ. sa eva punas tenaivāvaghāhena dvir utpannas tathā tris tathā catur ity evaṃ yāvad ghanāṃgulasyāsaṃkheyabhāgapramitākāśapradeśās tāvat kṛtvas tatraiva janitvā punar ekaikapradeśādhikabhāvena sarvo loka ātmano jamakṣetrabhāvam upanīto bhavati yāvat tāvat kṣetraparivartanam. uktaṃ ca — 
	  “savvam hi loyakhette kamaso taṃ ṇatthi jam ṇa uppaṇṇaṃ |
	  ogāhaṇāe bahuso paribhamido khetttasaṃsāre || 
 § 277. kālaparivartanam ucyate — utsarpiṇyāḥ prathamasamaye jātaḥ kaścij jīvaḥ svāyuṣaḥ parisamāptau mṛtaḥ. sa eva punar dvitīyāyā utsarpiṇyā dvitīyasamaye jātaḥ svāyuṣaḥ kṣayān mṛtaḥ. sa eva punas tṛtīyāyā utsarpiṇyās tṛtīyasamaye jātaḥ. evam anena krameṇotsarpiṇī parisamāptā. tathāvasarpiṇī ca. evaṃ janmanair antaryam uktam. maraṇasyāpi nairantaryaṃ tathaiva grāhyam. etāvat kālaparivartanam. uktaṃ ca — 
 ussappiṇiavasappiṇisamayāvaliyāsu ṇiravasesāsu |
	  jādo mudo ya bahuso bhamaṇeṇa du kālasaṃsāre || 
 § 278. bhavaparivartanam ucyate — narakagatau sarvajaghanyam āyurdaśavarṣasahasrāṇi. tenāyuṣā tatrotpannaḥ punaḥ paribhramya tenaivāyuṣā jātaḥ. evaṃ daśavarṣasahasrāṇāṃ yāvantaḥ samayās tāvat kṛtvas tatraiva jāto mṛtaḥ. punar ekaikasamayādhikabhāvena trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi parisamāpitāni. tataḥ pracyutya tiryaggatāv antarmuhūrtāyuḥ samutpannaḥ. pūrvoktenaiva krameṇa trīṇi palyopamāni tena parisamāpitāni. evaṃ manuṣyagatau ca. devagatau ca nārakavat. ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ — ekatriṃśatsāgaropamāṇi parisamāpitāni yāvat tāvad bhavaparivartanam. uktaṃ ca — 
 ṇirayādijahaṇṇādisu jāva du uvarillayā du gevajjā |
	  micchattasaṃsideṇa du bahuso vi bhavaṭṭhidī bhamidā || 
 § 279. bhāvaparivartanam ucyate — pañcendriyaḥ saṃjñī paryāptako mithyādṛṣṭiḥ kaścij jīvaḥ sa sarvajaghanyāṃ svayogyāṃ jñānāvaraṇaprakṛteḥ sthitim antaḥkoṭīkoṭīsaṃjñikām āpadyate. tasya kaṣāyādhyavasāyasthānānyasaṃkhyeyalokapramitāni ṣaṭsthānapatitāni tatsthitiyogyāni bhavanti. tatra sarvajaghanyakaṣāyādhyavasāyasthānanimittāny anubhāgādhyavasāyasthānāny asaṃkhyeyalokapramitāni bhavanti. evaṃ sarvajaghanyāṃ sthitiṃ sarvajaghanyaṃ ca kaṣāyādhyavasāyasthānaṃ sarvajaghanyam evānubhāgabandhasthānam āskandatas tadyogyaṃ sarvajaghanyaṃ yogasthānaṃ bhavati. teṣām eva sthitikaṣāyānubhāgasthānānāṃ dvitīyam asaṃkhyeyabhāgavṛddhiyuktaṃ yogasthānaṃ bhavati. evaṃ ca tritīyādiṣu catuḥsthānapatitāni śreṇyasaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitāni yogasthānāni bhavanti. tathā tām eva sthitiṃ tad eva kaṣāyādhyavasāyasthānaṃ ca pratipadyamānasya dvitīyam anubhavādhyavasāyasthānaṃ bhavati. tasya ca yogasthānāni pūrvavadveditavyāni. evaṃ tritīyādiṣv api anubhavādhyavasāyasthāneṣu ā asaṃkhyeyalokaparisamāpteḥ. evaṃ tām eva sthitim āpadyamānasya dvitīyaṃ kaṣāyādhyavasāyasthānaṃ bhavati. tasyāpy anubhavādhyavasāyasthānāni yogasthānāni ca pūrvavadveditavyāni. evaṃ tritīyādiṣv api kaṣāyādhyavasāyasthāneṣu ā asaṃkyeyalokaparisamāpter vṛddhikramo veditavyaḥ. uktāyā jaghanyāyāḥ sthiteḥ samayādhikāyāḥ kaṣāyādisthānāni pūrvavat. evaṃ samayādhikakrameṇa ā utkṛṣṭasthites triṃśatsāgaropamakoṭīkoṭīparimitāyāḥ kaṣāyādisthānāni veditavyāni. anantabhāgavṛddhiḥ asaṃkhyeyabhāgavṛddhiḥ saṃkhyeyabhāgavṛddhiḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇavṛddhiḥ asaṃkhyeyaguṇavṛddhiḥ anantaguṇavṛddhiḥ imāni ṣaṭ vṛddhisthānāni. hānir api tathaiva. anantabhāgavṛddhyanantaguṇavṛddhirahitāni catvāri sthānāni. evaṃ sarveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ mūlaprakṛtīnām uttaraprakṛtīnāṃ ca parivatanakramo veditavyaḥ. tadetat sarvaṃ samuditaṃ bhāvaparivartanam. uktam ca — 
 savvā payaḍiṭṭhidīo aṇubhāgapadesabaṃdhaṭhāṇāṇi |
	  micchattasaṃsideṇa ya bhamidā puṇa bhāvasaṃsāre || 
 § 280.  uktāt pañcavidhāt saṃsārān nivṛttā ye te muktāḥ. saṃsāriṇāṃ pragupādānaṃ tatpūrvakatvān muktavyapadeśasya. 
 § 281. ya ete saṃsāriṇas te dvividhāḥ — 
 samanaskāmanaskāḥ || 
 § 282. mano dvitīdham — dravyamano bhāvamanaś ceti. tatra pudgalavipākikarmodayāpekṣaṃ dravyamanaḥ. vīryāntarāyanoindriyāvaraṇakṣayopaśamāpekṣā ātmano viśuddhir bhāvamanaḥ. tena manasā saha vartanta iti samanaskāḥ. na vidyate mano yeṣāṃ ta ime amanaskāḥ. evaṃ manaso bhāvābhāvābhyāṃ samsāriṇo dvividhā vibhajyante. samanaskāś cāmanaskāś ca samanaskāmanaskā iti. abhyarhitatvāt samanaskaśabdasya pūrvanipātaḥ. katham abhyarhitatvam? guṇadoṣavicārakatvāt. 
 § 283. punar api saṃsāriṇāṃ bhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 saṃsāriṇas trasasthāvarāḥ || 
 § 284. ‘saṃsāri’ grahaṇam anarthakam; prakṛtatvāt. kva prakṛtam? ‘saṃsāriṇo muktaś ca’ iti. nānarthakam, pūrvāpekṣārtham, ye uktāḥ samanaskā amanaskās te saṃsāriṇa iti. yadi hi pūrvasya viśeṣạṇaṃ na syāt, samanaskāmanaskagrahaṇaṃ saṃsāriṇo muktāś cety anena yathāsaṃkhyam abhisaṃbadhyeta. evaṃ ca kṛtvā ‘saṃsāri’ grahaṇam adau kriyamāṇam upapannaṃ bhavati. tatpūrvāpekṣaṃ saduttarārtham api bhavati. te saṃsāriṇo dvividhāḥ — trasāḥ sthāvarā iti. trasanāmakarmodayavaśīkṛtās trasā. sthāvaranāmakarmodayavaśavartinaḥ sthāvarāḥ. trasyantīti trasāḥ, sthānaśīlāḥ sthāvara iti cet? na; āgamavirodhāt. āgame hi kāyānuvādena trasā dvīndriyād ārabhya ā ayogakevalina iti. tasmān na calanācalanāpekṣaṃ trasasthāvaratvam. karmodayāpekṣam eva. trasagrahaṇam ādau kriyate; alpāctaratvād abhyarhitatvāc ca. sarvopayogasambhavād abhyarhitatvam. 
 § 285. ekendriyāṇām atibahuvaktavyābhāvād ullaṅghyānupūrvīṃ sthāvarabhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 pṛthivyaptejovāyuvanaspatayaḥ sthāvarāḥ || 
 § 286. sthāvaranāmakarmabhedāḥ pṛthivīkāyādayaḥ santi. tadudayanimittā jīveṣu pṛthivyādayaḥ saṃjñā veditavyāḥ. prathanādiprakṛtiniṣpannā api rūḍhivaśāt prathanādyanapekṣā vartante. eṣāṃ pṛthivyādīnām ārṣe cāturvidhyam uktaṃ pratyekam. tatkatham iti cet? ucyate — pṛthivī pṛthivīkāyaḥ pṛthivīkāyikaḥ pṛthivījīva ity ādi. tatra acetanā vaiśrasikapariṇāmanirvṛttā kāṭhinyaguṇātmikā pṛthivī. acetanatvād asaty api pṛthivīkāyanāmakarmodaye prathanakriyopalakṣitaiveyam. athavā pṛthivīti sāmānyam; uttaratraye ’pi sadbhāvāt. kāyaḥ śarīram. pṛthivīkāyikajīvaparityaktaḥ pṛthivīkāyo mṛtamanuṣyādikāyavat. pṛthivīkāyo ’syāstīti pṛthivīkāyikaḥ. tatkāyasaṃbandhavaśīkṛta ātmā. samavāptapṛthivīkāyanāmakarmodayaḥ kārmaṇakāyayogastho yo na tāvat pṛthivīṃ kāyatvena gṛhṇāti sa pṛthivījīvaḥ. evam abādiṣv api yojyam. ete mañcavidhāḥ prāṇinaḥ sthāvarāḥ. *  kati punar eṣāṃ prāṇāḥ? catvāraḥ — sparśanendriyaprāṇāḥ kāyabalaprāṇāḥ ucchvāsaniśvāsaprāṇaḥ āyuḥprānaś ceti. 
 § 287. atha trasāḥ ke te, ity atrocyate — 
 dvīndriyādayas trasāḥ || 
 § 288. dve indriye yasya so ’yaṃ dvīndriyaḥ. dvīndriṣa ādir yeyāṃ te dvīndriyādayaḥ. *  ‘ādi’ śabdo vyavasthāvācī. kva vyavasthitāḥ? āgame. katham? dvīndriyas trīndriyaś caturindriyaḥ pañcendriyaś ceti. tadguṇasaṃvijñānavṛttigrahaṇād dvīndriyasyāpy antarbhāvaḥ. kati punar eṣāṃ prāṇāh? dvīndriyasya tāvat ṣaṭ prāṇāḥ, pūrvoktā eva rasanavākprāṇādhikāḥ. trīndriyasya sapta ta eva ghrāṇaprāṇādhikāḥ. caturindriyasyāṣṭau ta eva cakṣuḥprāṇādhikāḥ. pañcendriyasya tiraśco ’saṃjñino nava ta eva śrotraprāṇādhikāḥ. saṃjñino daśa ta eva manobalaprāṇādhikāḥ. 
 § 289. ‘ādi’ śabdena nirdiṣṭānām anirjñātasaṃkhyānām iyattāvadhāraṇaṃ karttavyām ity ata āha — 
 pañcendriyāṇi || 
 § 290. ‘indriya’ śabdo vyākhyātārthaḥ. ‘pañca’ grahaṇam avadhāraṇārtham, paṃcaiva nādhikasaṃkhyānīti. karmendriyāṇāṃ vāgādinām iha grahaṇaṃ kartavyam? na kartavyam; upayogaprakaraṇāt. upayogasādhanānām iha grahaṇaṃ, na kriyāsādhanānām; anavasthānāc ca. kriyāsādhanānām aṅgopāṅganāmakarmanivartitānāṃ sarveṣām api kriyāsādhanatvam astīti na paṃcaiva karmendriyāṇi. 
 § 291. teṣām antarbhedapradarśanārtham āha — 
 dvividhāni || 
 § 292. ‘vidha’ śabdaḥ prakāravācī. dvau vidhau yeṣāṃ tāni dvividhāni, dviprakārāṇīty arthaḥ. kau punas tau dvau prakārau? dravyendriyaṃ bhāvendriyam iti. 
 § 293. tatra dravyendriyasvarūpapratipattyartham āha — 
 nirvṛttyupakaraṇo dravyendriyam || 
 § 294. nirvartyate ity nirvṛttiḥ. kena nirvartyate? karmanā. sā dvividhā; bāhyābhyantarabhedāt. utsedhāṅgulāsaṃkhyeyabhāgapramitānāṃ śuddhānām ātmapradeśānāṃ pratiniyatacakṣurādīndriyasaṃsthānenāvasthitānāṃ vṛttir ābhyantarā nirvṛttiḥ. teṣv ātmapradeśeṣv indriyavyapadeśabhākṣu yaḥ pratiniyatasaṃsthāno nāmakarmodayāpāditāvasthāviśeṣaḥ pudgalapracayaḥ sā bāhyā nirvṛttiḥ. yena nirvṛtter upakāraḥ kriyate tadupakaraṇam. pūrvavat tadapi dvividham. tatrābhyantaraṃ kṛṣṇaśuklamaṇḍalaṃ, bāhyam akṣipatrapakṣmadvayādi. evaṃ śeṣeṣv apīndriyeṣu jñeyam. 
 § 295. bhāvendriyam ucyate — 
 labdhyupayogau bhāvendriyam || 
 § 296. lambhanaṃ labdhiḥ. kā punar asau? jñānāvaraṇakarmakṣayopaśamaviśeṣaḥ. yat saṃnidhānād ātmā dravyendriyanirvṛttiṃ prati vyāpriyate tan nimitta ātmanaḥ pariṇāma upayogaḥ. tadubhaye bhāvenindriyam. indriyaphalam upayogaḥ, tasya katham indriyatvam? kāraṇadharmasya kārye darśanāt. yathā ghaṭākārapariṇataṃ vijñānaṃ ghaṭa iti. svārthasya tatra mukhyatvāc ca. indrasya liṅgam indriyam iti yaḥ svārthaḥ sa upayoge mukhyaḥ, ‘upayogalakṣaṇo jīva’ iti vacanāt. ata upayogasyendriyatvaṃ nyāyyaṃ. 
 § 297. uktānām indriyāṇāṃ saṃjñānupūrvīpratipādanārtham āha — 
 sparśanarasanaghrāṇacakṣuḥśrotrāṇi || 
 § 298. loke indriyāṇāṃ pāratantryavivakṣā dṛśyate. anenākṣaṇā suṣṭhu paśyāmi, anena karṇena suṣṭhu śṛṇomīti. tataḥ pāratantryāt sparśanādīnāṃ karaṇatvam. vīryāntarāyamatijñānāvaraṇakṣayopaśamāṅgopāṅganāmalābhāvaṣṭambhād ātmanā spṛśyate ’neneti sparśanam. rasyate ’neneti rasanam. ghrāyate ’neneti ghrāṇam. cakṣer anekārthatvād darśanārthavivakṣāyāṃ caṣṭe arthān paśyaty aneneti cakṣuḥ. śrūyate ’neneti śrotram. svātantryavivakṣā ca dṛśyate. idaṃ me akṣi suṣṭhu paśyati. ayaṃ me karṇaḥ suṣṭhu śṛṇoti. tataḥ sparśanādīnāṃ kartari niṣpattiḥ. spṛśatīti sparśanam. rasatīti rasanam. jighratīti ghrāṇam. caṣṭe iti cakṣuḥ. śṛṇotīti śrotram. eṣāṃ nirdeśakramaḥ ekaikavṛddhikramaprajñāpanārthaḥ. 
 § 299. teṣām indriyāṇāṃ viṣayapradarśanārtham āha — 
 sparśarasagandhavarṇaśabdās tadarthāḥ || 
 § 300. dravyaparyāyayoḥ prādhānyavivakṣāyāṃ karmabhāvasādhanatvaṃ sparśādiśabdānāṃ veditavyam. dravyaprādhānyavivakṣāyāṃ karmanirdeśaḥ. spṛśyata iti sparśaḥ. rasyata iti rasaḥ. gandhyata iti gandhaḥ. varṇyata iti varṇaḥ. śabdyata iti śabdaḥ. paryāyaprādhānyavivakṣāyāṃ bhāvanirdeśaḥ. sparśanaṃ sparśaḥ. rasanaṃ rasaḥ. gandhanaṃ gandhaḥ. varṇanaṃ varṇaḥ. śabdanaṃ śabda iti. eṣāṃ krama indriyakrameṇaiva vyākhyātaḥ. 
 § 301. atrāha, yat tāvan mano ’navasthānād indriyaṃ na bhavatīti pratyākhyātaṃ tat kim upayogasyopakāri uta neti. tad apy upakāryeva. tena vinendriyāṇāṃ viṣayeṣu svaprayojanavṛttyabhāvāt. kiñcāsyaiṣāṃ sahakāritvamātram eva prayojanam utānyad apīty ata āha — 
 śrutam anindriyasya || 
 § 302. śrutajñānaviśayo ’rthaḥ śrutam. sa viṣayo ’nindriyasya; pariprāptaśrutajñānāvaraṇakṣayopaśamasyātmanaḥ śrutārthe ’nindriyālambanajñānapravṛtteḥ. athavā śrutajñānaṃ śrutam, tadanindriyasyārthaḥ prayojanam iti yāvat. svātantryasādhyam idaṃ prayojanam anindriyasya. 
 § 303. uktānām indriyānāṃ pratiniyataviṣayāṇāṃ svāmitvanirdeśe kartavye yat prathamaṃ gṛhītaṃ sparśanaṃ tasya tāvat svāmitvāvadhāraṇārtham āha — 
 vanaspatyantānām ekam || 
 § 304. ekaṃ prathamam ity arthaḥ. kiṃ tat? sparśanam. tat keṣām? pṛthivyādīnāṃ vanaspatyantānāṃ veditavyam. tasyotpattikāraṇam ucyate — vīryāntarāyasparśanendriyāvaraṇakṣayopaśame sati śeṣendriyasarvaghātispardhakodaye ca śarīranāmalābhāvaṣṭambhe ekendriyajātinamodayavaśartitāyāṃ ca satyāṃ sparśanam ekam indriyam āvirbhavati. 
 § 305. itareṣām indriyāṇāṃ svāmitvapradarśanārtham āha — 
 kṛimipipīlakābhramaramanuṣyādinām ekaikavṛddhāni || 
 § 306. ‘ekaikam’ iti vīpsāyāṃ dvitvam. ekaikena vṛddhāni ekaikavṛddhāni. kṛimim ādiṃ kṛtvā, sparśanādhikārāt sparśanam ādiṃ kṛtvā ekaikavṛddhānīty abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate. ‘ādi’ śabdaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate. kṛmyādīnāṃ sparśanaṃ rasanādhikam, pipīlikādīnāṃ sparśanarasane ghrāṇadhike, bhramarādīnāṃ sparśanarasanaghrāṇāni cakṣuradhkāni, manuṣyādīnāṃ tāny eva śrotrādhikānīti yathāsaṃkhyenābhisaṃbandho vyākhyātaḥ. teṣāṃ niṣpattiḥ sparśnotpatyā vyākhyātā uttarottarasarvaghātispardhakodayena. 
 § 307. evam eteṣu saṃsāriṣu dvibhedeṣu indriyabhedāt pañcavidheṣu ye pañcendriyās tadbhedasyānuktasya pratipādanārtham āha — 
 saṃjñinaḥ samanaskāḥ || 
 § 308. mano vyākhyātam. saha tena ye vartante te samanaskāḥ. saṃjñina ity ucyante. pāriśeṣyād itare saṃsāriṇaḥ prāṇino ’saṃjñina iti siddham. nanu ca saṃjñina ity anenaiva gatārthatvāt samanaskā iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam. yato manovyāpāro hitāhitaprāptiparihāraparīkṣā. saṃjñāpi saiveti. naitad yuktam, saṃjñāśabdārthavyabhicārāt. saṃjñā nāmety ucyate. tadvantaḥ saṃjñina iti sarveṣām atiprasaṅgaḥ. saṃjñā jñānam iti cet; sarveṣām prāṇiṇāṃ jñānātmakatvād atiprasaṅgaḥ. āhārādiviṣayābhilāṣaḥ saṃjñeti cet. tulyam. tasmāt samanaskā ity ucyate. evaṃ ca kṛtvā garbhāṇḍajamūrcchitasuṣuptyādyavasthāsu hitāhitaparīkṣābhāve’ pi manaḥsaṃnidhānāt saṃjñitvam upapannaṃ bhavati. 
 § 309. yadi hitāhitādiviṣayaparispandaḥ prāṇināṃ manaḥpraṇidhānapūrvakaḥ. athābhi–navaśarīragrahaṇaṃ pratyāgūrṇasya viśīrṇapūrvamūrter nirmanaskasya yatkarma tatkuta ity ucyate — 
 vigrahagatau karmayogaḥ || 
 § 310. vigraho dehaḥ. vigrahārthā gatir vigrahagatiḥ. athavā viruddho graho vigraho vyāghātaḥ. karmādāne ’pi nokarmapudgalādānanirodha ity arthaḥ. vigraheṇa gatir vigrahagatiḥ. sarvaśarīraprarohaṇabījabhūtaṃ kārmaṇaṃ śarīraṃ karmety ucyate. yogo vāṅmanasakāyavargaṇānimitta ātmapradeśaparispandaḥ. karmaṇā kṛto yogaḥ karmayogo vigrahagatau bhavatīty arthaḥ. tena karmādānaṃ deśāntarasaṃkramaś ca bhavati. 
 § 311. āha jīvapudgalānāṃ gatim āskandatāṃ deśāntarasaṃkramaḥ kim ākāśapradeśakramavṛtyā bhavati, utāviśeṣeṇety ata āha — 
 anuśreṇi gatiḥ || 
 § 312. lokamadhyād ārabhya ūrdhvam adhas tiryak ca ākāśāpradeśānāṃ kramasaṃniviṣṭānāṃ paṅktiḥ śreṇiḥ ity ucyate. ‘anu’ śabdasyānupurvyeṇa vṛttiḥ. *  śreṇer ānupūrvyeṇānuśreṇīti jīvānāṃ pudgalānāṃ ca gatir bhavatīty arthaḥ. anadhikṛtānāṃ pudglānāṃ kathaṃ grahaṇam iti cet. gatigrahaṇāt. yadi jīvānām eva gatir iṣṭā syād gatigrahaṇam anarthakam; adhikārāt tatsiddheḥ. uttaratra jīvagrahaṇāc ca pudgalasaṃpratyayaḥ. nanu candrādīnāṃ jyotiṣkāṇāṃ merupradakṣiṇākāle vidyādharādīnāṃ ca viśreṇigatir api dṛśyate, tatra kim ucyate, ‘anuśreṇi gatiḥ’ iti. kāladeśaniyamo ’tra veditavyaḥ. tatra kālaniyamas tāvaj jīvānāṃ maraṇakāle bhavāntarasaṃkrame muktānāṃ cordhvagamanakāle anuśreṇy eva gatiḥ. deśaniyamo ’pi ūrdhvalokād adho gatiḥ, adho lokād ūrdhvagatiḥ, tiryaglokād adho gatir ūrdhvā vā tatrānuśreṇy eva. pudgalānāṃ ca yā lokāntaprāpiṇī sā niyamād anuśreṇy eva. itarā gatir bhajanīya. 
 § 313. punar api gativiśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 avigrahā jīvasya || 
 § 314. vigraho vyāghātaḥ kauṭilyam ity arthaḥ. sa yasyāṃ na vidyate ’sāv avigrahā gatiḥ. kasya? jīvasya. kīdṛśasya? muktasya. kathaṃ gamyate muktasyeti? uttarasūtre saṃsārigrahaṇād iha muktasyeti vijñāyate. nanu ca ‘anuśreṇi gatiḥ’ ity anenaiva śreṇyantarasaṃkramābhāvo vyākhyātaḥ. nārtho ’nena. pūrvasūtre viśreṇi gatir api kvacid astīti jñāpanārtham idaṃ vacanam. nanu tatraiva deśakālaniyama uktaḥ. na; atas tatsiddheḥ. 
 § 315. yady asaṅgasyātmano ’pratibandhena gatir ālokāntād avadhṛtakālā pratijñāyate, sadehasya punar gatiḥ kiṃ pratibandhinī uta muktātmavad ity ata āha — 
 vigrahavatī ca saṃsāriṇaḥ prāk caturbhyaḥ || 
 § 316. kālāvadhāraṇārthaṃ ‘prāk caturbhyaḥ’ ity ucyate. ‘prāg’ ity vacanaṃ maryādārtham, caturthāt samayāt prag vigrahavatī gatir bhavati na caturthe iti. kuta iti cet? sarvotkṛṣṭavigrahanimittaniṣkuṭakṣetre utpitsuḥ prāṇī niṣkuṭakṣetrānupūrvyanuśreṇyabhāvādiṣu gatyabhāve niṣkuṭakṣetraprāpaṇanimittāṃ trivigrahāṃ gatim ārabhate nordhvām; tathāvidhopapādakṣetrābhāvāt. ‘ca’ śabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ. vigrahavatī cāvigrahā ceti. 
 § 317. vigrahavatyā gateḥ kālo ’vadhṛtaḥ. avigrahāyāḥ kiyān kāla ity ucyate — 
 ekasamayā ’vigrahā || 
 § 318. ekaḥ samayo yasyāḥ sā ekasamayā. na vidyate vigraho yasyāḥ sā avigrahā. gatimatāṃ hi jīvapudgalānām avyāghātenaikasamayikī gatir ālokāntād apīti. 
 § 319. anādikarmabandhasaṃtatau mithyādarśanādipratyayavaśāt karmāṇyād adāno vigrahagatāv atyāhārakaḥ prasaktas tato niyamārtham idam ucyate — 
 ekaṃ dvau trīn vā ’nahārakaḥ || 
 § 320. adhikārāt samayābhisaṃbandhaḥ. ‘vā’ śabdo vikalpārthaḥ. vikalpaś ca yathecchātisargaḥ. ekaṃ vā dvau vā trīn vā samayān anāhārako bhavitīty arthaḥ. trayāṇāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṇām paryāptīnāṃ yogyapudgalagrahaṇam āhāraḥ. *  tadabhāvād anāhārakaḥ. karmādānaṃ hi nirantaraṃ kārmaṇaśarīrasadbhāve. upapādakṣetraṃ prati ṛjvyāṃ gatau āhārakaḥ. itareṣu triṣu samayeṣu anāhārakaḥ. 
 § 321. evaṃ gacchato ’bhinavamūrtyantaranirvṛttiprakārapratipādanārtham āha — 
 saṃmūrcchanagarbhopapādā janma || 
 § 322. triṣu lokeṣūrdhvam adhas tiryak ca dehasya samantato mūrcchanaṃ saṃmūrcchanaṃ avayavaprakalpanam. striyā udare śukraśoṇitayor garaṇaṃ miśraṇaṃ garbhaḥ. mātrupabhuktāhāragaraṇād vā garbhaḥ. upetya padyate ’sminn iti upapādaḥ. devanārakotpattisthānaviśeṣasaṃjñā. ete trayaḥ saṃsāriṇām jīvānāṃ janmaprakārāḥ śubhāśubhapariṇāmanimittakarmabhedavipākakṛtāḥ. 
 § 323. athādhikṛtasya saṃsāraviṣayopabhogopalabdhyadhiṣṭhānapravaṇasya janmano yogivikalpā vaktavyā ity ata āha —  * 
 sacittaśītasaṃvṛtāh setarā miśrāś caikaśas tadyonaḥ || 
 § 324. ātmanaś caitanyaviśeṣapariṇāmaś cittam. saha cittena vartata iti sacittaḥ. śīta iti sparśaviśeṣaḥ; śuklādivad ubhayavacanatvād tadyuktaṃ dravyam apy āha. samyagvṛtaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ. saṃvṛta iti durupalakṣyapradeśa ucyate. saha itarair vartanta iti setarāḥ. sapratipakṣā ity arthaḥ. ke punar itare? acittoṣṇavivṛtāḥ. ubhayātmako miśraḥ. sacittācittaḥ śītoṣṇaḥ saṃvṛtavivṛta iti. ‘ca’ śabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ miśrāś ca yonayo bhavantīti. itarathā hi pūvoktānām eva viśeṣaṇaṃ syāt. ‘ekaśaḥ’ iti vīpsārthaḥ. tasya grahaṇaṃ kramamiśrapratipattyarthaṃ. yathaivaṃ vijñāyeta — sacittaś ca acittaś ca, śītaś ca uṣṇaś ca, saṃvṛtaś ca vivṛtaś ceti. maivaṃ vijñāyi — sacittaś ca śītaś cety ādi. ‘tadgrahaṇaṃ’ janmaprakārapratinirdeśārtham. teṣāṃ saṃmūrcchanādīnāṃ janmanāṃ yonaya iti. ta ete nava yonayo veditavyāḥ. yonijanmanor aviśeṣa iti cet? na; ādhārādheyabhedāt tadbhedaḥ. ta ete sacittādayo yonaya ādhārāḥ. ādheyā janmaprakārāḥ. yataḥ sacittādiyonyadhiṣṭhāne ātmā saṃmūrcchanādinā janmanā śarīrāhārendriyādiyogyān pudgalān upādatte. devanārakā acittayonayaḥ. teṣām hi yonir upapādadeśapudgalapracayo ’cittaḥ. garbhajā miśrayonayaḥ. teṣāṃ hi mātur udare śukraśoṇitam acittam, tadātmanā cittavatā miśraṇān miśrayoniḥ. saṃmūrcchanajās trivikalpayonayaḥ. kecit sacittayonayaḥ. anye acittayonayaḥ. apare miśrayonayaḥ. sacittayonayaḥ sādhāraṇaśarīrāḥ. kutaḥ? paraparāśrayatvāt. itare acittayonayo miśrayonayaś ca. śītoṣṇayonayo devanārakāḥ. teṣāṃ hi upapādasthānāni kānicic chītāni kānicid uṣṇānīti. uṣṇayonayas taijaskāyikāḥ. itare trivikalpayonayaḥ. kecic chītayonayaḥ. kecid uṣṇayonayaḥ apare miśrayonaya iti. devanārakaikendriyāḥ saṃvṛtayonayaḥ. vikalendriyā vivṛtayonayaḥ. garbhajāḥ miśrayonayaḥ. tadbhedāś caturaśītiśatasahasrasaṃkhyā āgamato veditavyāḥ. uktaṃ ca —
	   ṇiccidaradhādu satta ya taru dasa viyaliṃdiesu chacceva | 
 suraṇirayatiriya cauro coddasa maṇue sadasahassā || 
 § 325. evam etasmin navayonibhedasaṃkaṭe trividhajanmani sarvaprāṇabhṛtām aniyamena prasakte tadavadhāraṇārtham āha — 
 jarāyujāṇḍajapotānāṃ garbhaḥ || 
 § 326. yaj jālavatprāṇiparivaraṇaṃ vitatamāṃsaśoṇitaṃ taj jarāyuḥ. yan nakhatvaksadṛśam upāttakāṭhinyaṃ śukraśoṇitaparivaraṇaṃ parimaṇḍalaṃ tad aṇḍam. kiṃcit parivaraṇam antareṇa paripūrṇāvayavo yoninirgatamātra eva parispandādisāmarthyopetaḥ potaḥ. jarāyau jātā jarāyujāḥ. aṇḍe jātā aṇḍajāḥ. jarāyujāś ca aṇḍajāś ca potāś ca jarāyujāṇḍajapotā garbhayonayaḥ. 
 § 327. yady amīṣāṃ jarāyujāṇḍajapotānāṃ garbho ’vadhriyate, athopapādaḥ keṣāṃ bhavatīty ata āha — 
 devanārakāṇām upapādaḥ || 
 devānāṃ nārakāṇām copapādo janma veditavyam. 
 § 328. athānyeṣāṃ kiṃ janmety ata āha — 
 śeṣāṇāṃ saṃmūrcchanam || 
 § 329. garbhajebhya aupapādikebhyaś cānye śeṣāḥ. saṃmūrcchanaṃ janmeti. ete trayo ’pi yogā niyamārthāḥ. ubhayato niyamaś ca draṣṭavyaḥ. jarāyujāṇḍajapotānām eva garbhaḥ. garbha eva ca jarāyujāṇḍajapotānām. devanārakāṇām evopapādaḥ. upapāda eva ca devanārakāṇām. śeṣāṇām eva saṃmūrcchanam. saṃmūrcchanam eva śeṣāṇām iti. 
 § 330. teṣāṃ punaḥ saṃsāriṇāṃ trividhajanmanāmāhitabahuvikalpanavayonibhedānāṃ śubhāśubhanāmakarmavipākanirvartitāni bandhaphalānubhavanādhiṣṭhānāni śarīrāṇi kānīty ata āha — 
 audārikavaikriyikāhārakataijasakārmaṇāni śarīrāṇi || 
 § 331. viśiṣṭanāmakarmodayāpāditavṛttīni śīryanta iti śarīrāṇi. audārikādiprakṛtiviśeṣodayaprāptavṛttīni audārikādīni. udāraṃ sthūlam. udāre bhavaṃ udāraṃ prayojanam asyeti vā, audārikam. aṣṭaguṇaiśvaryayogād ekānekāṇumahac charīravidhikaraṇaṃ vikriyā, sā prayojanam asyeti vaikriyikam. sūkṣmapadārthanirjñānārtham asaṃyamaparijihīrṣayā vā pramattasaṃyatenāhriyate nirvartyate tad ity āhārakam. yat tejor nimittaṃ tejasi vā bhavaṃ tat taijasam. karmaṇāṃ kāryaṃ kārmaṇam. sarveṣāṃ karmanimittattve ’pi rūḍhivaśāt viśiṣṭaviṣaye vṛttir avaseyā. 
 § 332. yathaudārikasyendriyair upalabdhis tathetareṣāṃ kasmān na bhavatīty ata āha — 
 paraṃ paraṃ sūkṣmam || 
 § 333. ‘para’ śabdasyānekārthavṛttitve ’pi vivakṣāto vyavasthārthagatiḥ. pṛthagbhūtānāṃ śarīrāṇāṃ sūkṣmaguṇena vīpsānirdeśaḥ kriyate paramparam iti. audārikaṃ sthūlam, tataḥ sūkṣmaṃ vaikriyikam, tataḥ sūkṣmam āhārakaṃ tataḥ sūkṣmaṃ taijasam, taijasāt kārmaṇaṃ sūkṣmam iti. 
 § 334. yadi paramparaṃ sūkṣmam, pradeśato ’pi nyūnaṃ paramparaṃ hīnam iti viparītapratipattinivṛttyartham āha — 
 pradeśato ’samkhyeyaguṇaṃ prāktaijasāt || 
 § 335. pradiśyanta iti pradeśāḥ paramāṇavaḥ. saṃkhyām atīto ’saṃkhyeyaḥ. asaṃkhyeyo guṇo ’sya tad idam asaṃkhyeyaguṇam. kutaḥ? pradeśataḥ. nāvagāhataḥ. paramparam ity anuvṛtter ā kārmaṇāt prasaṅge tannivṛttyartham āha prāktaijasād iti. audārikād asaṃkhyeyaguṇapradeśaṃ vaikriyikam. vaikriyikād asaṃkhyeyaguṇapradeśam āhārakam iti. ko guṇakāraḥ. palyopamāsaṃkhyeyabhāgaḥ. yady evam, paramparaṃ mahāparimāṇaṃ prāpnoti? naivam; bandhaviśeṣāt parimāṇabhedābhāvas tūlanicayāyaḥpiṇḍavat. 
 § 336. athottarayoḥ kiṃ samapradeśatvam utāsti kaścid viśeṣa ity ata āha — 
 anantaguṇe pare || 
 § 337. pradeśata ity anuvartate, tenaivam abhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate — āhārakāt taijasaṃ pradeśato ’nantaguṇam, taijasāt kārmaṇaṃ pradeśato ’nantaguṇam iti. ko guṇakāraḥ? abhavyānām anantaguṇaḥ siddhānām anantabhāgaḥ. 
 § 338. tatraitat syāc chalyakavanmūrtimaddravyopacitatvāt saṃsāriṇo jīvasyābhipretagatinirodhaprasaṅga iti? tan na; kiṃ kāraṇam. yasmād ubhe apy ete — 
 apratīghate || 
 § 339. mūrtimato mūrtyantareṇa vyāghātaḥ pratīghātaḥ. sa nāsty anayor ity apratīghāte; sūkṣmapariṇāmāt ayaḥpiṇḍe tejo ’nupraveśavattaijasakārmaṇayor nāsti vajrapaṭalādiṣu vyāghātaḥ. nanu ca vaikriyikāhārakayor api nāsti pratīghātaḥ? sarvatrāpratīghāto ’tra vivakṣitaḥ. yathā taijasakārmaṇāyor ā lokāntāt sarvatra nāsti pratīghātaḥ, na tathā vaikriyikāhārakayoḥ. 
 § 340. āha kim etāvān eva viśeṣa uta kaścid anyo ’apy astīty āha — 
 anādisaṃbandhe ca || 
 § 341. ‘ca’ śabdo vikalpārthaḥ. anādisaṃbandhe sādisaṃbandhe ceti. kāryakāraṇabhāvasaṃtatyā anādisaṃbandhe, viśeṣāpekṣayā sādisaṃbandhe ca bījavṛkṣavat. yathaudārikavaikriyikāhārakāṇi jīvasya kadācit kāni, na tathā taijasakārmaṇe. nityasaṃbandhinī hi te ā saṃsārakṣayāt. 
 § 342. ta ete taijasakārmaṇe kiṃ kasyacid eva bhavata utāviśeṣeṇety ata āha — 
 sarvasya || 
 § 343. ‘sarva’ śabdo niravaśeṣavācī. niravaśeṣasya saṃsāriṇo jīvasya te dve api śarīre bhavata ity arhaḥ. 
 § 344. aviśeṣābhidhānāt tair audārikādibhiḥ sarvasya saṃsāriṇo yaugapadyena saṃbandhaprasaṃge saṃbhaviśarīrapradarśanārtham idam ucyate — 
 tadādīni bhājyāni yugapad ekasyā caturbhyaḥ || 
 § 345. ‘tad’ śabdaḥ prakṛtataijasakārmaṇapratinirdeśārthaḥ. te taijasakārmaṇe ādir yeṣāṃ tāni tadādini. bhājyāni vikalpyāni. ā kutaḥ? āṃ caturbhyaḥ. yugapad ekasyātmanaḥ. kasyācid dve taijasakārmaṇe. aparasya trīṇi audārikataijasakārmaṇāni vaikriyikataijasakārmaṇāni vā. anyasya catvāri audārikāhārakataijasakārmaṇānīti vibhāgaḥ kriyate. 
 § 346. punar api teṣāṃ viśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 nirupabhogam antyam || 
 § 347. ante bhavam antyam. kiṃ tat? kārmaṇam. indriyapraṇālikayā śabdādīnām upalabdhir upabhogaḥ. tadabhāvān nirupabhogam. vigrahagatau satyām api indriyalabdhau dravyendriyanirvṛttyabhāvāc chabdādyupabhogābhāva iti. nanu taijasam api nirupabhogam tatra kim ucyate nirupabhogam antyam iti? taijasaṃ śarīraṃ yoganimittam api na bhavati, tato ’syopabhogavicāre ’nadhikāraḥ. 
 § 348. evaṃ tatroktalakṣaṇeṣu janmasu amūni śarīrāṇi prādurbhāvam āpadyamānāni kim aviśeṣeṇa bhavanti, uta kaścid asti prativiśeṣa ity ata āha — 
 garbhasaṃmūrcchanajam ādyam || 
 § 349. sūtrakramāpekṣayā ādau bhavam ādyam. audārikam ity arthaḥ. yad garbhajaṃ yac ca saṃmūrcchanajaṃ tat sarvam audārikaṃ draṣṭavyam. 
 § 350. tadantaraṃ yan nirdiṣṭaṃ tat kasmin janmanīty ata āha — 
 aupapādikaṃ vaikriyikam || 
 § 351. upapāde bhavam aupapādikam, tatsarvaṃ vaikriyikaṃ veditavyam. 
 § 352. yady aupapādikaṃ vaikriyikam, anaupapādikasya vaikriyikatvābhāva ity ata āha — 
 labdhipratyayaṃ ca || 
 § 353. ‘ca’ śabdena vaikriyikam abhisaṃbadhyate. tapoviśeṣād ṛddhiprāptir labdhiḥ. labdhiḥ pratyayaḥ kāraṇam asya labdhipratyayam. vaikriyikaṃ labdhipratyayaṃ ca bhavatīty abhisaṃbadhyate. 
 § 354. kim etad eva labdhyapekṣam utānyad apy astīty ata āha — 
 taijasam api || 
 § 355. ‘api’ śabdena labdhipratyayam abhisaṃbadhyate. taijasam api labdhipratyayaṃ bhavatīti 
 § 356. vaikriyikānantaraṃ yad upadiṣṭaṃ tasya svarūpanirdhāraṇārthaṃ svāminirdeśārthaṃ cāha — 
 śubhaṃ viśuddham avyāghāti cāhārakaṃ pramattasaṃyatasyaiva || 
 § 357. śubhakāraṇatvāc chubhavyapadeśaḥ. śubhakarmaṇa āhārakakāyayogasya kāraṇatvāc chubham ity ucyate annasya prāṇavyapadeśavat. viśuddhakāryatvād viśuddhavyapadeśaḥ. viśuddhasya puṇyakarmaṇaḥ aśabalasya niravadyasya kāryatvād viśuddham ity ucyate tantūnāṃ kārpāsavyapadeśavat. ubhayato vyāghātābhāvād avyāghāti. na hy āhārakaśarīreṇānyasya vyāghātaḥ. nāpy anyenāhārakasyeti. tasya prayojanasamucyārthaḥ  ‘ca’ śabdaḥ kriyate. *  tad yathā — kadācil labdhiviśeṣasadbhāvajñāpanārthaṃ kadācit sūkṣmapadārthanirdhāraṇārthaṃ saṃyamaparipālanārthaṃ ca. āhārakam iti prāguktasya pratyāmnāyaḥ. yadāhārakaśarīraṃ nirvartayitum ārabhate tadā pramatto bhavatīti ‘pramattasaṃyatasya’ ity ucyate. iṣṭato ’vadhāraṇārthaṃ ‘eva’kāropādānam. yathaivaṃ vijñāyeta pramattasaṃyatasyaivāhārakaṃ nānyasyeti. maivaṃ vijñāyi pramattasaṃyatasyāhārakam eveti. mā bhūd audārikādinivṛttir iti. 
 § 358. evaṃ vibhaktāni śarīrāṇi bibhratāṃ saṃsāriṇāṃ pratigati kiṃ triliṅgasaṃnidhānaṃ uta liṅganiyamaḥ kaścid astīty ata āha — 
 nārakasaṃmūrcchino napuṃsakāni || 
 § 359. nārakāṇi vakṣyante. narakeṣu bhavā nārakāḥ. saṃmūrcchanaṃ saṃmūrcchaḥ sa yeṣām asti te saṃmūrcchinaḥ. nārakāś ca saṃmūrcchinaś ca nārakasaṃmūrcchinaḥ. cāritramohavikalpanokaṣāyabhedasya napuṃsakavedasyāśubhanāmnaś codayān na striyo na pumāṃsa iti napuṃsakāni bhavanti. nārakasaṃmūrcchino napuṃsakāny eveti niyamaḥ. tatra hi strīpuṃsaviṣayamanojñaśabdagandharūparasasparśasaṃbandhanimittā svalpāpi sukhamātrā nāsti. 
 § 360. yady evam avaghriyate, arthād āpannam etad uktebhyo ’nye saṃsāriṇas triliṅgā iti yatrātyantaṃ napuṃsakaliṅgasyābhāvas tatpratipādanārtham āha — 
 na devāḥ || 
 § 361. straiṇaṃ pauṃsnaṃ ca yan niratiśayasukhaṃ śubhagatināmodayāpekṣaṃ tad devā anubhavantīti na teṣu napuṃsakāni santi. 
 § 362. athetare kiyal liṅgā ity ata āha — 
 śeṣās trivedāḥ || 
 § 363. trayo vedā yeṣāṃ te trivedāḥ. ke punas te vedāḥ? strītvaṃ puṃstvaṃ napuṃsakatvam iti. kathaṃ teṣāṃ siddhiḥ? vedyata iti vedaḥ. liṃgam ity arthaḥ. tad dvividhaṃ dravyaliṃgaṃ bhāvaliṃgaṃ ceti. dravyaliṃgaṃ yonimehanādi nāmakarmodayanirvartitam. nokaṣāyodayāpāditavṛtti bhāvaliṃgam. strīvedodayāt styāyastyasyāṃ garbha iti strī. puṃvedodayāt sūte janayatyapatyam iti pumān. napuṃsakavedodayāt tadubhayaśaktivikalaṃ napuṃsakam. rūḍhiśabdāś caite. rūḍhiṣu ca kriyā vyutpattyarthaṃ ca. yathā gacchatīti gaur iti. itarathā hi garbhadhāraṇādikriyāprādhānye bālavṛddhānāṃ tiryaṅmanuṣyāṇāṃ devānāṃ kārmaṇakāyayogasthānāṃ ca tadabhāvāt strītvādivyapadeśo na syāt. ta ete trayo vedāḥ śeṣāṇāṃ garbhajānāṃ bhavanti. 
 § 364. ya ime janmayoniśarīraliṃgasaṃbandhāhitaviśeṣāḥ prāṇino nirdiśyante devādayo vicitradharmādharmavaśīkṛtāś catasṛṣu gatiṣu śarīrāṇi dhārayantas te kiṃ yathākālam upabhuktāyuṣo mūrtyantarāṇy āskandanti utāyathākālam apīty ata āha — 
 aupapādikacaramottamadehāsaṃkhyeyavarṣāyuṣo ’napavartyāyuṣaḥ || 
 § 365. aupapādikā vyākhyātā devanārakā iti. caramaśabdo ’ntyavācī. uttama utkṛṣṭaḥ. carama uttamo deho yeṣāṃ te caramottamadehāḥ. parītasaṃsārās tajjanmanirvāṇārhā ity arthaḥ. asaṃkhyeyam atītasaṃkhyānam upamāpramāṇena palyādinā gamyam āyur yeṣāṃ ta ime asaṃkhyeyavarṣāyuṣas tiryaṅmanuṣyā uttarakurvādiṣu prasūtāḥ. aupapādikāś ca caramottamadehāś ca asaṃkhyeyavarṣāyuṣaś ca aupapādikacaramottamadehāsaṃkhyeyavarṣāyuṣaḥ. bāhyasyopaghātanimittasya viṣaśastrādeḥ sati saṃnidhāne hrasvaṃ bhavatīty apavartyam. apavartyam āyur yeṣāṃ ta ime apavartyāyuṣaḥ. na apavartyāyuṣaḥ anapavartyāyuṣaḥ. na hy eṣām aupapādikādīnāṃ bāhyanimittavaśād āyur apavartyate, ity ayaṃ niyamaḥ. itareṣām aniyamaḥ. caramasya dehasyotkṛṣṭatvapradarśanārtham uttamagrahaṇaṃ nārthāntaraviśeṣo ’sti. ‘caramadehā’ iti vā pāṭhaḥ. 
 iti tattvārthavṛttau sarvārthasiddhisaṃjñikāyāṃ dvitīyo ’dhyāyaḥ || 2 || 
 
 
	  atha tṛtīyo ’dhyāyaḥ
	   §§ 366–441 
 § 366. ‘bhavapratyayo ’vadhir devanārakāṇām’ ity evam ādiṣu nārakāḥ śrutās tataḥ pṛcchati ke te nārakā iti. tatpratipādanārthaṃ tadadhikaraṇanirdeśaḥ kriyate — 
 ratnaśarkarāvālukāpaṅkadhūmatamomahātamaḥprabhā bhūmayo ghanāmbuvātākāśaprathiṣṭhāḥ saptādho ’dhaḥ || 
 § 367. ratnaṃ ca śarkarā ca vālukā ca paṅkaś ca dhūmaś ca tamaś ca mahātamaś ca ratnaśarkarāvālukāpaṅkadhūmatamomahātamāṃsi. ‘prabhā’ śabdaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate. sāhacaryāt tācchabdyam. citrādiratnaprabhāsahacaritā bhūmiḥ ratnaprabhā, śarkarāprabhāsahacaritā bhūmiḥ śarkarāprabhā, vālukāprabhāsahacaritā bhūmir vālukāprabhā, paṅkaprabhāsahacaritā bhūmiḥ pańkaprabhā, dhūmaprabhāsahacaritā bhūmir dhūmaprabhā, tamaḥprabhāsahacaritā bhūmis tamaḥprabhā, mahātamaḥprabhāsahacaritā bhūmir mahātamaḥprabhā iti. etāḥ saṃjñā anenopāyena vyutpādyante. ‘bhūmi’ grahaṇam adhikaraṇaviśeṣapratipattyartham. yathā svargapaṭalāni bhūmim anāśritya vyavasthitāni na tathā nārakāvāsāḥ. kiṃ tarhi. bhūmim āśritā iti. āsāṃ bhūmīnāmālmbananirjñānārthaṃ ghanāmbuvātādigrahaṇaṃ kriyate. ghanāmbu ca vātaś ca ākāśaṃ ca ghanāmbuvātākāśāni. tani pratiṣṭhā āśrayo yāsāṃ tā ghanāmbuvātākāśapratiṣṭhāḥ. sarvā etā bhūmayo ghanodadhivalayapratiṣṭhāḥ. ghanodadhivalayaṃ ghanavātavalayapratiṣṭham. ghanavātavalayaṃ tanuvātavalayapratiṣṭham. tanuvātavalayam ākāśapratiṣṭham. ākāśam ātmapratiṣṭham, tasyaivādhārādheyatvāt. trīṇy apy etāni valayāni pratyekaṃ viṃśatiyojanasahasrabāhulyāni. ‘sapta’ grhaṇaṃ saṃkhyāntaranivṛttyartham. sapta bhūmayo nāṣṭau na nava ceti. ‘adho ’dhaḥ’ vacanaṃ tiryakpracayanivṛttyartham. 
 § 368. kiṃ tā bhūmayo nārakāṇāṃ sarvatrāvāsā āhosvit kvacit kvacid iti prannirdhāraṇārtham āha —  * 
 tāsu triṃśatpañcaviṃśatipañcadaśadaśatripañconaikanarakaśatasahasrāṇi paṃca caiva yathākramam || 
 § 369. tāsu ratnaprabhādiṣu bhūmiṣu narakāṇy anena saṃkhyāyante yathākramam. ratnaprabhāyāṃ triṃśannarakaśatasahasrāṇi, śarkarāprabhāyāṃ pañcaviṃśatir narakaśatasahasrāṇi, vālukāprabhāyāṃ pañcadaśa narakaśatasahasrāṇi, paṃkaprabhāyāṃ daśa narakaśatasahasrāṇi, dhūmaprabhāyāṃ trīṇi narakaśatasahasrāṇi, tamaḥprabhāyāṃ pañconam ekaṃ narakaśatasahasraṃ, mahātamaḥprabhāyāṃ pañca narakāni. ratnaprabhāyāṃ narakaprastārās trayodaśa. tato ’dha ā saptamyā dvau dvau narakaprastārau hīnau. itaro viśeṣo lokānuyogato veditavyaḥ. 
 § 370. atha tāsu bhūmiṣu nārakānāṃ kaḥ prativiśeṣa ity ata āha — 
 nārakā nityāśubhataraleśyāpariṇāmadehavedanāvikriyāḥ || 
 § 371. leśyādayo vyākhyātārthāḥ. aśubhatarā iti prakarṣanirdeśaḥ tiryaggativiṣayāśubhaleśyādyapekṣayā adho ’dhaḥ svagatyapekṣayā ca veditavyaḥ. ‘nitya’ śabda ābhīkṣṇyavacanaḥ. nityam aśubhatarā leśyādayo yeṣāṃ te nityāśubhataraleśyāpariṇāmadehavedanāvikriyā nārakāḥ. prathamādvitīyayoḥ kāpotī leśyā, tṛtīyāyam upariṣṭāt kāpotī adho nīlā, caturthyāṃ nīlā, pañcamyām upari nīlā adhaḥ kṛṣṇā, ṣaṣṭhyāṃ kṛṣṇā, saptamyāṃ paramakṛṣṇā. svāyuḥpramāṇāvadhṛtā dravyaleśyā uktāḥ. bhāvaleśyāsu antarmuhūrtaparivartinyaḥ. pariṇāmāḥ sparśarasagandhavarṇaśabdāḥ kṣetraviśeṣanimittavaśād atiduḥkhahetavo ’śubhatarā. dehāś ca teṣām aśubhanāmakarmodayād atyantāśubhatarā vikṛtākṛtayo huṇḍasaṃsthānā durdarśanāḥ. teṣām utsedhaḥ prathamāyāṃ sapta dhanūṃṣi trayo hastāḥ ṣaḍaṃgulayaḥ. adho ’dho — dviguṇadviguṇa utsedhaḥ. abhyantarāsadvedyodaye sati anādipāriṇāmikaśītoṣṇabāhyanimittajanitā atitīvrā vedanā bhavanti nārakāṇām. prathamādvitīyātṛtīyācaturthīṣu uṣṇavedanāny eva narakāṇi. pañcamyām upari uṣṇavedene dve narakaśatasahasre. adhaḥ śītavedanam ekaṃ śatasahasram. ṣaṣṭhīsaptamyoḥ śītavedanāny eva. śubhaṃ vikariṣyāma iti aśubhataram eva vikurvanti, sukhahetūn utpādayāma iti duḥkhahetūn evotpādayanti. ta ete bhāvā adho ’dho ’śutarā veditavyāḥ. * 
 § 372. kim eteṣāṃ nārakāṇāṃ śītoṣṇajanitam eva duḥkham utānyathāpi bhavatīty ata āha — 
 parasparodīritaduḥkhāḥ || 
 § 373. kathaṃ parasparodīrītaduḥkhatvam? nārakāḥ bhavapratyayenāvadhinā mithyādarśanodayād vibhaṅgavyapadeśabhājā ca dūrād eva duḥkhahetūn avagamyotpannaduḥkhāḥ pratyāsattau parasparālokanāc ca prajvalitakopāgnayaḥ pūrvabhavānusmaraṇāc cātitīvrānubaddhavairāś ca śvaśṛgālādivatsvābhighāte pravartamānāḥ svavikriyākṛtāsivāsīparaśubhiṇḍimālaśaktitomarakuntāyodhanādibhir āyudhaiḥ svakaracaraṇadaśanaiś ca chedanabhedanatakṣaṇadaṃśanādibhiḥ parasparasyātitīvraṃ duḥkham utpādayanti. 
 § 374. kim etāvān eva duḥkhotpattikāraṇaprakāra utānyo ’pi kaścid astīty ata āha — 
 saṃkliṣṭāsurodīritaduḥkhāś ca prāk caturthyāḥ || 
 § 375. devagatināmakarmavikalpasyāsuratvasaṃvartanasya karmaṇa udayād asyanti parān ity asurāḥ. pūrvajanmani bhāvitenātitīvreṇa saṃkleśapariṇāmena yad upārjitaṃ pāpakarma tasyodayāt satataṃ kliṣṭāḥ saṃkliṣṭāḥ, saṃvikliṣṭā asurāḥ saṃvikliṣṭāsurāḥ. saṃkliṣṭā iti viśeṣaṇān na sarve asurā nārakāṇāṃ duḥkham utpādayanti. kiṃ tarhi? ambāvarīṣādaya eva kecaneti. avadhipradarśanārthaṃ ‘prak caturthyāḥ’ iti viśeṣaṇam. upari tisṛṣu pṛthvīṣu saṃkliṣṭāsurā bādhāhetavo nātaḥ param iti pradarśanārtham. ‘ca’ śabdaḥ pūrvoktaduḥkhahetusamuccayārthaḥ. sutatptāyorasapāyananiṣṭaptāyastambhāliṅganakūṭaśālmalyārohaṇāvataraṇāyoghanābhighātavāsīkṣuratakṣaṇakṣārataptatailāvasecanāyaḥkumbhīpākāmbarīṣabharjanavaitaraṇīmajjanayantraniṣpīḍanādibhir nārakāṇāṃ duḥkham utpādayanti. evaṃ chedanabhedanādibhiḥ śakalīkṛtamūrtīnām api teṣāṃ na maraṇam akāle bhavati. kutaḥ? anapavartyāyuṣkatvāt. 
 § 376. yady evaṃ, tad eva tāvad ucyatāṃ nārakāṇām āyuḥparimāṇam ity ata āha — 
 teṣv ekatrisaptadaśasaptadaśadvāviṃśatitrayāstriṃśatsāgaropamā sattvānāṃ parā sthitiḥ || 
 § 377. yathākramam ity anuvartate. teṣu narakeṣu bhūmikrameṇa yathāsaṃkhyam ekādayaḥ sthitayo ’bhisaṃbadhyante. ratnaprabhāyām utkṛṣṭā sthitir ekasāgaropamā. śarkarāprabhāyāṃ trisāgaropamā. vālukāprabhāyāṃ saptasāgaropamā. paṃkaḥprabhāyāṃ daśasāgaropamā. dhūmaprabhāyāṃ saptadaśasāgaropamā. tamaḥprabhāyāṃ dvāviṃśatisāgaropamā. mahātamaḥprabhāyāṃ trayāstriṃśatsāgaropamā iti. parā utkṛṣṭety arthaḥ. ‘sattvānām’ iti vacanaṃ bhūminivṛttyartham. bhūmiṣu sattvānām iyaṃ sthitiḥ, na bhūmīnām iti. 
 § 378. uktaḥ saptabhūmivistīrṇo ’dholokaḥ. idānīṃ tiryagloko vaktavyaḥ. kathaṃ punas tiryaglokaḥ. yatho ’saṃkhyeyāḥ svayaṃbhūramaṇaparyantās tiryakpracayaviśeṣeṇāvasthitā dvīpasamudrās tatas tiryagloka iti. ke punas tiryagvyavasthitā ity ata āha — 
 jambūdvīpalavaṇodādayaḥ śubhanāmāno dvīpasamudrāḥ || 
 § 379. jambūdvīpādayo dvīpāḥ. lavaṇodādayaḥ samudrāḥ. yāni loke śubhāni nāmāni tan nāmānas te. tad yathā — jambūdvīpo dvīpaḥ. lavaṇodaḥ samudraḥ. dhātakīkhaṇḍo dvīpaḥ. kālodaḥ samudraḥ. puṣkaravaro dvīpaḥ. puṣkaravaraḥ samudraḥ. vāruṇīvaro dvīpaḥ. vāruṇīvaraḥ samudraḥ. kṣīravaro dvīpaḥ. kṣīravaraḥ samudraḥ. ghṛtavaro dvīpaḥ. ghṛtavaraḥ samudraḥ. ikṣuvaro dvīpaḥ. ikṣuvaraḥ samudraḥ. nandīśvaravaro dvīpaḥ. nandīśvaravaraḥ samudraḥ. aruṇavaro dvīpaḥ. aruṇavaraḥ samudraḥ. ity evam asaṃkhyeyā dvīpasamudrāḥ svayambhūramaṇaparyantā veditavyāḥ. 
 § 380. amīṣāṃ viṣkambhasaṃniveśasaṃsthānaviśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 dvir dvir viskambhāḥ pūrvapūrvaparikṣepiṇo valayākṛtayaḥ || 
 § 381. dvir dvir iti vīpsābhyāvṛttivacanaṃ viṣkambhadviguṇatvavyārpttham. *  ādyasya dvīpasya yo viṣkambhaḥ tad dviguṇaviṣkambho lavaṇajaladhiḥ. taddviguṇaviṣkambho dvitīyo dvīpaḥ. taddviguṇaviṣkambho dvitīyo jaladhir iti. dvir dvir viṣkambho yeṣāṃ te dvir dvir viṣkambhāḥ. pūrvapūrvaparikṣepivacanaṃ grāmanagarādivadviniveśo mā vijñāyīti. valayākṛtivacanaṃ caturasrādisaṃsthānāntaranivṛttyartham. 
 § 382. atrāha, jambūdvīpasya pradeśasaṃsthānaviṣkambhā vaktavyās tanmūlatvāditaraviṣkambhādivijñānasyety ucyate — 
 tanmadhye merunābhir vṛtto yojanaśatasahasraviṣkambho jambūdvīpaḥ || 
 § 383. teṣāṃ madhye tanmadhye. keṣām? pūrvoktānāṃ dvīpasamudrāṇām. nābhir iva nābhiḥ. merur nābhir yasya sa merunābhiḥ. vṛtta ādityamaṇḍalopamānaḥ. śatānāṃ sahasraṃ śatasahasram. yojanānāṃ śatasahasraṃ yojanaśatasahasraṃ. yojanaśatasahasraṃ viṣkambho yasya so ’yaṃ yojanaśatasahasraviṣkambhaḥ. ko ’sau? jambūdvīpaḥ. kathaṃ jambūdvīpaḥ? jambūvṛkṣopalakṣitatvāt. uttarakurūṇāṃ madhye jambūvṛkṣo ’nādinidhanaḥ pṛthivīpariṇāmo ’kṛtrimaḥ saparivāras tadupalakṣito ’yaṃ dvīpaḥ. 
 § 384. tatra jambūdvīpe ṣaḍabhiḥ kalaparvatair vibhaktāni sapta kṣetrāṇi kāni tānīty ata āha —  * 
 bharatahaimavataharivideharamyakahairaṇyavatairāvatavarṣāḥ kṣetraṇi || 
 § 385. bharatādayaḥ saṃjñā anādikālapravṛttā amimittāḥ. *  tatra bharatavarṣaḥ kva saṃniviṣṭaḥ? dakṣiṇadigbhāge himavato ’dres trayāṇāṃ samudrāṇāṃ madhye āropitacāpākāro bharatavarsaḥ. vijayārddhena gaṅgāsindhubhyāṃ ca vibhaktaḥ sa ṣaṭkhaṇḍaḥ. kṣudrahimavantam uttareṇa dakṣiṇena mahāhimavantaṃ pūrvāparasamudrayor madhye haimavatavarṣaḥ. niṣadhasya dakṣiṇato mahāhimavata uttarataḥ pūrvāparasamudrayor antarāle harivarṣaḥ. niṣadhasyottarān nīlato dakṣiṇataḥ pūrvāparasamudrayor antare videhasya saṃniveśo draṣṭavyaḥ. nīlata uttarāt (d) rukmiṇo dakṣiṇāt pūrvāparasamudrayor madhye ramyakavarṣaḥ. rukmiṇa uttarāc chikhariṇo dakṣiṇāt pūrvāparasamudrayor madhye saṃniveśī hairaṇyavatavarṣaḥ. śikhariṇa uttaratas trayāṇāṃ samudrāṇāṃ madhye airāvatavarṣaḥ. vijayārddhena raktāraktodābhyāṃ ca vibhaktaḥ sa ṣaṭkhaṇḍaḥ. 
 § 386. ṣaṭ kulaparvatā ity uktaṃ ke punas te kathaṃ vā vyavasthitā ity ata āha — 
 tadvibhājinaḥ pūrvāparāyatā himavanmahāhimavanniṣadhanīlarukmiśikhariṇo varṣadharaparvatāḥ || 
 § 387. tāni kṣetrāṇi vibhajanta ity evaṃ śīlās tadvibhājinaḥ. pūrvāparāyatā iti pūrvāparakoṭibhyāṃ lavaṇajaladhisparśina ity arthaḥ. himavadādayo ’nādikālapravṛttā animittasaṃjñā varṣavibhāgahetutvād varṣadharaparvatā ity ucyante. tatra kva himavān? bharatasya haimavatasya ca sīmani vyavasthitaḥ. kṣudrahimavān yojanaśatocchrāyaḥ. haimavatasya harivarṣasya ca vibhāgakaro mahāhimavān dviyojanaśatocchrāyaḥ. videhasya dakṣiṇato harivarṣasyottarato niṣadho nāma parvataś caturyojanaśatocchrāyaḥ. uttare trayo ’pi parvatāḥ svavarṣavibhājino vyākhyātāḥ. ucchrāyaś ca teṣāṃ catvāri dve ekaṃ ca yojanaśataṃ veditavyam. sarveṣāṃ parvatānām ucchrāyasya caturbhāgo ’vagāhaḥ. 
 § 388. tesāṃ varṇaviśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 hemārjunatapanīyavaiḍūryarajatahemamayāḥ || 
 § 389. ta ete himavadādayaḥ parvatā hemādimayā viditavyā yathākramam. hemamayo himavān cīnapaṭṭavarṇaḥ. arjunamayo mahāhimavān śuklavarṇaḥ. tapanīyamayo niṣadhas taruṇādityavarṇaḥ. vaiḍūryamayo nīlo māyuragrīvābhaḥ. rajatamayo rukmī śuklaḥ. hemamayaḥ śikharo cīnapaṭṭavarṇaḥ. 
 § 390. punar api tadviśeṣaṇārtham āha — 
 maṇivicitrapārśvā upari mūle ca tulyavistārāḥ || 
 § 391. nānavarṇaprabhādiguṇopetair maṇibhir vicitrāṇi pārśvāṇi yeṣāṃ te maṇivicitrapārśvāḥ. aniṣṭasaṃsthānasya nivṛttyartham uparyādivacanaṃ kriyate. ‘ca’ śabdo madhyasamuccayārthaḥ. ya eṣāṃ mūle vistāraḥ sa upari madhye ca tulyaḥ. 
 § 392. teṣāṃ madhye labdhāspadā hradā ucyante — 
 padmamahāpadmatigiñchakesarimahāpuṇḍarīkapuṇḍarīkā hradās teṣām upari || 
 § 393. padmo mahāpadmas tigiñchaḥ kesarī mahāpuṇḍarīkaḥ puṇḍarīka iti teṣāṃ himavadādīnām upari yathākramam ete hradā veditavyāḥ. 
 § 394. tatrādyasya saṃsthānaviśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 prathamo yojanasahasrāyāmas tadarddhaviṣkambho hradaḥ || 
 § 395. prākpratyag yojanasahasrāyām udagavāk pañcayojanaśatavistāro vajramayatalo vividhamaṇikanakavicitritataṭaḥ padmanāmāhradaḥ. 
 § 396. tasyāvagāhapraklṛptyartham idam ucyate — 
 daśayojanāvagāhaḥ || 
 § 397. avagāho ’dhaḥ praveśo nimnatā. daśayojanāny avagāho ’sya daśayojanāvagāhaḥ. 
 § 398. tanmadye kim — 
 tanmadhye yojanaṃ puṣkaram || 
 § 399. yojanapramāṇam yojanam, krośāyāmapatratvāt krośadvayaviṣkambhakarṇikatvāc ca yojanāyāmaviṣkambham. jalatalāt krośadvayocchrāyanālaṃ yāvad bahulapatrapracayaṃ puṣkaram avagantavyam. 
 § 400. itareṣāṃ hradānāṃ puṣkarāṇāṃ cāyāmādinirjñānārtham āha — 
 taddviguṇadviguṇā hrdāḥ puṣkarāṇi ca || 
 § 401. sa ca tacca te, tayor dviguṇā dviguṇās taddviguṇadviguṇā iti dvitvaṃ vyāptijñā–panārtham. kena dviguṇāḥ? āyāmādinā. padmahradasya dviguṇāyāmaviṣkambhāvagāho mahāpadmo hradaḥ. tasya dviguṇāyāmaviṣkambhāvagāhas tigiñcho hradaḥ. puṣkarāṇi ca. kiṃ? dviguṇāni dviguṇānīty abhisaṃbadhyate. 
 § 402. tannivāsinīnāṃ devīnāṃ saṃjñājīvitaparivārapratipādanārtham āha — 
 tannivāsinyo devyaḥ śrīhrīdhṛtikīrtibuddhilakṣmyaḥ palyopamasthitayaḥ sasāmānikapariṣatkāḥ || 
 § 403. teṣu puṣkareṣu karṇikāmadhyadeśaniveśinaḥ śaradvimalapūrṇacandradyutiharāḥ krośāyāmāḥ krośārddhaviṣkambhā deśonakrośotsedāḥ prāsādāḥ. teṣu nivasantīty evaṃ śīlās tannivāsinyaḥ, devyaḥ śrīhrīdhṛtikīrtibuddhilakṣmīsaṃjñikās teṣu padmādiṣu yathākramaṃ veditavyāḥ. ‘palyopamasthitayaḥ’ ity anenāyuṣaḥ pramānam uktam. samāne sthāne bhavāḥ sāmānikāḥ. sāmānikāś ca pariṣadaś ca sāmānikapariṣadaḥ. saha sāmānikapariṣadbhir vartanta iti sasāmānikapariṣatkāḥ. tasya padmasya parivārapadmeṣu prāsādānām upari sāmānikāḥ pariṣadaś ca vasanti. 
 § 404. yakābhiḥ saridbhis tāni kṣetrāṇi pravibhaktāni tā ucyate — 
 gaṅgāsindhurohidrohitāsyāhariddharikāntāsītāsītodānārīnarakāntāsuvarṇarūpyakūlāraktāraktodāḥ saritas tanmadhyagāḥ || 
 § 405. sarito na vāpyaḥ. tāḥ kim antarā uta samīpā iti? āha — tanmadhyagāḥ teṣāṃ kṣetrāṇām madhyaṃ tanmadhyam. tanmadhyaṃ tanmadhyena vā gacchatīti tanmadhyagāḥ. ekatra sarvāsāṃ prasaṃganivṛttyarthaṃ digviśeṣapratipattyarthaṃ cāha — 
 dvayor dvayoḥ pūrvāḥ pūrvagāḥ || 
 § 406. dvayor dvayoḥ saritor ekaikaṃ kṣetraṃ viṣaya iti vākyaśeṣābhisaṃbandhād ekatra sarvāsāṃ prasaṃganivṛttiḥ kṛtā. ‘pūvaḥ pūrvagāḥ’ iti vacanaṃ digviśeṣapratipattyartham. tatra pūrvā yāḥ saritas tāḥ pūrvagāḥ. pūrvajaladhiṃ gacchantīti pūrvagāḥ. kim apekṣaṃ pūrvatvam? sūtranirdeśāpekṣam. yady evaṃ gaṅgāsindhvādayaḥ sapta pūvagā iti prāptam? naiṣa doṣaḥ; dvayor dvayor ity abhisaṃbandhāt. dvayor dvayoḥ pūvāḥ pūrvagā iti veditavyāḥ. 
 § 407. itarāsaṃ digvibhāgapratipattyartham āha — 
 śeṣāstv aparagāḥ || 
 § 408. dvayor dvayor yā avaśiṣṭās tā aparagāḥ pratyetavyāḥ. aparasamudraṃ gacchantīty aparagāḥ. tatra padmahradaprabhavā pūrvatoraṇadvāranirgatā gaṅgā. aparatoraṇadvāranirgatā sindhuḥ. udīcyatoraṇadvāranirgatā rohitāsyā. mahāpadmahradaprabhavā avācyatoraṇadvāranirgatā rohit. udīcyatoraṇadvāranirgatā harikāntā. tigiñchahradaprabhavā dakṣiṇatoraṇadvāranirgatā harit. udīcyatoraṇadvāranirgatā sītodā. kesarihradaprabhavā avācyatoraṇadvāranirgatā sītā. udīcyatoraṇadvāranirgatā narakāntā. mahāpuṇḍarīkahradaprabhavā dakṣiṇatoraṇadvāranirgatā nārī. udīcyatoraṇadvāranirgatā rūpyakūlā. puṇḍarīkahradaprabhavā avācyatoraṇadvāranirgatā suvarṇakūlā. pūrvatoraṇadvāranirgatā raktā. pratīcyatoraṇadvāranirgatā raktodā. 
 § 409. tāsāṃ parivārapratipādanārtham āha — 
 caturdaśanadīsahasraparivṛtā gaṅgāsindhvādayo nadyaḥ || 
 § 410. kim arthaṃ ‘gaṅgāsindhvādi’ grahanaṃ kriyate? nadīgrahṇārtham. prakṛtās tā abhisaṃbhadyante? naivaṃ śaṃkyam; ‘anantarasya vidhir vā bhavati pratiṣedho vā’ iti aparagāṇām eva grahaṇaṃ syāt. gaṅgādigrahaṇam evāstīti cet? pūrvagāṇām eva grahaṇaṃ syāt. ata ubhayīnāṃ grahaṇārthaṃ ‘gaṅgāsindhvādi’ grahaṇaṃ kriyate. ‘nadī’ grahaṇaṃ dviguṇā dviguṇā ity abhisaṃbandhārtham, gaṅgā caturdaśanadīsahasraparivṛtā. sindhur api. evam uttarā api nadyaḥ pratikṣetraṃ taddviguṇadviguṇā bhavanti; ā videhāntāt. tata uttarā arddhārddhahīnāḥ. 
 § 411. uktānāṃ kṣetrāṇāṃ viṣkambhapratipattyartham āha — 
 bharataḥ ṣaḍviṃśapañcayojanaśatavistāraḥ ṣaṭ caikonaviṃśatibhāgā yojanasya || 
 § 412. ṣaḍadhikā viṃśatiḥ ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ. ṣaḍviṃśatir adhikā yeṣu tāni ṣaḍviṃśāni. ṣaḍviṃśāni pañcayojanaśatāni vistāro yasya ṣaḍviṃśapañcayojanaśatavistāro bharataḥ. kim etāvān eva? na; ity āha ṣaṭ caikonaviṃśatibhāgā yojanasya vistāro ’syety abhisaṃbadhyate. 
 § 413. itareṣāṃ viṣkambhaviśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 taddviguṇadviguṇavistārā varṣadharavarṣā videhāntāḥ || 
 § 414. tato bharatād dviguṇo dviguṇo vistāro yesāṃ ta ime taddviguṇadviguṇavistārāḥ. ke te varṣadharavarṣāḥ. kiṃ sarve? na; ity āha videhāntā iti. 
 § 415. athottareṣāṃ katham ity ata āha — 
 uttarā dakṣiṇatulyāḥ || 
 § 416. uttarā airāvatādayo nīlāntā bharatādibhir dakṣiṇais tulyā draṣṭavyāḥ. atītasya sarvasyāyaṃ viśeṣo veditavyaḥ. tena hradapuṣkarādīnāṃ tulyatā yojyā. 
 § 417. attrāha, uktesu bharatādiṣu kṣetreṣu manuṣyāṇāṃ kiṃ tulyo ’nubhavādiḥ, āho svid asti kaścit prativiśeṣa ity atrocyate — 
 bharatairāvatayor vṛddhihrāsau ṣaṭsamayābhyām utsarpiṇyavasarpiṇībhyām ||
