 § 612. yathā sarassalilāvāhidvāraṃ tadāsravakāraṇatvād āsrava ity ākhyāyate tathā yogapraṇālikayā ātmanaḥ karma āsravatīti yoga āsrava iti vyapadeśam arhati. 
 § 613. āha, karma dvividhaṃ puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ ceti. tasya kim aviśeṣeṇa yoga āsravahetur āhosvid asti kaścit prativiśeṣa ity atrocyate — 
 śubhaḥ puṇyasyāśubhaḥ pāpasya || 
 § 614. kaḥ śubho yogaḥ ko vā aśubhaḥ. prāṇātipātādattādānamaithunādir aśubhaḥ kāyayogaḥ. anṛtabhāṣaṇaparuṣāsabhyavacanādir aśubho vāgyogaḥ. vadhacintanerṣyāsūyādir aśubho manoyogaḥ. tato viparītaḥ śubhaḥ. kathaṃ yogasya śubhāśubhatvam. śubhapariṇāmanirvṛtto yogaḥ śubhaḥ. aśubhapariṇāmanirvṛttaś cāśubhaḥ. na punaḥ śubhāśubhakarmakāraṇatvena. yady evam ucyate śubhayoga eva na syāt, śubhayogasyāpi jñānāvaraṇādibandhahetutvābhyupagamāt. punāty ātmānaṃ pūyate ’neneti vā puṇyam. tat sadvedyādi. pāti rakṣati ātmānaṃ śubhād iti pāpam. tad asadvedyādi. 
 § 615. āha kim ayam āsravaḥ sarvasaṃsāriṇām samānaphalārambhahetur āhosvit kaścid asti prativiśeṣa ity atrocyate — 
 sakaṣāyākaṣāyayoḥ sāṃparāyikeryāpathayoḥ || 
 § 616. svāmibhedād āsravabhedaḥ. svāminau dvau sakaṣāyo ’kaṣāyaś cati. kaṣāyaḥ krodhādiḥ. kaṣāya iva kaṣāyaḥ. kaḥ upamārthaḥ. yathā kaṣāyo naiyagrodhādiḥ śleṣahetus tathā krodhādir apy ātmanaḥ karmaśleṣahetutvāt kaṣāya iva kaṣāya ity ucyate. saha kaṣāyeṇa vartata iti sakaṣāyaḥ. na vidyate kaṣāyo yasyety akaṣāyaḥ. sakaṣāyaś cākaṣāyaś ca sakaṣāyākaṣāyau tayoḥ sakaṣāyākaṣāyayoḥ. saṃparāyaḥ saṃsāraḥ tatprayojanaṃ karma sāmparāyikam. īraṇam īryā yogo gatir ity arthaḥ. taddvārakaṃ karma īryāpatham. sāṃparāyikaṃ ca īryāpathaṃ ca sāmparāyikeryāpathe. tayoḥ sāmparāyikeryāpathayoḥ. yathāsaṃkhyam abhisaṃbandhaḥ sakaṣāyasyātmano mithyādṛṣṭyādeḥ sāṃparāyikasya karmaṇa āsravo bhavati. akaṣāyasya upaśāntakaṣāyāder īryāpathasya karmaṇa āsravo bhavati. 
 § 617. ādāv uddiṣṭasyāsravasya bhedapratipādanārtham āha — 
 indriyakaṣāyāvratakriyāḥ pañcacatuḥpañcapañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyāḥ pūrvasya bhedāḥ || 
 § 618. atra indriyādīnāṃ paṃcādibhir yathāsaṃkhyam abhisaṃbandho veditavyaḥ, indriyāṇi paṃca. catvāraḥ kaṣāyāḥ. pañcāvratāni. pañcaviṃśatiḥ kriyā iti. tatra pañcendriyāṇi sparśanādīny uktāni. catvāraḥ kaśāyāḥ krodhādayaḥ. pañcāvratāni prāṇavyaparopaṇādīni vakṣyate. pañcaviṃśatiḥ kriyā ucyante — caityagurupravacanapūjādilakṣaṇā samyaktvavardhanī kriyā samyaktvakriyā. anyadevatāstavanādirūpā mithyātvahetukī pravṛttir mithyātvakriyā. gamanāgamanādipravartanaṃ kāyādibhiḥ prayogakriyā. saṃyatasya sataḥ aviratiṃ pratyābhimukhyaṃ samādānakriyā. īryāpathanimitteryāpathakriyā. tā etāḥ pañca kriyā. krodhāveśāt prādoṣikī kriyā. praduṣṭasya sato ’bhyudyamaḥ kāyikī kriyā. hiṃsopakaraṇādānādhikaraṇikī kriyā. duḥkotpattitantratvāt pāritāpikī kriyā. āyurindriyabalocchvāsaniḥśvāsaprāṇānāṃ viyogakaraṇāt prānātipātikī kriyā. tā etāḥ pañca kriyāḥ. rāgārdrīkṛtatvāt pramādino ramaṇīyarūpālokanābhiprāyo darśanakriyā. pramādavaśāt spṛṣṭavyasaṃcetanānubandhaḥ sparśanakriyā. apūrvādhikaraṇotpādanāt prātyayikī kriyā. srtīpuruṣapaśusampātideśe ’ntarmalotsargakaraṇaṃ samantānupātakriyā. apramṛṣṭādṛṣṭabhūmau kāyādinikṣepo ’nābhogakriyā. tā etāḥ pañca kriyā. yāṃ pareṇa nirvartyāṃ kriyāṃ svayaṃ karoti sā svahastakriyā. pāpādānādipravṛttiviśeṣābhyanujñānaṃ nisargakriyā. parācaritasāvadyādiprakāśanaṃ vidāraṇakriyā. yathoktām ājñām āvaśyakādiṣu cāritramohodayāt kartum aśaknuvato ’nyathāprarūpaṇad ājñāvyāpādikī kriyā. śāṭhyālasyābhyāṃ pravacanopadiṣṭavidhikartavyatānādaro ’nākāṅkṣakriyā. tā etāḥ pañca kriyā. chedanabhedanaviśasanādikriyāparatvam anyena vārambhe kriyamāṇe praharṣaḥ prārambhakriyā. parigrahāvināśārthā pārigrāhikī kriyā. jñānadarśanādiṣu nikṛtir vañcanaṃ māyākriyā. anyaṃ mithyādarśanakriyākaraṇakāraṇāviṣṭaṃ praśaṃsādibhir dṛḍhayati yathā sādhu karoṣīti sā mithyādarśanakriyā. saṃyamaghātikarmodayavaśād anivṛttir apratyākhyānakriyā. tā etāḥ pañca kriyāḥ. samuditāḥ pañcaviṃśatikriyāḥ. etānīndriyādīni kāryakāraṇabhedād bhedam āpadyamānāni sāṃparāyikasya karmaṇa āśravadvārāṇi bhavanti. 
 § 619. atrāha, yogatrayasya sarvātmakāryatvāt sarveṣāṃ saṃsāriṇāṃ sādhāraṇaḥ, tato bandhaphalānubhavanaṃ pratyaviśeṣa ity atrocyate — naitad evam. yasmāt saty api pratyātmasaṃbhave teṣāṃ jīvapariṇāmebhyo ’nantavikalpebhyo viśeṣo ’bhyanujñāyate katham iti ced ucyate — 
 tīvramandajñātājñātabhāvādhikaraṇavīryaviśeṣebhyas tadviśeṣaḥ || 
 § 620. bāhyābhyantarahetūdīraṇavaśād udriktaḥ pariṇāmas tīvraḥ. tadviparīto mandaḥ. ayaṃ prāṇī mayā hantavya iti jñātvā pravṛttir jñātam ity ucyate. madāt pramādād vānavabudhya pravṛttir ajñātam. adhikriyante ’sminn arthā ity adhikaraṇaṃ dravyam ity arthaḥ. dravyasya svaśaktiviśeṣo vīryam. bhāvaśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate — tīvrabhāvo mandabhāva ity ādiḥ. etebhyas tasyāsravasya viśeṣo bhavati. kāraṇabhedād dhi kāryabheda iti. 
 § 621. atrāha, adhikaraṇam uktam, tatsvarūpam anirjñātam atas taducyatām iti. tatra bhedapratipādanadvārenādhikaraṇasvarūpanirjñānārtham āha — 
 adhikaraṇaṃ jīvājīvāḥ || 
 § 622. uktalakṣaṇā jīvājīvāḥ. yady uktalakṣaṇāḥ punarvacanaṃ kiṃ artham? adhikaraṇaviśeṣajñāpanārthaṃ punarvacanaṃ. jīvājīvā adhikaraṇam ity ayaṃ viśeṣo jñāpayitavya iti. kaḥ punar asau? hiṃsādyupakaraṇabhāva iti. syād etan mūlapadārthayor dvitvāj jīvājīvāv iti dvivacanaṃ nyāyaprāptam iti. tan na, paryāyāṇām adhikaraṇatvāt. yena kenacit paryāyeṇa viśiṣṭaṃ dravyam adhikaraṇam, na sāmānyam iti bahuvacanaṃ kṛtam. jīvājīvā adhikaraṇaṃ kasya? āsravasyeti. arthavaśād abhisaṃbandho bhavati. 
 § 623. tatra jīvādhikaraṇabhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 ādyaṃ saṃrambhasamārambhārambhayogakṛtakāritānumatakaṣāyaviśeṣais tris tris triś catuś caikaśaḥ || 
 § 624. prāṇavyaparopaṇādiṣu pramādavataḥ prayatnāveśaḥ saṃrambhaḥ. sādhanasamabhyāsīkaraṇaṃ samārambhaḥ prakrama ārambhaḥ. ‘yoga’ śabdo vyākhyātārthaḥ. kṛtavacanaṃ svātantryapratipattyārtham. kāritābhidhānaṃ paraprayogāpekṣam. anumataśabdaḥ prayojakasya mānasapariṇāmapradarśanārthaḥ. abhihitalakṣaṇāḥ kaṣāyāḥ krodhādayaḥ. viśiṣyate ’rtho ’rthāntarād iti viśeṣaḥ. sa pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate — saṃrambhaviśeṣaḥ samārambhaviśeṣa ity ādi. ādyaṃ jīvādhikaraṇam etair viśeṣaiḥ ‘bhidyate’ iti vākyaśeṣaḥ. ete catvāraḥ sujantās tryādiśabdā yathākramam abhisaṃbadhyante — saṃrambhasamārambhārambhās trayaḥ, yogās trayaḥ, kṛtakāritānumatās trayaḥ, kaṣāyāś catvāra iti. eteṣāṃ gaṇanābhyāvṛttiḥ sucā dyotyate. ekaśa iti vīpsānirdeśaḥ. ekaikaṃ tryādīn bhedān nayed ity arthaḥ. yad yathā  *  — krodhakṛtakāyasaṃrambhaḥ mānakṛtakāyasaṃrambhaḥ māyākṛtakāyasaṃrambhaḥ lobhakṛtakāyasaṃrambhaḥ krodhakāritakāyasaṃrambhaḥ mānakāritakāyasaṃrambhaḥ māyakāritakāyasaṃrambhaḥ lobhakāritakāyasaṃrambhaḥ krodhānumatakāyasaṃrambhaḥ mānānumatakāyasaṃrambhaḥ māyānumatakāyasaṃrambhaḥ lobhānumatakāysaṃrambhaś ceti dvādaśadhā kāyasaṃrambhaḥ. evaṃ vāgyoge manoyoge ca dvādaśadhā saṃrambhaḥ. ta ete saṃpiṇḍitāh ṣaṭtriṃśat, tathā samārambhā api ṣaṭtriṃśat, ārambhā api ṣaṭtriṃśat. ete saṃpiṇḍitā jīvādhikaraṇāsravabhedā aṣṭottaraśatasaṃkhyāḥ saṃbhavanti. ‘ca’ śabdo ’nantānubandyapratyākhyānapratyākhyānasaṃjvalanakaśāyabhedakṛtāntarbhedasamuccyārthaḥ. 
 § 625. parasyājīvādhikaraṇasya bhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 nirvartanānikṣepasaṃyoganisargā dvicaturdvitribhedāḥ param || 
 § 626. nirvartyata iti nirvartanā niṣpādanā. nikṣipyata iti nikṣepaḥ sthāpanā. saṃyujyate iti saṃyogo miśrīkṛtam. nisṛjyata iti nisargaḥ pravartanam. ete dvyādibhir yathākramam abhisaṃbadhyante — nirvartanā dvibhedā nikṣepaś caturbhedaḥ saṃyogo dvibhedaḥ nisargas tribheda iti. ta ete bhedā ajīvādhikaraṇasya veditavyāḥ. paravacanam anarthakam, pūrvasūtre ādyam iti vacanād idam avaśiṣṭārthaṃ bhavatīti. nānarthakam. anyārthaḥ paraśabdaḥ. saṃrambhādibhyo ’nyāni nirvarttanādīni. *  itarathā hi nirvartanādīnām ātmapariṇāmasadbhāvāj jīvādhikaraṇavikalpā eveti vijñāyeta. nirvatanādhikaraṇaṃ dvividhaṃ mūlaguṇanirvatanādhikaraṇam uttraraguṇanirvatanādhikaraṇaṃ ceti. tatra mūlaguṇanirvatanaṃ pañcavidham, śarīravāṅmanaḥprāṇāpānāś ca. uttraraguṇanirvartanaṃ kāṣṭhapustacitrakarmādi. nikṣepaś caturvidhaḥ apratyavekṣitanikṣepādhikaraṇaṃ duḥpramṛṣṭanikṣepādhikaraṇaṃ sahasānikṣepādhikaraṇam anābhoganikṣepādhikaraṇaṃ ceti. nisargas trividhaḥ — kāyanisargādhikaraṇaṃ vāgnisargādhikaraṇaṃ manonisargādhikaraṇaṃ ceti. 
 § 627. uktaḥ sāmānyena karmāsravabhedaḥ. idānīṃ karmaviśeṣāsravabhedo vaktavyaḥ. tasmin vaktavye ādyayor jñānadarśanāvaraṇayor āsravabhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 tatpradoṣanihnavamātsaryāntarāyāsādanopaghātā jñānadarśanāvaraṇayoḥ || 
 § 628. tattvajñanasya mokṣasādhanasya kīrtane kṛte kasyācid anabhivyāharataḥ antaḥpaiśunyapariṇāmaḥ pradoṣaḥ. kutaś citkāraṇān nāsti na vedmīty ādi jñānasya vyapalapanaṃ nihnavaḥ. kutaścit kāraṇād bhāvitam api vijñanaṃ dānārham api yato na dīyate tan mātsaryam. jñānavyavacchedakaraṇam antarāyaḥ. kāyena vācā ca paraprakāśyajñānasya varjanam āsādanam. praśastajñānadūṣaṇam upaghātaḥ. āsādanam eveti cet? sato jñānasya vinayapradānādiguṇakīrtanānuṣṭhānam āsādanam. upaghātas tu jñānam ajñānam eveti jñānanāśābhiprāyaḥ. iti anayor ayaṃ bhedaḥ. ‘’tat’ śabdena jñānadarśanayoḥ pratinirderśaḥ kriyate. kathaṃ punar aprakṛtayor anirdiṣṭayos tac chabdena parāmarśaḥ kartuṃ śakyaḥ? praśnāpekṣayā. jñānadarśanāvaraṇayoḥ ka āsrava iti praśne kṛte tadapekṣayā tac chabdo jñānadarśane pratinirdiśati. etena jñānadarśanavatsu tatsādhaneṣu ca pradoṣādayo yojyāḥ; tannimittatvāt. ta ete jñānadarśanāvaraṇayor āsravahetavaḥ. ekakāraṇasādhyasya kāryasyānekasya darśanāt tulye ’pi pradoṣādau jñānarśanāvaraṇāsravasiddhiḥ. *  athavā viṣayabhedād āsravabhedaḥ. jñānaviṣayāḥ pradoṣādayo jñānāvaraṇasya. darśanaviṣayāḥ pradoṣādayo darśanāvaraṇasyeti. 
 § 629. yathānayoḥ karmaprakṛtyor āsravabhedās tathā — 
 duḥkhaśokatāpākrandanavadhaparidevanāny ātmaparobhayasthāny asadvedyasya || 
 § 630. pīḍālakṣaṇaḥ pariṇāmo duḥkham. anugrāhakasaṃbandhavicchede vaiklavyaviśeṣaḥ śokaḥ. parivādādinimittād āvilāntaḥkaraṇasya tīvrānuśayas tāpaḥ. paritāpajātāśrupātapracuravipralāpādibhir vyaktakrandanam ākrandanam. āyurindriyabalaprāṇaviyogakaraṇaṃ vadhaḥ. saṃkleśapariṇāmāvalambanaṃ guṇasmaraṇānukīrtanapūrvakaṃ svaparānugrahābhilāṣaviṣayam anukampāpracuraṃ rodanaṃ paridevanam. nanu ca śokādīnāṃ duḥkhaviśeṣatvād duḥkhagrahaṇam evāstu? satyam evam; tathāpi katipayaviśeṣapratipādanena duḥkhajātyanuvidhānaṃ kriyate. yathā gaur ity ukte anirjñāte viśeṣe tatpratipādanārthaṃ khaṇḍamuṇḍakṛṣṇaśuklādyupādānaṃ kriyate tathā duḥkhaviṣayāsrvāsaṃkhyeyalokabhedasaṃbhavād duḥkham ity ukte viśeṣānirjñānāt katipayaviśeṣanirdeśena tadviśeṣapratipattiḥ kriyate. tāny etāni duḥkhādīni krodhādyāveśād ātmasthāni bhavanti parasthāny ubhayasthāni ca. etāni sarvāṇy asadvedyāsravakāraṇāni veditavyāni. atra codyate — yadi duḥkhādīny ātmaparobhayasthāny asadvedyāsravanimittāni, kim artham ārhataiḥ keśaluñcanānaśanātapasthānādīni duḥkhanimittāny āsthīyante pareṣu ca pratipādyante iti? naiṣa doṣaḥ — antarańgakrodhādyāveśapūrvakāṇi duḥkhādīny asadvedyāsravanimittānīti viśeṣyoktatvāt. yathā kasyacid bhiṣajaḥ paramakaruṇāśasya niḥśalyasya saṃyatasyopari gaṇḍaṃ pāṭayato duḥkhahetutve saty api na pāpabandho bāhyanimittamātrād eva bhavati. evaṃ saṃsāraviṣayamahāduḥkhād udvignasya bhikṣos tannivṛttyupāyaṃ prati samāhitamanaskasya śāstravihite karmaṇi pravartamānasya saṃkleśapariṇāmābhāvād duḥkhanimittatve saty api na pāpabandhaḥ. uktaṃ ca — 
 na duḥkhaṃ na sukhaṃ yadvad dhetur dṛṣṭaś cikitsite |
	  cikitsāyāṃ tu yuktasya syād duḥkham athavā sukham ||
	  na duḥkhaṃ na sukhaṃ tadvad dhetur mokṣasya sādhane |
	  mokṣopāye tu yuktasya syād duḥkham athavā sukham || 
 § 631. uktā asadvedyāsravahetavaḥ. sadvedyasya punaḥ ke ity atrocyate — 
 bhūtavratyanukampādānasarāgasaṃyamādiyogaḥ kṣāntiḥ śaucam iti sadvedyasya || 
 § 632. tāsu tāsu gatiṣu karmodayavaśād bhavantīti bhūtāni prāṇina ity arthaḥ. vratāny ahiṃsādīni vakṣyante, tadvanto vratinaḥ. te dvividhāḥ. āgāraṃ prati nivṛttautsukyāḥ. saṃyatāḥ gṛhiṇaś ca saṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ. anugrahārdrīkṛtacetasaḥ parapīḍām ātmasthām iva kurvato ’nukampanam anukampā. bhūteṣu vratiṣu cānukampā bhūtavratyanukampā. parānugrahabuddhyā svasyātisarjanaṃ dānam. saṃsārakāraṇavinivṛttiṃ pratyāgūrṇo ’kṣīṇāśayaḥ sarāga ity ucyate. prāṇīnidriyeṣv aśubhapravṛtter viratiḥ saṃyamaḥ. sarāgasya saṃyama sarāgo vā saṃyamaḥ sarāgasaṃyamaḥ. *  ‘ādi’-śabdena saṃyamāsaṃyamākāmanirjarābālatapo ’nurodhaḥ. yogaḥ samādhiḥ samyakpraṇidhānam ity arthaḥ. bhūtavratyanukampādānasarāgasaṃyamādīnāṃ yogo bhūtavratyanukampādānasarāgasaṃyamādiyogaḥ. krodhādinivṛttiḥ kṣāntiḥ. lobhaprakārāṇām uparamaḥ śaucam. ‘iti’ śabdaḥ prakārārthaḥ. ke te punas te prakārāḥ. arhatpūjākaraṇatatparatābālavṛddhatapasvivaiyāvṛttyādayaḥ. ‘bhūta’ grahaṇāt siddhe ‘vrati’ grahaṇaṃ tadviṣayānukampāprādhānyakhyāpanārtham. ta ete sadvedyasyāsravā jñeyāḥ. 
 § 633. atha tadantaroddeśabhājo mohasyāsravahetau vaktavye tadbhedasya darśanamohasyāsravahetupratipādanārtham idam ucyate — 
 kevaliśrutasaṃghadharmadevāvarṇavādo darśanamohasya || 
 § 634. nirāvaraṇajñānāḥ kevalinaḥ. tadupadiṣṭaṃ buddhyatiśayarddhiyuktagaṇadharānusmṛtaṃ grantharacanaṃ śrutaṃ bhavati. ratnatrayopetaḥ śramaṇagaṇaḥ saṃghaḥ. ahiṃsālakṣaṇas tadāgamadeśito dharmaḥ. devāś caturṇikāya uktāḥ. guṇavatsu mahatsu asadbhūtadoṣodbhāvanam avarṇavādaḥ. eteṣv avarṇavādo darśanamohasyāsravahetuḥ. kavalābhyavahārajīvinaḥ kevalina ity evam ādi vacanaṃ kevalinām avarṇavādaḥ. māṃsabhakṣaṇādyanavadyābhidhānaṃ śrutāvarṇavādaḥ. śūdratvāśucitvādyāvirbhāvanaṃ saṃghāvarṇavādaḥ. jinopadiṣṭo dharmo nirguṇas tadupasevino ye te cāsurā bhaviṣyantīty evam ādy abhidhānaṃ dharmāvarṇavādaḥ. surāmāṃsopasevādyāghoṣaṇaṃ devāvarṇavādaḥ. 
 § 635. dvitīyasya mohasyāsravabhedapratipādanārtham āha — 
 kaṣāyodayāt tīvrapariṇāmaś cāritramohasya || 
 § 636. kaṣāyā uktāḥ. udayo vipākaḥ. kaṣāyāṇām udayāt tīvrapariṇāmaś cāritramohasyāsravo veditavyaḥ. tatra svaparakaṣāyotpādanaṃ tapasvijanavṛttadūṣaṇaṃ saṃkliṣṭaliṅgavratadhāraṇādiḥ kaṣāyavedanīyasyāsravaḥ. saddharmopahasanadīnātihāsakandarpopahāsabahuvipralāpopahāsaśīlatādir hāsyavedanīyasya. vicitrakrīḍanaparatāvrataśīlārucyādiḥ rativedanīyasya. parāratiprādurbhāvanarativināśanapāpāśīlasaṃsargādiḥ arativedanīyasya. svaśokotpādanaparaśokaplutābhinandanādiḥ śokavedanīyasya. svabhayapariṇāmaparabhayotpādanādir bhayavedanīyasya. kuśalakriyācārajugupsāparivādaśīlatvādir jugupsāvedanīyasya. alīkābhidhāyitātisaṃdhānaparatvapararandhraprekṣitvapravṛddharāgādiḥ strīvedanīyasya. stokakrodhānutsukatvasvadārasaṃtoṣādiḥ puṃvedanīyasya. pracurakaṣāyāguhyendriyavyaparopaṇaparāṅganāvaskandādir napuṃsakavedanīyasya. 
 § 637. nirdiṣṭo mohanīyasyāsravabhedaḥ. idānīṃ tadanantaranirdiṣṭasyāyuṣa āsravahetau vaktavye ādyasya niyatakālaparipākasyāyuṣaḥ kāraṇapradarśanārtham idam ucyate — 
 bahvārambhaparigrahatvaṃ nārakasyāyuṣaḥ || 
 § 638. ārambhaḥ prāṇipīḍāhetur vyāpāraḥ. mamedaṃ buddhilakṣaṇaḥ parigrahaḥ. ārambhāś ca parigrahāś ca ārambhaparigrahāḥ. bahava ārambhaparigrahā yasya sa bahvārambhaparigrahaḥ. tasya bhāvo bahvārambhaparigrahatvam. hiṃsādikrūrakarmājasrapravartanaparasvaharaṇaviṣayātigṛddhikṛṣṇaleśyābhijātaraudradhyānamaraṇakālatādilakṣaṇo nārakasyāyuṣa āsravo bhavati. 
 § 639. āha, ukto nārakasyāyuṣa āsravaḥ. tairyagyonasyedānīṃ vaktavya ity atrocyate — 
 māyā tairyagyonasya || 
 § 640. cāritramohakarmaviśeṣasyodayād āvirbhūta ātmanaḥ kuṭilabhāvo māyā nikṛtiḥ tairyagyonasyāyuṣa āsravo veditavyaḥ. tatprapañco mithyātvopetadharmadeśanā niḥśīlatātisaṃdhānapriyatā nīlakāpotaleśyārtadhyānamaraṇakālatādiḥ. 
 § 641. āha, vyākhyātas tairyagyonasyāyuṣa āsravaḥ. idānīṃ mānuṣasyāyuṣuḥ ko hetur ity atrocyate — 
 alpārambhaparigrahatvaṃ mānuṣasya || 
 § 642. nārakāyur āsravo vyākhyātaḥ. tadviparīto mānuṣasyāyuṣa iti saṃkṣepaḥ. tadvyāsaḥ — vinītasvabhāvaḥ prakṛtibhadratā praguṇavyavahāratā tanukaṣāyatvaṃ maraṇakālāsaṃkleśatādiḥ. 
 § 643. kim etāvān eva mānuṣasyāyuṣa āsrava ity atrocyate — 
 svabhāvamārdavaṃ ca || 
 § 644. mṛdor bhāvo mārdavam. svabhāvena mārdavaṃ svabhāvamārdavaṃ. upadeśānapekṣam ity arthaḥ. etad api mānuṣasyāyuṣa āsravaḥ. pṛthagyogakaraṇaṃ kim artham? uttarārtham, devāyuṣa āsravo ’yam api yathā syāt. 
 § 645. kim etad eva dvitīyaṃ mānuṣasyāsravaḥ? na; ity ucyate — 
 niśśīlavratatvaṃ ca sarveṣām || 
 § 646. ‘ca’ śabdo ’dhikṛtasamucyayārthaḥ. *  alpārambhaparigrahatvaṃ ca niḥśīlavratatvaṃ ca. śīlāni ca vratāni ca śīlavratāni tāni vakṣyate. niṣkrāntaḥ śīlavratebhyo niḥśīlavrataḥ. tasya bhāvo niḥśīlavratatvam. ‘sarveṣāṃ’ grahaṇaṃ sakalāyurāsravapratipattyartham. kiṃ devāyuṣo ’pi bhavati? satyam, bhavati bhogabhūmijāpekṣayā. 
 § 647. atha caturthasyāyuṣaḥ ka āsrava ity atrocyate — 
 sarāgasaṃyamasaṃyamāsaṃyamākāmanirjarābālatapāṃsi daivasya || 
 § 648. sarāgasaṃyamaḥ saṃyamāsaṃyamaś ca vyākhyātau. akāmanirjarā akāmaś cārakanirodhabandhanabaddheṣu kṣuttṛṣṇānirodhabrahmacaryabhūśayyāmaladhāraṇaparitāpādiḥ. akāmena nirjarā akāmanirjarā. bālatapo mithyādarśanopetam anupāyakāyakleśapracuraṃ nikṛtibahulavratadhāraṇam. tāny etani daivasyāyuṣa āsravahetavo veditavyāḥ. 
 § 649. kim etāvan eva daivasyāyuṣa āsravaḥ. nety āha — 
 samyaktvam ca || 
 § 650. kim? daivasyāyuṣa āsrava ity anuvartate. aviśeṣābhidhāne ’pi saudharmādiviśeṣagatiḥ. kutaḥ? pṛthakkaraṇāt. yady evam, pūrvasūtre, ukta āsravavidhir aviśeṣeṇa prasaktaḥ tena sarāgasaṃyamasaṃyamāsaṃyamāv api bhavanavāsyādyāyuṣa āsravau prāpnutaḥ. naiṣa doṣaḥ; samyaktvābhāve sati tadvyapadeśābhāvāt tadubhayam apy atrāntarbhavati. 
 § 651. āyuṣo ’nantaram uddiṣṭasya nāmna āsravavidhau vaktavye, tatrāśubhānāmna āsravapratipattyartham āha — 
 yogavakratā visaṃvādanaṃ cāśubhasya nāmnaḥ || 
 § 652. yogas triprakāro vyākhyātaḥ. tasya vakratā kauṭilyam. visaṃvādanam anyathāpravartanam. nanu ca nārthabhedaḥ. yogavakrataivānyathāpravartanam? satyam evam etat — svagatā yogavakratety ucyate. paragataṃ visaṃvādanam. samyagabhyudayaniḥśreyasārthāsu kriyāsu pravartamānam anyaṃ tadviparītakāyavāṅmanobhir visaṃvādayati maivaṃ kārṣīr evam kurvīti. etad ubhayam aśubhanāmakarmāsravakāraṇaṃ veditavyam. ‘ca’ śabdena mithyādarśanapaiśunyāsthiracittatākūṭamānatulākaraṇaparanindātmapraśaṃsādiḥ samuccīyate. 
 § 653. atha śubhanāmakarmaṇaḥ ka āsrava ity atra ucyate — 
 tadviparītaṃ śubhasya || 
 § 654. kāyavāṅmanasām ṛjutvam avisaṃvādanaṃ ca tadviparītam. ‘ca’ śabdena samuccitasya ca viparītaṃ grāhyam. dhārmikadarśanasaṃbhramasadbhāvopanayanasaṃsaraṇabhīrutāpramādavarjanādiḥ. tadetac chubhanāmakarmāsravakāraṇaṃ veditavyam. 
 § 655. āha kim etāvān eva śubhanāmna āsravavidhir uta kaścid asti prativiśeṣa ity atrocyate — yad idaṃ tīrthakaranāmakarmānantānupamaprabhāvam acintyavibhūtiviśeṣakāraṇaṃ trailokyavijayakaraṃ tasyāsravavidhiviśeṣo ’stīti. yady evam ucyatām ke tasyāsravaḥ. ity ata idam ārabhyate — 
 darśanaviśuddhir vinayasampannatā śīlavrateṣv anatīcāro ’bhīkṣṇajñānopayogasaṃvegau śaktitas tyāgatapasī sādhusamādhir vaiyāvṛttyakaraṇam arhadācāryabahuśrutapravacanabhaktir āvaśyakāparihāṇir mārgaprabhāvanā pravacanavatsalatvam iti tīrthakaratvasya || 
 § 656. jinena bhagavatārhatparameṣṭhinopadiṣṭe nirgranthalakṣaṇe mokṣavartmani rucir darśanaviśuddhiḥ prāguktalakṣaṇā. tasyā aṣṭāv aṅgāni niśśaṅkitatvaṃ niḥkāṅkṣitā vicikitsāvirahatā amūḍhadṛṣṭitā upabṛṃhaṇaṃ sthitīkaraṇaṃ vātsalyaṃ prabhāvanaṃ ceti. samyagjñānādiṣu mokṣamārgeṣu tatsādhaneṣu ca gurvādiṣu svayogyavṛttyā satkāra ādaro vinayas tena saṃpannatā vinayasaṃpannatā. ahiṃsādiṣu vrateṣu tatpratipālanārtheṣu ca krodhavarjanādiṣu śīleṣu niravadyā vṛttiḥ śīlavrateṣv anatīcāraḥ. jīvādipadārthasvatattvaviṣaye samyagjñāne nityaṃ yuktatā abhīkṣaṇajñānopayogaḥ. saṃsāraduḥkhān nityabhīrutā saṃvegaḥ. tyāgo dānam. tat trividham — āhāradānam abhayadānaṃ jñādānaṃ ceti. tacchaktito yathāvidhi prayujyamānaṃ tyāga ity ucyate. anigūhitavīryasya mārgāvirodhi kāyakleśas tapaḥ. yathā bhāṇḍāgāre dahane samutthite tatpraśamanam anuṣṭhīyate bahūpakāratvāt tathānekavrataśīlasamṛddhasya munes tapasaḥ kutaścit pratyūhe samupasthite tatsaṃdhāraṇaṃ samādhiḥ. guṇavadduḥkhopanipāte niravadyena vidhinā tadapaharaṇaṃ vaiyāvṛttyam. arhadācāryeṣu bahuśruteṣu pravacane ca bhāvaviśuddhiyukto ’nurāgo bhaktiḥ. ṣaṇṇām āvaśyakakriyāṇāṃ yathākālaṃ pravartanam āvaśyakāparihāṇiḥ. jñānatapodānajinapūjāvidhinā dharmaprakāśanaṃ mārgaprabhāvanā. vatse dhenuvatsadharmaṇi snehaḥ pravacanavatsalatvam. tāny etāni ṣodaṣakāraṇāni samyagbhāvyamānāni vyastāni ca tīrthakaranāmakarmāsrvakāraṇāni pratyetavyāni. 
 § 657. idānīṃ nāmāsravābhidhānānantaraṃ gotrāsrave vaktavye sati nīcairgotrasyāsravavidhānārtham idam āha — 
 parātmanindāpraśaṃse sadasatguṇocchādanodbhāvane ca nīcairgotrasya || 
 § 658. tathyasya vātathyasya vā doṣasyodbhāvanaṃ prati icchā nindā. guṇodbhāvanābhiprāyaḥ praśaṃsā. yathāsaṃkhyam abhisaṃbandhaḥ — paranindā ātmapraśaṃseti. pratibandhakahetusaṃnidhāne sati anudbhūtavṛttitā anāvirbhāva ucchādanam. pratibandhakābhāve prakāśavṛttitā udbhāvanam. atrāpi ca yathākramam abhisaṃbandhaḥ — sadguṇocchādanam asadguṇodbhāvanam iti. tāny etāni nīcairgotrasyāsravakāraṇāni veditavyāni. 
 § 659. athoccairgotrasya ka āsravavidhir atrocyate — 
 tadviparyayo nīcair vṛttyanutsekau cottarasya || 
 § 660. ‘tat’ ity anena pratyāsatter nīcairgotrasyāsravaḥ pratinirdiśyate. anyena prakāreṇa vṛttir viparyayaḥ. tasya viparyayas tadviparyayaḥ. kaḥ punar asau viparyayaḥ? ātmanindā, parapraśaṃsā, sadguṇodbhāvanam asadguṇocchādanaṃ ca. guṇotkṛṣṭeṣu vinayenāvanatir nīcair vṛttiḥ. vijñānādibhir utkṛṣṭasyāpi satas tatkṛtamadaviraho ’nahaṃkāratānutsekaḥ. tāny etāny uttarasyoccair gotrasyāsravakāraṇāni bhavanti. 
 § 661. atha gotrānantaram uddiṣṭasyāntarāyasya ka āsrava ity ucyate — 
 vighnakaraṇam antarāyasya || 
 § 662. dānādīny uktāni ‘dānalābhabhogopahogavīryāṇi ca’ ity atra. teṣāṃ vihananaṃ vighnaḥ. vighnasya karaṇaṃ vighnakaraṇam antarāyasyāsravavidhir veditavyaḥ. atra codyate — tatpradoṣanihnavādayo jñānadarśanāvaraṇādīnāṃ pratiniyatā āsravahetavo varṇitāḥ, kiṃ te pratiniyatajñānāvaraṇādyāsravahetava eva utāviśeṣeṇeti. yadi pratiniyatajñānāvaraṇādyāsravahetavaḥ eva, āgamavirodhaḥ prasajyate. āgame hi sapta karmāṇi āyurvarjyāni pratikṣaṇaṃ yugapad āsravantīty uktam. tadvirodhaḥ syāt. athāviśeṣeṇa āsravahetavo viśeṣanirdeśo na yukta iti? atrocyate — yady api tatpradoṣādibhir jñānāvaraṇādīnāṃ sarvāsāṃ karmaprakṛtīnāṃ pradeśabandhaniyamo nāsti, tathāpy anubhāganiyamahetutvena tatpradoṣanihnavādayo vibhājyante. 
 iti tattvārthavṛttau sarvārthasiddhisaṃjñikāyāṃ ṣaṣṭho ’dhyāyaḥ || 6 || 
 
 
	  atha saptamo ’dhyāyaḥ
	   §§ 663–728 
 § 663. āsravapadārtho vyākhyātaḥ. tatprārambhakāle evoktaṃ ‘śubhaḥ puṇyasya’ iti tatsāmānyenoktam. tadviśeṣapratipattyarthaṃ kaḥ punaḥ śubha ity ukte idam ucyate — 
 hiṃsānṛtasteyābrahmaparigrahebhyo viratir vratam || 
 § 664. ‘pramattayogāt prāṇavyaparopaṇaṃ hiṃsā’ ity evam ādibhiḥ sūtrair hiṃsādayo nirdekṣyante. tebhyo viramaṇaṃ viratir vratam ity ucyate. vratam abhisandhikṛto niyamaḥ, idaṃ kartavyam idaṃ na kartavyam iti vā. nanu ca hiṃsādayaḥ pariṇāmaviśeṣā adhruvāḥ, kathaṃ teṣām apādānatvam ucyate? buddhyapāye dhruvatvavivakṣopapatteḥ. yathā dharmād viramatīty atra ya eṣa manuṣyaḥ saṃbhinnabuddhiḥ sa paśyati — duṣkaro dharmaḥ, phalaṃ cāsya śraddhāmātragamyam iti sa buddhyā saṃprāpya nivartate. evam ihāpi ya eva manuṣyaḥ prekṣāpūrvakārī sa paśyati — ya ete hiṃsādayaḥ pariṇāmās te pāpahetavaḥ. pāpakarmaṇi pravartamānān janān ihaiva rājāno daṇḍayanti paratra ca duḥkham āpnuvantīti sa buddhyā saprāpya nivartate. tato buddhyā dhruvatvavivakṣopapatter apādānanatvaṃ yuktam. ‘virati’ śabdaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate hiṃsāyā viratiḥ anṛtād viratir ity evam ādi. tatra ahiṃsāvratam ādau kriyate pradhānatvāt. satyādīni hi tatparipālanārthāni sasyasya vṛtiparikṣepavat. sarvasāvadyanivṛttilakṣaṇasāmāyikāpekṣayā ekaṃ vrataṃ, tadeva chedopasthāpanāpekṣayā pañcavidham ihocyate. nanu ca asya vratasyāsravahetutvam anupapannaṃ saṃvarahetuṣv antarbhāvāt. saṃvarahetavo vakṣyante guptisamityādayaḥ. tatra daśavidhe dharme saṃyame vā vratānām antarbhāva iti? naiṣa doṣaḥ; tatra saṃvaro nivṛttilakṣaṇo vakṣyate. pravṛttiś cātra dṛśyate; hiṃsānṛtādattādānādiparityāge ahiṃsāsatyavacanadattādānādikriyāpratīteḥ guptyādisaṃvaraparikarmatvāc ca. vrateṣu hi kṛtaparikarmā sādhuḥ sukhena saṃvaraṃ karotīti tataḥ pṛthaktvenopadeśaḥ kriyate. nanu ca ṣaṣṭham aṇuvratam asti rātribhojanaviramaṇaṃ tadihopasaṃkhyātavyam? na; bhāvanāsv antarbhāvāt. ahiṃsāvratabhāvanā hi vakṣyante. tatra ālokitapānabhojanabhāvanā kāryeti. 
 § 665. tasya pañcatayasya vratasya bhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 deśasarvato ’ṇumahatī || 
 § 666. deśa ekadeśaḥ. sarvaḥ sakalaḥ. deśaś ca sarvaś ca deśasarvau tābhyaṃ deśasarvataḥ. ‘viratiḥ’ ity anuvartate. aṇu ca mahac cāṇumahatī. vratābhisaṃbandhān napuṃsakaliṅganirdeśaḥ. yathāsaṃkhyam abhisaṃbadhyate. deśato viratir aṇuvrataṃ sarvato viratir mahāvratam iti dvidhā bhidyate pratyekaṃ vratam. etāni vratāni bhāvitāni varauṣadhavadyatnavate duḥkhanivṛttinimittāni bhavanti. 
 § 667. kim arthaṃ kathaṃ vā bhāvanaṃ teṣām ity atrocyate — 
 tatsthairyārthaṃ bhāvanāḥ pañca pañca || 
 § 668. teṣāṃ vratānāṃ sthirīkaraṇāyaikaikasya vratasya pañca pañca bhāvanā veditavyāḥ. yady evam ādyasyāhiṃsāvratasya bhāvanāḥ kā ity atrocyate — 
 vāńmanoguptīryādānanikṣepaṇasamityālokitapānabhojanāni pañca || 
 § 669. vāgguptīḥ manoguptīḥ īryāsamitiḥ ādānānanikṣepaṇasamitiḥ ālokitapānabhojanam ity etāḥ pañcāhiṃsāvratasya bhāvanāḥ. 
 § 670. atha dvitīyasya vratasya kā ity atrocyate — 
 krodhalobhabhīrutvahāsyapratyākhyānāny anuvīcībhāṣaṇaṃ ca pañca || 
 § 671. krodhapratyākhyānaṃ lobhapratyākhyānaṃ bhīrutvapratyākhyānaṃ hāsyapratyākhyānam anivīcībhāṣaṇaṃ cety etāḥ pañca bhāvanā satyavratasya jñeyāḥ. anuvīcībhāṣaṇaṃ niravadyānubhāṣaṇam ity arthaḥ. 
 § 672. idānīṃ tṛtīyasya vratasya kā bhāvanā ity atrāha — 
 śūnyāgāravimocitāvāsaparoparodhākaraṇabhaikṣaśuddhisadharmāvisaṃvādāḥ pañca || 
 § 673. śūnyāgāreṣu giriguhātarukoṭarādiṣv āvāsaḥ. parakīyeṣu ca vimociteṣv āvāsaḥ. pareṣām uparodhākaraṇam. ācāraśāstramārgeṇa bhaikṣaśuddhiḥ. mamedaṃ tavedam iti sadharmabhir avisaṃvādaḥ. ity etāḥ pañcādattādānaviramaṇavratasya bhāvanāḥ. 
 § 674. athedānīṃ brahmacaryavratasya bhāvanā vaktavyā ity atrāha — 
 strīrāgakathāśravaṇatanmanoharāṅganirīkṣaṇapūrvaratānusmaraṇavṛṣyeṣṭarasasvaśarīrasaṃskāratyāgāḥ pañca || 
 § 675. tyāgaśabdaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate. strīrāgakathāśravaṇatyāgaḥ tanmanoharāṅganirīkṣaṇatyāgaḥ pūrvaratānusmaraṇatyāgaḥ vṛṣyeṣṭarasatyāgaḥ svaśarīrasaṃskāratyāgaś ceti caturthavratasya bhāvanāḥ pañca vijñeyāḥ. 
 § 676. atha pañcamavratasya bhāvanā kā ity atrocyate — 
 manojñāmanojñendriyaviṣayarāgadveṣavarjanāni pañca || 
 § 677. pañcānām indriyāṇāṃ sparśanādīnām iṣṭāniṣṭeṣu viṣayeṣūpanipatiteṣu sparśādīṣu rāgavarjanāni pañca ākiṃcanyasya vratasya bhāvanāḥ pratyetavyāḥ. 
 § 678. kiṃcānyadyathāmīṣāṃ vratānāṃ draḍhimārthaṃ bhāvanāḥ pratīyante tadvipaścidbhir iti bhāvanopadeśaḥ, tathā tadarthaṃ tadvirodhiṣv apīty āha — 
 hiṃsādiṣv ihāmutrāpāyāvadyadarśanam || 
 § 679. abhyudayaniḥśreyasārthānāṃ kriyāṇāṃ vināśakaḥ prayogo ’pāyaḥ. avadyaṃ garhyam. apāyaś cāvadyaṃ cāpāyāvadye tayor darśanam apāyāvadyadarśanaṃ bhāvayitavyam. kva? ihāmutra ca. keṣu? hiṃsādiṣu. katham iti ced ucyate — hiṃsāyāṃ tāvat, hiṃsro hi nityodvejanīyaḥ satatānubaddhavairaś ca iha ca vadhabandhaparikleśādīn pratilabhate pretya cāśubhāṃ gatiṃ garhitaś ca bhavatīti hiṃsāyā vyuparamaḥ śreyān. tāthā anṛtavādī aśraddheyo bhavati ihaiva ca jihvācchedādīn pratilabhate mithyābhyākhānaduḥkhitebhyaś ca baddhavairebhyo bahūni vyasanāny avāpnoti pretya cāśubhāṃ gatiṃ garhitaś ca bhavatīti anṛtavacanād uparamaḥ śreyān. tathā stenaḥ paradravyāharaṇāsaktaḥ sarvasyodvejanīyo bhavati. ihaiva cābhighātavadhabandhahastapādakarṇanāsottarauṣṭhachedanabhedanasarvasvaharaṇādīn pratilabhate pretya cāśubhāṃ gatiṃ garhitaś ca bhavatīti steyād vyuparatiḥ śreyasī. tathā abrahmacarī madavibhramodbhrāntacitto vanagaja iva vāsitāvañcito vivaśo vadhabandhanaparikleśān anubhavati mohābhibhūtatvāc ca kāryākāryānabhijño na kiṃcit kuśalam ācarati parāṅganāliṅganasaṅgakṛtaratiś cehaiva vairānubandhano liṃgacchedanavadhabandhasarvasvaharaṇādīn apāyān prāpnoti pretya cāśubhāṃ gatim aśnute garhitaś ca bhavati ato viratir ātmahitā. tathā parigrahavān śakunir iva gṛhītamāṃsakhaṇḍo ’nyeṣāṃ tadarthināṃ patattriṇām ihaiva taskarādīnām abhibhavanīyo bhavati tadarjanarakṣaṇaprakṣayakṛtāṃś ca doṣān bahūn avāpnoti na cāsya tṛptir bhavati indhanair ivāgneḥ lobhābhibhūtatvāc ca kāryākāryānapekṣo bhavati pretya cāśubhāṃ gatim āskandate lubhdo ’yam iti garhitaś ca bhavatīti tadviramaṇaṃ śreyaḥ. evaṃ hiṃsādiṣv apāyāvadyadarśanaṃ bhāvanīyam. 
 § 680. hiṃsādiṣu bhāvanāntarapratipādanārtham āha — 
 duḥkham eva vā || 
 § 681. hiṃsādayo duḥkham eveti bhāvayitavyāḥ. kathaṃ hiṃsādayo duḥkham? duḥkhakāraṇatvāt. yathā  annaṃ vai prāṇāḥ  iti. kāraṇasya kāranatvād vā. yathā  dhanaṃ prāṇāḥ  iti. dhanakāraṇam annapānakāraṇāḥ prāṇā iti. tathā hiṃsādayo ’sadvedyakarmakāraṇam. asadvedyakarma ca duḥkhakāraṇam iti duḥkhakāraṇe duḥkhakāraṇakāraṇe vā duḥkhopacāraḥ. tadete duḥkham eveti bhāvanaṃ parātmasākṣikam avagantavyam. nanu ca tatsarvaṃ na duḥkham eva; viṣayaratisukhasadbhāvāt? na tatsukham; vedanāpratīkāratvāt kacchūkaṇḍūyanavat. 
 § 682. punar api bhāvanāntaram āha — 
 maitrīpramodakāruṇyamādhyasthyāni ca sattvaguṇādhikakliśyamānāvineyeṣu || 
 § 683. pareṣāṃ duḥkhānutpattyabhilāṣo maitrī. vadanaprasādādibhir abhivyajyamānāntarbhavitarāgaḥ pramodaḥ. dīnānugrahabhāvaḥ kāruṇyam. rāgadveṣapūrvakapakṣapātābhāvo mādhyasthyam. duṣkarmavipākavaśān nānāyoniṣu sīdantīti sattvā jīvāḥ. samyagjñānādibhiḥ prakṛṣṭā guṇādhikāḥ. asadvedyodayāpāditakleśāḥ kliśyamānāḥ. tattvārthaśravaṇagrahaṇābhyām asaṃpāditaguṇā avineyāḥ. eteṣu sattvādiṣu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ maitryādīni bhāvayitavyāni. sarvasattveṣu maitrī, guṇādikeṣu pramodaḥ, kliśyamāneṣu kāruṇyam, avineyeṣu mādhyasthyam iti. evaṃ bhāvayataḥ pūrṇāny ahiṃsādīni vratāni bhavanti. 
 § 684. punar api bhāvanāntaram āha — 
 jagatkāyasvabhāvau vā saṃvegavairāgyārtham || 
 § 685. jagatsvabhāvas tāvad anādir anidhano vetrāsanajhallarīmṛdaṃganibhaḥ. atra jīvā anādisaṃsāre ’nantakālaṃ nānāyoniṣu duḥkhaṃ bhojaṃ bhojaṃ paryaṭanti. na cātra kiṃcin niyatam asti. jalabudbudopamaṃ jīvitam, vidyunmeghādivikāracapalā bhogasaṃpada iti. evam ādi jagatsvabhāvacintanāt saṃsārāt saṃvego bhavati. kāyasvabhāvaś ca anityatā duḥkhahetutva niḥsāratā aśucitvam iti. *  evam ādi kāyasvabhāvacintanād viṣayarāganivṛtter vairāgyam upajāyate. iti jagatkāyasvabhāvau bhāvayitavyau. 
 § 686. atrāha; uktaṃ bhavatā hiṃsādinivṛttivratam iti, tatra na jānīmaḥ ke hiṃsādayaḥ kriyāviśeṣā ity atrocyate. yugapad vaktum aśakyatvāt tallakṣaṇanirdeśasya kramaprasaṃge yāsāv ādau coditā saiva tāvad ucyate — 
 pramattayogāt prāṇavyaparopaṇaṃ hiṃsā || 
 § 687. pramādaḥ sakaṣāyatvaṃ tadvānātmapariṇāmaḥ pramattaḥ. pramattasya yogaḥ pramattayogaḥ, tasmāt pramattayogāt indriyādayo daśaprāṇās teṣāṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vyaparopaṇaṃ viyogakaraṇaṃ hiṃsety abhidhīyate. sā prāṇino duḥkhahetutvād adharmahetuḥ. ‘pramattayogāt’ iti viśeṣaṇaṃ kevalaṃ prāṇavyaparopaṇaṃ nādharmāyeti jñāpanārtham. uktaṃ ca —
	   viyojayati cāśubhir na ca vadhena saṃyujyate ||  iti ||
	  uktaṃ ca —
	   uccālidamhi pāde iriyāsamidassa ṇiggamaṭṭhāṇe | 
 āvāde [dhe] jja kuliṃgo marejja tajjogamāsejja || 
 ṇa hi tassa taṇṇimitto baṃdho suhumo vi desido samae | 
 mucchāpariggaho tti ya ajjhappapamāṇado bhaṇido || 
	  nanu ca prāṇavyaparopaṇābhāve ’pi pramattayogamātrād eva hiṃseṣyate. uktaṃ ca —
	   maradu va jiyadu va jīvo ayadācārassa ṇicchidā hiṃsā | 
 payadassa ṇatthi baṃdho hiṃsāmitteṇa samidassa || 
	  naiṣa doṣaḥ. atrāpi prāṇavyaparopaṇam asti bhāvalakṣaṇam. tathā coktam —
	   svayam evātmanātmānaṃ hinasty ātmā pramādavān | 
 pūrvaṃ prāṇyantarāṇāṃ tu paścāt syād vā na vā vadhaḥ || 
 § 688. āha abhihitalakṣaṇā hiṃsā. tadanantaroddiṣṭam anṛtaṃ kiṃ lakṣaṇam ity atrocyate — 
 asadabhidhānam anṛtam || 
 § 689. sacchandaḥ praśaṃsāvācī. sadasadapraśastam iti yāvat. asato ’rthasyābhidhānam asadabhidānam anṛtam. ṛtaṃ satyaṃ, na ṛtam anṛtam. kiṃ punar apraśastam? prāṇipīḍākaraṃ yat tad apraśastaṃ vidyamānārthaviṣayaṃ vā avidyamānārthaviṣayaṃ vā. uktaṃ ca prāgevāhiṃsāvrataparipālanārtham itaradvratam iti. tasmād dhiṃsākaraṃ vaco ’nṛtam iti niśceyam. 
 § 690. athānṛtānantaram uddiṣṭaṃ yat steyaṃ tasya kiṃ lakṣaṇam ity ata āha — 
 adattādānaṃ steyam || 
 § 691. ādānaṃ grahaṇam adattasyādānam adattādānaṃ steyam ity ucyate. yady evaṃ karmanokarmagrahaṇam api steyaṃ prāpnoti; anyenādattatvāt? naiṣa doṣaḥ, dānādāne yatra saṃbhavatas tatraiva steyavyavahāraḥ. kutaḥ. ‘adatta’ grahaṇasāmarthyāt. evam api bhikṣor grāmanagarādiṣu bhramaṇakāle rathyādvārādipraveśād adattādānaṃ prāpnoti? naiṣa doṣaḥ; sāmānyena muktatvāt. tathā hi — ayaṃ bhikṣuḥ pihitadvārādiṣu na praviśati amuktatvāt. athavā ‘pramattayogāt’ ity anuvartate. pramattayogād adattādānaṃ yat tat steyam ity ucyate. na ca rathyādi praviśataḥ pramattayogo ’sti. tenaitad uktaṃ bhavati, yatra saṃkleśapariṇāmena pravṛttis tatra steyaṃ bhavati bāhyvastuno grahaṇe cāgrahaṇe ca. 
 § 692. atha caturtham abrahma kiṃ lakṣaṇam ity atrocyate — 
 maithunām abrahma || 
 § 693. strīpuṃsayoś cāritramohodaye sati rāgapariṇāmāviṣṭayoḥ parasparasparśanaṃ prati icchā mithunam. mithunasya karma maithunam ity ucyate. na sarvaṃ karma. kutaḥ? loke śāstre ca tathā prasiddeḥ. loke tāvad āgopālādiprasiddhaṃ strīpuṃsayoḥ rāgapariṇāmanimittaṃ ceṣṭitaṃ maithunam iti. śāstre ’pi  aśvavṛṣabhayor maithuneccchāyām  ity evam ādiṣu tad eva gṛhyate. api ca ‘pramattayogāt’ ity anuvartate tena strīpuṃsamithunaviṣayaṃ ratisukhārtaṃ ceṣṭitaṃ maithunam iti gṛhyate, na sarvam. ahiṃsādayo guṇā yasmin paripālyamāne bṛṃhanti vṛddhim upayānti tad brahma. na brahma abrahma iti. kiṃ tat? maithunam. tatra hiṃsādayo doṣāḥ puṣyanti. yasmān maithunasevanapravaṇaḥ sthāsnūṃś cariṣṇūn prāṇino hinasti mṛṣāvādam ācaṣṭe adattam ādatte acetanam itaraṃ ca parigṛahaṃ gṛhṇāti. 
 § 694. atha pañcamasya parigrahasya kiṃ lakṣaṇam ity ata āha — 
 mūrcchā parigrahaḥ || 
 § 695. mūrcchety ucyate. kā mūrcchā? bahyānāṃ gomahiṣamaṇimuktāphalādīnāṃ cetanācetanānām ābyantarāṇāṃ ca rāgādīnām upadhīnām saṃrakṣaṇārjanasaṃskārādilakṣaṇāvyāvṛttir mūrcchā. nanu ca loke vātādiprakopaviśeṣasya mūrccheti prasiddhir asti tadgrahaṇaṃ kasmān na bhavati? satyam evam etat mūrcchir ayaṃ mohasāmānye vartate.  sāmānyacodanāś ca viśeṣeṣv avatiṣṭhante  ity ukte viśeṣe vyavasthitaḥ parigṛhyate; parigrahaprakaraṇāt. evam api bāhyasya parigrahatvaṃ na prāpnoti; ādhyātmikasya saṃgrahāt? satyam evam etat; pradhānatvād abhyantara eva saṃgṛhītaḥ. asaty api bāhye mamedam iti saṃkalpabān saparigraha eva bhavati. *  atha bāhyaḥ parigraho na bhavaty eva, bhavati ca mūrcchākāraṇatvāt yadi mamedam iti saṃkalpaḥ parigrahaḥ; saṃjñānādy api parigrahaḥ prāpnoti, tad api hi mamedam iti saṃkalpyate rāgādipariṇāmavat? naiṣa doṣaḥ; ‘pramattayogāt’ ity anuvartate. tato jñānadarśanacāritravato ’pramattasya mohābhāvān na mūrcchāstīti niṣparigarahatvaṃ siddham. kiṃ ca teṣāṃ jñanādīnām aheyatvād ātmasvabhāvatvād aparigrahatvam. rāgādayaḥ punaḥ karmodayatantrā iti anātmasvabhāvatvād dheyāḥ. tatas teṣụ saṃkalpaḥ parigraha iti yujyate. tanmulāḥ sarve doṣāḥ. mamedam iti hi sati saṃkalpe saṃrakṣanādayaḥ saṃjāyante. tatra ca hiṃsāvaśyaṃ bhāvinī. tadartham anṛtaṃ jalpati. cauryaṃ vā ācarati. maithune ca karmaṇi prayatate. tatprabhavā narakādiṣu duḥkhaprakārāḥ. 
 § 696. evam uktena prakāreṇa hiṃsādidoṣadarśino ’hiṃsādiguṇāhitacetasaḥ paramaprayatnasyā hiṃsādīni vratāni yasya santi saḥ — 
 niśśalyo vratī || 
 § 697. śṛṇāti hinastīti śalyam. śarīrānupraveśi kāṇḍādipraharaṇaṃ śalyam iva śalyaṃ, yathā tat prāṇino bādhākaraṃ tathā śārīramānasabādhāhetutvāt karmodayavikāraḥ śalyam ity upacaryate. tat trividham — māyāśalyaṃ nidānaśalyaṃ mithyādarśanaśalyam iti. māyā nikṛtir vañcanā. nidānaṃ viṣayabhogākāṅkṣā. mithyādarśanam atatvaśraddhānam. etasmāt trividhāc chalyān niṣkrānto niśśalyo vratī ity ucyate. atra codyate — śalyābhāvān niḥśalyo vratābhisaṃbandhād vratī, na niśśalyatvād vratī bhavitum arhati. na hi devadatto daṇḍasaṃbandhāc chatrī bhavatīti. attrocyate — ubhayaviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭasyeṣṭatvāt. na hiṃsādyuparatimātravratābhisaṃbandhād vratī bhavaty antareṇa śalyābhāvam. sati śalyāpagame vratasaṃbandhād vratī vivakṣito yathā bahukṣīraghṛto gomān iti vyapadiśyate. bahukṣīraghṛtābhāvāt satīṣv api goṣu na gomāṃs tathā saśalyatvāt satsv api vrateṣu na vratī. yas tu niḥśalyaḥ sa vratī. 
 § 698. tasya bhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 agāry anagāraś ca || 
 § 699. pratiśrayārthibhiḥ aṃgyate iti agāraṃ veśma, tad vānagārī. na vidyate agāramasyety anagāraḥ. dvividho vratī agārī anagāraś ca. nanu cātra viparyayo ’pi prāpnoti śūnyāgāradevakulādyāvāsasya muner agāritvam anivṛttaviṣayatṛṣṇasya kutaścit kāraṇād gṛhaṃ vimucya vane vasato ’nagāratvaṃ ca prāpnotīti? naiṣa doṣaḥ; bhāvāgārasya vivakṣitatvāt. cāritramohodaye saty agārasaṃbandhaṃ pratyanivṛttaḥ pariṇāmo bhāvāgāram ity ucyate. sa yasyāsty asāv agārī vane vasann api. gṛhe vasann api tadabhāvād anagāra iti ca bhavati. nanu cāgāriṇo vratitvaṃ na prāpnoti; asakalavratatvāt? naiṣa doṣaḥ; naigamādinayāpekṣayā agāriṇo ’pi vratitvam upapadyate nagarāvāsavat. yathā gṛhe apavarake vā vasann api nagarāvāsa ity ucyeta tathā asakalavrato ’pi naigamasaṃgrahavyavahāranayāpekṣayā vratīti vyapadiśyate. 
 § 700. atrāha kiṃ hiṃsādīnām anyatam asmād yaḥ pratinivṛttaḥ sa khalv agārī vratī? naivam. kiṃ tarhi? paṃcatayyā api virater vaikalyena vivakṣita ity ucyate — 
 aṇuvrato ’gārī || 
 § 701. ‘aṇu’ śabdo ’lpavacanaḥ. aṇūni vratāny asya aṇuvrato ’gārīty ucyate. katham asya vratānām aṇuvratam? sarvasāvadyanivṛttyasaṃbhavāt. kutas tarhy asau nivṛttaḥ? trasaprāṇivyaparopaṇān nivrattaḥ agārīty ādyam aṇuvratam. snehamohādivaśād gṛhavināśe grāmavināśe vā kāraṇam ity abhimatād asatyavacanān nivṛtto gṛhīti dvitīyam aṇuvratam. anyapīḍākaraṃ pārthivabhayādivaśād avaśyaṃ parityaktam api yadadattaṃ tataḥ pratinivṛttādaraḥ śrāvaka iti tṛtīyam aṇuvratam. upāttāyā anupāttāyāś ca paraṃganāyāḥ saṃgān nivṛttaratir gṛhīti caturtham aṇuvratam. dhanadhānyakṣetrādīnām icchāvaśāt kṛtaparicchedo gṛhīti paṃcamam aṇuvratam. 
 § 702 āha aparityaktāgārasya kim etāvān eva viśeṣa āhosvid asti kaścid anyo ’pīty ata āha — 
 digdeśānarthadaṇḍaviratisāmāyikaproṣadhopavāsopabhogaparibhogaparimāṇātithisaṃvibhāgavratasaṃpannaś ca || 
 § 703. ‘virati’ śabdaḥ pratyekaṃ parisamāpyate. digviratiḥ deśaviratiḥ anarthadaṇḍaviratir iti etāni trīṇi guṇavratāni; ‘vrata’ śabdasya pratyekam abhisaṃbandhāt. tathā sāmāyikavrataṃ proṣadhopavāsavrataṃ upabhogaparibhogaparimāṇavrataṃ atithisaṃvibhāgavrataṃ etāni catvāri śikṣāvratāni. etair vrataiḥ saṃpanno gṛhī viratāvirata ity ucyate. tad yathā — dikprācyādiḥ tatra prasiddhair abhijñānair avadhiṃ kṛtvā niyamanaṃ digvirativratam. tato bahis trasasthāvaravyaparopaṇanivṛtter mahāvratatvam avaseyam. tatra lābhe saty api pariṇāmasya nivṛtter lobhanirāsaś ca kṛto bhavati. grāmādīnām avadhṛtaparimāṇaḥ pradeśo deśaḥ. tato bahir nivṛttir deśavirativratam. pūrvavad bahir mahāvratatvaṃ vyavasthāpyam. asaty upakāre pāpādānahetur anarthadaṇḍaḥ. tato viratir anarthadaṇḍaviratiḥ. anarthadaṇḍaḥ paṃcavidhaḥ — apadhyānaṃ pāpopadeśaḥ pramādācaritaṃ hiṃsāpradānaṃ aśubhaśrutir iti. tatra pareṣāṃ jayaparājayavadhabandhanāṅgacchedaparasvaharaṇādi kathaṃ syād iti manasā cintanam apadhyānam. tiryakkleśavāṇijyaprāṇivadhakārambhādiṣu pāpasaṃyuktaṃ vacanaṃ pāpopadeśaḥ. prayojanam antareṇa vṛkṣādichedanabhūmikuṭṭanasalilasecanādyavadhyakarma pramādācaritam. viṣayakaṇṭakaśāstrāgnirajjukaśādaṇḍādihiṃsopakaraṇapradānaṃ hiṃsāpradānam. hiṃsārāgādipravardhanaduṣṭakathāśravaṇaśikṣaṇavyāpṛtir aśubhaśrutiḥ. samekībhāve vartate. tadyathā saṃgataṃ ghṛtaṃ saṃgataṃ tailām ity ucyate ekībhūtam iti gamyate. ekatvena ayanaṃ gamanaṃ samayaḥ, samaya eva sāmāyikaṃ, samayaḥ prayojanam asyeti vā vigṛhya sāmāyikam. iyati deśe etāvati kāle ity avadhārite sāmāyike sthitasya mahāvratatvaṃ pūrvavad veditavyam. kutaḥ? aṇusthūlakṛtahiṃsādinivṛtteḥ. saṃyamaprasaṃga iti cet? na; tadghātikarmodayasadbhāvāt. mahāvratatvābhāva iti cet? tan na; upacārād rājakule sarvagatacaitrābhidhānavat. proṣadhaśabdaḥ parvaparyāyavācī. śabdādigrahaṇaṃ prati nivṛttautsukyāni paṃcānīṇdriyāṇy upetya tasmin vasantīty upavāsaḥ. caturvidhāhāraparityāga ity arthaḥ. proṣadhe upavāsaḥ proṣadhopavāsaḥ. svaśarīrasaṃskārakāraṇasnānagandhamālyābharaṇādivirahitaḥ śucāv avakāśe sādhunivāse caityālaye svaproṣadhopavāsagṛhe vā dharmakathāśravaṇaśrāvaṇacintanavihitāntaḥkaraṇaḥ sann upavasen nirārambhaḥ śrāvakaḥ. upabhogo ’śanapānagandhamālyādiḥ. paribhoga ācchādanaprāvaraṇālaṃkāraśayanāsanagṛhayānavāhanādiḥ tayoḥ parimāṇam upabhogaparibhogaparimāṇam. madhu māṃsaṃ madyaṃ ca sadā parihartavyaṃ trasaghātān nivṛttacetasā. ketakyarjunapuṣpādīni śṛṅgaveramūlakādīni bahujantuyonisthānāny anantakāyavyapadeśārhāṇi parihartavyāni bahughātālpaphalatvāt. yānavāhanābharaṇādiṣv etāvad eveṣṭam ato ’nyad aniṣṭam ity aniṣṭān nivartanaṃ kartavyaṃ kālaniyamena yāvaj jīvaṃ vā yathā śakti. saṃyamam avināśayann atatīty atithiḥ. athavā nāsya tithir astīty atithiḥ aniyatakālāgamana ity arthaḥ. atithaye saṃvibhāgo ’tithisaṃvibhāgaḥ. sa caturvidhaḥ; bhikṣopakaraṇauṣadhapratiśrayabhedāt. mokṣārtham abhyudyatāyātithaye saṃyamaparāyaṇāya śuddhāya śuddhacetasā niravadyā bhikṣā deyā. dharmopakaraṇāni ca samyagdarśanādyupabṛṃhaṇāni dātavyāni. auṣadham api yogyam upayojanīyam. pratiśrayayaś ca paramadharmaśraddhayā pratipādayitavya iti. ‘ca’ śabdo vakṣyamāṇagṛhasthadharmasamuccayārthaḥ. 
 § 704. kaḥ punar asau — 
 māraṇāntikīṃ sallekhanāṃ joṣitā || 
 § 705. svapariṇāmopāttasyāyuṣa indriyāṇāṃ balānāṃ ca kāraṇavaśāt saṃkṣayo maraṇam. ‘anta’ grahaṇaṃ tadbhavamaraṇapratipattyartham. maraṇam anto maraṇāntaḥ. sa prayojanam asyeti māraṇāntikī. samyakkāyakaṣāyalekhanā sallekhanā. kāyasya bāhyasyābhyantarāṇāṃ ca kaṣāyāṇāṃ tatkāraṇahāpanakrameṇa samyaglekhanā sallekhanā. tām māraṇāntikīṃ sallekhanāṃ joṣihtā sevitā gṛhīty abhisaṃbadhyate. nanu ca vispaṣṭārthaṃ sevitety evaṃ vaktavyam? na; arthaviśeṣopapatteḥ. na kevalam iha sevanaṃ parigṛhyate. kiṃ tarhi? prītyartho ’pi. yasmād asatyāṃ prītau balān na salllekhanā kāryate. satyāṃ hi prītau svayam eva karoti. syān matam ātmavadhaḥ prāpnoti; svābhisandhipūrvakāyurādinivṛtteḥ? naiṣa doṣaḥ; apramattatvāt. ‘pramattayogāt prāṇavyaparopaṇaṃ hiṃsā’ ity uktam. na cāsya pramādayogo ’sti. kutaḥ. rāgādyabhāvāt. rāgadveṣamohāviṣṭasya hi viṣaśāstrādyupakaraṇaprayogavaśād ātmānaṃ ghnataḥ svaghāto bhavati. na sallekhanāṃ pratipannasya rāgādayaḥ santi tato nātmavadhadoṣaḥ. uktaṃ ca —
	   rāgādīṇam aṇuppā ahiṃsagattaṃ ti desidaṃ samaye |
	  tesiṃ ce uppattī hiṃseti jiṇehi ṇiddiṭṭhā || 
	  kiṃ ca maraṇasayāniṣṭatvād yathā vaṇijo vividhapaṇyadānādānasaṃcayaparasya svagṛhavināśo ’niṣṭaḥ. tadvināśakāraṇe ca kutaścid upasthite yathāśakti pariharati. duṣparihāre ca paṇyavināśo yathā na bhavati tathā yatate. evaṃ gṛhastho ’pi vrataśīlapaṇyasaṃcaye pravartamānaḥ tadāśrayasya na pātam abhivāṃchati. tadupaplavakāraṇe copasthite svaguṇavirodhena pariharati. duṣparihāre ca yathā svaguṇavināso na bhavati tathā prayatata iti katham ātmavadho bhavet. 
 § 706. atrāha, ‘niḥśalyo vratī’ ity uktaṃ tatra ca tṛtīyaṃ śalyaṃ mithyādarśanam. tataḥ samyagdṛṣṭinā vratinā niḥśalyena bhavitavyam ity uktam. tatsamyagdarśanaṃ kiṃ sāpavādaṃ nirapavādam iti. ucyate — kasyacin mohanīyāvasthāviśeṣāt kadācid ime bhavaty apavādāḥ — 
 śaṅkākāṅkṣāvicikitsā ’nyadṛṣṭipraśaṃsāsaṃstavāḥ samyagdṛṣṭer aticārāḥ || 
 § 707. niḥśaṃkitatvādayo vyākhyātāḥ ‘darśanaviśuddhiḥ’ ity atra. tatpratipakṣabhūtāḥ śaṃkādayo veditavyāḥ. atha praśaṃsāsaṃstavayoḥ ko viśeṣaḥ? manasā mityādṛṣṭer jñānacāritraguṇodbhāvanaṃ praśaṃsā, bhūtābhūtaguṇodbhāvavacanaṃ saṃstava ity ayam anayor bhedaḥ. nanu ca samyagdarśanam aṣṭāṅgam uktaṃ tasyāticārair apy aṣṭabhir bhavitavyam. naiṣa doṣaḥ; vrataśīleṣu paṃca paṃcāticārā ity uttaratra vivakṣuṇācāryeṇa praśaṃsāsaṃstavayor itarān aticārānantarbhāvya paṃcaivāticārā uktāḥ. 
 § 708. āha, samyagdṛṣṭer aticārā uktāḥ. kim evaṃ vrataśīleṣv api bhavantīti? om ity uktvā tadaticārasaṃkhyānirdeśārtham āha 
 vrataśīleṣu pañca pañca yathākramam || 
 § 709. vratani ca śīlāni ca vrataśīlāni teṣu vrataśīleṣu. śīlagrahaṇam anarthakam; vratagrahaṇenaiva siddheḥ? nānarthakam; viśeṣajñāpanārthaṃ vratparirakṣaṇārthaṃ śīlām iti digviratyādīnīha ‘śīla’ grahaṇena gṛhyante. 
 § 710. agāryadhikārād agāriṇo vrataśīleṣu paṃca paṃcāticārā vakṣyamāṇā yathākramaṃ veditavyāḥ. tad yathā — ādyasya tāvad ahiṃsāvratasya — 
 bandhavadhacchedātibhārāropaṇānnapānanirodhāḥ || 
 § 711. abhimatadeśagatinirodhahetur bandhaḥ. danḍakaśāvetrādibhir abhighātaḥ prāṇiṇāṃ vadhaḥ, na prāṇavyaparopaṇam; tataḥ prāgevāsya vinivṛttatvāt. karṇanāsikādīnām avayavānām apanayanaṃ chedaḥ. nyāyyabhārād atiriktavāhanam atibhārāropaṇam. gavādīnāṃ kṣutpipāsābādhākaraṇam annapānanirodhaḥ. ete paṃcāhiṃsāṇuvratasyāticārāḥ. 
 mithyopadeśarahobhyākhyānakūṭalekhakriyānyāsāpahārasākāramantrabhedāḥ || 
 § 712. abhyudayaniḥśreyasārtheṣu kriyāviśeṣeṣu anyasyānyathā pravartanam atisaṃdhāpanaṃ vā mityopadeśaḥ. yat strīpuṃsābhyām ekānte ’nuṣṭhitasya kriyāviśeṣasya prakāśanaṃ tad rahobhyākhyānaṃ veditavyam. anyenānuktam ananuṣṭhitaṃ yat kiṃcit paraprayogavaśād evaṃ tenoktam anuṣṭhitam iti vaṃcanānimittaṃ lekhanaṃ kūṭalekhakriyā. hiraṇyāder dravyasya nikṣeptur vismṛtasaṃkhyālpasaṃkhyeyam ādadānasyaivam ity anujñāvacanaṃ nyāsāpahāraḥ. arthaprakaraṇāṅgavikārabhrūvikṣepādibhiḥ parākūtam upalabhya tadāviṣkaraṇam asūyādinimittaṃ yattatsākāramantrabheda iti kathyate. ta ete satyāṇuvratasya paṃcāticārā boddhavyāḥ. 
 stenaprayogatadāhṛtādānaviruddharājyātikramahīnādhikamānonmānapratirūpakavyavahārāḥ || 
 § 713. muṣṇantaṃ svayam eva vā prayuṅkte ’nyena vā prayojayati prayuktam anumanyate vā yataḥ sa stenaprayogaḥ. aprayuktenānumatena ca caureṇānītasya grahaṇaṃ tadāhṛtādānam. ucitanyāyād anyena prakāreṇa dānagrahaṇam atikramaḥ. viruddhaṃ rājyaṃ viruddharājyam viruddharājye ’tikramaḥ viruddharājyātikramaḥ. tatra hy alpamūlyalabhyāni mahārghyāṇi dravyāṇīti prayatnaḥ. prasthādi mānam, tulādyunmānam. etena nyūnenānyasmai deyam adhikenātmano grāhyam ity evam ādi kūṭaprayogo hīnādhikamānonmānam. kṛtrimair hiraṇyādibhir vañcanāpūrvako vyavahāraḥ pratirūpakavyavahāraḥ. ta ete pañcādattādānāṇuvratasyāticārāḥ. 
 paravivāhakaraṇetvarikāparigṛhītāparigṛhītāgamanānaṅgakṛīḍākāmatīvrābhiniveśāḥ || 
 § 714. kanyādānaṃ vivāhaḥ. parasya vivāhaḥ paravivāḥ. paravivāhasya karaṇaṃ paravivāhakaraṇam. parapuruṣāneti gacchatīity evaṃ śīlā itvarī. kutsitā itvarī kutsāyāṃ ka itvarikā. yā ekapuruṣabhartṛkā sā parigṛhītā. yā gaṇikātvena puṃścalītvena vā parapuruṣagamanaśīlā asvāmikā sā aparigṛhītā. parigṛhītā cāparigṛhītā ca parigṛhītāparigṛhīte. itvarike ca te parigṛhītāparigṛhīte ca itvarikāparigṛhītāparigṛhīte, tayor gamane itvarikāparigṛhītāparigṛhītāgamane. aṃga prajananaṃ yoniś ca, tato ’nyatra krīḍā anaṅgakrīḍā. kāmasya pravṛddhaḥ pariṇāmaḥ kāmatīvrābhiniveśaḥ. ta ete paṃca svadārasaṃtoṣavratasyāticārāḥ. 
 kṣetravāstuhiraṇyasuvarṇadhanadhānyadāsīdāsakupyapramāṇātikramāḥ || 
 § 715. kṣetraṃ sasyādhikaraṇam. vāstu agāram. hiraṇyaṃ rūpyādivyavahāratantram. suvarṇaṃ pratītam. dhanaṃ gavādi. dhānyaṃ vrīhyādi. dāsidāsaṃ bhṛtyastrīpuṃsavargaḥ. kupyaṃ kṣaumakārpāsakauśeyacandanādi. kṣetraṃ ca vāstu ca kṣetravāstu, hiraṇyaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ ca hiraṇyasuvarṇam, dhanaṃ ca dhānyaṃ ca dhanadhānyam, dāsī ca dāsaś ca dāsīdāsam. kṣetravāstu ca hiraṇyasuvarṇaṃ ca dhanadhānyaṃ ca dāsīdāsaṃ ca kupyaṃ ca kṣetravāstuhiraṇyasuvarṇadhanadhānyadāsīdāsakupyāni. etāvān eva parigraho mama nānya iti paricchinnāṇupramāṇāt kṣetravāstvādiviṣayād atirekā atilobhavaśāt pramāṇātikramā iti pratyākhyāyante. ta ete parigrahaparimāṇavratasyāticārāḥ. 
 § 716. uktā vratānām aticārāḥ śīlānām aticārā vakṣyante. tad yathā — 
 ūrdhvādhas tiryagvyatikramakṣetravṛddhismṛtyantarādhānāni || 
 § 717. parimitasya digavadher atilaṃghanam atikramaḥ. sa samāsatas trividhhaḥ — ūrdhvātikramaḥ adho ’tikramas tiryagatikramaś ceti. tatra parvatādyārohaṇād ūrdhvātikramaḥ. kūpāvataraṇāder adho ’tikramaḥ. bilapraveśādes tiryagatikramaḥ. parigṛhītāyā diśo lobhāveśād ādhikyābhisandhiḥ kṣetravṛddhiḥ. sa eṣo ’tikramaḥ pramādān mohād vyāsaṃgād vā bhavatīty avaseyaḥ. ananusmaraṇaṃ smṛtyantarādhānam. ta ete digviramaṇasyāticārāḥ. 
 ānayanapreṣyaprayogaśabdarūpānupātapudgalakṣepāḥ || 
 § 718. ātmanā saṃkalpite deśe sthitasya prayojanavaśād yatkiṃcid ānayety ājñāpanam ānayanam. evaṃ kurv iti niyogaḥ preṣyaprayogaḥ. vyāpārakarān puraṣān pratyabhyutkāsikādikaraṇaṃ śabdānupātaḥ. *  svavigrahadarśanaṃ rūpānupātaḥ. loṣṭādinipātaḥ pudgalakṣepaḥ. ta ete deśaviramaṇasya pañcāticārāḥ. 
 kandarpakautkucyamaukharyāsamīkṣyādhikaraṇopabhogaparibhogānarthakyāni || 
 § 719. rāgodrekāt prahāsamiśro ’śiṣṭavākprayogaḥ kandarpaḥ. tadevobhayaṃ paratra duṣṭakāyakarmaprayuktaṃ kautkucyam. dhārṣṭyaprāyaṃ yatkiṃ vanānarthakaṃ bahupralāpitvaṃ maukharyam. asamīkṣya prayojanam ādhikyena karaṇam asamīkṣyādhikaraṇam. yāvatā ’rthenopabhogaparibhogau so ’rthas tato ’nyasyādhikyamānarthakyam. ta ete pañcānarthadaṇḍavirater aticārāḥ. 
 yogaduṣpraṇidhānānādarasmṛtyanupasthānāni || 
 § 720. yogo vyākhyātas trividhaḥ. tasya duṣṭaṃ praṇidhānaṃ yogaduṣpraṇidhānam — kāyaduṣpraṇidhānaṃ vāgduṣpraṇidhānaṃ manoduṣpraṇidhānam iti. anādaro ’nutsāhaḥ. anaikāgryaṃ smṛtyanupasthānam. ta ete pañca sāmāyikasyātikramāḥ. 
 apratyavekṣitāpramārjitotsargādānasaṃstaropakramaṇānādarasmṛtyanupasthānāni || 
 § 721. jantavaḥ santi na santi veti pratyavekṣaṇaṃ cakṣurvyāpāraḥ. mṛdunopakaraṇena yat kriyate prayojanaṃ tat pramārjitam. tadubhayaṃ pratiṣedhaviśiṣṭam utsargādibhis tribhir abhisaṃbadhyate — apratyavekṣitāpramārjitotsarga ity evam ādi. tatra apratyavekṣitāpramārjitāyāṃ bhūmau mūtrapurīṣotsargaḥ apratyavekṣitāpramārjitotsargaḥ. apratyavekṣitāpramārjitasyārhadācāryapūjopakaraṇasya gaṃdhamālyadhūpāder ātmaparidhānādyarthasya ca vastrāder ādānam apratyavekṣitāpramārjitādānam. apratyavekṣitāpramārjitasya prāvaraṇādeḥ saṃstarasyopakramaṇaṃ apratyavekṣitāpramārjitasaṃstaropakramaṇam. kṣudabhyarditatvād āvaśyakeṣv anādaro ’nutsāḥ. smṛtyanupasthānaṃ vyākhyātam. ta ete pañca proṣadhopavāsasyāticārāḥ. 
 sacittasaṃbandhasaṃmiśrābhiṣavaduṣpakvāhārāḥ || 
 § 722. saha cittena vartate iti sacittaṃ cetanāvad dravyam. tadupaliṣṭaḥ saṃbandhaḥ. tadvyatikīrṇaḥ saṃmiśraḥ. kathaṃ punar asya sacittādiṣu pravṛttiḥ? pramādasaṃmohābhyām. dravo vṛṣyo vābhiṣavaḥ. asamyakpakvo duṣpakvaḥ. etair āhāro viśeṣyate — sacittāhāraḥ saṃbandhāhāraḥ saṃmiśrāhāro ’bhiṣavāhāro duṣpakvāhāra iti. ta ete pañca bhogopabhogaparisaṃkhyānasyāticāraḥ. 
 sacittanikṣepāpidhānaparavyapadeśamātsaryakālātikramāḥ || 
 § 723. sacitte padmapatrādau nikṣepaḥ sacittanikṣepaḥ. apidhānam āvaraṇam. sacittenaiva saṃbadhyate sacittāpidhānam iti. anyadātṛdeyārpaṇaṃ paravyapadeśaḥ. prayacchato ’py ādarābhāvo ’nyadātṛguṇāsahanaṃ vā mātsaryam. akāle bhojanaṃ kālātikramaḥ. ta ete pañcātithisaṃvibhāgaśīlāticārāḥ. 
 jīvitamaraṇāśaṃsāmitrānurāgasukhānubandhanidānāni || 
 § 724. āśaṃsanam āśaṃsā ākāṅkṣaṇam ity arthaḥ. jīvitaṃ ca maraṇaṃ ca jīvitamaraṇam, jīvitamaraṇasyāśaṃse jīvitamaraṇāśaṃse. pūrvasuhṛtsahapāṃsukrīḍanādyanusmaraṇaṃ mitrānurāgāḥ. anubhūtaprītiviśeṣasmṛtisamanvāhāraḥ sukhānubandhaḥ. bhogākā–ṅkṣayā niyataṃ dīyate cittaṃ tasmiṃs teneti vā nidānam. ta ete pañca sallekhanāyā aticārāḥ. 
 § 725. atrāha, uktaṃ bhavatā tīrthakaratvakāraṇakarmāsravanirdeśe ‘śaktitas tyāgatapasī ’ iti, punaś coktaṃ śīlavidhāne ‘atithisaṃvibhāga’ iti. tasya dānasya lakṣaṇam anirjñātaṃ taducyatām ity ata āha — 
 anugrahārthaṃ svasyātisargo dānam || 
 § 726. svaparopakāro ’nugrahaḥ. svopakāraḥ puṇyasaṃcayaḥ; paropakāraḥ samyagjñānādivṛddhiḥ. ‘sva’ śabdo dhanaparyāyavacanaḥ. anugrahārthaṃ svasyātisargas tyāgo dānaṃ veditavyam. 
 § 727. atrāha — uktaṃ dānaṃ tat kim aviśiṣṭaphalam āhosvid asti kaścit prativiśeṣa ity ata āha — 
 vidhidravyadātṛpātraviśeṣāt tadviśeṣaḥ || 
 § 728. pratigrahādikramo vidhiḥ. viśeṣo guṇakṛtaḥ. tasya pratyekam abhisambandhaḥ kriyate — vidhiviśeṣo dravyaviśeṣo dātṛviseṣaḥ pātraviśeṣa iti. tatra vidhiviśeṣaḥ pratigrahādiṣv ādarānādarakṛto bhedaḥ. tapaḥsvādhyāyaparivṛddhihetutvādir dravyaviśeṣaḥ. anasūyāviṣādādir dātṛviśeṣaḥ. mokṣakāraṇaguṇasaṃyogaḥ pātraviśeṣaḥ. tataś ca puṇyaphalaviśeṣaḥ kṣityādiviśeṣād bījaphalaviśeṣavat. 
 iti tattvārthavṛttau sarvārthasiddhisaṃjñikāyāṃ saptamo ’dhyāyaḥ || 7 || 
 
 
	  athāṣṭhamo ’dhyāyaḥ
	   §§ 729–783 
 § 729. vyākhyāta āsravapadārthaḥ. tadanantaroddeśabhāgbandhapadārtha idānīṃ vyākhyeyaḥ. tasmin vyākhyeye sati pūrvaṃ bandhahetūpanyāsaḥ kriyate; tatpūrvakatvād bandhasyeti — 
 mithyādarśanāviratipramādakaṣāyayogā bandhahetavaḥ || 
 § 730. mithyādarśanādaya uktāḥ. kva? mithyādarśanaṃ tāvad uktam, ‘tattvārthaśraddhānaṃ samyagdarśanam’ ity atra tatpratipakṣabhūtam, āsravavidhāne ca kriyāsu vyākhyātaṃ mithyādarśanakriyeti. viratir uktā. tatpratipakṣabhūtā aviratir grāhyā. ājñāvyāpādanakriyā anākaṅkṣākriyety anayoḥ pramādasyāntarbhāvaḥ. sa ca pramādaḥ kuśaleṣv anādaraḥ. kaṣāyāḥ krodhādayaḥ anantānubandhyapratyākyānapratyākyānasaṃjvalanavikalpāḥ proktāḥ. kva? ‘indriyakaṣāyā’ ity atraiva. yogāḥ kāyādivikalpāḥ proktāḥ. kva? ‘kāyavāṅmanaḥkarma yogaḥ’ ity atra. 
 § 731. mithyādarśanaṃ dvividham; naisargikaṃ paropadeśapūrvakaṃ ca. tatra paropadeśam antareṇa mithyātvakarmodayavaśād yad āvirbhavati tattvārthāśraddhānalakṣaṇaṃ tan naisargikam. paropadeśanimittaṃ caturvidham; kriyākriyāvādyajñānikavainayikavikalpāt. athavā pañcavidhaṃ mithyādarśanam — ekāntamithyādarśanaṃ viparītamithyādarśanaṃ saṃśayamithyādarśanaṃ vainayikamithyādarśanam ajñānikamithyādarśanaṃ ceti. tatra idam eva ittham eveti dharmidharmayor abhiniveśa ekāntaḥ.  puruṣa evedaṃ sarvam  iti vā nitya eva vā anitya eveti. sagrantho nirgranthaḥ, kevali kavalāhārī, strī sidhyatīty evam ādiḥ viparyayaḥ. samyagdarśanajñānacāritrāṇi kiṃ mokṣamāragaḥ syād vā na vety antarapakṣāparigrahaḥ saṃśayaḥ. sarvadevatānāṃ sarvasamayānāṃ ca samadarśanaṃ vainayikam. hitāhitaparīkṣāviraho ’jñānikatvam. uktaṃ ca — 
 āsidisadaṃ kiriyāṇaṃ akkiriyāṇaṃ taha ya hoi culasīdī |
	  sattaṭṭhamaṇṇāṇīṇaṃ veṇaiyāṇaṃ tu battisaṃ || 
 § 732. aviratir dvādaśavidhāḥ; ṣaṭkāyaṣaṭkaraṇaviṣayabhedāt. ṣodaśa kaṣāyā nava nokaṣāyās teṣām īṣadbhedo na bheda iti paṃcaviṃśatiḥ kaṣāyāḥ. catvāro manoyogaś catvāro vāgyogāḥ pañca kāyayogā iti trayodaśavikalpo yogaḥ. āhārakakāyayogāhārakamiśrakāyayogayoḥ pramattasaṃyate saṃbhavāt pañcadaśāpi bhavanti. pramādo ’nekavidhaḥ; śuddhyaṣṭakottamakṣamādiviṣayabhedāt. ta ete pañca bandhahetavaḥ samastā vyastāś ca bhavanti. tad yathā — mithyādṛṣṭeḥ paṃcāpi samuditā bandhahetavo bhavanti. sāsādhanasamyagdṛṣṭisamyaṅmithyādṛṣṭyasaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭīnām aviratyādayaś catvāraḥ. saṃyatāsaṃyatasyāviratir viratimiśrā pramādakaṣāyayogaś ca. pramattasaṃyatasya pramādakaṣāyayogāḥ. apramattādīnāṃ caturṇāṃ yogakaṣāyau. upaśāntakaṣāyakṣīṇakaṣāyasayogakevalinām eka eva yogaḥ. ayogakevalino na bandhahetuḥ. 
 § 733. uktā bandhahetavaḥ. idānīṃ bandho vaktavya ity ata āha — 
 sakaṣāyatvāj jīvaḥ karmaṇo yogyān pudgalān ādatte sa bandhaḥ || 
 § 734. saha kaṣāyeṇa vartata iti sakaṣāyaḥ. sakaṣāyasya bhāvaḥ sakaṣātvam. tasmāt sakaṣāyatvād iti. punar hetunirdeśaḥ jaṭharāgnyāśayānurūpāhāragrahaṇavattīvramandamadhyamakaṣāyāśayānurūpasthityanubhavaviśeṣapratipattyartham. amūrtir ahasta ātmā kathaṃ karmādatta iti coditaḥ san ‘jīvaḥ’ ity āha. jīvanāj jīvaḥ prāṇādhāraṇād āyuḥsaṃbandhān nāyurvirahād iti. ‘karmayogyān’ iti laghunirdeśāt siddhe ‘karmaṇo yogyān’ iti pṛthagvibhaktyuccāraṇaṃ vākyāntarajñāpanārtham. kiṃ punas tadvākyāntaram? karmaṇo jīvaḥ sakaṣāyo bhavatīty ekaṃ vākyam. etad uktaṃ bhavati — ‘karmaṇaḥ’ iti hetunirdeśaḥ karmaṇo hetor jīvaḥ sakaṣāyo bhavati, nākarmasya kaṣāyalepo ’sti. tato jīvakarmaṇor anādisaṃbandha iti uktaṃ bhavati. tenāmūrto jīvo mūrtena karmaṇā kathaṃ badhyate iti codyam apākṛtaṃ bhavati. itarathā hi bandhasyādimattve ātyantikīṃ śuddhiṃ dadhataḥ siddhasyeva bandhābhāvaḥ prasajyeta. dvitīyaṃ vākyaṃ ‘karmaṇo yogyān pudgalān ādatte’ iti. arthavaśād vibhaktipariṇāma iti pūrvahetusaṃbandham tyaktvā ṣaṣṭhīsaṃbandham upaiti ‘karmaṇo yogyān’ iti. ‘pudgala’ vacanaṃ karmaṇas tādātmyakhyāpanārtham. tenātmaguṇo ’dṛṣṭo nirākṛto bhavati; tasya saṃsārahetutvānupapatteḥ. ‘ādatte’ iti hetuhetumadbhāvakhyāpanārtham. ato mithyādarśanādyāveśād ārdrīkṛtasyātmanaḥ sarvato yogaviśeṣāt teṣāṃ sūkṣmaikakṣetrāvagāhinām anantānantapradeśānāṃ pudgalānāṃ karmabhāvayogyānām avibhagenopaśleṣo bandha ity ākhyāyate. yathā bhājanaviśeṣe prakṣiptānāṃ vividharasabījapuṣpaphalānāṃ madirābhāvena pariṇāmas tathā pudgalānām apy ātmani sthitānāṃ yogakaṣāyavaśāt karmabhāvena pariṇāmo veditavyaḥ. ‘saḥ’ vacanam anyanivṛttyartham. sa eṣa bandho nānyo ’stīti. tena guṇaguṇibandho nivartito bhavati. karmādisādhano ‘bandha’-śabdo vyākhyeyaḥ. 
 § 735. āha kim ayaṃ bandha ekarūpa eva, āhosvit prakārā apy asya santīty ata idam ucyate — 
 prakṛtisthityanubhavapradeśās tadvidhayaḥ || 
 § 736. prakṛtiḥ svabhāvaḥ. nimbasya kā prakṛtiḥ? tiktatā. guḍasya kā prakṛtiḥ? madhuratā. tathā jñānāvaraṇasya kā prakṛtiḥ? arthānavagamaḥ. darśanāvaraṇasya kā prakṛtiḥ? arthānālokanam. vedyasya sadasallakṣaṇasya sukhaduḥkhasaṃvedanam. darśanamohasya tattvārthāśraddhānam. cāritramohasyāsaṃyamaḥ. āyuṣo bhavadhāraṇam. nāmno nārakādināmakaraṇam. gotrasyoccair nīccaiḥ sthānasaṃśabdanam. anantarāyasya dānādivighnakaraṇam. tadevaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ prakriyate prabhavaty asyā iti prakṛtiḥ. tatsvabhāvād apracyutiḥ sthitiḥ. yathā — ajāgomahiṣyādikṣīrāṇāṃ mādhuryasvabhāvād apracyutiḥ sthitiḥ. tathā jñānāvaraṇādīnām arthāvagamādisvabhāvād apracyutiḥ sthitiḥ. tadrasaviśeṣo ’nubhavaḥ yathā — ajāgomahiṣyādikṣīrāṇāṃ tīvramandādibhāvena rasaviśeṣaḥ. tathā karmapudgalānāṃ svagatasāmarthyaviśeṣo ’nubhavaḥ. iyattāvadhāraṇaṃ pradeśaḥ. karmabhāvapariṇatapudgalaskandhānāṃ paramāṇuparicchedenāvadhāraṇaṃ pradeṣaḥ. ‘vidhi’-śabdaḥ prakāravacanaḥ. ta ete prakṛtyādayaś catvāras tasya bandhasya prakārāḥ. tatra yoganimittau prakṛtipradeśau. kaṣāyanimittau sthityanubhavau. tatprakarṣāprakarṣabhedād tadbaṃdhavicitrabhāvaḥ. tathā coktam — 
 jogā payaḍi-paesā ṭhidiaṇubhāgā kasāyado kuṇadi |
	  apariṇaducchiṇṇesu ya baṃdhaṭṭhidikāraṇaṃ ṇatthi || 
 § 737. tatrādyasya prakṛtibandhasya bhedapradarśanārtham āha — 
 ādyo jñānadarśanāvaraṇavedanīyamohanīyāyurnāmagotrāntarāyāḥ || 
 § 738. ādyaḥ prakṛtibandho jñānāvaraṇādyaṣṭavikalpo veditavyaḥ. āvṛṇoty āvriyate ’neneti vā āvaraṇam. tat pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate — jñānāvaraṇaṃ darśanāvaraṇam iti. vedayati vedyata iti vā vedanīyam. mohayati mohyate ’neneti vā mohanīyam. ety anena nārakādibhavam ity āyuḥ. namayaty ātmānaṃ namyate ’neneti vā nāma. uccair nīcaiś ca gūyate śabdyata iti vā gotram. dātṛdeyādīnām antaraṃ madhyametīty antarāyaḥ. ekenātmapariṇāmenādīyamānāḥ pudgalā jñānāvaraṇādyanekabhedaṃ pratipadyante sakṛdupabhuktānnapariṇāmarasarudhirādivat. 
 § 739. āha, ukto mūlaprakṛtibandho ’ṣṭavidhaḥ. idānīm uttaraprakṛtibandho vaktavya ity ata āha — 
 pañcanavadvyaṣṭāviṃśaticaturdvicatvāriṃśaddvipañcabhedā yathākramam || 
 § 740. dvitīyagrahaṇam iha kartavyaḥ; dvitīya uttaraprakṛtibandha evaṃ vikalpa iti? na kartavyam; pāriśeṣyāt siddheḥ. ādyo mūlaprakṛtibandho ’ṣṭavikalpa uktaḥ. tataḥ pāriśeṣyād ayam uttaraprakṛtivikalpavidhir bhavati. ‘bheda’ śabdaḥ pañcādibhir yathā kramam abhisaṃbandhyate — pañcabhedaṃ jñānāvaraṇīyaṃ navabhedaṃ darśanāvaraṇīyaṃ dvibhedaṃ vedanīyaṃ aṣṭāviṃśatibhedaṃ mohanīyaṃ caturbhedam āyuḥ dvicatvāriṃśadbhedaṃ nāma dvibhedaṃ gotraṃ paṃcabhedo ’ntarāya iti. 
 § 741. yadi jñānāvaraṇīyaṃ paṃcabhedaṃ tatpratipattir ucyatām ity ata āha — 
 matiśrutāvadhimanaḥparyayakevalānām || 
 § 742. matyādīni jñānāni vyākhyātāni. teṣām āvṛter āvaraṇabhedo bhavatīti paṃcottaraprakṛtayo veditavyāḥ. atra codyate — abhavyasya manaḥparyayajñānaśaktiḥ kevalajñānaśaktiś ca syād vā na vā. yadi syāt tasyābhavyatvābhāvaḥ. atha nāsti tatrāvaraṇadvayakalpanā vyartheti? ucyate — ādeśavacanān na doṣaḥ. dravyārthādeśān manaḥparyayakevalajñānaśaktisaṃbhavaḥ. paryāyārthādeśāt tacchaktyabhāvaḥ. yady evaṃ bhavyābhavyavikalpo nopapadyate; ubhayatra tacchaktisadbhāvāt? na śaktibhāvābhāvāpekṣayā bhavyābhavyavikalpa ity ucyate. kutas tarhi? vyaktisadbhāvāsadbhāvāpekṣayā. samyagdarśanādibhir vyaktir yasya bhaviṣyati sa bhavyaḥ. yasya tu na bhaviṣyati so ’bhavya iti. kanaketarapāṣāṇavat. 
 § 743. āha, ukto jñānāvaraṇottaraprakṛtivikalpaḥ. idānīṃ darśanāvaraṇasya vaktavya ity ata āha — 
 cakṣuracakṣuravadhikevalānāṃ nidrānidrānidrāpracalāpracalāpracalāstyānagṛddhayaś ca || 
 § 744. cakṣuracakṣuravadhikevalānām iti darśanāvaraṇāpekṣayā bhedanirdeśaḥ — cakṣurdarśanāvaraṇam acakṣurdarśanāvaraṇam avadhidarśanāvaraṇaṃ kevaladarśanāvaraṇam iti. madakhedaklamavinodanārthaḥ svāpo nidrā. tasyā upary upari vṛttir nidrānidrā. yā kriyātmānaṃ pracalayati sā pracalā śokaśramamadādiprabhavā āsīnasyāpi netragātravikriyāsūcikā. saiva punaḥ punar āvartamānā pracalāpracalā. svapne yathā vīryaviśeṣāvirbhāvaḥ sā styānagṛddhiḥ. styāyater anekārthatvāt svapnārtha iha gṛhyate, gṛddher api dīptiḥ. styāne svapne gṛddhyati dīpyate yad udayād ātmā raudraṃ bahukarma karoti sā styānagṛddhiḥ. iha nidrādibhir darśanāvaraṇaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyenābhisaṃbadhyate — nidrādarśanāvaraṇam nidrānidrādarśanāvaraṇam ity ādi. 
 § 745. tṛtīyasyāḥ prakṛter uttaraprakṛtipratipādanārtham āha — 
 sadasadvedye || 
 § 746. yad udayād devādigatiṣu śarīramānasasukhaprāptis tat sadvedyam. praśastaṃ vedyaṃ sadvedyam iti. yat phalaṃ duḥkham anekavidhaṃ tad asadvedyam. apraśastaṃ vedyam asadvedyam iti. 
 § 747. caturthyāḥ prakṛter uttaraprakṛtivikalpanidarśanārtham āha — 
 darśanacāritramohanīyākaṣāyakaṣāyavedanīyākhyās tridvinavaṣoḍaśabhedāh samyaktvamithyātvatadubhayānyakaṣāyakaṣāyau hāsyaratyaratiśokabhayajugupsāstrīpunnapuṃsakavedā anantānubandhyapratyākhyānapratyākhyānasaṃjvalanavikalpāścaikaśaḥ krodhamānamāyālobhāḥ || 
 § 748. darśanādayaś catvāraḥ tryādayo ’pi. tatra yathāsaṃkhyena saṃbandho bhavati — darśanamohanīyaṃ tribhedham, cāritramohanīyaṃ dvibhedam, akaṣāyavedanīyaṃ navavidham, kaṣāyavedanīyaṃ ṣoḍaśavidham iti. 
 § 749. tatra darśanamohanīyaṃ tribhedham — samyaktvaṃ mithyātvaṃ tadubhayam iti. tad bandhaṃ pratyekaṃ bhūtvā satkarmāpekṣayā tridhā vyavatiṣṭhate. tatra yasyodayāt sarvajñapraṇītamārgaparāṅmukhas tattvārthaśraddhānanirutsuko hitāhitavicārāsamartho mithyādṛṣṭir bhavati tan mithyātvam. tad eva samyaktvaṃ śubhapariṇāmaniruddhasvarasaṃ yad audāsīnyenāvasthitam ātmanaḥ śraddhānaṃ na niruṇaddhi, tad vedayamānaḥ puruṣaḥ samyagdṛṣṭir ity abhidhīyate. tad eva mithyātvaṃ prakṣālanaviśeṣāt kṣīṇākṣīṇamadaśaktikodravavatsāmiśuddhasvarasaṃ tadubhayam ity ākhyāyate samyaṅmithyātvam iti yāvat. yasyodayād ātmano ’rdhaśuddhamadakodravaudanopayogāpāditamiśrapariṇāmavadubhayātmako bhavati pariṇāmaḥ. 
 § 750. cāritramohanīyaṃ dvidhā; akaṣāyakaṣāyabhedāt. īṣad arthe nañaḥ prayogād īṣat kaṣāyo ’kaṣāya iti. akaṣāyavedanīyaṃ navavidham. kutaḥ. hāsyādibhedāt. yasyodayād dhāsyāvirbhāvas tad dhāsyam. yad udayād deśādiṣv autsukyaṃ sā ratiḥ. aratis tadviparītā. yad vipākāc chocanaṃ sa śokaḥ. yad udayād udvegas tad bhayam. yad udayād ātmadoṣasaṃvaraṇaṃ paradoṣāviṣkaraṇaṃ sā jugupsā. yad udayāt straiṇān bhāvān pratipadyate sa strīvedaḥ. yasyodayāt pauṃsnān bhāvānāskandati sa puṃvedaḥ. yad udayān nāpuṃsakān bhāvān upavrajati sa napuṃsakavedaḥ. 
 § 751. kaṣāyavedanīyaṃ ṣoḍaśavidham. kutaḥ. anantānubandhyādivikalpāt. tad yathā — kaṣāyāḥ krodhamānamāyālobhāḥ. teṣām catasro ’vasthāḥ — anantānubandhino ’pratyākhyānāvaraṇāḥ pratyākhyānāvaraṇāḥ saṃjvalanāś ceti. anantasaṃsārakāraṇatvān mithyādarśanam anantam. tadanubandhino ’nantānubandhinaḥ krodhamānamāyālobhāḥ. yadudayād deśaviratiṃ saṃyamāsaṃyamākhyām alpām api kartuṃ na śaknoti te deśapratyākhyānam āvṛṇvanto ’pratyākhyānāvaraṇāḥ krodhamānamāyālobhāḥ. yadudayād viratiṃ kṛtsnāṃ saṃyamākhyāṃ na śaknoti kartuṃ te kṛtsnaṃ pratyākhyānam āvṛṇvantaḥ pratyākhyānāvaraṇāḥ krodhamānamāyālobhāḥ. samekībhāve vartate. saṃyamena sahāvasthānād ekībhūya jvalanti saṃyamo vā jvalaty eṣu satsv apīti saṃjvalanāḥ krodhamānamāyālobhāḥ. ta ete samuditāḥ santaḥ ṣoḍaśa kaṣāyā bhavanti. 
 § 752. mohanīyānantaroddeśabhāja āyuṣa uttaraprakṛtinirjñāpanārtham āha — 
 nārakatairyagyonamānuṣadaivāni || 
 § 753. nārakādiṣu bhavasaṃbandhenāyuṣo vyapadeśaḥ kriyate. narakeṣu bhavaṃ nārakam āyuḥ, tiragyoniṣu bhavaṃ tairyagyonam, mānuṣeṣu bhavaṃ mānuṣam, deveṣu bhavaṃ daivam iti. narakeṣu tīvraśītoṣṇavedaneṣu yannimittaṃ dīrghajīvanaṃ tannārakam. evaṃ śeṣv api. 
 § 754. āyuś caturvidhaṃ vyākhyātam. tadanantaram uddiṣṭaṃ yan nāmakarma tad uttaraprakṛtinirṇayārtham āha — 
 gatijātiśarīrāṅgopāṅganirmāṇabaṃdhanasaṃghātasaṃsthānasaṃhananasparśarasagaṃdhavarṇānupūrvyāgurulaghūpaghātaparaghātātapodyotocchvāsavihāyogatayaḥ pratyekaśarīratrasasubhagasusvaraśubhasūkṣmaparyāptisthirādeyayaśaḥkīrtisetarāṇi tīrthakaratvaṃ ca || 
 § 755. yad udayātmā bhavāntaraṃ gacchati sā gatiḥ. sā carturvidhā — narakagatis tiryaggatir manuṣyagatir devagatiś ceti. yan nimitta ātmano nārako bhāvas tan narakagatināma. evaṃ śeṣv api yojyam. tāsu narakādigatiṣv avyabhicāriṇā sādṛśyenaikīkṛto ’rthātmā jātiḥ. tannimittaṃ jātināma. tatpañcavidham — ekendriyajātināma dvīndriyajātināma trīndriyajātināma caturindriyajātināma pañcendriyajātināma ceti. yad udayād ātmā ekendriya iti śabdyate tad ekendriyajātināma. evaṃ śeṣv api yojyam. yad udayād ātmanaḥ śarīranirvṛttis tac charīranāma. tat pañcavidham — audārikaśarīranāma vaikriyikaśarīranāma āhārakaśarīranāma taijasaśarīranāma kārmaṇaśarīranāma ceti. teṣāṃ viśeṣo vyākhyātaḥ. yad udayād āṅgopāṅgavivekas tad āṅgopāṅganāma. tat trividham — audārikaśarīrāṅgopāṅganāma vaikriyikaśarīrāṅgopāṅganāma āhārakaśarīrāṅgopāṅganāma ceti. yan nimittāt pariniṣpattis tan nirmāṇam. tad dvividhaḥ — sthānanirmāṇaṃ pramāṇanirmāṇaṃ ceti. tajjātināmodayāpekṣaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ sthānaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca nirvartayati. nirmīyate ’neneti nirmāṇam. śarīranamakarmodayavaśād upāttānāṃ pudgalānām anyonyapradeśasaṃśleṣaṇaṃ yato bhavati tad bandhananāma. yadudayād audārikādiśarīrāṇāṃ vivaravirahitānyo ’nyapradeśānupraveśena ekatvāpādanaṃ bhavati satsaṃghātanāma. yad udayād audārikādisarīrākṛtinirvṛttir bhavati tat saṃsthānanāma. tat ṣoḍhā vibhajyate — samacaturasrasaṃsthānanāma nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalasaṃsthānanāma svātisaṃsthānanāma kubjasaṃsthānanāma vāmanasaṃsthānanāma huṇḍasaṃsthānanāma ceti. yasyodayāt asthibandhanaviśeṣo bhavati tatsaṃhanananāma. tat ṣaḍvidham — vajrarṣabhanārācasaṃhanananāma vajranārācasaṃhanananāma nārācasaṃhanananāma ardhanārācasaṃhanananāma kīlikāsaṃhanananāma asaṃprāptāsṛpāṭikāsaṃhanananāma ceti. yasyodayāt sparśaprādurbhāvas tat sparśanāma. tad aṣṭavidham — karkaśanāma mṛdunāma gurunāma laghunāma snigdhanāma rūkṣanāma śītanāma uṣṇanāma ceti. yan nimitto rasavikalpas tad rasanāma. tat pañcavidham — tiktanāma kaṭukanāma kaṣāyanāma āmlanāma madhuranāma ceti. yad udayaprabhavo gandhas tad gandhanāma. tad dvividham — surabhigandhanāma asurabhigandhanāma ceti. yad dhetuko varṇavibhāgas tad varṇanāma. tat paṃcavidham — kṛṣṇavarṇanāma nīlavarṇanāma raktavarṇanāma hāridravaṛnanāma śuklavarṇanāma ceti. pūrvaśarīrākārāvināśo yasyodayād bhavati tad ānupūrvyanāma. tac caturvidham — narakagatiprāyogyānupūrvyanāma tiryaggatiprāyogyānupūrvyanāma manuṣyagatiprāyogyānupūrvyanāma devagatiprāyogyānupūrvyanāma ceti. yasyodayād ayaḥpiṇḍavad gurutvān nādhaḥ patati na cārkatūlavallaghutvād ūrdhvaṃ gacchati tad gurulaghunāma. yasyodayāt svayaṃkṛtodbandhanamaruprapatanādinimitta upaghāto bhavati tad upaghātanāma. yannimittaḥ paraśastrāder vyāghātas tat paraghātanāma. yadudayān nirvṛttam ātapanaṃ tadātapanama. tadāditye vartate. yan nimittam udyotananaṃ tad udyotanāma. tac candrakhadyotādiṣu vartate. yaddhetur ucchvāsas tad ucchvāsanāma. vihāya ākāśam. tatra gatinirvartakaṃ tad vihāyogatināma. tad dvividham — praśastāpraśastabhedāt. śarīranāmakarmodayān nirvartyamānaṃ śarīram ekātmopabhogakāraṇaṃ yato bhavati tat pratyekaśarīranāma. bahūnām ātmanām upabhogahetutvena sādhāraṇaṃ śarīraṃ yato bhavati tat sādhāraṇaśarīranāma. yadudayād dvīndriyādiṣu janma tat trasanāma. yannimitta ekendriyeṣu prādurbhāvas tat sthāvaranāma. yadudayād anyaprītiprabhavas tat subhaganāma. yadudayād rūpādiguṇopeto ’py aprītikaras tad durbhaganāma. yannimittaṃ manojñasvaranirvartanaṃ tat susvaranāma. tadviparītaṃ duḥsvaranāma. yad udayād ramaṇīyatvaṃ tac chubhanāma. tadviparītaṃ aśubhanāma. sūkṣmaśarīranirvartakaṃ sūkṣmanāma. anyabādhākaraśarīrakāraṇaṃ bādaranāma. yadudayād āhārādiparyāptinirvṛttiḥ tat paryāptināma. tat ṣaḍvidham — āhāraparyāptināma śarīraparyāptināma indriyaparyāptināma prāṇāpanaparyāptināma bhāṣāparyāptināma manaḥparyāptināma ceti. ṣaḍvidhaparyāptyabhāvahetur aparyāptināma. sthirabhāvasya nirvartakaṃ sthiranāma. tadviparītam asthiranāma. prabhopetaśarīrakāraṇam ādeyanāma. niṣprabhaśarīrakāraṇam anādeyanāma. puṇyaguṇakhyāpanakāraṇaṃ yaśaḥkīrtināma. tatpratyanīkaphalam ayaśaḥkīrtināma. ārhantyakāraṇaṃ tīrthakaratvanāma. 
 § 756. ukto nāmakarmaṇa uttaraprakṛtibhedaḥ. tadanantaroddeśabhājo gotrasya prakṛtibhedo vyākhyāyate — 
 uccairnīcaiś ca || 
 § 757. gotraṃ dvividham — uccairgotraṃ nīcairgotram iti. yasyodayāl lokapūjiteṣu kuleṣu janma tac uccairgotram. yadudayād garhiteṣu kuleṣu janma tan nīcairgotram. 
 § 758. aṣṭamyāḥ karmaprakṛter uttaraprakṛtinirdeśārtham āha — 
 dānalābhabhogopabhogavīryāṇām || 
 § 759. antarāyāpekṣayā bhedanirdeśaḥ kriyate — dānasyāntarāyo lobhasyāntarāya ity ādi. dānādipariṇāmavyāghātahetutvāt tad vyapadeśaḥ. yadudayād dātukāmo ’pi na prayacchati, labdhukāmo ’pi na labhate, bhoktum icchann api na bhuṅkte, upabhoktum abhivāñchann api nopabhuṅkte, utsahitukāmo ’pi notsahate ta ete pañcāntarāyasya bhedāḥ. 
 § 760. vyākhyātāḥ prakṛtibandhavikalpāḥ. idānīṃ sthitibandhavikalpo vaktavyaḥ. sā sthitir dvividhā — utkṛṣṭā jaghanyā ca. tatra yāsāṃ karmaprakṛtīṇām utkṛṣṭā sthitiḥ samānā tannirdeśārtham ucyate — 
 āditas tisṛṇām antarāyasya ca triṃśatsāgaropamakoṭīkoṭyaḥ parā sthitiḥ || 
 § 761. madhye ’nte vā tisṛṇām grahaṇaṃ mābhūd iti ‘āditaḥ’ ity ucyate. ‘antarāyasya’ iti vacanaṃ vyavahitagrahaṇārtham. sāgaropamam uktaparimāṇam. koṭīṇāṃ koṭyaḥ koṭīkoṭyaḥ. para utkṛṣṭety arthaḥ. etad uktaṃ bhavati — jñānāvaraṇadarśanāvaraṇavedanīyāntarāyāṇām utkṛṣṭā sthitis triṃśatsāgaropamakoṭīkoṭya iti. sā kasya bhavati? mithyādṛṣṭeḥ saṃjñinaḥ paṃcendriyasya paryaptikasya. anyeṣām āgamāt saṃpratyayaḥ kartavyaḥ. 
 § 762. mohanīyasyotkṛṣṭasthitipratipattyartham āha — 
 saptatir mohanīyasya || 
 § 763. ‘sāgaropamakoṭīkoṭyaḥ parā sthitiḥ’ ity anuvartate. iyam api parā sthitir mithyādṛṣṭeḥ saṃjñinaḥ paṃcendriyasya paryāptakasyāvaseyā. itareṣāṃ yathāgamam avagamaḥ kartavyaḥ. 
 § 764. nāmagotrayor utkṛṣṭasthitipratipattyartham āha — 
 viṃśatir nāmagotrayoḥ || 
 § 765. ‘sāgaropamakoṭīkoṭyaḥ para sthitiḥ’ ity anuvartate. iyam api utkṛṣṭā sthitir mithyādṛṣṭeḥ saṃjñipaṃcendriyaparyāptakasya. itareṣāṃ yathāgamam avaboddhavyā. 
 § 766. athāyuṣaḥ kotkṛṣṭā sthitir ity ucyate — 
 trayastriṃśatsāgaropamāṇy āyuṣaḥ || 
 § 767. punaḥ ‘sāgaropama’ grahaṇaṃ koṭīkoṭīnivṛttyartham. ‘parā sthitiḥ’ ity anuvartate. iyam api pūvoktasyaiva. śeṣāṇām āgamato ’vaseyā. 
 § 768. uktotkṛṣṭā sthitiḥ. idānīṃ jaghanyā sthitir vaktavyā. tatra samānajaghanyasthitīḥ paṃca prakṛtīr avasthāpya tisṛṇāṃ jaghanyasthitipratipattyarthaṃ sūtradvayam upanasyate laghvartham — 
 aparā dvādaśa muhūrtā vedanīyasya || 
 § 769. aparā jaghanyā ity arthaḥ. vedanīyasya dvādaśa muhūrtāḥ. 
 nāmagotrayor aṣṭau || 
 § 770. ‘muhūrtā’ ity anuvartate. ‘aparā sthitiḥ’ iti ca. 
 § 771. avasthāpitaprakṛtijaghanyasthitipratipādanārtham āha — 
 śeṣāṇām antarmuhūrtā || 
 § 772. śeṣāṇām pañcānāṃ prakṛtīnām antarmuhūrtāparā sthitiḥ. jñānadarśanāvaraṇāntarāyāṇāṃ jaghanyā sthitiḥ sūkṣmasāṃparāye, mohanīyasya anivṛttibādarasāṃparāye. āyuṣaḥ saṃkhyeyavarṣāyuṣṣu tiryakṣu manuṣyeṣu ca. 
 § 773. āha, ubhayī sthitir abhihitā. jñānāvaraṇādīnām athānubhavaḥ kiṃ lakṣaṇa ity ata āha — 
 vipāko ’nubhavaḥ || 
 § 774. viśiṣṭo nānāvidho vā pāko vipākaḥ. puṛvoktakaṣāyatīvramandādibhāvāsravaviśeṣād viśiṣṭaḥ pāko vipākaḥ. athavā dravyakṣetrakālabhavabhāvalakṣaṇanimittabhedajanitavaiśvarūpyo nānāvidhaḥ pāko vipākaḥ. asāv anubhava ity ākhyāyate. śubhapariṇāmānāṃ prakarṣabhāvāc chubhaprakṛtīnāṃ prakṛṣṭo ’nubhavaḥ aśubhaprakṛtīnāṃ nikṛṣṭaḥ. aśubhapariṇāmānāṃ prakarṣabhāvād aśubhaprakṛtīnāṃ prakṛṣṭo ’nubhavaḥ śubhaprakṛtīnāṃ nikṛṣṭaḥ. sa evaṃ pratyayavaśād upātto ’nubhavo dvividhā pravartate svamukhena paramukhena ca. sarvāsāṃ mūlaprakṛtīnāṃ svamukhenaivānubhavaḥ. uttaraprakṛtīnāṃ tulyajātīyānāṃ paramukhenāpi bhavati āyurdarśanacāritramohavarjānām. na hi narakāyurmukhena tiryagāyurmanuṣyāyur vā vipacyate. nāpi darśanamohaś cāritramohamukhena, cāritramoho vā darśanamohamukhena. 
 § 775. āha abhyupemaḥ prāgupacitanānāprakārakarmavipāko ’nubhavaḥ. idaṃ tu na vijānīmaḥ kim ayam prasaṃkhyāto ’prasaṃkhyātaḥ? ity atrocyate prasaṃkhyāto ’nubhūyata iti brūmahe. kutaḥ? yataḥ — 
 sa yathānāma || 
 § 776. jñānāvaraṇasya phalaṃ jñānābhāvo darśanāvaraṇasyāpi phalaṃ darśanaśaktyuparodha ity evam ādy anvarthasaṃjñānirdeśāt sarvāsāṃ karmaprakṛtīnāṃ savikalpānām anubhavasaṃpratyayo jāyate. 
 § 777. āha, yadi vipāko ’nubhavaḥ pratijñāyate, tatkarmānubhūtaṃ sat, kim ābharaṇavadavatiṣṭhate āhosvin niṣpītasāraṃ pracyavate? ity atrocyate — 
 tataś ca nirjarā || 
 § 778. pīḍānugrahāv ātmane pradāyābhyavahṛṭaudanādivikāravatpūrvasthitikṣayād avasthānābhāvāt karmaṇo nivṛttir nirjarā. sā dviprakārā — vipākajā itarā ca. tatra caturgatāv anekajātiviśeṣāvaghūrṇite saṃsāramahārṇave ciraṃ paribhramataḥ śubhāśubhasya karmaṇaḥ krameṇa paripākakālaprāptasyānubhavodayāvalisroto ’nupravaviṣṭasyārabdhaphalasya yā nivṛttiḥ sā vipākajā nirjarā. yatkarmāprāptavipākakālam aupakramikakriyāviśeṣasāmarthyād anudīrṇaṃ balād udīryodayāvaliṃ praveśya vedyate āmrapanasādipākavat sā avipākajā nirjarā. ’ca’ śabdo nimittāntarasamuccayārthaḥ. ‘tapasā nirjarā ca’ iti vakṣyate tataś ca bhavati anyataś ceti sūtrārtho yojitaḥ. kim artham iha nirjarānirdeśaḥ kriyate, saṃvarāt parā nirdeṣṭavyā uddeśavat? laghvartham iha vacanam. tatra hi pāṭhe ‘vipāko ’nubhavaḥ’ iti punar anuvādaḥ kartavyaḥ syāt. 
 § 779. āha abhihito ’nubhavabandhaḥ. idānīṃ pradeśabandho vaktavyaḥ. tasmiṃś ca vaktavye sati ime nirdeṣṭavyāḥ — kiṃ hetavaḥ kadā kutaḥ kiṃ svabhāvāḥ kasmin kiṃ parimāṇaś ceti? tadartham idaṃ krameṇa parigṛhītapraśnāpekṣabhedaṃ sūtraṃ praṇīyate — 
 nāmapratyayāḥ sarvato yogaviśeṣāt sūkṣmaikakṣetrāvagāhasthitāḥ sarvātmapradeśeṣv anantānantapradeśāḥ || 
 § 780. nāmnaḥ pratyayā nāmapratyayāh ‘nāma’ iti sarvāḥ karmaprakṛtayo ’bhidhīyante; ‘sa yathānāma’ iti vacanāt. anena hetubhāva uktaḥ. sarveṣu bhaveṣu sarvataḥ ‘dṛśyante anyato ’pi’ iti tasi kṛte sarvataḥ. anena kālopādānaṃ iti kṛtam. ekaikasya hi jīvasyātikrāntā anantā bhavā āgāminaḥ saṃkhyeyā asaṃkhyeyā anantānantā vā bhavantīti. yogaviśeṣān nimittāt karmabhāvena pudgalā ādīyanta iti nimittaviśeṣanirdeśaḥ kṛto bhavati. ‘sūkṣma’ ādigrahaṇaṃ karmagrahaṇayogyapudgalasvabhāvānuvartanārtham, grahaṇayogyāḥ pudgalāḥ sūkṣmā na sthūlā iti. ‘ekakṣetrāvagāha’ vacanaṃ kṣetrāntaranivṛttyartham. ‘sthitāḥ’ iti vacanaṃ kriyāntaranivṛttyartham, sthitā na gacchanta iti. ‘sarvātmapradeśeṣu’ iti vacanam ādhāranirdeśārthaṃ naikapradeśādiṣu karmapradeśā vartante. kva tarhi? ūrdhvam adhas tiryak ca sarveṣv ātmapradeśeṣu vyāpya sthitā iti. ‘anantānantapradeśa’ vacanaṃ parimāṇāntaravyapohārtham, na saṃkhyeyā na cāsaṃkhyeyā nāpy anantā iti. te khalu pudgalaskandhā abhavyānantaguṇāḥ siddhānantabhāgapramitapradeśā ghanāṅgulasyāsaṃkhyeyabhāgakṣetrāvagāhina ekadvitricatuḥsaṃkhyeyasamayasthitikāḥ pañcavarṇapañcarasa-dvigandha-catuḥsparśasvabhāvā aṣṭavidhakarmaprakṛtiyogyā yogavaśād ātmanātmasāt kriyante. iti pradeśa-bandhaḥ samāsato veditavyaḥ. 
 § 781. āha, bandhapadārthāntaraṃ puṇyapāpopasaṃkhyānaṃ coditaṃ tadbandhe ’ntarbhūtam iti pratyākhyātam. tatredaṃ vaktavyaṃ ko ’tra puṇyabandhaḥ kaḥ pāpabandha iti. tatra puṇyaprakṛtiparigaṇanārtham idam ārabhyate — 
 sadvedyaśubhāyurnāmagotrāṇi puṇyam || 
 § 782. śubhaṃ praśastam iti yāvat. taduttaraiḥ pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate śubham āyuḥ śubhaṃ nāma śubhaṃ gotram iti. śubhāyus tritayaṃ tiryagāyur manuṣyāyur devāyur iti. śubhanāma saptatriṃśad vikalpam. tad yathā — manuṣyagatir devagatiḥ paṃcendriyajāti paṃca śarīrāṇi trīṇy aṅgopāṅgāni samacaturasrasaṃsthānaṃ vajrarṣabhanārācasaṃhananaṃ praśastavarṇarasagandhasparśā manuṣyadevagatyānupūrvyadvayam agurulaghuparaghātocchvāsātapodyotapraśastavihāyogatayas trasabādaraparyāptipratyekaśarīrasthiraśubhasubhagasusvarādeyayaśaḥkīrtayo nirmāṇaṃ tīrthakaranāma ceti. śubham ekam uccairgotraṃ, sadvedyam iti. etā dvācatvāriṃśatprakṛtayaḥ ‘puṇya’ saṃjñāḥ. 
 ato ’nyat pāpam || 
 § 783. asmat puṇyasaṃjñikarmaprakṛtisamūhād anyat karma ‘pāpam’ ity ucyate. tad dvyaśītividham. tad yathā — jñānāvaraṇasya prakṛtayaḥ paṃca darśanāvaraṇasya nava mohanīyasya ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ paṃcāntarāyasya narakagatitiryaggatī catasro jātayaḥ paṃca saṃsthānāni paṃca saṃhananānyapraśastavarṇarasagandhasparśā narakagatitiryaggatyānupūrvyadvayam upaghātāpraśastavihāyogatisthāvarasūkṣmāparyāptisādhāraṇaśarīrāsthirāśubhadurbhagaduḥsvarānādeyāyaśaḥkīrtayaś ceti nāmakṛtayaś catustriṃśat. asad vedyaṃ narakāyur nīcairgotram iti. evaṃ vyākhyātaḥ saprapañco bandhapadārthaḥ. avadhimanaḥparyayakevalajñānapratyakṣapramāṇagamyas tadupadiṣṭāgamānumeyaḥ. 
 iti tattvārthavṛttau sarvārthasiddhisaṃjñikāyāṃ aṣṭamo ’dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ || 8 || 
 
 
	  atha navamo ’dhyāyaḥ
	   §§ 784–919 
 § 784. bandhapadārtho nirdiṣṭaḥ. idānīṃ tadantaroddeśabhājaḥ saṃvarasya nirdeśaḥ prāptakāla ity ata idam āha — 
 āsravanirodhaḥ saṃvaraḥ || 
 § 785. abhinavakarmādānahetur āsravo vyākhyātaḥ. tasya nirodhaḥ saṃvara ity ucyate. sa dvividho bhāvasaṃvaro dravyasaṃvaraś ceti. tatra saṃsāranimittakriyānivṛttir bhāvasaṃvaraḥ. tannirodhe tatpūrvakarmapudgalādānavicchedo dravyasaṃvaraḥ. 
 § 786. idaṃ vicāryate — kasmin guṇasthāne kasya saṃvara iti? atra ucyate — mithyādarśanakarmodayavaśīkṛta ātmā mithyādṛṣṭiḥ. tatra mithyādarśanaprādhānyena yatkarma āsravati tannirodhāc cheṣe sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyādau tatsaṃvaro bhavati. kiṃ punas tat? mithyātvanapuṃsakavedanarakāyur narakagatyekadvitricaturindriyajātihuṇḍasaṃsthānāsaṃprāptāsṛpāṭikāsaṃhanananarakagatiprāyogyānupūrvyātapasthāvarasūkṣmāparyāptakasādhāraṇaśarīrasaṃjñakaṣoḍaśaprakṛtilakṣaṇam. 
 § 787. asaṃyamas trividhaḥ; anantānubandhyapratyākhyānapratyākhyānodayavikalpāt. tatpratyayasya karmaṇas tadabhāve saṃvaro ’vaseyaḥ. tad yathā — nidrānidrāpracalāpracalāstyānagṛddhyanantānubandhikrodhamānamāyālobhastrīvedatiryagāyustiryaggaticatuḥ-saṃsthānacatuḥsaṃhananatiryaggatiprāyogyānupūrvyodyotāpraśastavihāyogatidurbhagaduḥsvarānādeyanīcairgotrasaṃjñikānāṃ pañcaviṃśatiprakṛtīnām anantānubandhikaṣāyodayakṛtāsaṃyamapradhānāsravāṇām ekendriyādayaḥ sāsādanasamyagdṛṣṭyantā bandhakāḥ. tadabhāve tāsām uttaratra saṃvaraḥ. apratyākhyānāvaraṇakrodhamānamāyālobhamanuṣyāyurmanuṣyagatyaudārikaśarīratadaṅgopāṅgavajrarṣabhanārācasaṃhananamanuṣyagatiprāyogyānupūrvyanāmnā daśānāṃ prakṛtīnām apratyākhyānakaṣāyodayakṛtāsaṃyamahetukānām ekendriyādayo ’saṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyantā bandhakāḥ. tadabhāvād ūrdhvaṃ tāsāṃ saṃvaraḥ. samyaṅmithyātvaguṇenāyur na badhyate. pratyākhyānāvaraṇakrodhamānamāyālobhānāṃ catasṛṇāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ pratyākhyānakaṣāyodayakāraṇāsaṃyamāsravāṇām ekendriyaprabhṛtayaḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāvasānā bandhakāḥ. tadabhāvād upariṣṭāt tāsāṃ saṃvaraḥ. pramādopanītasya tadabhāve nirodhaḥ. pramādenopanītasya karmaṇaḥ pramattasaṃyatād ūrdhvaṃ tadabhāvān nirodhaḥ pratyetavyaḥ. kiṃ punas tat. asadvedyāratiśokāsthirāśubhāyaśaḥkīrtivikalpam. devāyurbandhārambhasya pramāda eva hetur apramādo ’pi tat pratyāsannaḥ. tadūrdhvaṃ tasya saṃvaraḥ. kaṣāya evāsravo yasya karmaṇo na pramādādiḥ tasya tannirodhe nirāso ’vaseyaḥ. sa ca kaṣāyaḥ pramādādivirahitas tīvramadhyamajaghanyabhāvena triṣu guṇasthāneṣu vyavasthitaḥ. tatrāpūrvakaraṇasyādau saṃkhyeyabhāge dve karmaprakṛtī nidrāpracale badhyete. tata ūrdhvaṃ saṃkhyeyabhāge triṃśat prakṛtayo devagatipañcendriyajātivaikriyikāhārakataijasakārmaṇaśarīrasamacaturasrasaṃsthānavaikriyikāhārakaśarīrāṃgopāṃgavarṇagandharasasparśadevagatiprāyogyānupūrvyāgurulaghūpaghātaparaghātocchvāsapraśastavihāyogatitrasabādaraparyāptapratyekaśarīrasthiraśubhasubhagasusvarādeyanirmāṇatīrthakarākhyā badhyante. tasyaiva caramasamaye catasraḥ prakṛtayo hāsyaratibhayajugupsāsaṃjñā bandham upayānti. tā etās tīvrakaṣāyāsravās tadabhāvān nirddiṣṭād bhāgād ūrdhvaṃ saṃvriyante. anivṛttibādarasāṃparāyasyādisamayād ārabhya saṃkhyeyeṣu bhāgeṣu puṃvedakrodhasaṃjvalanau badhyete. tata ūrdhvaṃ śeṣeṣu saṃkhyeyeṣu bhāgeṣu mānasaṃjvalanamāyāsaṃjvalanau bandham upagacchataḥ. tasyaiva caramasamaye lobhasaṃjvalano bandham eti. tā etāḥ prakṛtayo madhyamakaṣāyāsravās tadabhāve nirdiṣṭasya bhāgasyopariṣṭāt saṃvaram āpnuvanti. pañcānāṃ jñānāvaraṇānāṃ caturṇāṃ darśanāvaraṇānāṃ yaśaḥkīrter uccairgotrasya pañcānām antarāyāṇāṃ ca mandakaṣāyāsravāṇāṃ sūkṣmasāṃparāyo bandhakaḥ. tadabhāvād uttararatra teṣāṃ saṃvaraḥ. kevalenaiva yogena sadvedyasopaśāntakaṣāyakṣīṇakaṣāyasayogānāṃ bandho bhavati. tadabhāvād ayogakevalinas tasya saṃvaro bhavati. 
 § 788. uktaḥ saṃvaras taddhetupratipādanārtham āha — 
 sa guptisamitidharmānuprekṣāpariṣahajayacāritraiḥ ||
