 § 789. yataḥ saṃsārakāraṇād ātmano gopanaṃ bhavati sā guptiḥ. prāṇipīḍāparihārārthaṃ samyagayanaṃ samitiḥ. iṣṭe sthāne dhatte iti dharmaḥ. śarīrādīnāṃ svabhāvānucintanam anuprekṣā. kṣudādivedanotpattau karmanirjarārthaṃ sahanaṃ pariṣahaḥ. pariṣahasya jayaḥ pariṣahajayaḥ. cāritraśabda ādisūtre vyākhyātārthaḥ. eteṣāṃ guptyādīnāṃ saṃvaraṇakriyāyāḥ sādhakatamatvād karaṇanirdeśaḥ. saṃvaro ’dhikṛto ’pi ‘sa’ iti tacchabdena parāmṛśyate guptyādibhiḥ sākṣāt saṃbandhanārthaḥ. kiṃ prayojanam? avadhāraṇārtham. sa eṣa saṃvaro guptyādibhir eva nānyenopāyeneti. tena tīrthābhiṣekadīkṣāśīrṣopahāradevatārādhananādayo nivartitā bhavanti; rāgadveṣamohopāttasya karmaṇo ’nyathā nivṛttyabhāvāt. 
 § 790. saṃvaranirjarāhetuviśeṣapratipādanārtham āha — 
 tapasā nirjarā ca || 
 § 791. tapo dharme ’ntarbhūtam api pṛthagucyate ubhayasādhanatvakhyāpanārthaṃ saṃvaraṃ prati prādhānyapratipādanārthaṃ ca. nanu ca tapo ’bhudayāṃgam iṣtaṃ devendrādisthānaprāptihetutvābhyupagamāt, tat kathaṃ nirjarāṃgaṃ syād iti? naiṣa doṣaḥ; ekasyānekakāryadarśanād agnivat. yathāgnir eko ’pi vikledanabhasmāṃgārādiprayojana upalabhyate tathā tapo ’bhudayakarmakṣayahetur ity atra ko virodhaḥ. 
 § 792. saṃvarahetuṣv ādāv uddiṣṭāyā gupteḥ svarūpapratipattyartham āha — 
 samyagyoganigraho guptiḥ || 
 § 793. yogo vyākhyātaḥ ‘kāyavāṅmanaḥkarma yogaḥ’ ity atra. tasya svecchāpravṛttinivartanaṃ nigrahaḥ. viṣayasukhābhilāṣārthapravṛttiniṣedhārthaṃ samyagviśeṣaṇam. tasmāt samyagviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭāt saṃkleśāprādurbhāvaparātkāyādiyoganirodhe sati tannimittaṃ karma nāsravatīti saṃvaraprasiddhir avagantavyā. sā tritayī kāyaguptir vāgguptir manoguptir iti. 
 § 794. tatrāśaktasya muner niravadyapravṛttikhyāpanārtham āha — 
 īryābhāṣaiṣaṇādānanikṣepotsargāḥ samitayaḥ || 
 § 795. ‘samyag’ ity anuvartate. teneryādayo viśeṣyante. samyagīryā samyagbhāṣā samyageṣaṇā samyagādānanikṣepau samyagutsarga iti. sā etāḥ pañca samitayo viditajīvasthānādividher muneḥ prāṇipīḍāparihārābhyupāyā veditavyāḥ. tathā pravartamānsyāsaṃyamapariṇāmanimittakarmāsravāt saṃvaro bhavati. 
 § 796. tṛitīyasya saṃvarahetor dharmasya bhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 uttamakṣamāmārdavārjavasaucasatyasaṃyamatapastyāgākiṃcanyabrahmacaryāṇi dharmaḥ || 
 § 797. kim artham idam ucyate? ādyaṃ pravṛttinigrahārtham, tatrāsamarthānāṃ pravṛttyupāyadarśanārtham dvitīyam. idaṃ punar daśāvidhadharmākhyānaṃ samitiṣu pravartamānasya pramādaparihārārthaṃ veditavyam. śarīrasthitihetumārgaṇārthaṃ parakulāny upagacchato bhikṣor duṣṭajanākrośaprahasanāvajñātāḍanaśarīravyāpādanādīnāṃ saṃnidhāne kāluṣyānupattiḥ kṣamā. jātyādimadāveśād abhimānābhāvo mārdavaṃ mānanirharaṇam. yogasyāvarkratā ārjavam. prakarśaprāptalobhān nivṛttiḥ śaucam. satsu praśasteṣu janeṣu sādhu vacanaṃ satyam ity ucyate. nanu caitad bhāṣāsamitāv antarbhavati? naiṣa doṣaḥ; samitau pravartamāno muniḥ sādhuṣv asādhuṣu ca bhāṣāvyavahāraṃ kurvan hitaṃ mitaṃ ca brūyāt anyathā rāgād anarthadaṇḍadoṣaḥ syād iti vāksamitir ity arthaḥ. iha punaḥ saṃtaḥ pravrajitās tadbhaktā vā teṣu sādhu satyaṃ jñānacāritraśikṣaṇādiṣu bahvapi kartavyam ity anujñāyate dharmopabṛṃhaṇārtham. samitiṣu vartamānasya prāṇīndriya -parihāras saṃyamaḥ. karmakṣayārthaṃ tapyata iti tapaḥ. taduttrartra vakṣyamāṇaṃ dvādaśavikalpam avaseyam. saṃyatasya yogyaṃ jñānādidānaṃ tyāgaḥ. upātteṣv api śarīrādiṣu saṃskārāpohāya mamedam ity abhisandhinivṛttir ākiṃcanyam. nāsya kiṃcanāstīty akiṃcanaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ karma vā ākiṃcanyam. anubhūtāṅganāsmaraṇakathāśravaṇastrīsaṃsaktaśayanāsanādivarjanād brahmacaryaṃ paripūrṇam avatiṣṭhate. svatantravṛttinirvṛttyartho vā gurukulavāso brahmacaryam. dṛṣṭaprayojanaparivarjanārtham uttamaviśeṣaṇam. tāny evaṃ bhāvyamānāni dharmavyapadeśabhāñjisvaguṇapraptipakṣadoṣasadbhāvanāpraṇihitāni saṃvarakāraṇāni bhavanti. 
 § 798. āha, krodhādyanutpattiḥ kṣamādiviśeṣapratyanīkālambanād ity uktam. tatra kasmāt kṣamādīn ayam avalambate nānyathā pravartata ity ucyate. yasmāt taptāyaḥpiṇḍavatkṣamādipariṇatenātmahitaiṣiṇā kartavyāḥ — 
 anityāśaraṇasaṃsāraikatvānyatvāśucyāsravasaṃvaranirjarālokabodhidurlabhadharmasvākhyātatvānucintanam anuprekṣāḥ || 
 § 799. imāni śarīrendriyaviṣayopabhogadravyāṇi samudayarūpāṇi jalabudbudvadanavasthitasvabhāvāni garbhādiṣv avasthāviśeṣeṣu sadupalabhyamānasaṃyogaviparyayāṇi, mohād atrājño nityatāṃ manyate. na kiṃcit saṃsāre samuditaṃ dhruvam asti ātmano jñānadarśanopayogasvabhāvād anyad iti cintanam anityatānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asya bhavyasya cintayatas teṣv abhiṣv aṅgābhāvād bhuktojjhitagandhamālyādiṣv iva viyogakāle ’pi vinipāto notpadyate. 
 § 800. yathā — mṛgaśāvasyaikānte balavatā kṣudhitenāmiṣaiṣiṇā vyāghreṇābhibhūtasya na kiṃcic charaṇam asti, tathā janmajarāmṛtyuvyādhiprabhṛtivyasanamadhye paribhramato jantoḥ śaraṇaṃ na vidyate. paripuṣtam api śarīraṃ bhojanaṃ prati sahāyībhavati na vyasanopanipāte. yatnena saṃcitā arthā api na bhavāntaram anugacchanti. saṃvibhaktasukhaduḥkhāḥ suhṛdo ’pi na maraṇakāle paritrāyante. bāndhavāḥ samuditāś ca rujā parītaṃ na paripālayanti. asti cet sucarito dharmo vyasanamahārṇave taraṇopāyayo bhavati. mṛtyunā nīyamānasya sahasranayanādayo ’pi na śaraṇam. tasmād bhavavyasanasaṃkaṭe dharma eva śaraṇam. suhṛdartho ’py anapāyī, nānyakiṃcic charaṇam iti bhāvanā aśaraṇānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asyādhyavasyato nityam aśaraṇo ’smīti bhṛśam udvignasya sāṃsārikeṣu bhāveṣu mamatvavigamo bhavati. bhagavadarhatsarvajñapraṇīta eva mārge prayatno bhavati. 
 § 801. karmavipākavaśād ātmano bhavāntarāvāptiḥ saṃsāraḥ. sa purastāt pañcavidhaparivartanarūpeṇa vyākhyātaḥ. tasminn anekayonikulakoṭibahuśatasahasrasaṃkaṭe saṃsāre paribhraman jīvaḥ karmayantrapreritaḥ pitā bhūtvā bhrātā putraḥ pautraś ca bhavati. mātā bhūtvā bhaginī bhāryā duhitā ca bhavati. svāmī bhūtvā dāso bhavati. dāso bhūtvā svāmy api bhavati. naṭa iva raṅge. athavā kiṃ bahunā, svayam ātmanaḥ putro bhavatīty evam ādi saṃsārasvabhāvacintanaṃ saṃsārānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asya bhāvayataḥ saṃsāraduḥkhabhayād udvignasya tato nirvedo bhavati. nirviṇṇaś ca saṃsāragrahāṇāya prayatate. 
 § 802. janmajarāmaraṇāvṛttimahāduḥkhānubhavanaṃ prati eka evāhaṃ na kaścin me svaḥ paro vā vidyate. eka eva jāye ’ham. eka eva mriye. na me kaścit svajanaḥ parajano vā vyādhijarāmaraṇādīni duḥkhāny apaharati. bandhumitrāṇi smaśānaṃ nātivartante. dharma eva me sahāyaḥ sadā anapāyīti cintanam ekatvānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asya bhāvayataḥ svajaneṣu prītyanubandho na bhavati. parajaneṣu ca dveṣānubandho nopajāyate. tato niḥsaṅgatām abhyupagato mokṣāyaiva ghaṭate. 
 § 803. śarīrād anyatvacintanam anyatvānuprekṣā. tad yathā — bandhaṃ pratyekatve saty api lakṣaṇabhedād anyo ’ham aindriyakaṃ śarīram atīndriyo ’ham ajñaṃ śarīraṃ jño ’ham anityaṃ śarīraṃ nityo ’ham ādy antavaccharīram anādyananto ’ham. bahuni me śarīraśatasahasrāṇy atītāni saṃsāre paribhramataḥ. sa evāham anyas tebhya ity evaṃ me kim aṅga, punarbāhyebhyaḥ parigrahebhyaḥ ity evaṃ hy asya manaḥ samādadhānasya śarīrādiṣu sprhā notpadyate. tatas tattvajñānabhāvanāpūrvake vairāgyaprakarṣe sati ātyantikasya mokṣasukhasyāvāptir bhavati. 
 § 804. śarīram idam atyantāśuciyoni śukraśonitāśucisaṃvardhitam avaskaravadaśucibhājanaṃ tvaṅmātrapracchāditam atipūtirasaniṣyandisrotobilam aṅgāravadātmabhāvam āśritam apy āśvevāpādayati. snānānulepanadhūpapragharṣavāsamālyādibhir api na śakyam aśucitvam apahartum asya. samyagdarśanādi punarbhāvyamānaṃ jīvasyātyantikīṃ śuddhim āvirbhāvayatīti tattvato bhāvanam aśucitavānuprekṣā. evam hy asya saṃsmarataḥ śarīranirvedo bhavati. nirviṇṇaś ca janmodadhitaraṇāya cittaṃ samādhatte. 
 § 805. āsravasaṃvaranirjarāḥ pūrvoktā api ihopanyasyante tadgataguṇadoṣabhāvanārtham. tad yathā — āsravā ihāmutrāpāyayuktā mahānadīsrotovegatīkṣṇā indriyakaṣāyā vratādayaḥ. *  tatrendriyāṇi tāvat sparśanādīni vanagajavāyasapannagapataṅgahariṇādīn vyavasanārṇavam avagāhayanti tathā kaṣādayo ’pīha vadhabandhāpayaśaḥparikleśādīn janayanti. amutra ca nānāgatiṣu bahuvidhaduḥkhaprajvalitāsu paribhramayantīty evam āsravadoṣānucintanam āsravānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asya cintayataḥ kṣamādiṣu śreyas tv abuddhir na pracyavate. sarva ete āsravadoṣāḥ kūrmavatsaṃvṛtātmano na bhavanti. 
 § 806. yathā mahārṇave nāvo vivarapidhāne ’sati kramāt sratajalābhiplave sati tadāśrayāṇāṃ vināśo ’vaśyaṃbhāvī, *  chidrapidhāne ca nirupadravam abhilaṣitadeśāntaraprāpaṇaṃ, tathā karmāgamadvārasaṃvaraṇe sati nāsti śreyaḥpratibandha iti saṃvaraguṇānucintanaṃ saṃvarānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asya cintayataḥ saṃvare nityodyuktatā bhavati. tataś ca niḥśreyasapadaprāptir iti. 
 § 807. nirjarā vedanāvipāka ity uktam. sā dvedhā — abuddhipūrvā kuśalamūlā ceti. tatra narakādiṣu karmaphalavipākajā abuddhipūrvā sā akuśalānubandhā. pariṣahajaye kṛte kuśalamūlā sā śubhānubandhā niranubandhā ceti. ity evaṃ nirjarāyā guṇadoṣabhāvanaṃ nirjarānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asyānusmarataḥ karmanirjarāyai pravṛttir bhavati. 
 § 808. lokasaṃsthānādividhir vyākhyātaḥ samantād anantasyālokākāśasya bahumadhyadeśabhāvino lokasya saṃsthānādividhir vyākhyātaḥ. tatsvabhāvānucintanaṃ lokānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asyādhyavasyatas tattvajñānaviśuddhir bhavati. 
 § 809. ekasmin nigotaśarīre jīvāḥ siddhānām anantaguṇāḥ. evaṃ sarvaloko nirantaraṃ nicitaḥ sthāvarair atas tatra trasatā vālukāsamudre patitā vajrasikatākaṇikeva durlabhā. tatra ca vikalendriyāṇāṃ bhūyiṣṭhatvāt pañcendriyatā guṇeṣu kṛtajñateva kṛcchralabhyā. tatra ca tiryaṃkṣu paśumṛgapakṣisarīsṛpādiṣu bahuṣu satsu manuṣyabhāvaś catuṣpathe ratnarāśir iva durāsadaḥ. tatpracyave ca punas tadutpattir dagdhatarupudgalatadbhāvopapattivad durlabhā. tallābhe ca deśakulendriyasaṃpannīrogatvāny uttarottaratto ’tidurlabhāni. sarveṣv api teṣu labdheṣu saddharmapratilambho yadi na syād vyarthaṃ janma vadanam iva dṛṣṭivikalam. tam evaṃ kṛcchalabhyaṃ dharmam avāpya viṣayasukhe rañjanaṃ bhasmārthacandanadahanam iva viphalam. viraktaviṣayasukhasya tu tapobhāvanādharmaprabhāvanāsukhamaraṇādilakṣaṇaḥ samādhir duravāpaḥ. tasmin sati bodhilābhaḥ phalavān bhavatīti cintanaṃ bodhidurlabhānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asya bhāvayato bodhiṃ prāpya pramādo na kadācid api bhavati. 
 § 810. ayaṃ jinopadiṣṭo dharmo ’hiṃsālakṣaṇaḥ satyādiṣṭhito vinayamūlaḥ. kṣamābalo bhrahmacaryagupta upaśamapradhānī niyatilakṣaṇo niṣparigrahatālambanaḥ. asyālābhād anādisaṃsāre jīvāḥ paribhramanti duṣkarmavipākajaṃ duḥkham anubhavantaḥ. asya punaḥ pratilambhe vividhābhudayaprāptipūrvikā niḥśreyasopalabdir niyateti cintanaṃ dharmasvākhyātatvānuprekṣā. evaṃ hy asya cintayato dharmānurāgāt sadā pratiyatno bhavati. 
 § 811. evam anityatvādyanuprekṣāsaṃnidhāne uttamakṣamādidhāraṇān mahān saṃvaro bhavati. madhye ‘anuprekṣā’ vacanam ubhayārtham. anuprekṣā hi bhāvayann uttamakṣmādīṃś ca pratipālayati parīṣahāṃś ca jetum utsahate. 
 § 812. ke punas te pariṣahāḥ kim arthaṃ vā te sahyanta itīdam āha — 
 mārgācyavananirjarārthaṃ pariṣahoḍhavyāḥ parīṣahāḥ || 
 § 813. saṃvarasya prakṛtatvāt tena mārgo viśiṣyate. saṃvaramārga iti. tadacyavanārthaṃ nirjarārthaṃ ca pariṣoḍhavyāḥ parīṣahāḥ. kṣutpipāsādisahanaṃ kurvantaḥ jinopadiṣṭān mārgād apracyavamānās tanmārgaparikramaṇaparicayena karmāgamadvāraṃ saṃvṛṇvanta aupakramikaṃ karmaphalam anubhavantaḥ krameṇa nirjīrṇakarmāṇo mokṣam āpnuvanti. 
 § 814. tatsvarūpasaṃkhyāsaṃpratipattyartham āha — 
 kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇadaṃśamaśakanāgnyāratistrīcaryāniṣadyāśayyākrośavadhayācanālābharogatṛṇasparśamalasatkārapuraskāraprajñājñānādarśanāni || 
 § 815. kṣudādayo vedanāviśeṣā dvāviṃśatiḥ. eteṣāṃ sahanaṃ mokṣārthinā kartavyam. tad yathā — bhikṣor niravadyāhāragaveṣiṇas tadalābhe īṣallābhe ca anivṛttavedanasyākāle adeśe ca bhikṣāṃ prati nivṛtteccchasyāvaśyakaparihāṇiṃ manāg apy asahamānasya svādhyāyadhyānabhāvanāparasya bahukṛtvaḥ svakṛtaparakṛtānaśanāvam audaryasya nīrasāhārasya saṃtaptabhrāṣṭrapatitajalabindukatipayavatsahasā pariśuṣkapānasyodīrṇakṣudvedanasyāpi sato bhikṣālābhād alābham adhikaguṇaṃ manyamānasya kṣudbādhāṃ pratyacintanaṃ kṣudvijayaḥ. 
 § 816. jalasnānāvagāhanapariṣekaparityāginaḥ patatrivadaniyatāsanāvasathasyātilavaṇasnigdharūkṣaviruddhāhāragraiṣmātapapittajvarānaśanādibhir udīrṇāṃ śarīrendriyonmāthinīṃ pipāsāṃ pratyanādriyamāṇapratīkārasya pipāsānalaśikhāṃ dhṛtinavamṛdghaṭapūritaśītalasugandhisamādhivāriṇā praśamayataḥ pipāsāsahanaṃ praśasyate. 
 § 817. parityaktapracchādanasya pakṣivadanavadhāritālayasya vṛkṣamūlapathiśilātalādiṣu himānīpatanaśītalānilasaṃpāte tatpratikāraprāptiṃ prati nivṛttecchasya pūrvānubhūtaśītapratikārahetuvastūnām asmarato jñānabhāvanāgarbhāgāre vasataḥ śītavedanāsahanaṃ parikīrtyate. 
 § 818. nivāte nirjale grīṣmaravikiraṇapariśuṣkapatitaparṇavyapetacchāyātaruṇyaṭavyantare yadṛcchayopanipatitasyānaśanādyabhyantarasādhanotpāditadāhasya davāgnidāhaparuṣavātātapajanitagalatāluśoṣasya tatpratīkārahetūn bahūn anubhūtān acintayataḥ prāṇipīḍāparihārāvahitacetasaś cāritrarakṣaṇam uṣṇasahanam ity upavarṇyate. 
 § 819. ‘daṃśamaśaka’ grahaṇam upalakṣaṇam. yathā  kākebhyo rakṣyatāṃ sarpiḥ  iti upaghātakopalakṣaṇaṃ kākagrahaṇaṃ, tena daṃśamaśakamakṣikāpiśukaputtikāmatkuṇakīṭapipīlikāvṛścikādayo gṛhyante. tatkṛtāṃ bādhāmapratīkārāṃ sahamānasya teṣāṃ bādhāṃ tridhāpyakurvāṇasya nirvāṇaprāptimātrasaṃkalpaprāvaraṇasya tadvedanāsahanaṃ daṃśamaśakapariṣahakṣamety ucyate. 
 § 820. jātarūpavanniṣkalaṃkajātarūpadhāraṇamaśakyaprārthanīyaṃ yācanarakṣaṇahiṃsanādidoṣavinirmuktaṃ niṣparigrahatvān nirvāṇaprāptiṃ pratyekaṃ sādhanam ananyabādhanaṃ nāgnyaṃ bibhrato manovikriyāviplutivirahāt strīrūpāṇy atyantāśucikuṇaparūpeṇa bhāvayato rātrindivaṃ brahmacaryam akhaṇḍam ātiṣṭhamānasyācelavratadhāraṇam anavadyam avagantavyam. 
 § 821. saṃyatasyendriyeṣṭaviṣayasaṃbandhaṃ prati nirutsakasya gītanṛtyavāditrādivirahiteṣu śūnyāgāradevakulatarukoṭaraśilāguhādiṣu svādhāyadhyānabhāvanāratim āskandato dṛṣṭaśrutānubhūtaratismaraṇatatkathāśravaṇakāmaśarapraveśanirvivarahṛdayasya prāṇiṣu sadā sadayasyāratipariṣahajayo ’vaseyaḥ. 
 § 822. ekānteṣv ārāmabhavanādipradeśeṣu navayauvanamadavibhramamadirāpānapramattāsu pramadāsu bādhamānāsu kūrmavatsaṃvṛtendriyavikārasya lalitasmitamṛdukathitasavilāsavīkṣaṇaprahasanamadamantharagamanamanmathaśaravyāpāraviphalīkaraṇasya strībādhāpariṣahanam avagantavyam. 
 § 823. dīrghakālam uṣitagurukulabrahmacaryasyādhigatabandhamokṣapadārthatattvasya saṃyamāyatanabhaktihetor deśāntarātither guruṇābhyanujñātasya pavanavanniḥsaṃgatām aṅgīkurvato bahuśo ’naśanāvamaudaryavṛttiparisaṃkhyānarasaparityāgādibādhāpariklāntakāyasya deśakālapramāṇāpetam adhvagamanaṃ saṃyamavirodhi pariharato nirākṛtapādāvaraṇasya paruṣaśarkarākaṇṭakādivyadhanajātacaraṇakhedasyāpi sataḥ pūrvocitayānavāhanādigamanam asmarato yathākālam āvaśyakāparihāṇimāskandataś caryāpariṣahasahanam avaseyam. 
 § 824. smaśānodyānaśūnyāyatanagiriguhāgahvarādiṣv anabhyastapūrveṣu nivasata ādityaprakāśasvendriyajñānaparīkṣitapradeśe kṛtaniyamakriyasya niṣadyāṃ niyamitakālām āsthitavataḥ siṃhavyāghrādivividhabhīṣaṇadhvaniśravanān nivṛttabhayasya caturvidhopasargasahanād apracyutamokṣamārgasya vīrāsanotkuṭikādyāsanād avicalitavigrahasya tatkṛtabādhān sahanaṃ niṣadyāpariṣahavijaya iti niścīyate. 
 § 825. svādhyāyadhyānādhvaśramaparikheditasya mauhūrtikīṃ kharaviṣam apracuraśarkarākapālasaṃkaṭātiśītoṣṇeṣu bhūmipradeśeṣu nidrām anubhavato yathākṛtaikaparśvadaṇḍāyitādiśāyinaḥ prāṇibādhāparihārāya patitadāruvad vyapagatāsuvadaparivartamānasya jñānabhāvanāvahitacetaso ’nuṣṭhitavyantarādivividhopasargād apy acalitavigrahasyāniyamitakālāṃ tatkṛtabādhāṃ kṣamamāṇasya śayyā pariṣahakṣamā kathyate. 
 § 826. mithyādarśanodṛiktāmarṣaparuṣāvajñānindāsabhyavacanāni krodhāgniśikhāpravardhanāni niśṛṇvato ’pi tadartheṣv asamāhitacetasaḥ sahasā tatpratīkāraṃ kartum api śaknuvataḥ pāpakarmavipākam abhicintayatas tāny ākarṇya tapaścaraṇabhāvanāparasya kaṣāyaviṣalavamātrasyāpy anavakāśam ātmahṛdayaṃ kurvata ākrośapariṣahasahanam avadhāryate. 
 § 827. niśitaviśasanamuśalamudgarādripraharaṇatāḍanādibhir vyāpādyamānaśarīrasya vyāpādakeṣu manāg api manovikāram akurvato mama purākṛtaduṣkarmaphalam idam ime varākāḥ kiṃ kurvanti, śarīram idaṃ jalabudbudvadviśaraṇasvabhāvaṃ vyasanakāraṇam etair bābādhyate, saṃjñānadarśanacāritrāṇi mama na kenacid upahanyante iti cintayato vāsitakṣaṇacandanānulepanasamadarśino vadhapariṣahakṣamā manyate. 
 § 828. bāhyābhyantaratapo ’nuṣṭhānaparasya tadbhāvanāvaśena nissārīkṛtamūrteḥ paṭutapanatāpaniṣpītasārataror iva virahitacchāyasya tvagasthiśirājālamātratanuyantrasya prāṇātyaye saty apy āhārabasatibheṣajādīni dīnābhidhānamukhavaivarṇyāṅgasaṃjñādibhir ayācamānasya bhikṣākāle ’pi vidyududyotavad durupalakṣyamūrter yācanāpariṣahasahanam avasīyate. 
 § 829. vāyuvadasaṅgād anekadeśacāriṇo ’bhupagataikakālasaṃbhojanasya vācaṃyamasya tatsamitasya vā sakṛtsvatanudarśanamātratantrasya pāṇipuṭamātrapātrasya bahuṣu divaseṣu bahuṣu ca gṛheṣu bhikṣām anavāpyāpy asaṃkliṣṭacetaso dātṛviśeṣaparīkṣānirutsukasya lābhād apy alābho me paramaṃ tapa iti saṃtuṣṭasyālābhavijayo ’vaseyaḥ. 
 § 830. sarvāśucinidhānam idam anityam aparitrāṇam iti śarīre niḥsaṃkalpatvād vigatasaṃskārasya guṇaratnabhāṇḍasaṃcayapravardhanasaṃrakṣaṇasaṃdhāraṇakāraṇatvād abhyupagatasthitividhānasyākṣamrakṣaṇavad vraṇānulepanavad vā bahūpakāram āhāram abhupagacchato viruddhāhārapānasevanavaiṣamyajanitavātādivikārarogasya yugapad anekaśatasaṃkhyavyādhiprakope saty api tadvaśavartitāṃ vijahato jallauṣadhiprāptyādyanekatapoviśeṣarddhiyoge saty api śarīranisspṛhatvāt tatpratikārānapekṣiṇo rogapariṣahasahanam avagantavyam. 
 § 831. tṛṇagrahanam upalakṣaṇaṃ kasyācid vyadhanaduḥkhakāraṇasya. tena śuṣkatṛṇaparuṣaśarkarākaṇṭakaniśitamṛttikāśūlādivyadhanakṛtapādavedanāprāptau satyāṃ tatrāpraṇihitatacetasaś caryāśayyāniṣadyāsu prāṇipīḍāparihāre nityam apramattacetasas tṛṇādisparśabādhāpariṣahavijayo veditavyaḥ. 
 § 832. apkāyikajantupīḍāparihārāyāmaraṇād asnānavratadhāriṇaḥ paṭur avikiraṇapratāpajanitaprasvedāktapavanānītapāṃsunicayasya sidhmakacchūdadrūdīrṇakaṇḍūyāyām utpannāyām api kaṇḍūyanavimardanasaṃghaṭṭanavivarjitamūrtheḥ svagatamalopacayaparagatamalāpacayayor asaṃkalpitamanasaḥ sajjñānacāritravimalasalilaprakṣālanena karmamalapaṃkanirākaraṇāya nityam udyatamater malapīḍāsahanam ākhyāyate. 
 § 833. satkāraḥ pūjāpraśaṃsātmakaḥ. puraskāro nāma kriyārambhādiṣv agrataḥ karaṇam āmaṃtraṇaṃ vā, tatrānādaro mayi kriyate. ciroṣitabrahmacaryasya mahātapasvinaḥ svaparasamayanirṇajñasya bahukṛtvaḥ paravādivijayinaḥ praṇāmabhaktisaṃbrahmāsanapradānādīni me na kaścit karoti. *  mithyādṛṣṭaya evātīva bhaktim antaḥ kiṃcid ajānantam api sarvajñasaṃbhāvanayā saṃmānya svasamayaprabhāvanaṃ kurvanti. vyantarādayaḥ purā atyugratapasāṃ pratyagrapūjāṃ nirvartayantīti mithyā śrutir yadi na syād idānīṃ kasmān mādṛśāṃ na kurvantīti duṣpraṇidhānavirahitacittasya satkārapuraskārapariṣahavijaya iti vijñāyate. 
 § 834. aṅgapūrvaprakīrṇakaviśāradasya śabdanyāyādhyātmanipuṇasya mama purastāditare bhāskaraprabhābhibhūtakhadyotodyotavannitarāṃ nāvabhāsanta iti vijñānamadanirāsaḥ prajñāpariṣahajayaḥ pratyetavyaḥ. 
 § 835. ajño ’yaṃ na vetti paśusama ity evam ādy adhikeṣpavacanaṃ sahamānasya paramaduścaratapo ’nuṣṭhāyino nityam apramattacetaso me ’dyāpi jñānātiśayo notpadyata iti anabhisaṃdadhato ’jñānapariṣahajayo ’vagantavyaḥ. 
 § 836. paramavairāgyabhāvanāśuddhahṛdayasya viditasakalapadārthatattvasyārhadāyatanasadhudharmapūjakasya cirantanapravrajitasyādyāpi me jñānātiśayo notpadyate. mahopavāsādyanuṣṭhāyināṃ prātihāryaviśeṣāḥ prādur abhūvann iti pralāpamātram anarthikeyaṃ pravrajyā. viphalaṃ vrataparipālanam ity evam asamādadhānasya darśanaviśuddhiyogād adarśanapariṣahasahanam avasātavyam. 
 § 837. evaṃ pariṣahān asaṃkalpopasthitān sahamānasyāsaṃkliṣṭacetaso rāgādipariṇāmāsravanirodhān mahān saṃvaro bhavati. 
 § 838. āha, kim ime pariṣahāḥ sarve saṃsāramahāṭavīm atikramitum abhyudyatam abhidravanti uta kaścit prativiśeṣa ity atrocyate — amī vyākhyātalakṣaṇāḥ kṣudādayaś cāritrāntarāṇi prati bhājyāh. niyamena punaranayoḥ pratyetavyāḥ — 
 sūkṣmasāṃparāyachadmasthavītarāgayoś caturdaśa || 
 § 839. kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇadaṃśamaśakacaryāśayyāvadhālābharogatṛṇasparśamalaprajñājñānāni. ‘caturdaśa’ iti vacanād anyeṣāṃ pariṣahāṇām abhāvo veditavyaḥ. āha yuktaṃ tāvad vītarāgachadmasthe mohanīyābhāvāt tatkṛtavakṣyamāṇāṣṭapariṣahābhāvāc caturdaśaniyamavacanam. sūkṣmasāṃparāye tu mohodayasadbhāvāt ‘caturdaśa’ iti niyamo nopapadyata iti? tad ayuktam; sanmātratvāt. tatra hi kevalo lobhasaṃjvalanakaṣāyodayaḥ so ’py atisūkṣmaḥ. tato vītarāgachadmasthakalpatvāt ‘caturdaśa’ iti niyamas tatrāpi yujyate. nanu mohodayasahāyābhāvān mandodayayatvāc ca kṣudādivedanābhāvāt tatsahanakṛtapariṣahavyapadeśo na yuktim avatarati. tan na? kiṃ kāraṇam. *  śaktimatrasya vivakṣitatvāt. sarvārthasiddhidevasya saptamapṛthivīgamanasāmarthyavyapadeśāvat. 
 § 840. āha, yadi śarīravaty ātmani pariṣahasaṃnidhānaṃ pratijñāyate atha bhavati utpannakevalajñāne karmacatuṣṭayaphalānubhavanavaśavartini kiyanta upanipatantīty atrocyate. tasmin punaḥ — 
 ekādaśa jine || 
 § 841. nirastaghātikarmacatuṣṭaye jine vedanīyasadbhāvāt tadāsrayā ekādaśapariṣahāḥ saṃti. nanu ca mohanīyodayasahāyābhāvāt kṣudādivedanābhāve pariṣahavyapadeśo na yuktaḥ? satyam evam etat — vedanābhāve ’pi dravyakarmasadbhāvāpekṣayā pariṣahopacāraḥ kriyate, niravaśeṣanirastajñānātiśaye cintānirodhābhāve ’pi tatphalakarma nirharaṇaphalāpekṣayā dhyānopacāravat. athavā — ekādaśa jine ‘na saṃti’ iti vākyaśeṣaḥ kalpanīyaḥ, sopaskāratvāt sūtrāṇām.  kalpyo hi vākyaśeṣo vākyaṃ ca vaktary adhīnam  ity upagamāt. mohodayasahāyīkṛtakṣudādivedanābhāvāt ‘na santi’ iti vākyaśeṣaḥ. 
 § 842. āha, yadi sūkṣmasāṃparāyādiṣu vyastāḥ pariṣahāḥ atha samastāḥ tāḥ kveti — 
 bādarasāṃparāye sarve || 
 § 843. sāṃparāyaḥ kaṣāyaḥ. bādaraḥ sāṃparāyo yasya sa bādarasāṃparāya iti. nedaṃ guṇasthānaviśeṣagrahaṇam. kiṃ tarhi? arthanirdeśaḥ. tena pramattādīnāṃ saṃyatānāṃ grahaṇam. teṣu hi akṣīṇakaṣāyadoṣatvāt sarve saṃbhavanti. kasmin punaś cāritre sarveṣāṃ saṃbhavaḥ? sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanaparihāraviśuddhisaṃyameṣu pratyekaṃ sarveṣāṃ saṃbhavaḥ. 
 § 844. āha, gṛhītam etat pariṣahāṇāṃ sthānaviśeṣāvadhāraṇaṃ, idaṃ tu na vidmaḥ kasyāḥ prakṛteḥ kaḥ kārya ity atrocyate — 
 jñānāvaraṇe prajñājñāne || 
 § 845. idam ayuktam vartate. kim atrāyuktam? jñānāvaraṇe satyajñānapariṣaha upapadyate, prajñāpariṣahaḥ punas tadapāye bhavatīti kathaṃ jñānāvaraṇe syāt? ity atrocyate — kṣāyopaśamikī prajñā anyasmin jñānāvaraṇe sati madaṃ janayati na sakalāvaraṇakṣaye iti jñānāvaraṇe satīty upapadyate. 
 § 846. punar aparayo pariṣahayoḥ prakṛtiviśeṣanirdeśārtham āha — 
 darśanamohāntarāyayor adarśanālābhau || 
 § 847. yathāsaṃkhyam abhisaṃbandhaḥ. darśanamohe adarśanapariṣaho, lābhāntarāye alābhapariṣaha iti.
	  āha, yady ādye mohanīyabhede ekaḥ pariṣahaḥ atha dvitīyasmin kati bhavantīty atrocyate — 
 cāritramohe nāgnyāratistrīniṣadyākrośayācanāsatkārapuraskārāḥ || 
 § 848. puṃvedodayādinimittatvān nāgnyādipariṣahāṇāṃ mohodayanimittatvaṃ pratipadyāmahe. niṣadyāpariṣahasya katham? tatrāpi prāṇipīḍāparihārārthatvāt. mohodaye sati prāṇipīḍāpariṇāmaḥ saṃjāyata iti. 
 § 849. avaśiṣṭapariṣahaprakṛtiviśeṣapratipādanārtham āha — 
 vedanīye śeṣāḥ || 
 § 850. uktā ekādaśa pariṣāhāḥ. tebhyo ’nye śeṣāḥ vedanīye sati ‘bhavanti’ iti vākyaśeṣaḥ. ke punas te? kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇadaṃśamaśakacaryāśayyāvadharogatṛṇasparśamalapariṣahāḥ. 
 § 851 āha, vyākhyātanimittalakṣaṇavikalpāḥ pratyātmani prādurbhavantaḥ kati yugapad avatiṣṭhanta ity atrocyate — 
 ekādayo bhājyā yugapad ekasminn aikonaviṃśateḥ || 
 § 852. āṅabhividhyarthaḥ. tena ekonaviṃśatir api kvacit yugapat saṃbavatīty avagamyate. tat katham? iti ced ucyate — śītoṣṇapariṣahayor ekaḥ śayyāniṣadyācaryāṇāṃ cānyatama eva bhavati ekasminn ātmani. kutaḥ? virodhāt. tattrayāṇām apagame yugapad ekātmanītareṣāṃ saṃbhavād ekonaviṃśativikalpā boddhavyāḥ. nanu prajñājñānayor api virodhād yugapad asaṃbhavaḥ? śrutajñānāpekṣayā prajñāpariṣahaḥ avadhijñānādyabhāvāpekṣayā ajñānapariṣaha iti nāsti virodhaḥ. 
 § 853. āha, uktā guptisamitidharmānuprekṣāpariṣahajayāḥ saṃvarahetavaḥ pañca. saṃvarahetuś cāritrasaṃjño vaktavya iti tadbhedapradarśanārtham ucyate — 
 sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanāparihāraviśuddhisūkṣmasāmparāyayathākhyātam iti cāritram || 
 § 854. atra codyate — daśavidhe dharme saṃyama uktaḥ sa eva cāritram iti punar grahaṇam anarthakam iti? nānarthahakam; dharme ’ntarbhūtam api cāritram ante gṛhyate mokṣaprāpteḥ sakṣātkāraṇam iti jñāpanārtham. sāmāyikam uktam. kva? ‘digdeśānarthadaṇḍaviratisāmāyika — ’ ity atra. tad dvividhaṃ niyatakālam aniyatakālaṃ ca. svādhyāyādi niyatakālam. īryāpathādyaniyatakālam. pramādakṛtānarthaprabandhavilope samyakpratikriyā chedopasthāpanā vikalpanivṛttir vā. pariharaṇaṃ parihāraḥ prāṇivadhān nivṛttiḥ. tena viśiṣṭā śuddhir yasṃims tatparihāraviśuddhicāritram. atiśūkṣmakaṣāyatvāt sūkṣmasāṃparāyacāritram. mohanīyasya niravaśeṣasyopaśamāt kṣayāc ca ātmasvabhāvāvasthāpekṣālakṣaṇaṃ athākhyātacāritram ity ākhyāyate. pūrvacāritrānuṣṭhāyibhir ākhyātaṃ na tatprāptaṃ prāṅmohakṣayopaśamābhyām ity athākhyātam. athaśabdasyānantaryārthavṛttitatvān niravaśeṣamohakṣayopaśamānantaram āvirbhavatīty arthaḥ. ‘yathākhyātam’ iti vā; yathātmasvabhāvo ’vasthitas tathaivākhyātatvāt. ‘iti’ śabdaḥ parisamāptau draṣṭavyaḥ. tato yathākhyātacāritrāt sakalakarmakṣayaparisamāptir bhavtīti jñāpyate. sāmāyikādīnām ānupūrvyavacanam uttarottaraguṇaprakarṣakhyāpanārthaṃ kriyate. 
 § 855. āha, uktaṃ cāritram. tadanantaram uddiṣṭaṃ yat ‘tapasā nirjarā ca’ iti tasyedānīṃ tapaso vidhānaṃ kartavyam ity atrocyate. tad dvividhaṃ bāhyam ābhyantaraṃ ca. tatpratyekaṃ ṣaḍvidham. tatra bāhyabhedapratipattyartham āha — 
 anaśanāvamaudaryavṛttiparisaṃkhyānarasaparityāgaviviktaśayyāsanakāyakleśā bāhyaṃ tapaḥ || 
 § 856. dṛṣṭaphalānapekṣaṃ saṃyamaprasiddhirāgocchedakarmavināśadhyānāgamāvāptyartham anaśanam. saṃyamaprajāgaradoṣapraśamasaṃtoṣasvādhyāyādisukhasiddhyartham avamaudaryam. bhikṣārthino muner ekāgārādiviṣayaḥ saṃkalpaḥ cintāvarodho vṛttiparisaṃkhyānam āśānivṛttyartham avagantavyam. indriyadarpanigrahanidrāvijayasvādhyāyasukhasiddhyādyartho ghṛtādivṛṣyarasaparityāgaś caturthaṃ tapaḥ. śūnyāgārādiṣu vivikteṣu jantupīḍāvirahiteṣu saṃyatasya śayyāsanam ābādhātyayabrahmacaryasvādhyāyadhyānādiprasiddhyarthaṃ kartavyam iti paṃcamaṃ tapaḥ. ātapasthānaṃ vṛkṣamūlanivāso nirāvaraṇaśayanaṃ bahuvidhapratimāsthānam ity evam ādiḥ kāyakleśaḥ tat ṣaṣṭaṃ tapaḥ. tatkim artham? dehaduḥkhatitikṣāsukhānabhiṣvaṅgapravacanaprabhāvanādyartham. pariṣahasyāsya ca ko viśeṣaḥ? yadṛcchayopanipatitaḥ pariṣahaḥ. svayaṃkṛtaḥ kāyakleśaḥ. bāhyatvam asya kutaḥ? bāhyadravyāpekṣatvāt parapratyakṣatvāc ca bāhyatvam. 
 § 857. ābyantaratapobhedapradarśanārtham āha — 
 prāyaścittavinayavaiyāvṛttyasvādhyāyavyutsargadhyānāny uttaram || 
 § 858. katham asyābhyantaratvam? manoniyamanārthatvāt. pramādadoṣaparihāraḥ prāyaścittam. pūjyeṣv ādaro vinayaḥ. kāyaceṣṭayā dravyāntareṇa copāsanaṃ vaiyāvṛttyam. jñānabhāvanālasyatyāgaḥ svādhyāyaḥ. ātmātmīyasaṃkalpatyāgo vyutsargaḥ. cittavikṣepatyāgo dhyānam. 
 § 859. tadbhedapratipādanārtham āha — 
 navacaturdaśapañcadvibhedā yathākramaṃ prāgdhyānāt || 
 § 860. ‘yathākramam’ iti vacanān navabhedaṃ prāyaścittam, vinayaś caturvidhaḥ, vaiyāvṛttyaṃ daśavidham, svādhyāyaḥ pañcavidhaḥ, dvibhedo vyutsarga ity abhisaṃbadyate. ‘prāgdhyānāt’ iti vacanaṃ dhyānasya bahuvaktavyatvāt paścād vakṣyata iti. 
 § 861. ādyasya bhedasvarūpanirjñānārtham āha — 
 ālocanapratikramaṇatadubhayavivekavyutsargatapaśchedaparihāropasthāpanāḥ || 
 § 862. tatra gurave pramādanivedanaṃ daśadoṣavivarjitam ālocanam. mithyāduṣkṛtābhidhānād abhivyaktapratikriyaṃ pratikramaṇam. [tadubhaya] saṃsarge sati viśodhanāt tadubhayam. saṃsaktānnapānopakaraṇādivibhajanaṃ vivekaḥ. kāyotsargādikaraṇaṃ vyutsargaḥ. anaśanāvamaudaryādilakṣaṇaṃ tapaḥ. divasapakṣamāsādinā pravrajyāhāpanaṃ chedaḥ. pakṣamāsādivibhāgena dūrataḥ parivarjanaṃ parihāraḥ. punar dīkṣāprāpaṇam upasthāpanā. 
 § 863. vinayavikalpapratipattyartham āha — 
 jñānadarśanacāritropacārāḥ || 
 § 864. ‘vinayaḥ’ ity adhikāreṇābhisaṃbandhaḥ kriyate. jñānavinayo darśanavinayaś cāritravinaya upacāravinayaś ceti. sabahumānaṃ mokṣārthaṃ jñānagrahaṇābhyāsasmaraṇādir jñānavinayaḥ. śaṃkādidoṣavirahitaṃ tattvārthaśraddhānaṃ darśanavinayaḥ. tadvataś cāritre samāhitacittatā cāritravinayaḥ. pratyakṣeṣv ācāryādiṣv abhyuthānābhigamanāñjalikaraṇādir upacāravinayaḥ. parokṣeṣv api kāyavāṅmano ’bhiraṃjalikriyāguṇasaṃkīrtanānusmaraṇādiḥ. 
 § 865. vaiyāvṛttyabhedapratipādanārtham āha — 
 ācāryopādhyāyatapasviśaikṣaglānagaṇakulasaṃghasādhumanojñānām || 
 § 866. vaiyāvṛttyaṃ daśadhā bhidyate. kutaḥ? viṣayabhedāt. ācāryavaiyāvṛttyam upādhyāyavaiyāvṛttyam ity ādi. tatra ācaranti tasmād vratānīty ācāryaḥ. mokṣārthaṃ śāstram upetya tasmād adhīyata ity upādhyāyaḥ. mahopavāsādyanuṣṭhāyī tapasvī. śikṣāśīlaḥ śaikṣaḥ. rujādikliṣṭaśarīro glānaḥ. gaṇaḥ sthavirasaṃtatiḥ. dīkṣakācāryaśiṣyasaṃstyāyaḥ kulam. cāturvarṇaśramaṇanivahaḥ saṃghaḥ. cirapravrajitaḥ sādhuḥ. manojño lokasaṃmataḥ. teṣāṃ vyādhipariṣahamithyātvādyupanipāte kāyaceṣṭayā dravyāntareṇa vā tatpratīkāro vaiyāvṛttyaṃ samādhyādhānavicikitsābhāvapravacanavātsalyādyabhivyaktyartham. 
 § 867. svādhyāyavikalpavijñānārtham āha — 
 vācanāpracchanānuprekṣāmnāyadharmopadeśāḥ || 
 § 868. niravadyagranthārthobhayapradānaṃ vācanā. saṃśayachedāya niścitabalādhānāya vā parānuyogaḥ pracchanā. adhigatārthasya manasābhyāso ’nuprekṣā. ghoṣaśuddhaṃ parivartanam āmnāyaḥ. dharmakathādyanuṣṭhānaṃ dharmopadeśaḥ. sa eṣa pañcavidhaḥ svādhyāyaḥ kim arthaḥ? prajñātiśayaḥ praśastādhyavasāyaḥ pramasaṃvegas tapovṛddhir aticāraviśuddhir ity evam ādy arthaḥ. 
 § 869. vyutsargabhedanirjñānārtham āha — 
 bāhyābhyantaropadhyoḥ || 
 § 870. vyutsarjanaṃ vyutsargas tyāgaḥ. sa dvividhaḥ — bāhyopadhityāgo ’bhyantaropadhityāgaś ceti. anupāttaṃ vastudhanadhānyādi bāhyopadiḥ. krodhādir ātmabhāvo ’bhyantaropadhiḥ kāyatyāgaś ca niyatakālo yāvaj jīvaṃ vābhyantaropadhityāga ity ucyate. sa kim arthaḥ? nissaṅgatvanirbhayatvajīvitāśāvyudāsādyarthaḥ. 
 § 871. yad bahuvaktavyaṃ dhyānam iti pṛthagvyavasthāpitaṃ tasyedānīṃ bhedābhidhānaṃ prāptakālam. tadullaṅghya tasya prayoktṛsvarūpakālanirddhāraṇārtham ucyate — 
 uttamasaṃhananasyaikāgracintānirodho dhyānam āntarmuhūrtāt || 
 § 872. ādyaṃ tritayaṃ saṃhananam uttamaṃ vajrarṣabhanārācasaṃhananaṃ vajranārācasaṃhananaṃ nārācasaṃhananam iti. tat tritayam api dhvānasya sādhanaṃ bhavati. *  mokṣasya tu ādyam eva. taduttamaṃ saṃhananaṃ yasya so ’yam uttamasaṃhananaḥ, tasyottamasaṃhananasyeti. anena prayoktṛnirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ. agraṃ mukham. ekam agramasyety ekāgraḥ. nānārthāvalambanena cintā parispandavatī, tasyā anyāśeṣamukhebyo vyāvartya ekasminn agre niyama ekāgracintānirodha ity ucyate. anena dhānyasvarūpam uktaṃ bhavati. muhūrta iti kālaparimāṇam. antargato muhūrto ’ntarmuhūrtaḥ. ‘ā antarmuhūrtāt’ ity anena kālavidhiḥ kṛtaḥ. tataḥ paraṃ durdharatvāt ekagracintāyāḥ. cintāyā nirodho yadi dhyānaṃ, nirodhaś cābhāvaḥ, tena dhyānam asatkharaviṣāṇavatsyāt? naiṣa doṣaḥ; anyacintānivṛttyapekṣayāsad iti cocyate, svaviṣayākārapravṛtteḥ sad iti ca; abhāvasya bhāvāntaravād hetvaṅgatvādibhir abhāvasya vastudharmatvasiddheś ca. athavā nāyaṃ bhāvasādhanaḥ, nirodhanaṃ nirodha iti. kiṃ tarhi? karmasādhanaḥ, ‘nirudhyata iti nirodhaḥ’. cintā cāsau nirodhaś ca cintānirodha iti. etad uktaṃ bhavati — jñānam evāparispandāgniśikhāvadavabhāsamānaṃ dhyānam iti. 
 § 873. tadbhedapradarśanārtham āha — 
 ārttaraudradharmyaśuklāni || 
 § 874. ṛtaṃ duḥkhaṃ, ardanam ārtivā, tatra bhavam ārtam. rudraḥ krūrāśayas tasya karma tatra bhavaṃ vā raudram. dharmo vyākhyātaḥ. dharmād anapetaṃ dharmyam. śuciguṇayogāc chuklam. tadetac caturvidhaṃ dhyānaṃ dvaividhyam aśnute. kutaḥ? praśastāpraśastabhedāt. apraśastam apuṇyāsravakāraṇatvāt. karmanirdahanasāmarthyāt praśastam. 
 § 875 kiṃ punas tad iti ced ucyate — 
 pare mokṣahetū || 
 § 876. param uttaram antyam. antyaṃ śuklam. tatsāmīpyād dharmyam api ‘param’ ity upacaryate. dvivacananirdeśasāmarthyād gaunam api gṛhyate. ‘pare mokṣahetū’ iti vacanāt pūrve ārtaraudre saṃsārahetū ity uktam bhavati. kutaḥ? tṛtīyasya sādhyasyābhāvāt. 
 § 877. tatrārtraṃ caturvidham. tatrādivikalpalakṣaṇanirdeśārtham āha — 
 ārtam amanojñasya saṃprayoge tadviprayogāya smṛtisamanvāhāraḥ || 
 § 878. amanojñam apriyaṃ viṣakaṇṭakaśatruśastrādi, tadbādhākaraṇatvād ‘amanojñam’ ity ucyate. tasya saṃprayoge, sa kathaṃ nāma me na syād iti saṃkalpaś cintāprabandhaḥ smṛtisamanvāhāraḥ prathaman ārtam ity ākhyāyate. 
 § 879. dvitīyasya vikalpasya lakṣaṇanirdeśārtham āha — 
 viparitaṃ manojñasya || 
 § 880. kuto viparitam? pūvoktāt. tenaitad uktam bhavati — manojñasyeṣṭasya svaputradāradhanāder viprayoge tatsaṃprayogāya saṃkalpaś cintāprabandho dvitīyam ārtam avagantavyam. 
 § 881. tṛtīyasya vikalpasya lakṣaṇapratipādanārtham āha — 
 vedanāyāś ca || 
 § 882. ‘vedanā’ śabdaḥ sukhe duḥkhe ca vartamāno ’pi ārtasya prakṛtatvād duḥkhavedanāyāṃ pravartate, tasyā vātādivikārajanitavedanāyā upanipāte tasyā apāyaḥ katham nāma me syād iti saṃkalpaś cintāprabandhas tṛtīyam ārtam ucyate. 
 § 883. turīyasārtasya lakṣaṇanirdeśārtham āha — 
 nidānaṃ ca || 
 § 884. bhogākāṅṣāturyasyānāgataviṣayaprāptiṃ prati manaḥpraṇidhānaṃ saṃkalpaś cintāprabandhas turīyam ārtaṃ nidānam ity ucyate. 
 § 885. tadetac caturvidham ārtam kiṃ svāmikam iti ced ucyate — 
 tadaviratadeśaviratapramattasaṃyatānām || 
 § 886. aviratā asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyantāḥ. deśaviratāḥ saṃyatāsaṃyatāḥ. pramattasaṃyatāḥ paṃcadaśapramādopetāḥ kriyānuṣṭhāyinaḥ. tatrāviratadeśaviratānāṃ caturvidham apy ārtaṃ bhavati; asaṃyamapariṇāmopetatvāt. pramattasaṃyatānāṃ tu nidānavarjyam anyad ārtatrayaṃ pramādodayodrekāt kadācit syāt. 
 § 887. vyākhyātam ārtaṃ saṃjñādibhiḥ. dvitīyasya saṃjñāhetusvāminirddhāraṇārtham āha — 
 hiṃsānṛtasteyaviṣayasaṃrakṣaṇebhyo raudram aviratadeśaviratayoḥ || 
 § 888. hiṃsādīny uktalakṣaṇāni. tāni raudradhyānotpatter nimittī bhavantīti hetunirdeśo vijñāyate. tena hetunirdeśenānuvartamānaḥ ‘smṛtisamanvāhāraḥ’ abhisaṃbadhyate. hiṃsāyāḥ smṛtisamanvāhāra ity ādi. tadraudradhyānam aviratadeśaviratayor veditavyam. aviratasya bhavatu raudradhyānaṃ, deśaviratasya katham? tasyāpi hiṃsādyāveśād vittādisaṃrakṣaṇatantratvāc ca kadācid bhavitum arhati. tatpunar nārakādīnām akāraṇaṃ; samyagdarśanasāmarthyāt. saṃyatasya tu na bhavaty eva; tadārambhe saṃyamapracyuteḥ. 
 § 889. āha ‘pare mokṣahetū’ upadiṣṭe. tatrādyasya mokṣahetor dhyānasya bhedasvarūpasvāminirdeśaḥ kartavya ity ata āha — 
 ājñāpāyavipākasaṃsthānavicayāya dharmyam || 
 § 890. vicayanaṃ vicayo viveko vicāraṇety arthaḥ. ājñāpāyavipākasaṃsthānānāṃ vicaya ajñāpāyavipākasaṃsthānavicayaḥ. ‘smṛtisamanvāhāraḥ’ ity anuvartate. sa pratyekaṃ saṃbadhyate — ājñāvicayāya smṛtisamanvāhāraḥ ity ādi. tad yathā — upadeṣṭur abhāvān mandabuddhitvāt karmodayāt sūkṣmatvāc ca padārthanāṃ hetudṛṣṭāntoparame sati sarvajñapraṇītam āgamaṃ pramāṇī kṛtya ittham evedaṃ  nānyathāvādino jināḥ  iti gahanapadārthaśraddhānād arthāvadhāraṇam ājñāvicayaḥ. athavā — svayaṃ viditapadārthatattvasya sataḥ paraṃ prati pipādayiṣoḥ svasiddhāntāvirodhena tattvasamarthanārthaṃ tarkanayapramāṇayojanaparaḥ smṛtisamanvāhāraḥ sarvajñājñāprakāśanārthatvād ājñāvicaya ity ucyate. jātyandhavanmityhyādṛṣṭayaḥ sarvajñapraṇītamārgād vimukhā mokṣārtinaḥ samyaṅmārgāparijñānāt sudūram evāpayantīti sanmārgāpāyacintanam apāyavicayaḥ. athavā — mithyādarśanajñānacāritrebhyaḥ kathaṃ nama ime prāṇino ’peyur iti smṛtisamanvāhāro ’pāyavicayaḥ. karmaṇāṃ jñānāvaraṇādīnāṃ dravyakṣetrakālabhavabhāvapratyayaphalānubhavanaṃ prati praṇidhānaṃ vipākavicayaḥ. lokasaṃsthānasvabhāvavicayāya smṛtisamanvāhāraḥ saṃsthānavicayaḥ. uttamakṣamādilakṣaṇo dharma uktaḥ. tasmād anapetaṃ dharmyaṃ dhyānaṃ caturvikalpam avaseyam. tadaviratadeśaviratapramattāpramattasaṃyatānāṃ bhavati. 
 § 891. trayāṇāṃ dhyānānāṃ nirupaṇaṃ kṛtam. idānīṃ śukladhyānaṃ nirūpapayitavyam. tadvakṣyamāṇacaturvikalpam. tatrādyayoḥ svāminirdeśārtham idam ucyate — 
 śukle cādye pūrvavidaḥ || 
 § 892. vakṣyamāṇeṣu śukladhyānavikalpeṣu ādye śukladhyāne pūrvavido bhavataḥ śrutakevalina ity arthāḥ. ‘ca’ śabdena dharmyam api samuccīyate. tatra  vyākhyānato viśeṣapratipattiḥ  iti śreṇyārohaṇāt prāgdharmyaṃ, śreṇyoḥ śukle iti vyākhyāyate. 
 § 893. avaśiṣṭe kasya bhavata ity atrocyate — 
 pare kevalinaḥ || 
 § 894. prakṣīṇasakalajñānāvaraṇasya kevalinaḥ sayogasyāyogasya ca pare uttare śukladhyāne bhavataḥ. 
 § 895. yathāsaṃkhyaṃ tadvikalpapratipādanārtham idam ucyate — 
 pṛthaktvaikatvavitarkasūkṣmakriyāpratipātivyuparatakriyānivartīni || 
 § 896. pṛthaktvavitarkam ekatvavitarkaṃ sūkṣmakriyāpratipāti vyuparatakriyānivarti ceti caturvidhaṃ śukladhyānam. vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇam apekṣya sarveṣām anvarthatvam avaseyam. 
 § 897. tasyālambanaviśeṣanirdhāraṇārtham āha — 
 tryekayogakāyayogāyogānām || 
 § 898. ‘yoga’ śabdo vyākhyātārthaḥ ‘kāyavāṅmanaḥkarma yogaḥ’ iti atra. uktaiś caturbhiḥ śukladhyānavikalpais triyogādīnāṃ caturṇāṃ yathāsaṃkhyenābhisaṃbandho veditavyaḥ. triyogasya pṛthaktvavitarkam, triṣu yogeṣv ekayogasyaikatvavitarkam, kāyayogasya sūkṣmakriyāpratipāti, ayogasya vyutparatakriyānivartīti. 
 § 899. tatrādyayor viśeṣapratipattyartham idam ucyate — 
 ekāśraye savitarkavīcāre pūrve || 
 § 900. eka āśrayo yayos te ekāśraye. ubhe ’pi pariprāptaśrutajñānaniṣṭhenārabhyete, ity arthaḥ. vitarkaś ca vīcāraś ca vitarkavīcārau, saha vitarkavīcārābhyāṃ varteta iti savitarkavīcāre. pūrve pṛthaktvaikatvavitarke ity arthaḥ. 
 § 901. tatra yathāsaṃkhyaprasaṃge ’niṣṭanivṛttyartham idam ucyate — 
 avīcāraṃ dvitīyam || 
 § 902. pūrvayor yad dvitīyaṃ tad avīcāraṃ pratyetavyam. etad uktaṃ bhavati — ādyaṃ savitarkaṃ savīcāraṃ ca bhavati. dvitīyaṃ savitarkam avīcāraṃ ceti. 
 § 903. atha vitarkavīcārayoḥ kaḥ prativiśeṣa ity atrocyate — 
 vitarkaḥ śrutam || 
 § 904. viśeṣeṇa tarkaṇam ūhanaṃ vitarkaḥ śrutajñānam ity arthaḥ. 
 § 905. atha ko vīcāraḥ. 
 vīcāro ’rthavyaṃjanayogasaṃkrāntiḥ || 
 § 906. artho dhyeyo dravyaṃ paryāyo vā. vyañjanaṃ vacanam. yogaḥ kāyavāṅmanaḥkarmalakṣaṇaḥ. saṃkrāntiḥ parivartanam. dravyaṃ vihāya paryāyam upaiti paryāyaṃ tyaktvā dravyam ity arthasaṃkrāntiḥ. ekaṃ śrutavacanam upādāya vacanāntaram ālambate tad api vihāyānyad iti vyañjanasaṃkrāntiḥ. kāyayogaṃ tyaktvā yogāntaraṃ gṛhṇāti yogāntaraṃ ca tyaktvā kāyayogam iti yogasaṃkrāntiḥ. evaṃ parivartanaṃ vīcāra ity ucyate. tad etat sāmānyaviśeṣanirdiṣṭaṃ caturvidhaṃ dharmyaṃ śuklaṃ ca pūvoditaguptyādibahuprakāropāyaṃ saṃsāranivṛttaye munir dhyātum arhati kṛtaparikarmā. tatra dravyaparamāṇuṃ bhāvaparamāṇuṃ vā dhyāyan nāhitavitarkasāmarthyaḥ arthavyaṃjane kāyavācasī ca pṛthaktvena saṃkrāmatā manasāparyaptibālotsāhavadavyavasthitenāniśitenāpi śastreṇa cirāt taruṃ chindann iva mohaprakṛtīr upaśamayan kṣapayaṃś ca pṛthaktvavitarkavīcāradhyānabhāgbhavati. sa eva punaḥ samūlatūlaṃ mohanīyaṃ nirdidhakṣann anantaguṇaviśuddhiyogaviśeṣam āśritya bahutarāṇāṃ jñānāvaraṇasahāyībhūtānāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ bandhaṃ nirundhan sthiti hrāsakṣayau ca kurvan śrutajñānopayogo nivṛttārthavyaṃjanayogasaṃkrāntiḥ avicalitamanāḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyo vaiḍūryamaṇir iva nirupalepo dhyātvā punar na nivartata ity uktam ekatvavitarkam. evam ekatvavitarkaśukladhyānavaiśvānaranirdagdhavātikarmendhanaḥ prajvalitakevalajñānagabhastimaṇḍalo meghapañjaranirodhanirgata iva gharmaraśmir vā bhāsamāno bhagavāṃs tīrthakara itaro vā kevalī lokeśvarāṇām abhigamanīyo ’rcanīyaś cotkarṣeṇāyuṣaḥ pūvakoṭīṃ deśonāṃ viharati. sa yadāntarmuhūrtaśeṣāyuṣkas tattulyasthitivedyanāmagotraś ca bhavati tadā sarvaṃ vāṅmanasayogaṃ bādarakāyayogaṃ ca parihāpya sukṣmakāyayogālambanaḥ sukṣmakriyāpratipātidhyānam āskanditum arahatīti. yadā punar antarmuhūrtaśeṣāyuṣkas tato ’dhikasthitiśeṣakarmatrayo bhavati sayogī tadātmopayogātiśayasya sāmāyikasahāyasya viśiṣṭakaraṇasya mahāsaṃvarasya laghukarmaparipācanasyāśeṣakarmareṇupariśātanaśaktisvābhāvyād daṇḍakapāṭaprataralokapūraṇāni svātmapradeśavisarpaṇataś caturbhiḥ samayaiḥ kṛtvā punar api tāvadbhir eva samayaiḥ samupahṛtapradeśavisaraṇaḥ samīkṛtasthitiśeṣakarmacatuṣṭayaḥ pūrvaśarīrapramāṇo bhūtvā sūkṣmakāyayogena sūkṣmakriyāpratipāti dhyānaṃ dhyāyati. tatas tadantaraṃ samucchinnakriyānivartidhyānam ārabhate. samucchinnaprāṇāpānapracārasarvakāyavāṅmanoyogasarvapradeśaparispandakriyāvyāpāratvāt samucchinnakriyānivartīty ucyate. tasmin samucchinnakriyānivartini dhyāne sarvabandhāsravanirodhasarvaśeṣakarmaśātanasāmarthyopapatter ayogikevalinaḥ saṃpūrṇayathākhyātacāritrajñānadarśanaṃ sarvasaṃsāraduḥkhajālapariṣvaṅgocchedajananaṃ sākṣān mokṣakāraṇam upajāyate. sa punar ayogakevalī bhagavāṃs tadā dhyānātiśayāgninirdagdhasarvamalakalaṃkabandhano nirastakiṭṭadhātupāṣāṇajātyakanakavallabdhātmā parinirvāti. tadetad dvividhaṃ tapo ’bhinavakarmāsravanirodhahetutvāt saṃvarakāraṇaṃ prāktanakarmarajovidhūnananimittatvān nirjarāhetur api bhavati. 
 § 907. atrāha samyagdṛṣṭayaḥ kiṃ sarve samanirjarā āhosvit kaścid asti prativiśeṣa ity atrocyate — 
 samyagdṛṣṭiśrāvakaviratānantaviyojakadarśanamohakṣapakopaśamakopaśāntamohakṣapakakṣīṇamohajināḥ kramaśo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇanirjarāḥ || 
 § 908. ta ete daśa samyagdṛṣṭyādayaḥ kramaśo ’saṃkhyeyaguṇanirjarāḥ. tad yathā — bhavyaḥ paṃcedndriyasaṃjñī paryāptakā pūrvoktakālalabdhyādisahāyaḥ pariṇāmaviśuddhyā vardhamānaḥ krameṇāpūrvakaraṇādisopānapaṅktyotplavamāno bahutarakarmanirjaro bhavati. sa eva punaḥ prathamasamyaktvaprāptinimittasaṃnidhāne sati samyagdṛṣṭir bhavann asaṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. sa eva punaś cāritramohakarmavikalpāpratyākhyānāvaraṇakṣayopaśamanimittapariṇāmaprāptikāle viśuddhiprakarṣayogāt śrāvako bhavan tato ’saṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. sa eva punaḥ pratyātyākhyānāvaraṇakṣayopaśamakāraṇapariṇāmaviśuddhiyogād viratavyapadeśabhāk san tato ’saṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. sa eva punar anantānubandhikrodhamānamāyālobhānāṃ viyojanaparo bhavati yadā tadā pariṇāmaviśuddhiprakarṣayogāt tato ’saṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. sa eva punar darśanamohaprakṛtitrayatṛṇanicayaṃ nirdidhakṣan pariṇāmaviśuddhyatiśayayogād darśanamohakṣapakavyapadeśabhāk pūvoktād asaṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. evaṃ saḥ kṣāyikasamyagdṛṣṭir bhūtvā śreṇyārohanābhimukhaś cāritramohopaśamaṃ prati vyāpriyamāṇo viśuddhiprakarṣayogād upaśamakavyapadeśam anubhavan pūrvoktād asaṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. sa eva punar aśeṣacāritramohopaśamanimittasaṃnidhāne pariprāprāptopaśāntakaṣāyavyapadeśaḥ pūrvoktād asaṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. sa eva punaś cāritramohakṣapaṇaṃ pratyabhimukhaḥ pariṇāmaviśuddhyā varddhamānaḥ kṣapakavyapadeśam anubhavan pūrvoktād asaṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. sa yadā niḥśeṣacāritramohakṣapaṇakāraṇapariṇāmābhimukhaḥ kṣīṇakaṣāyavyapadeśam āskandan pūrvoktād asaṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. sa eva dvitīyaśukladhyānānalanirdagdhaghātikarmanicayaḥ san jinavyapadeśabhāk pūrvoktād asaṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaro bhavati. 
 § 909. āha, samyagdarśanasaṃnidhāne ’pi yady asaṃkhyeyaguṇanirjaratavāt parasparato na sāmyam esāṃ kiṃ tarhi śravakavad amī viratādayo guṇabhedān na nirgranthatām arhantīti? ucyate, naitad evam. kutaḥ. yasmād guṇabhedād anyo ’nyaviśeṣe ’pi naigamādinayavyāpārāt sarve ’pi hi bhavanti — 
 pulākabakuśakuśīlanirgranthasnātakā nirgranthāḥ || 
 § 910. uttaraguṇabhāvanāpetamanaso vrateṣv api kvacit kadācit paripūrṇatām apariprāpnuvanto ’viśuddhapulākasādṛśyāt pulākā ity ucyante. nairgranthyaṃ prati sthitā akhaṇḍitavratāḥ śarīropakaraṇavibhūṣānuvartino ’viviktaparivārā mohaśabalayuktā bakuśāh. śabalaparyāyavācī bakuśaśabdaḥ. kuśīlā dvividhāḥ — pratisevanākuśīlāḥ kaṣāyakuśīlā iti. aviviktaparigrahāḥ paripūrṇobhayāḥ kathaṃcid uttaraguṇavirādhinaḥ pratisevanākuśīlāḥ. vaśīkṛtānyakaṣāyodayāḥ saṃjvalanamātratantrāḥ kaṣāyakuśīlāḥ. udakadaṇḍarājivadanabhivyaktodayakarmāṇaḥ ūrdhvaṃ muhūrtād udbhidyamānakevalajñānadarśanabhājo nirgranthāḥ. prakṣīṇaghātikarmāṇaḥ kevalino dvividhāḥ snātakāḥ. ta ete paṃcāpi nirgranthāḥ. cāritrapariṇāmasya prakarṣāprakarṣabhede saty api naigamasaṃgrahādinayāpekṣayā sarve ’pi te nirgranthā ity ucyante. 
 § 911. teṣāṃ pulākādīnāṃ bhūyo ’pi viśeṣapratipattyartham āha — 
 saṃyamaśrutapratisevanātīrthaliṃgaleśyopapādasthānavikalpataḥ sādhyāḥ || 
 § 912. te ete pulākādayaḥ saṃyamādibhir aṣṭabhir anuyogaiḥ sādhyā vyākheyāḥ. tad yathā — pulākabakuśapratisevanākuśīlā dvayoḥ saṃyamayoḥ sāmāyikacchedopasthāpanayor vartante. kaṣāyakuśīlā dvayoḥ saṃyamayoḥ parihāraviśuddhisūkṣamasāmparāyayoḥ pūrvayoś ca. nirgranthasnātakā ekasminn eva yathākhyātasaṃyame santi. 
 § 913. śrutaṃ — pulākabakuśapratisevanākuśīlā utkarṣenābhinnākṣaradaśapūrvadharāḥ. kaṣāyakuśīlā nirgranthāś caturdaśapūrvadharāḥ. jaghanyena pulākasya śrutam ācāravastu. bakuśakuśīlanirgranthānāṃ śrutam aṣṭau pravacanamātaraḥ. snātakā apagataśrutāḥ kevalinaḥ. 
 § 914. pratisevanā — pañcānāṃ mūlaguṇanāṃ rātribhojanavarjanasya ca parābhiyogād balād anyatamaṃ pratisevamānaḥ pulāko bhavati. bakuśo dvividhaḥ — upakaraṇabakuśaḥ śarīrabakuśaś ceti. tatropakaraṇabakuśo bahuviśeṣayuktopakaraṇākāṃkṣī. śarīrasaṃskārasevī śarīrabakuśaḥ. pratisevanākuśīlo mūlaguṇān avirādhayann uttaraguṇeṣu kāṃcid virādhanāṃ pratisevate. kaṣāyakuśīlanirgranthasnātakānāṃ pratisevanā nāsti. 
 § 915. tīrtham iti sarve sarveṣāṃ tīrthakarāṇāṃ tīrtheṣu bhavanti. 
 § 916. liṅgaṃ dvividhaṃ — dravyaliṅgaṃ bhāvaliṅgaṃ ceti. bhāvaliṅgaṃ pratītya sarve paṃca nirgranthā liṃgino bhavanti. dravyaliṃgaṃ pratītya bhājyāḥ. 
 § 917. leśyāḥ — pulākasyottarās tisraḥ bakuśapratisevanākuśīlayoḥ ṣaḍ api. kaṣāyakuśīlasya catasra uttaraḥ. sūkṣmasāmparāyasya nirgranthasnātakayoś ca śuklaiva kevalā. ayogā aleśyāḥ. 
 § 918. upapādaḥ — pulākasyotkṛṣṭa upapāda utkṛṣṭasthitideveṣu sahasrāre. bakuśapratisevanākuśīlayor dvāviṃśatisāgaropamasthitiṣu āraṇācyutakalpayoḥ. kaṣāyakuśīlanirgranthayos trayastriṃśatsāgaropamasthitiṣu sarvārthasiddhau. sarveṣām api jaghanyaḥ saudharmakalpe dvisāgaropamasthitiṣu. snātakasya nirvāṇam iti. 
 § 919. sthānam — asaṃkhyeyāni saṃyamasthānāni kaṣāyanimittāni bhavanti. tatra sarvajaghanyāni labdhisthānāni pulākakaṣāyakuśīlayoḥ. tau yugapad asaṃkhyeyāni sthānāni gacchataḥ. tataḥ pulāko vyucchidyate. kaṣāyakuśīlas tato ’saṃkhyeyāni sthānāni gacchaty ekākī. tataḥ kaṣāyakuśīlapratisevanākuśīlabakuśā yugapad asaṃkhyeyāni sthānāni gacchanti. tato bakuśo vyucchidyate. tato ’py asaṃkhyeyāni sthānāni gatvā pratisevanākuśīlo vyucchidyate. tato ’py asaṃkhyeyāni sthānāni gatvā kaṣāyakuśīlo vyucchidyate. ata ūrdhvam akaṣāyasthānāni nirgranthaḥ pratipadyate. so ’py asaṃkhyeyāni sthānāni gattvā vyucchidyate. ata ūrdhvam ekaṃ sthānaṃ gatvā snātako nirvāṇaṃ prāpnotīty eteṣāṃ saṃyamalabdhir anantaguṇā bhavati. 
 iti tattvārthavṛttau sarvārthasiddhisaṃjñikāyāṃ navamo ’dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ || 9 || 
 
 
	  atha daśamo ’dhyāyaḥ
	   §§ 920–937 
 § 920. āha, ante nirdiṣṭasya mokṣasyedānīṃ svarūpābhidhānaṃ prāptakālam iti. satyam evam. mokṣaprāptiḥ kevalajñānāvāptir pūrvaketi kevalajñānotpattikāraṇam ucyate — 
 mohakṣayāj jñānadarśanāvaraṇāntarāyakṣayāc ca kevalam || 
 § 921. iha vṛttikaraṇaṃ nyāyyam. kutaḥ? laghutvāt. katham? ekasya ‘kṣaya’ śabdasyākaraṇād vibhaktyantaranirdeśasya cābhāvāt ‘ca’ śabdasya cāprayogāl laghu sūtraṃ bhavati ‘mohajñānadarśanāvaraṇāntarāyakṣayāt kevalam’ iti. satyam etat, kṣayakramapratipādanārtho vākyabhedena nirdeśaḥ kriyate. prāgeva mohaṃ kṣayam upanīyāntarmuhūrtaṃ kṣīṇakaṣāyavyapadeśam avāpya tato yugapaj jñānadarśanāvaraṇāntarāyāṇāṃ kṣayam kṛtvā kevalam avāpnoti iti. tatkṣayo hetuḥ kevalotpatter iti hetulakṣaṇo vibhaktinirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ. kathaṃ prageva mohaḥ kṣayam upanīyate iti ced ucyate — bhavyaḥ samyagdṛṣṭiḥ pariṇāmaviśuddhyā vardhamāno ’saṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭisaṃyatāsaṃyatapramattāpramattaguṇasthāneṣu kasmiṃs cin mohasya sapta prakṛtīḥ kṣayam upanīya kṣāyikasamyagdṛṣṭir bhūtvā kṣapakaśreṇyārohanābhimukho ’dhaḥpravṛttakaraṇam apramattasthāne pratipādyāpūrvakaraṇaprayogeṇāpūrvakaraṇakṣapakaguṇasthānavyapadeśam anubhūya tatrābhinavaśubhābhisandhitanūkṛtapāpaprakṛtisthityanubhāgo vivardhitaśubhakarmānubhavo ’nivṛttikaraṇaprāptyānivṛttibādarasāṃparāyakṣapakaguṇasthānam adhiruhya tatra kaṣāyāṣṭakaṃ naṣṭaṃ kṛtvā napuṃsakavedanāśaṃ samāpādya strīvedam unmūlya nokakaṣāyaṣaṭkaṃ puṃvede prakṣipya kṣapayitvā puṃvedaṃ krodhasaṃjvalane, krodhasaṃjvalanaṃ mānasaṃjvalane, mānasaṃjvalanaṃ māyāsaṃjvalane, māyāsaṃjvalanaṃ ca lobhasaṃjvalane krameṇa bādarakṛṣṭivibhāgena vilayam upanīya lobhasaṃjvalanaṃ tanūkṛtya sūkṣmasāmparāyakṣapakatvam anubhūya niravaśeṣaṃ mohanīyaṃ nirmūlakaṣāyaṃ kaṣitvā kṣīṇakaṣāyatām adhiruhyāvatāritamohanīyabhāra upāntyaprathame samaye nidrāpracale pralayam upanīya pañcānāṃ jñānāvaraṇānāṃ caturṇām darśanāvaraṇānāṃ pañcānām antarāyāṇāṃ cāntam ante samupanīya tadanantraṃ jñānadarśanasvabhāvaṃ kevalaparyāyam apratarkyavibhūtiviśeṣam avāpnoti. 
 § 922. āha kasmād dhetor mokṣaḥ kiṃ lakṣaṇaś cety atrocyate — 
 bandhahetvabhāvanirjarābhyāṃ kṛtsnakarmavipramokṣo mokṣaḥ || 
 § 923. mithyādarśanādihetvābhāvād abhinavakarmābhāvaḥ pūrvoditanirjarāhetusaṃnidhāne cārjitakarmanirāsaḥ. tābhyāṃ bandhahetvabhāvanirjarābhyām iti hetulakṣaṇavibhaktinirdeśaḥ. tato bhavasthitihetusamīkṛtaśeṣakarmāvasthasya yugapad ātyantikaḥ kṛtsnakarmavipramokṣo mokṣaḥ pratyetavyaḥ. karmābhāvo dvividhaḥ — yatnasādhyo ’yatnasādhyaś ceti. tatra caramadehasya nārakatiryagdevāyuṣām abhāvo na yatnasādhyaḥ, asattvāt. yatnasādhya ita ūrdhvam ucyate — asaṃyatasamyagdṛṣṭyādiṣu caturṣu guṇasthāneṣu kasmiṃś cit saptaprakṛtikṣayaḥ kriyate. nidrānidrāpracalāpracalāstyānagṛddhinarakagatitiryaggatyekadvitricaturindriyajātinarakagatitiryaggatiprāyogyānupūrvyātapodyotasthāvarasūkṣmasādhāraṇasaṃjñikānāṃ ṣoḍaśānāṃ karmaprakṛtināmanivṛttibādarasāmparāyasthāne yugapat kṣayaḥ kriyate. tataḥ paraṃ tatraiva kaṣāyāṣṭakaṃ naṣṭaṃ kriyate. napuṃsakavedaḥ strīvedaś ca krameṇa tatraiva kṣayam upayāti. nokaṣāyaṣaṭkaṃ ca sahaikenaiva prahāreṇa vinipātayati. tataḥ puṃvedasaṃjvalanakrodhamānamāyāḥ krameṇa tatraivātyantikaṃ dvaṃsam āskandanti. lobhasaṃjvalanaḥ sūkṣmasāmparāyānte yātyantam. nidrāpracale kṣīṇakaṣāyavītarāgacchadmasthasyopāntyasamaye pralayam upavrajataḥ. paṃcānāṃ jñānāvaraṇānāṃ caturṇāṃ darśanāvaraṇānāṃ paṃcānām antarāyāṇāṃ ca tasyaivāntyasamaye prakṣayo bhavati. anyataravedanīyadevagatyaudārikavaikriyikāhārakataijasakārmaṇaśarī * -paṃcabandhanapaṃcasaṃghātasaṃsthānaṣaṭkaudārikavaikriyikāhārakaśarīrāṅgopāṅgaṣaṭsaṃhananapaṃcapraśastavarṇapaṃcāpraśastavarṇagandhadvayapaṃcapraśastarasapañcāpraśastarasasparśāṣṭakadevagatiprāyogyānupūrvyāgurulaghūpaghātaparaghātochvāsapraśastāpraśastavihāyogatyaparyāptakapratyekaśarīrasthirāsthiraśubhāśubhadurbhagasusvaraduḥsvarānādeyāyaśaḥkīrtinirmāṇanāmanīcair gotrākhyā dvāsaptatiprakṛtayo ’yogakevalina upāntyasamaye vināśam upayānti. anyataravedanīyamanuṣyāyurmanuṣyagatipañcendriyajātimanuṣyagatiprāyogyānupūrvītrasabādaraparyāptakasubhagādeyayaśaḥkīrtitīrthakaranāmoccairgotrasaṃjñikānāṃ trayodaśānāṃ prakṛtīnām ayogakevalinaś caramasamaye vyucchedo bhavati. 
 § 924. āha, kim āsāṃ paudgalikīnām eva dravyakarmaprakṛtīnāṃ nirāsān mokṣo ’vasīyate uta bhāvakarmaṇo ’pīty atrocyate — 
 aupaśamikādibhavyatvānāṃ ca || 
 § 925. kim? ‘mokṣaḥ’ ity anuvartate. bhavyatvagrahaṇam anyapāriṇāmikanivṛttyartham. tena pāriṇāmikeṣu bhavyatvasyaupaśamikādīnāṃ ca bhāvānām abhāvān mokṣo bhavatīty abhyupagamyate. 
 § 926. āha, yady apavargo bhāvoparateḥ pratijñāyate, nanu aupaśamikādibhāvanivṛttivatsarvakṣāyikabhāvanivṛttivyapadeśo muktasya prāpnotīti. syād etat evaṃ yadi viśeṣo nocyate. asty atra viśeṣa ity apavādavidhānārtham idam ucyate — 
 anyatra kevalasamyaktvajñānadarśanasiddhatvebhyaḥ || 
 § 927. anyatraśabdāpekṣayā ‘kā’ nirdeśaḥ. kevalasamyaktvajñānadarśanasiddhatvebhyo ’nyatrānyasminn ayaṃ vidhir iti. yadi catvāra evāvaśiṣyante, anantavīryādīnāṃ nivṛttiḥ prāpnoti? naiṣa doṣaḥ, jñānadarśanāvinābhāvitvād anantavīryādīnām aviśeṣaḥ, anantasāmarthyahīnasyānantāvabodhavṛttyabhāvāj jñānamayatvāc ca sukhasyeti. anākaratvān muktānām abhāva ity cen na; atītānantaraśarīrākāratvāt. 
 § 928. syān mataṃ, yadi śarīrānuvidhāyī jīvaḥ, tadabhāvāt svābhāvikalokākāśapradeśaparimāṇatvāt tāvad visarpaṇaṃ prāpnotīti. naiṣa doṣaḥ. kutaḥ? kāraṇāhāvāt. nāmakarmasaṃbandho hi saṃharaṇavisarpaṇakāraṇam. tadabhāvāt punaḥ saṃharaṇavisarpaṇābhāvaḥ. 
 § 929. yadi kāraṇābhāvān na saṃharaṇaṃ na visarpaṇaṃ tarhi gamanakāraṇābhāvād ūrdhvagamanam api na prāpnoti adhastiryaggamanābhāvāt, tato yatra muktas tatraivāvasthānaṃ prāpnotīty. atrocyate — 
 tadanantaram ūrdhvaṃ gacchatyā lokāntāt || 
 § 930. tasyānantaram. kasya? sarvakarmavipramokṣasya. āṅabhividhyarthaḥ. ūrdhvaṃ gacchatyā lokāntāt. 
 § 931. anupadiṣṭahetukam idam ūrdhvagamanaṃ katham adhyavasātum śakyam ity atrocyate — 
 pūrvayogād asaṅgatvād bandhacchedāt tathāgatipariṇāmāc ca || 
 § 932. āha, hetvarthaḥ puṣkalo ’pi dṛṣṭāntasamarthanam antareṇābhipretārthasādhanāya nālam ity atrocyate — 
 āviddhakulālacakravadvyapagatalepālābuvaderaṇḍabījavadagniśikhāvac ca || 
 § 933. pūrvasūtre vihitānāṃ hetūnām atroktānāṃ dṛṣṭāntānāṃ ca yathāsaṃkhyam abhisaṃbandho bhavati. tad yathā — kulālaprayogāpāditahastadaṇḍacakrasaṃyogapūrvakaṃ bhramaṇam. uparante ’pi tasmin pūrvaprayogād ā saṃskārakṣayād bhramati. evaṃ bhavasthenātmanāpavargaprāptaye bahuśo yatpraṇidhānaṃ tadabhāve ’pi tadāveśapūrvakaṃ muktasya gamanam avasīyate. kiṃ ca, asaṅgatvāt. yathā mṛttikālepajanitagauravam alābudravyaṃ jale ’dhaḥpatitaṃ jalakledaviśliṣṭamṛttikābandhanaṃ laghu sadūrdhvam eva gacchati tathā karmabhārākrāntivaśīkṛta ātmā tadāveśavaśāt saṃsāre aniyamena gacchati. tatsaṅgavimuktas tūparyevopayāti. kiṃ ca, bandhacchedāt. yathā bījakośabandhacchedāt eraṇḍabījasya gatir dṛṣṭā tathā manuṣyādibhavaprāpakagatijātināmādisakalakarmabandhacchedān muktasya ūrdhvagatir avasīyate. kiṃ ca, tathāgatipariṇāmāt. yathā tiryakplavanasvabhāvasamīraṇasaṃbandhanirutsukā pradīpaśikhā svabhāvād utpatati tathā muktātmāpi nānagativikārakāraṇakarmanirvāraṇe saty ūrdhvagatisvabhāvād ūrdhvam evārohati. 
 § 934. āha, yadi mukta ūrdhvagatisvabhāvo lokāntād ūrdhvam api kasmān notpatatīty atrocyate — 
 dharmāstikāyābhāvād || 
 § 935. gatyupagrahakāraṇabhūto dharmāstikāyo nopary astīty aloke gamanābhāvaḥ. tadabhāve ca lokālokavibhāgābhāvaḥ prasajyate. 
 § 936. āha, amī parinivṛttā gatijātyādibhedakāraṇābhāvād atītabhedavyavahārā eveti. asti kathaṃcid bhedo ’pi. kutaḥ — 
 kṣetrakālagatiliṅgatīrthacāritrapratyekabudddhabodhitajñānāvagāhanāntarasaṃkyālpabahutvataḥ sādhyāḥ || 
 § 937. kṣetrādibhir dvādaśābhir anuyogaiḥ siddhāḥ sadhyā vikalpyā ity arthaḥ, pratyutpannabhūtānugrahatantranayadvayavivakṣāvaśāt. tad yathā — kṣetreṇa tāvat kasmin kṣetre sidhyanti? pratyutpannagrāhinayāpekṣayā siddhikṣtre svapradeśe ākāśapradeśe vā siddhir bhavati. bhūtagrāhinayāpekṣayā janma prati pañcadaśasu karmabhūmiṣu, saṃharaṇaṃ prati mānuṣyakṣetre siddhiḥ. kālena kasmin kāle siddhiḥ? pratyutpannanayāpekṣayā ekasamaye siddhyan siddho bhavati. bhūtaprajñāpananayāpekṣayā janmato ’viśeṣeṇotsarpiṇyavasarpiṇyor jātaḥ sidhyati. viśeṣeṇāvarsarpiṇyāṃ suṣamaduḥṣamāyā antye bhāge duḥṣamasuṣamāyāṃ ca jātaḥ sidhyati. na tu duḥṣamāyāṃ jāto duḥṣamāyāṃ sidhyati. anyadā naiva sidhyati. saṃharaṇataḥ sarvasmin kāle utsarpiṇyām avasarpiṇyāṃ ca sidhyati. gatyā kasyāṃ gatau siddhiḥ? siddhigatau manuṣyagatau vā. liṃgena kena siddhiḥ? avedatvena tribhyo vā vedebhyaḥ siddhir bhāvito na dravyataḥ. dravyataḥ pulliṃgenaiva. athavā nirgranthaliṃgena. sagranthaliṃgena vā siddhir bhūtapūrvanayāpekṣayā. tīrthena, tīrthasiddhiḥ dvedhā tīrthakaretaravikalpāt. itare dvividhāḥ sati tīrthakare siddhā asati ceti. cāritreṇa kena sidhyati. avyapadeśenaikacatuḥpañcavikalpacāritreṇa vā siddhiḥ. svaśaktiparopadeśanimittajñānabhedāt pratyekabuddhabodhitavikalpaḥ. jñānena kena? ekena dvitricaturbhiś ca jñānaviśeṣaiḥ siddhiḥ. ātmapradeśavyāpitvam avagāhanam. tad dvividham, utkṛṣṭajaghanyabhedāt. tatrotkṛṣṭaṃ paṃcadhanuḥśatāni pañcaviṃśatyuttarāṇi. jaghanyam ardhacaturthāratnayo deṣonāḥ. madhye vikalpāḥ. ekasminn avagāhe sidhyati. kim antaram? sidhyatāṃ siddhānām anantaraṃ jaghanyena dvau samayau utkarṣeṇāṣṭau. antaraṃ jaghanyenaikaḥ samayaḥ utkarṣeṇa ṣaṇmāsāḥ. saṃkhyā, jaghanyena ekasamaye ekaḥ sidhyati. utkarṣeṇāṣṭottaraśatasaṃkhyāḥ. kṣetrādibhedabhinnānāṃ parasparataḥ saṃkhyāviśesṣo ’lpabahutvam. tad yathā — pratyutpannanayāpekṣayā siddhikṣetre sidhyantīti nāsty alpabahutvam. bhūtapūrvanayāpekṣayā tu cintyate, kṣetrasiddhā dvividhā — janmataḥ saṃharaṇataś ca. tatrālpe saṃharaṇasiddhāḥ. janmasiddhāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. kṣetrāṇāṃ vibhāgaḥ karmabhūmir akarmabhūmiḥ samudro dvīpa ūrdhvam adhas tiryag iti. tatra stokā ūrdhvalokasiddhāḥ. adholokasiddhāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. tiryaglokasiddhāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. sarvataḥ stokāḥ samudrasiddhāḥ. dvīpasiddhāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. evaṃ tāvad aviśeṣeṇa. sarvataḥ stokā lavaṇodasiddhāḥ. kālodasiddhāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. jambūdvīpasiddhāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. dhātakīkhaṇḍasiddhāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇāḥ. puṣkaradvīpārdhasiddhāḥ saṃkhyeyaguṇā iti. evaṃ kālādivibhāge ’pi yathā gamam alpabahutvaṃ veditavyam. || TAS 10 || 
 § 938.
	   
 svargāpavargasukham āptumanobhir āryair jainendraśāsanavarāmṛtasārabhūtā | 
 sarvārthasiddhir iti sadbhir upāttanāmā tattvārthavṛttir aniśaṃ manasā pradhāryā || 1 || 
 
 
 tattvārthavṛttim uditāṃ viditārthatattvāḥ śṛṇvanti ye paripaṭhanti ca dharmabhaktyā | 
 haste kṛtaṃ paramasiddhisukhāmṛtaṃ tair martyāmareśvarasukheṣu kim asti vācyam ||2|| 
 
 
 yenedam apratihataṃ sakalārthatattvam udyotitaṃ vimalakevalalocanena | 
 bhaktyā tam adbhutaguṇaṃ praṇamāmi vīramārānnarāmaragaṇārcitapādapīṭham || 3 || 
 
 
 iti tattvārthavṛttau sarvārthasiddhisaṃjñikāyāṃ daśamo ’dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ | 
 
 śubhaṃ bhavatu sarveṣām | 
 
 
	Notes to the transcript of Pūjyapāda’s Sarvārthasiddhi
	 Based on the [Digambara] edition by Phūlcandra Śāstrī:
	Srīmadācāryapūjyapādavirācitā sarvārthasiddhiḥ [with a Hindi translation, not included]
	Delhi: Bhāratīya Jñānapīṭha (fifth edition, 1991). A note is indicated by a superscript asterisk (*) in a § (almost always at the end of a sentence):
